Chapter 1680: Binding Mountains and Seas with Ropes

"The annihilation of the Mountains and Seas, the descent of the Star. What I witnessed just now was not a mere illusion, but a true event." The solitary star hung high, tearing through the desolate void like a divine gaze. Whenever Li Fan recalled this scene, a chill ran down his spine, as if an unknown entity within the desolate void was staring at him. But now, the Star was nowhere to be seen, and the Mountains and Seas had returned to their final, dilapidated state.

"The river of time exists only in reliance on the Mountains and Seas. After the destruction of the Mountains and Seas, it can return to its origin. This is not simply a matter of time reversal."

"It is the reversal of everything that has already occurred."

"The transformation of True and False?" Though filled with disbelief, everything Li Fan had experienced at the end of the Mountains and Seas seemed to unequivocally point to this conclusion. A fire seemed to burn in Li Fan's throat. If Qiu Xin Hui's path to Sainthood was the transformation of True and False, Then what exactly was 'True Return'? Li Fan stared intently at the phrase "True becomes false, false also becomes true" on the 'True Return' panel, countless questions swirling in his mind. Until Qiu Xin Hui, who had just healed the people of the Realm of Birth and Death, stood before him once more. Since the existence of 'True Return' had already been exposed, Li Fan had nothing left to hide. He directly voiced his doubts.

"The Great Dao of True and False..." The white-haired Qiu Xin Hui's eyes shimmered with longing, momentarily lost in thought. Then, with a sigh, he shook his head. "Only possesses [False becomes True], but not [True becomes False]."

This answer was both unexpected and reasonable. "False becomes True" was a further manifestation of the imaginary Dao. Recalling carefully, after the annihilation of the Mountains and Seas and the demise of the Saints, Qiu Xin Hui had single-handedly reversed the tide by continuously summoning Saints from nothingness to uphold the imaginary Mountains and Seas against the desolate void. This did indeed exhibit the essence of "[False becomes True]."

Li Fan let out a long sigh of relief. At the same time, his doubts only grew. He had not expected that the "True and False Transformation" of 'True Return' would have a counterpart in this world.

"A long time ago, before I achieved Sainthood, I witnessed the scene of the Mountains and Seas' annihilation."

"All the past events were vivid in my mind. Despair and regret filled my chest."

"As my own existence was about to vanish, guided by an unseen force, I comprehended the Dao of [False becomes True] amidst the final light of the Mountains and Seas."

"In the midst of annihilation and nothingness, I recreated the [End of the Mountains and Seas]..." Qiu Xin Hui spoke slowly, filled with emotion. As if sensing Li Fan's doubts, he continued without waiting for a question: "I was born at the end of the Mountains and Seas, and I grew up at the end of the Mountains and Seas."

"Furthermore, I achieved my Dao at the end of the Mountains and Seas. My entire life has been confined to this place. Although I can glimpse the past of the Mountains and Seas through mere fragments of light and shadow, it is only a limited perspective. To recreate the imaginary Mountains and Seas, I still have enough power."

"To truly recreate the full glory of the Mountains and Seas..." Qiu Xin Hui sighed, "My strength is insufficient."

"If you were to traverse {backwards in time} to the more ancient Mountains and Seas, to witness their complete form, would you not be able to achieve it?" Li Fan asked thoughtfully.

"With your strength, surely you could do it?" Li Fan was naturally referring to Qiu Xin Hui's ability to continuously summon Saints to resist the desolate void's encroachment.

To his surprise, Qiu Xin Hui gently shook his head, negating it.

"Traversing downstream is already arduous."

"To travel upstream is even more difficult. Daoist Friend Fan, you underestimate the dangers involved."

"Furthermore, if the Saints are still present, how can I recreate them?" Qiu Xin Hui pointed out the most critical factor. Li Fan suddenly understood. The Qiu Xin Hui he witnessed previously displaying his divine abilities was after the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas had sacrificed themselves. The Great Daos wielded by the Saints were now vacant, left unclaimed. Therefore, Qiu Xin Hui could summon phantom bodies and re-appropriate the Great Daos, wielding Saintly power. But in the current timeline, with the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas still alive… Imagination could only conjure the form, but not the power. Though the reasoning was sound, Li Fan felt a sense of skepticism.

"How does it matter? Telling the Saints the specific situation and reasons, I believe they would be willing to sacrifice themselves for the salvation of the Mountains and Seas. If that doesn't work, then find an opportunity..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, His gaze carrying a hidden glint of ruthlessness. Qiu Xin Hui immediately saw through Li Fan's thoughts and could only offer a wry smile.

"All the Saints came here at my summons, so how could I betray their trust?"

"We are united in our efforts to save the world. Their sacrifice represents one matter."

"Harm them while they are alive, even plotting against them, is another matter entirely."

"I will not do that," the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, Qiu Xin Hui, stated with utmost seriousness.

"Pedantic," Li Fan muttered inwardly, shaking his head. However, he did not argue with Qiu Xin Hui. Instead, he suddenly recalled something else. If, according to this final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, the Great Daos wielded by the Saints were inaccessible to others while they were alive, Then...

"What is the relationship between 'True Return's' transformation of True and False and Qiu Xin Hui's control?"

Qiu Xin Hui continued, "In the beginning of the Mountains and Seas, other Saints went there. My plan is indeed as I stated earlier: to use the imaginary Mountains and Seas, at the juncture of old and new, to seek a sliver of hope for survival."

"Through our repeated attempts, we seem to have finally glimpsed a glimmer of hope."

"Until... today, when we finally witnessed the face of the [Star]."

The terrifying image of the solitary Star hanging high flashed before Li Fan's eyes. Faint, forgotten memories resurfaced.

"After you called me to act... what exactly happened?" Li Fan's heart skipped a beat, and he hastily asked. Qiu Xin Hui looked at him carefully and shook his head slightly. "Daoist Friend Fan has his own destiny. If I were to easily reveal it, it would be detrimental to you."

"What happened is ultimately irrelevant. You only need to know that our struggle was futile the moment the [Star] appeared."

"Fortunately, there was still a turning point..." Qiu Xin Hui looked directly at Li Fan. Even though the enigmatic Qiu Xin Hui spoke ambiguously, Li Fan could broadly guess what had happened to him. It was also what he had always feared. 'True Return' had lost control and acted on its own, seemingly possessing his body. A shadow flickered in his eyes, and Li Fan felt a fire ignite within him. Though extremely angry, Li Fan pondered and realized he had no effective countermeasures. After all, he couldn't truly break his own barrier of true spirits and bring about mutual destruction. The situation had not yet reached that point. Without Qiu Xin Hui needing to persuade him, Li Fan quickly convinced himself, forcibly suppressing the anger in his eyes.

Witnessing the change in Li Fan's expression, Qiu Xin Hui nodded inwardly.

"For this operation, Daoist friend need not act. Simply observe silently."

"When everything settles down, you can then..."

"'Return to True.'" When Qiu Xin Hui uttered the words "[True Return]," Li Fan's heart couldn't help but skip a beat. This was the first time since his reincarnation that Li Fan had heard his 'True Return' mentioned by another person. Even though he had anticipated the exposure of 'True Return's' existence, The confirmation of his suspicions filled him with extreme unease.

"What about the true spirit infusion?" He chose to change the subject.

"It was merely futile; Daoist Friend Fan need not trouble himself," Qiu Xin Hui said with a smile, cupping his hands and departing. Thus, in this cycle of reincarnation at the end of the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan was like an invisible bystander. Although the other Saints knew of his existence, they only recognized him by his [Profound Embryo] identity. He did not participate in the Saints' plan to save the world. In the frozen end of the Mountains and Seas, time held no true significance. After an unknown period, not by the white-haired scholar's own will, but due to his exhaustion and demise. The river of time surged forth, carrying everyone towards their final destination. Without Li Fan's true spirit infusion, the imaginary Mountains and Seas performed even worse. They could barely withstand the full power of the desolate void's encroachment, Let alone face the solitary Star. Before even glimpsing the Star's face, the imaginary Mountains and Seas, along with the Saints, perished.

"All Saints are present!" Qiu Xin Hui's solemn declaration echoed alone in the darkness. Even though he knew his fate and the predetermined end, he did not abandon his struggle. Until, the desolate void's surging tides attacked, completely engulfing the imaginary light.

"Daoist Friend Fan..."

"It is time."

"This time, the experience may be different from before." Qiu Xin Hui's final words drifted through the air. And within the dark tide, Li Fan, having finally broken free from the confines of the Profound Embryo Great Dao, softly called out to 'True Return' once more. His heart leaped, his expression tense. Fortunately, there were no surprises. That familiar sensation finally returned. And as Qiu Xin Hui had said, this time the experience was indeed different. The characteristic billowing white mist of 'True Return' did not appear. Instead, Li Fan felt a peculiar and immense power isolating him from the surrounding desolate void, protecting his safety. It was as if he had returned to the womb; all restlessness and anxiety vanished, replaced by complete tranquility. Even though 'True Return' had not yet activated, seemingly waiting for some change to occur, Li Fan felt no tension whatsoever. He waited quietly alongside it. When the last spark of light from the imaginary Mountains and Seas was swallowed by darkness. When the two residual light dots of the original Mountains and Seas finally vanished. The turbulent desolate void fell into a brief silence. Then, the void unleashed unprecedented, rampaging waves, as if celebrating in wild revelry, heralding the arrival of an Emperor. Though unable to perceive these turbulent waves, Li Fan could sense their presence through the increasingly vibrating tremors within himself. Their power was several times greater than when they had engulfed the Mountains and Seas, and even 'True Return's' protection was severely impacted.

"This is the true full power of the desolate void."

At the same time, Li Fan understood what 'True Return' had been waiting for. It was waiting for the descent of the [Star]. Compared to before, when it directly tore through the desolate void and appeared in view. This time, the [Star] rose like the morning sun above the horizon. Initially, the Star's radiance was not very dazzling. But with each passing moment of its existence, the pressure it exerted on the outside world increased exponentially. 'True Return's' protection, like being caught in a hurricane, creaked and groaned. The desolate void also churned as if boiling. Bathed in the Star's unique radiance, the darkness evaporated completely. Where darkness had been, there was now only the peculiar brilliance of the Star. The Star's power was simply too overbearing. Except for itself, it tolerated no other existence. Not even the desolate void. Under the Star's illumination, the darkness evaporated. All that could be seen was the solitary Star, beginning to expand endlessly. Before the Star. Li Fan, protected by the power of 'True Return,' felt an uncontrollable urge to flee. At the same time, he understood the futility of Qiu Xin Hui's plan. Schemes of leaping out, of merging with the [Star]. All were pure nonsense. After the Star's descent, all would cease to exist. Except for the Star itself. What a terrifying power! Li Fan trembled uncontrollably. Even though he closed his eyes and severed his spiritual senses, Coupled with 'True Return's' protection. He could not stop the Star from slowly ascending within his mind. Its image grew larger and larger, as if poised to consume him entirely. The Star's divine pressure, the unfathomable disparity in strength, left Li Fan's mind blank. He could not even muster the thought of escape. His mind went blank, and he could only face his impending doom, silently awaiting death. Just then. A stream of seven-colored light drifted from nowhere. It was the familiar phrase Li Fan knew so well: "When true becomes false, false also becomes true!" The stream of light seemed to be cleaved in two, scattering with a resounding boom. The portion "When true becomes false" transformed into a sky full of light and shadows, confronting the solitary Star. The Star's endless expansion abruptly halted. As if a hand emerged from beneath the horizon, Forcibly dragging back the [Star] that had already leaped above the sea! This power was slow but firm. Irresistible and immutable, even for the Star! The solitary star trembled, filled with extreme rage. The Star's radiance seemed to erupt, blindingly intense a thousandfold. Judging from its previous display, perhaps the entire desolate void would have evaporated under this sudden burst of starlight. But at this moment, all that radiance was blocked by the four words of brilliance, "When true becomes false." The Star's fury, compared to before, seemed to have no effect. The two lights competed fiercely. Li Fan, who had witnessed the entire scene, was utterly stunned. Even though he was like an ant compared to the Star and 'True Return,' He was not completely incapable of understanding. His reincarnations through countless lifetimes, and his comprehension of the "True and False Transformation," were not in vain! At this moment, Li Fan's fear of the Star had completely vanished, replaced by an overwhelming excitement. He muttered to himself, "When true becomes false, when true becomes false..." "So that's how it is." "It's actually like this!" Li Fan had always believed that "true becomes false" referred to all Great Dao entities within the Mountains and Seas. Only now, after personally witnessing the brilliance of 'True Return' contending with the Star, did Li Fan finally comprehend. "[True becomes False] does not refer to the myriad things within the Mountains and Seas." "Or rather, it's not just the Mountains and Seas." "Most importantly..." "To erase the light of the Star's descent!" "To eliminate the Star's influence!" Li Fan's mind roared. "Only possesses [False becomes True], but not [True becomes False]," Qiu Xin Hui's complex expression recurred. Only now did Li Fan understand the meaning of those words. "Could the power of 'True Return' be limited to this?" Li Fan exclaimed in disbelief. Li Fan's internal emotions did not affect the external world in the slightest. In the direct confrontation, 'True Return' ultimately prevailed. The Star's radiance slowly dissipated. The darkness of the desolate void reappeared. When all returned to calm, the remaining three characters of "False becomes True" from the seven-colored stream of light... Exploded silently. Transforming into boundless Mountains and Seas, pushing back the desolate void. Li Fan, without time to fully process his emotions, was enveloped and drawn into it.

Chapter 1681: Sins of Bai Xiao Immortal

The Ten Thousand Ancient Heavenly Steps, collectively known as the bluestone slabs suspended on the river of time, served to aid those on the other shore who were not adept at the "Reverse" technique in traversing the river of time. Li Fan was unsure if there were other special uses.

At this moment, after deliberation, the Saints settled on a plan. The white circle emanated a faint jade-like glow, and the phantom image of the river of time split as if by a blade. Two figures appeared to be imprisoned beneath the Ten Thousand Ancient Heavenly Steps, as if bearing the weight of the entire river of time and countless bluestone steps, they sat with their legs crossed and heads bowed. Although they sensed the disturbance above, they could not look up.

Not both were released; only one was chosen, its form bound by white light like ropes, and brought before the Saints. As the jade-like light receded, the river of time closed once more, and the figure within, no longer seen. The summoned cultivator, perhaps due to prolonged imprisonment, remained motionless like a statue even after gaining freedom. The rope-like light instantly retracted. He frowned slightly and opened his eyes. Gazing at the twelve Saintly figures before him, towering like giants, a hint of confusion flashed in the cultivator's eyes.

"What year is it now?"

He distinctly remembered that when he was suppressed, there were only nine Saints in the other shore. How had the number suddenly jumped to twelve? "And I, of all people, was released."

"Could it be that the conflict between the Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm has already concluded?" A myriad of doubts arose in his heart, but facing the Saints, he dared not show disrespect.

"Junior Bai Xiao pays his respects to all Saints!"

"Having been suppressed for many years, have you reflected?" The karmic judge's phantom voice boomed, echoing like thunder, enveloping the scene. Bai Xiao Xian, however, remained unfazed and sighed softly, "Naturally, I have. I only regret acting too slowly and being discovered by the Saints. One misstep leads to a thousand years of regret..."

Seeing Bai Xiao Xian's unrepentant demeanor, the Saints' phantom images did not get angry. "The Heart's Desire is already destroyed, and you have been suppressed for a long time. Now, an opportunity has arisen for you to atone for your crimes. Are you willing?" the karmic judge continued to ask.

"To atone for my crimes?" Bai Xiao Xian was slightly stunned. "Can I truly regain my freedom?"

"Not only can you regain your freedom, but you can even ascend to Sainthood in one step," Duke Shou Qiu stated. Duke Shou Qiu's words clearly carried more weight in Bai Xiao Xian's heart. Upon hearing these incredible words, he was immediately shaken.

"If it is true, then Junior is naturally willing!"

"You agreed so quickly? Know that once you agree, there is no turning back."

"Given your past actions, we will also leave a restraint within you. Even with a Saintly body, escape will be difficult. If you break your promise, we will shatter your soul on the spot. This must be made clear beforehand," the Lianshan phantom image said. Bai Xiao Xian, however, appeared as if it were logical:

"Being suppressed under the Ten Thousand Ancient Heavenly Steps for countless years, until the Mountains and Seas were destroyed. Or perhaps there is a chance to achieve a Saintly body. Even if I must be controlled by others..."

"How can I not distinguish between these two choices?"

"The reason I chose to use [Heart's Desire] to 'attract the Star's gaze' back then was because I had no hope of becoming a Saint."

...

Without Li Fan needing to speak, the newly promoted Saint Jin Gui, after hearing Bai Xiao Xian's words, was the first to inquire. "This person actually intended to 'attract the Star's gaze'? Can he still be entrusted with important tasks?"

Duke Shou Qiu nodded, "Once one becomes a Saint, they are naturally on our side, with no risk of rebellion. Fellow Daoist, do not worry."

"As for his previous act of communicating with the Star..."

After Duke Shou Qiu's explanation, the three newly promoted Saints finally understood the entire story. It was almost identical to the version told by Wu Liang Bi in the cycle of reincarnation.

Originally, Bai Xiao Xian had comprehended the Dao's Shadow and, using it, forged a peculiar immortal artifact, [Heart's Desire]. This immortal artifact could act like a person's shadow, peeking into the paths and minds of the myriad immortals. And utilize their power for oneself. By rights, with such a treasure in hand before transcending, Bai Xiao Xian should have had limitless potential. Unfortunately, he was both blessed and cursed by [Heart's Desire]. The paths and minds of all beings were too vast and profound, too full of wonder. Once engrossed, he became unable to extricate himself. Lingering and forgetting, he neglected his own cultivation. Moreover, Bai Xiao Xian knew all the secrets of all beings, yet had no one to share them with, keeping everything bottled up in his heart. Over time, he grew increasingly frustrated. Eventually, unable to bear it any longer, he secretly found someone to confide in. Truly, a heart like a horse galloping on a plain, easily unleashed but difficult to restrain. The awe of others upon learning earth-shattering secrets, and the pleasure of revealing all his knowledge, brought Bai Xiao Xian immense satisfaction. Tasting the sweetness of it, Bai Xiao Xian became addicted, unable to stop. Even the secrets of Immortal Emperors became topics of his boasting. Relying on the miraculous nature of the Dao's Shadow, he repeatedly escaped capture. Thus, Bai Xiao Xian became even more unrestrained in his words. Until he intended to leak the secret of the "[Tomb of Scriptures]."

"The Tomb of Scriptures devours the Dao and starts the cycle, upon the desolate grave."

"Do you know what the true form of the Great Sage of the Tomb of Scriptures is?"

"Heh heh, if you knew, you would surely find it unbelievable..." While the crowd watched, Bai Xiao Xian spoke smugly.

"Brother Bai Xiao, stop playing coy. Tell us quickly." Seeing the eager gazms of the surrounding immortals, just as Bai Xiao Xian was about to speak, a gust of black wind suddenly blew. The onlookers, in an instant, were swept away and swallowed by that Great Sage of the Tomb of Scriptures. Bai Xiao Xian, protected by the Dao's Shadow, narrowly escaped death, but was suddenly awakened. He had spoken recklessly and offended someone he shouldn't have! However, the Great Sage of the Tomb of Scriptures, acting on impulse, ignored Bai Xiao Xian's pleas and was determined to swallow him, silencing him forever. Bai Xiao Xian hid and dodged, eventually running out of options. In desperation, he hardened his heart and actually conceived the idea of luring Dao Annihilation to bring about mutual destruction. If the confrontation between the Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation were considered a war, then the Bai Xiao Xian, who had comprehended the Dao's Shadow divine ability, if he defected, would be equivalent to a top spy who knew most of the secrets of the Mountains and Seas. He could greatly alter the course of the struggle between the two sides. Therefore, Bai Xiao Xian's act of betrayal went unexpectedly smoothly. He merely showed a hint of his intention, and Dao Annihilation surged unprecedentedly. Within Dao Annihilation, a consciousness could even be faintly heard. Urging him to defect to Dao Annihilation while also promising him a bright future. But just as he was about to completely rebel, the Saints Lianshan and Guihai acted, directly suppressing him.

...

"In the Void Realm, the foundations of all existence are gone. How can there be a bright future?" Jin Gui shook his head. "Perhaps it's a transformation of form. The tide of Dao Annihilation has its own consciousness. Moreover, what about the [Star] after Dao Annihilation? According to Bai Xiao Xian, when he communicated with the consciousness within Dao Annihilation, he clearly felt a vaster, even superior, intent. Hidden deep within Dao Annihilation, yet seemingly lurking beneath the darkness."

"He instinctively felt that if he sacrificed the Dao's Shadow of the Mountains and Seas as a sacrifice, he might be able to attract that attention."

"At that time, within Dao Annihilation, it would also be a scene of cataclysm..." Duke Shou Qiu spoke very calmly, his thoughts unreadable.

"Saints, what do you think of the truthfulness of Bai Xiao Xian's words?" Li Fan finally spoke, asking the Saints' phantom images for their opinions.

"There are no lies. However, it doesn't mean it's entirely true."

"Even we find it difficult to sense the true face of the Star. Even if the Star truly appeared before us, perhaps Bai Xiao Xian couldn't have perceived it. It's possible it was purely his illusion," the karmic judge Saint shook his head.

Duke Shou Qiu added, "However, this person's talent is indeed extraordinary. He was simply blinded before. Being suppressed by us in the Ten Thousand Ancient Heavenly Steps, with no secrets to pry, he could only focus on his cultivation. In these years, he has progressed further, reaching the realm of Transcendence."

"You Saints are indeed kind-hearted. To allow such a heinous criminal to have another chance to cultivate," Li Fan said with a smile.

"If he cannot become a Saint, even if he is heinous, he will be easily suppressed by us. If he can become a Saint??"

"After achieving Sainthood, he will naturally return to our side. What's the harm in letting him cultivate?" the karmic judge Saint said indifferently.

...

While the Saints conversed, Bai Xiao Xian had already regained his freedom. "It's a pity my Jade Ruyi is gone. It would be impossible to forge it anew," he muttered softly, glancing at the Saints present. "After achieving Sainthood, one's perspective naturally changes. The myriad beings of the Mountains and Seas are all like ants. What joys are there?" it was the Prying Opportunity Saint who spoke. The Prying Opportunity phantom image had remained silent for the most part. This time, when it spoke, Li Fan vaguely sensed a cold, snake-like aura circulating in the area. The portion of the Mountains and Seas' fortuitous encounters obtained from the remains of the Primal Origin King, due to the appearance of this cold aura, completely dissipated. As if stolen! It was not intentional on Prying Opportunity's part, but a natural anomaly triggered by its opening its mouth! Bai Xiao Xian also seemed to sense the inexplicable change in himself, his expression shifting slightly. However, he gritted his teeth and retorted, "Seniors are not ants, how would they know the joys of ants?"

Prying Opportunity no longer spoke, and the cold aura dissipated. Bai Xiao Xian felt bored and said dully, "Seniors, please proceed!"

The white circle suddenly shrank, condensing into Bai Xiao Xian's head. "Everyone just needs to leave a trace of power within it," Lord Tai Yi slowly said. The Saints each displayed their divine abilities, and rays of light flickered within the white circle. As if twelve Saintly phantoms were stationed within. Li Fan naturally left a wisp of his [Profound Embryo] aura within. In his perception, the power of the Saints residing within Bai Xiao Xian's body was no different from the other shore's white circle. As if the limitation of "within Bai Xiao Xian's body" did not exist. The white circle emitted a faint glow, completely integrating into Bai Xiao Xian's body. It seemed to disappear, but in reality, it had merged with him, becoming inseparable. Bai Xiao Xian's thoughts and actions, every move, were under the gaze and control of the Saints. Even after becoming a Saint, it would be the same!

"I have spied on all beings for a long time, yet in the latter half of my life, I have fallen into a fate of being watched by others," Bai Xiao Xian shook his head slightly, seemingly resigned, not caring much about his predicament. "We are not so bored as to pry into your heart. We are merely taking precautions. After all, this endeavor involves connecting the great undertaking of the Mountains and Seas; we cannot afford any mistakes," Duke Shou Qiu said with a solemn expression.

"Perhaps so," Bai Xiao Xian muttered inwardly, shaking his head, "I should still bow to the Saints again."

With the three suitable Transcendent cultivators now assembled, it was time for Li Fan to showcase his skills. Whether before or after becoming a Saint, the scale of Accumulated True Spirits he could summon remained largely unchanged. However, it was still enough to astonish onlookers. Bai Xiao Xian and the other two Transcendent beings silently operated the [Myriad Lives Boundless] technique. Li Fan summoned the Accumulated True Spirits, showering them down like a waterfall. As the phantom bodies of the three absorbed them, their cultivation aptitude increased almost visibly, filling the gap that they could never have crossed in their lifetimes. The Saints watched in silence. After a long time, when Li Fan had finished, the phantom image of Saint Gui Hai sighed, "Even seeing it again, this technique remains incredibly miraculous. It's a pity we cannot meet the Saint of the End of the Mountains and Seas."

"Perhaps after Dao Annihilation recedes and the Mountains and Seas are reshaped, we will have the chance to meet,"

...

Among the three Transcendent beings, except for Bai Xiao Xian, the other two followed the path of Sainthood through [Myriad Lives Unite]. Their respective Daos were [Square Inch] and [Great Qi]. As for Bai Xiao Xian... it was somewhat similar to the True Moral Immortal. Utilizing his unique characteristics, he established a separate realm within the Mountains and Seas, achieving Sainthood.

"It seems that Saints like Duke Shou Qiu, who naturally possess a Great Dao of the same level as the Mountains and Seas, are indeed rare."

"But it's just taking different paths. It's hard to say whose strength is truly greater." For instance, the karmic judge clearly did not possess the origin of the Mountains and Seas Great Dao. Yet, Li Fan instinctively felt that this person was not to be trifled with. In fact, his threat level was even higher than Duke Shou Qiu's.

"As for the other Saints..."

"Although we are in the same room, it's as if we are in a white fog, difficult to discern." These were merely Saintly phantoms. Even the newly promoted Saints Jin Gui and True Moral were still like this. This showed that after becoming a Saint, profound mysteries naturally arose. Even while sitting there immobile, their strength increased exponentially, beyond ordinary speculation.

"It seems that being clad in the outer garment of the Profound Embryo Great Dao is ultimately different from truly achieving Sainthood oneself," Li Fan secretly warned himself.

The three Transcendent beings, even after receiving the infusion of True Spirits, still needed time to achieve Sainthood. Fortunately, Emperor Tai Wei sent three more great elixirs as assistance. With the combined efforts of all parties, on this day, three more Saints appeared in the Mountains and Seas! However, unlike before, it was not earth-shattering. Masked by the radiance of the other shore's white circle, they did not manifest in the mortal world.

"Greetings, fellow Daoist!" The Saints present exchanged pleasantries. After becoming Saints, their identities were equal, with no distinction in status. This was true even for Bai Xiao, who was being monitored by the Saints.

"After a little preparation, we can set out for the Void Realm."

"The first time is for the newly promoted Saints to familiarize themselves with the conditions in the Void Realm. If they are uncomfortable, they can withdraw at any time," the Duke Shou Qiu phantom image said sternly.

"Flowing against the current to cross requires not only adhering to the path's foundation and preserving one's existence, but also, most importantly, [Discerning Ancient and Modern]." It was the Lianshan Saint's phantom image who was teaching the newly promoted Saints.

"Maintaining the foundation of one's existence is to resist the Void Realm's Dao Annihilation. What does [Discerning Ancient and Modern] mean?" The newly promoted Saint Fang Cun asked confusedly.

"In the Eternal Void Realm, it is a vast expanse of darkness. It is not just ancient and modern, but two directions. 'Modern' refers to the direction from which we came. 'Ancient' is our destination. As for other places..."

"Endless, infinite. If the initial direction is wrong, even if you have divine power and can withstand the Void Realm's erosion for ten million years, everything you see will still be void." The Lianshan Saint gently waved his hand, and together with Saint Gui Hai, they projected a scene of darkness to the Saints. Covered by a darkness like ominous clouds, Li Fan felt his senses stripped away. The surrounding Saintly figures, one after another, disappeared. It was as if he had truly fallen into the boundless void. The void's dead silence even began to erode his foundation of existence. Vast and boundless, without distinction of up or down, left or right, even self and other. Let alone anything else! Where is the ancient? Where is the modern? Forget about traversing and reaching further into the past. Even returning to the Mountains and Seas, which they had just left, became a problem!

"This is merely a simulated scenario by Saints Lianshan and Gui Hai??"

"The true Eternal Void Realm is actually so terrifying." Li Fan felt a sense of gravity in his heart. Although he had traversed the Void Realm before, he had done so by flowing with the current, all the way to the end of the Mountains and Seas. Most importantly, relying on the connection between Qiu Xin Hui's imagined clone and the main body, he could accurately determine his direction. He had no worries about getting lost. But now, without a guiding beacon, the difficulty was vastly different.

After a while, the two Saints dispelled the simulated void darkness. The newly promoted Saints, who reappeared in the projected image, all wore solemn expressions, just like Li Fan. "Everyone need not worry excessively. In the Void Realm, the strong set the path. In the true Eternal Void Realm, our main bodies already exist. For example, like knots on a rope, one only needs to use the closest Saint's Dao as an anchor." Lord Tai Yi's phantom image spoke to comfort them.

"According to our past calculations, to reconnect ourselves and the previous section of the Mountains and Seas, and to communicate across the vast Void Realm, requires at least thirteen Saints working together. But that is the extreme situation, with no room for error. Even the slightest accident could not only lead to complete failure but also the potential demise of the thirteen Saints."

"Therefore, we have been making preparations all along and have not truly begun. But now, with the creation brought by fellow Daoist Xuan Pin..."

"With six new Saints, while it's not entirely foolproof, the risk has indeed decreased significantly," Duke Shou Qiu said, looking at Li Fan slowly.

"The path through the Void Realm, the advanced lead the way. Before everyone truly enters the Eternal Void Realm, you must first discuss the order. The latter must follow closely behind the former, with no room for error. Otherwise, one wrong step leads to a cascade of errors," the karmic judge's phantom image said very seriously.

"Now, the sequence for the nine of us is set. The most ancient, and therefore the first, is Lianshan. Then successively Guihai, Tai Yi, Prying Opportunity, Guiming, Duancha, Shou Qiu..."

"Me, and Xing Cha."

"As for how you should be ranked, perhaps you can compete first." The six newly promoted Saints exchanged glances, most of them showing eagerness in their eyes.

"Real combat is bound to cause friction. Why not follow our old method, within this [Zuan Ji Ring], each differentiate a phantom image?" Before the Lianshan Saint Lord's voice could finish, the other shore's white circle had already brightened. Under the shining light, the six new Saints, under the gaze of the nine Saints, "Heh heh, I had this intention long ago!" The first to respond was Jin Gui. As his phantom image entered, the remaining Saints had no reason to refuse. In an instant, each differentiated a phantom image and entered the Zuan Ji Ring.

"Within the Zuan Ji Ring, one can see the whole from a small part. Fellow Daoists, if you intend to hide your strength, it will not work," Duke Shou Qiu said cheerfully. The six newly promoted Saints remained expressionless, nodding in response. The white circle's radiance seemed to transform into a battlefield. The Saints' phantom images entered, like points of light. Within the Zuan Ji Ring, time seemed to be accelerated infinitely. Every moment, the Saints' points of light were constantly and violently colliding. For Saints, even if it were just a differentiated phantom image, determining victory or defeat would require a prolonged battle. The Zuan Ji Ring accelerated this process.

Not long after, under the watchful eyes of the Saints, the first point of light completely dimmed and was defeated. Looking closely, it was [Xuan Pin]. Li Fan wore a helpless expression, shaking his head slightly, "Still injured and not recovered, it's truly a shame." Xuan Pin primarily governs the generation and growth of the Mountains and Seas, and it also came from the end of the Mountains and Seas, having only recently recovered its Saintly power. Its strength being the weakest was within the expectations of all Saints. As long as it possessed the ability to infuse True Spirits, even if it were a mere mortal, the Saints would not mind.

Next to be eliminated were [Fang Cun] and [Great Qi]. As for the last three Saints, they were locked in a fierce, inseparable battle. Within the Zuan Ji Ring, black and white energies crisscrossed, appearing and disappearing, separating and combining. Separated, they revealed their sharp edges and fierce attacks. Combined, they were like one entity, impregnable. In contrast, a spark of fire split into billions, forming a vast, eerie gray sea of fire. Each flame in the gray sea seemed to have its own consciousness. Even if destroyed, it could quickly regenerate from nothingness, inextinguishable and growing stronger with each attempt to extinguish it. Black and white clashed with gray, neither side gaining an advantage. Outside of them, shadows lurked. Sometimes transforming into black and white energies, ambushing the gray flames. Sometimes becoming Jin Gui's fire, attacking the circulating Tai Chi. And if True Moral and Jin Gui attacked simultaneously, the shadow would retaliate in kind, using their own methods against them. Facing the two with its own methods, the shadow remained undefeated. The three-way struggle, even with the Zuan Ji Ring's constant acceleration, could not be decided for a time.

"Indeed, they are evenly matched. This outcome is truly interesting," the karmic judge's phantom image shook his head and chuckled.

"Destiny has its own reasons," the Guiming Saint suddenly said. The karmic judge's smile froze. Followed by a look of contemplation. "I originally thought of letting it go at this. Since you say so, let's wait a bit longer. We'll see who wins."

Li Fan, hearing the conversation between Guiming and the karmic judge, also pondered inwardly. The scene fell into an eerie silence, with only the Zuan Ji Ring's brilliance flickering. After an unknown period, the balance between the three was finally broken. It was the [Bai Xiao] phantom image that shouted, "This is boring!" and voluntarily jumped out of the Zuan Ji Ring, its phantom image dissipating, ceasing to exist. Bai Xiao himself felt nothing unusual, even showing an appreciative expression of "As expected of me." The remaining True Moral and Jin Gui ultimately achieved victory, with True Moral being slightly superior. Thus, the strength ranking of the six new Saints was determined.

Li Fan suddenly spoke, "Should the six of us compete again with the previous fellow Daoists?"

"There's no need for that." It was [Xing Cha] who spoke. As a wooden boat laden with starlight gently sailed into the Zuan Ji Ring, The starlight erupted violently, shining like billions of stars simultaneously. Instantly, everything was engulfed. The black and white energies of True Moral transformed into Tai Chi, constantly rotating, attempting to resist the destruction of the starlight. But it was ultimately futile. Eventually, it was annihilated by the starlight. The strongest among the six new Saints was thus easily defeated by Xing Cha. Witnessing this scene, all six Saints fell silent.

Chapter 1682: The Saints Are in Rank

"To traverse against the current, besides adhering to the foundation of one's path and preserving the roots of one's existence, the most crucial aspect is to 'Discern Ancient and Modern.'"

It was the Phantom of Saint Lianshan who instructed the newly ascended Saints.

"Maintaining the roots of one's existence is to contend with the Dao Annihilation of the Void Realm. But what does 'Discern Ancient and Modern' mean?" asked Saint Fang Cun, one of the newly ascended, full of puzzlement.

"In the Eternal Silence Void, everything is a boundless expanse. There are not just two directions, past and present. 'Present' refers to the direction from which we came. 'Ancient' is our destination. As for other places..."

"They are endless, infinite. If the initial direction is wrong, even if you possess divine power and can endure the erosion of the Void Realm for ten million years, all that meets your gaze will still be nothingness," Saint Lianshan said, gently waving his hand. Together with Saint Gui Hai, they presented a scene of abyssal darkness to the assembled Saints.

Under the black, cloud-like shroud, Li Fan felt his own senses stripped away. The surrounding figures of Saints vanished one after another. It was as if he had truly fallen into the boundless void.

The dead silence of nothingness even began to slowly erode the very foundation of his existence.

Vast and boundless, without distinction of up or down, left or right, even self and other.

Let alone anything else!

Where was the ancient? Whither the modern?

Forget about traveling across and reaching a point further in the past.

Even returning to the Mountains and Seas, which they had just left, became a problem!

"This is merely a simulated scenario by Saints Lianshan and Gui Hai??"

"The true Eternal Silence Void is actually this terrifying." A sense of gravity settled in Li Fan's heart.

Though he had traversed it before, he had done so by flowing with the current, straight to the end of the Mountains and Seas. Most crucially, relying on the connection between Qiu Xin Hui's imaginary clone and his main body, he could precisely pinpoint his direction. He had no worries about getting lost.

But now, without a guiding beacon, the difficulty was vastly different.

Before long, the two Saints dispelled the simulated darkness of the void. The newly ascended Saints, whose images reappeared, all bore expressions of solemnity, just like Li Fan.

"However, you need not worry excessively. In the Void Realm, there is no path, but the strong forge one. Our true bodies already exist in the real Eternal Silence Void. Like knots on a rope, you only need to use the nearest Saintly companion as an anchor," Lord Tai Yi's phantom figure said, offering comfort.

"According to our past calculations, to reconnect ourselves with the previous section of the Mountains and Seas, and to communicate across the vast Void Realm, requires at least thirteen Saints working in unison. But that is the most extreme scenario; there is no room for the slightest error. Even a minor accident could not only lead to complete failure but also potentially the demise of all thirteen Saints."

"Therefore, we have been preparing all this time and have not truly begun our efforts. But now, with the fortune brought by Daoist Friend Profound Embryo..."

"With six new Saints, though we can't say it's foolproof, the risk has indeed significantly diminished," Duke Shou Qiu said, looking at Li Fan slowly.

"On the Void Path, the capable lead the way. Before you truly enter the Eternal Silence Void, you must first discuss and decide your order. The latter must follow closely behind the former, without the slightest error. Otherwise, one misstep leads to a cascade of errors," said the Phantom Judge's phantom fiercely.

"Currently, the sequence for the nine of us in the Void Realm is set. The most ancient, and thus the first, is Lianshan. Then, in order, Guihai, Tai Yi, Prying Opportunity, Guiming, Duancha, Shou Qiu..."

"And I, and Star Vessel."

"As for how you should be ranked, perhaps you can compete first."

The six newly ascended Saints exchanged glances, a spark of eagerness in the eyes of most.

"A real contest of strength would inevitably lead to friction. Why not follow our old method, within this Spinning Ring, each differentiate a phantom image?" Before Saint Lianshan's voice could finish, the White Circle of the Other Shore glowed brightly.

In the brilliant radiance, the newly ascended six Saints were observed by the nine Saints of the Other Shore.

"Heh heh, I had this intention long ago!" The first to respond was Jin Gui. As his phantom image flew into the Spinning Ring, the remaining Saints found it difficult to refuse.

In a flash, each differentiated a phantom image and cast it into the Spinning Ring.

"Within the Spinning Ring, one can discern the whole from a small part."

"One glimpse reveals all. If any of you wish to conceal your true strength, I'm afraid it will not work," Duke Shou Qiu said cheerfully, as all the Saints were now present.

The newly ascended six Saints remained impassive, nodding in response.

The radiance of the White Circle transformed, as if into a battlefield.

The phantom images of the Saints, like specks of light, entered.

Within the Spinning Ring, time seemed to accelerate countless times.

Every moment, the specks of light representing the Saints collided intensely.

For Saints, even a differentiated phantom image required a prolonged battle to determine victory or defeat. The Spinning Ring merely accelerated this process.

Not long after, under the gaze of the Saints, one speck of light completely dimmed and was defeated.

Upon closer inspection, it was the Profound Embryo.

Li Fan's face showed helplessness, and he shook his head slightly, "Still injured and not fully recovered, what a pity."

The Profound Embryo primarily governs the generation and growth of the Mountains and Seas, and having traversed from the end of the Mountains and Seas, it had only recently recovered its Saintly power. Its being the weakest was well within the Saints' expectations.

As long as it possessed the divine ability to infuse True Spirits, even if it were a mere mortal, the Saints would not mind.

Next to be eliminated were Fang Cun and Great Qi.

As for the last three Saints, they were locked in an inseparable, fierce battle.

Within the Spinning Ring, black and white energies crisscrossed, appearing and disappearing, separating and merging. When separated, their attacks were sharp and imposing. When merged, they were a seamless whole, impregnable.

In contrast, a single spark of fire fractured into billions, forming a vast, eerie gray sea of fire. Each wisp of flame in the gray sea seemed to possess its own consciousness. Even if destroyed, it could quickly regenerate from nothingness, inextinguishable and growing stronger with each attempt to suppress it.

Black and white clashed with gray, neither side gaining an advantage.

Beyond them, shadows lurked. Occasionally transforming into black and white energies to ambush the gray flames. Occasionally becoming Jin Gui's fire, attacking the circulating Tai Chi.

And if Moral and Jin Gui attacked simultaneously, the shadow would retaliate in kind, using their own methods against them. The continuous shadows, facing two adversaries, remained undefeated.

The three-way struggle, even with the Spinning Ring constantly accelerating, could not be decided for a time.

"So evenly matched, this outcome is truly interesting," the Phantom Judge's phantom chuckled softly, shaking his head.

"Destiny has its own reasons," Saint Guiming suddenly interjected.

The smile on the Phantom Judge's face froze.

Followed by an expression of deep thought.

"I had originally intended to let it go at that. Since you've spoken, let us wait a little longer. We shall see who ultimately prevails."

Li Fan, hearing the conversation between Guiming and the Phantom Judge, also pondered inwardly.

The scene fell into an eerie silence, with only the brilliance of the Spinning Ring flickering.

After an unknown period, the balance between the three was finally broken.

It was the Phantom of Bai Xiao who shouted, "How uninteresting!"

And then voluntarily leaped out of the Spinning Ring, its phantom image dissipating, ceasing to exist.

Bai Xiao's true self felt nothing amiss, even showing an appreciative expression of "As expected of me."

The remaining Moral and Jin Gui ultimately achieved victory, with Moral proving slightly superior.

Thus, the strength ranking of the six new Saints was determined.

Li Fan suddenly spoke, "Should the six of us compete again with our predecessors?"

"There's no need for that."

It was Star Vessel who spoke.

As a wooden boat laden with starlight gently sailed into the Spinning Ring.

The starlight erupted violently, like billions of stars shining simultaneously.

Instantly, everything was engulfed.

The black and white energies of Moral transformed into Tai Chi, constantly revolving, attempting to resist the destruction of the starlight.

But it was ultimately futile.

Eventually, it was annihilated by the starlight.

The strongest among the six new Saints was thus easily defeated by Star Vessel.

Witnessing this scene, all six Saints fell silent.

Chapter 1683: Entering the Void Realm

Even the strongest among the six newly ascended Saints was no match for the weakest of the Nine Saints of the Shore. This was despite the latter being merely a phantom image left within the Spinning Ring, not even their true form. This outcome took Li Fan completely by surprise.

Duke Shou Qiu chuckled, "We are all old-timers; we simply have a little more accumulated experience than you. As long as you live long enough, you will eventually catch up."

The six newly ascended Saints nodded slightly.

Li Fan knew that the "accumulated experience" Duke Shou Qiu referred to was the state of "daily growth" after achieving Sainthood. Once one became a Saint, profound mysteries arose naturally. Even sitting still, without actively cultivating, one's power would advance by leaps and bounds, beyond ordinary comprehension. Previously, Li Fan had only faintly sensed this from Moral and Jade Return, but now it was confirmed by Duke Shou Qiu.

"This passive cultivation, where strength increases, must slow down over time; otherwise, Duke Shou Qiu wouldn't have said 'eventually catch up.'"

"But how long 'eventually' is… is worth pondering."

"The three Saints, Lianshan, Guihai, and Taiyi, have existed for an incalculable number of eons. With the accumulation of such vast time, without some extraordinary means of replenishment, newly ascended Saints might never catch up in their lifetime."

"Duke Shou Qiu's words likely contained a degree of comfort."

This could be glimpsed from the ranking sequence of the Nine Saints of the Shore. Duke Shou Qiu wielded the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, and by rights, he should not be weak among the Saints. Yet, he was only ranked before the Karmic Judge and Star Vessel. The three Saints, Lianshan, Guihai, and Taiyi, on the other hand, deservedly held the top ranks.

"Saints, the more ancient, the stronger. Moreover, as the founders of Immortality, their innate talent must have been world-shaking. Their true forms have likely reached an unimaginable realm."

"No wonder that with the unrivalled talent of the Final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, he never entertained the thought of competing at the beginning of the Mountains and Seas. It's because he knew that being born at the end of the Mountains and Seas, he naturally lacked almost an entire life cycle's worth of accumulation compared to the ancient Saints."

"To reach the realm he did is already an astonishing feat."

Li Fan inwardly cautioned himself: "I am merely clad in the outer garment of the Profound Embryo and using the 'Infinite Selves' technique to divert their attention. I must be careful not to reveal any flaws in front of them."

Li Fan had not forgotten the terrifying outcome in the True Return simulation, where he was instantly exposed and all his thoughts and consciousness were read by the Saints, leaving his fate uncertain.

With the sequence now established, the next step was the initial exploration of the Eternal Silence Void. However, as a precaution, the six newly ascended Saints also had to leave phantom images of themselves in the Spinning Ring.

"These phantom images will also serve as anchor points."

"If you get lost in the Void Realm and can't sense your companions, or if you notice any disorder in the sequence..."

"Then prioritize your safety and you may withdraw at any time," the Taiyi phantom slowly said.

The newly ascended Saints naturally had no reason to refuse. Having gained experience from the previous competition, injecting their phantom images was a smooth process. The phantom images formally took their places in the Spinning Ring, and the white circle's radiance connected the six new Saints with the original nine Saints.

Li Fan squinted slightly. Through the binding connection of the Spinning Ring, he could actually sense the Dao paths of the other Saints! This wasn't merely observing and comprehending from an outsider's perspective. It was like experiencing them as his own cultivated Dao! Similar to Li Fan's process of comprehending the Profound Embryo—first grasping, then studying—the efficiency was naturally incomparable to ordinary enlightenment.

"To openly share one's Dao path like this."

"Is this the absolute confidence of the ancient Saints?"

Within the Spinning Ring, there was no hiding one's true strength. Fortunately, Li Fan was merely the "Profound Embryo" Saint. Since it wasn't the foundation of Li Fan's existence, even if he were to reveal it entirely, Li Fan wouldn't feel the slightest regret. With an unwavering heart, he simply focused on comprehending the Dao auras wielded by the other Saints.

The other newly ascended Saints, however, were less accustomed to this "sharing," appearing somewhat constrained. Noticing Li Fan's nonchalance, they, too, nodded inwardly: "As expected of a Saint who came against the current from the end of the Mountains and Seas!"

Feeling a faint twinge of guilt, they forced themselves to get used to the strangeness of the Spinning Ring. Once they became familiar with the Dao paths of the other Saints within the white circle, they would become like a single entity. They could even call upon a portion of the power of the other Saints' phantom images.

"Seeing the small, knowing the whole; one is all." Recalling Duke Shou Qiu's previous discourse on this, Li Fan felt a glimmer of understanding.

At this moment, Duke Shou Qiu spoke again: "The more familiar we are with each other's auras, the greater the maximum distance we can sense in the Void Realm. This significantly increases our chances of reconnecting the Mountains and Seas."

"Of course, this first journey is merely for everyone to familiarize themselves with the conditions of the Void Realm."

With all preparations complete, the Shore's white circle was suddenly torn open from the outside, revealing a dark rift.

"Follow me closely, and let us leap in together."

"Once you are in the darkness, do not panic, no matter what happens. Sense your surroundings, try to recall your origins. Then, attempt to arrange yourselves according to the predetermined order…" Duke Shou Qiu instructed with immense patience.

In front of the Eternal Silence Void, the six newly ascended Saints were as nervous as fledgling birds taking their first flight. Even though the Void's pressure had been significantly reduced, the fear within their hearts remained, yet to dissipate.

Seeing Duke Shou Qiu's phantom slowly drift in, Moral took a deep breath. After three breaths, he followed. The remaining Saints entered one after another.

The moment Li Fan stepped into the Void Realm, boundless darkness instantly enveloped him. Though he had traversed the Void Realm before, this encounter was entirely different from his previous journey, which utilized the Final Saint of the Mountains and Seas to flow with the current!

Beyond the pervasive cold and deathly silence, the very foundation of his existence was slowly being devoured by the darkness. Without the protection of the power of imagination, and perhaps to prevent the Saints around him from noticing, True Return also fell into a state of dormancy. Li Fan's memories began to gradually fade. And like an avalanche, the speed of memory loss accelerated. Soon, Li Fan's mind felt as if it had been emptied, becoming completely blank.

"Who… am I?"

"Where is this place?"

"It's too dark; I can't see anything."

Without memories, his actions were entirely governed by instinct. In the depths of his being, Li Fan sensed a familiar aura in a certain direction within the darkness. Fortunately, he hadn't delved too far into the Void Realm and still had some strength to resist its erosion.

Soon, he returned from the Void Realm, once again seeing the light. As he returned to the Shore, the Saints' phantom images, seeing Li Fan reappear so quickly, showed a subtle change in expression. They thought some mishap had occurred.

Li Fan, quickly regaining his memories upon returning to the Mountains and Seas, reacted swiftly. With a look of shame, he said, "It seems I haven't fully recovered. I got lost in the Void Realm and couldn't sense the others' auras, so I had to return first."

Chapter 1684: Holy Medicine Helps Explore the Realm

"The continuous infusion of Saints seems to have had a greater impact on me than imagined. Perhaps I need to rest longer."

Li Fan said this with a composed demeanor, while the Saints within the Other Shore's halo fell into silence.

"It's alright, as long as you have returned safely. We were also inconsiderate."

After a long pause, it was the Keeper of the Mound's phantom that broke the awkwardness.

After all, Li Fan's method of true spirit infusion was unique to the Mountains and Seas.

Even if he were to lose his means of traversing the Void Realm from now on and remain forever in the current segment of the Mountains and Seas, he could still provide a continuous supply of Saint-level reserve forces.

The Saints, therefore, saw nothing unusual.

Among the Saintly sequence, [Mysterious Conception] was ranked last.

The facts proved that even Li Fan's sudden disappearance would not cause any impact on this initial exploration of the Void Realm.

Li Fan sat within the Whirlwind Ring, taking the opportunity to comprehend the Daos of the other Saints.

After an unknown period, a fluctuation suddenly arrived.

It turned out the Saints had finally returned.

"It has been about eight hundred years in the mortal world of the Mountains and Seas."

"However, time has no practical meaning in the Other Shore."

The situation was largely similar to the end of the Mountains and Seas.

The brilliant white light of the Whirlwind Ring seemed to freeze time, making the Other Shore region appear as if it had leaped out of the river of time and existed independently. Within the Mountains and Seas, time surged forward, while in the Other Shore, everything remained eternally unchanged, existing in dependence on the Mountains and Seas themselves.

One could travel from the Other Shore to any possibility or any point in time in the current segment of the Mountains and Seas.

One could also depart from any point in the Mountains and Seas and traverse, searching for traces of the Other Shore.

This was how they could attract powerful transcendent beings, providing potential reserve forces for the grand plan of re-establishing the connection of the Mountains and Seas.

From transcendence to Sainthood required the accumulation of a long period.

Only within the solidified time of the Other Shore did these transcendent beings have the opportunity to attempt to prove their Dao and become Saints. Otherwise, if time were allowed to flow normally, they would likely perish in Dao Annihilation before even breaking through.

Of course, the appearance of Li Fan's ability to infuse true spirits undoubtedly greatly accelerated this process.

The newly ascended Saints returned to the Other Shore, their expressions, like Li Fan's, showing a moment of confusion before instantly regaining clarity.

Square Inch frowned, "The Void Realm is a vast expanse of nothingness. Not only is it difficult to distinguish between ancient and modern, but one even loses a sense of self. Even though I tried my best to maintain my clarity, in the end, I almost forgot my mission. Fortunately, I still remembered the agreed-upon order from the depths of my being, sensed the presence of my fellow Daoists before and after, and did not panic."

"I never imagined that staying in the Void Realm would be so difficult."

Bai Xiao smiled and said, "Speaking of which, perhaps you all won't believe it. In the Void Realm, I seemed to feel a certain intent trying to communicate with me. To protect me, the power that annihilates the foundations of all existence invisibly weakened. Unfortunately..."

The Keeper of the Mound's phantom lightly interrupted Bai Xiao's words, "That was merely your illusion. If you had not become a Saint, perhaps you truly could have surrendered to the Star. But now that you have proven your Dao and become a Saint, there is no turning back. Indeed, there is a consciousness hidden within the Void Realm. However, it is the collective intent of the [Eternal Silence Void]. Every time Dao Annihilation encroaches upon the Mountains and Seas, it is a manifestation of its consciousness."

"If you had truly harbored intentions of defecting at that time, I fear you would have already perished within the Void Realm without us needing to intervene."

Hearing the Keeper of the Mound's words, Bai Xiao's smile froze.

He did not doubt the truth of the Keeper of the Mound's words, after all, he was the foremost Immortal in the world.

His understanding of Dao Annihilation and the Mountains and Seas naturally surpassed that of these juniors.

It seemed Bai Xiao still had some unresolved questions: "Why is it that after proving one's Dao and becoming a Saint, one is no longer tolerated by the Star?"

It was the Keeper of the Mound's phantom that answered, "A Saint is as one with the Mountains and Seas. Regardless of the method used to become a Saint, it is so. And the Star's emergence is destined to devour the Mountains and Seas."

With a gentle wave of his hand, an image of the continuous Mountains and Seas appeared before the Saints.

A straight black line slowly rose, as if intending to engulf the Mountains and Seas.

As the magnificent phantom image of the Mountains and Seas slowly disappeared beneath the black line, the figures standing on the mountain peaks became increasingly conspicuous.

They even became the primary targets of the black line's encroachment.

"We were born and stood within the Mountains and Seas, and although we are as one with the Mountains and Seas, we cannot escape this fate."

"As the Mountains and Seas gradually decline, in a sense, we will also directly face the Star's gaze."

"Or rather, from the moment we became Saints, we have already fallen under the Star's gaze."

Outside the black line, a solitary Star seemed to hang high, rising slowly.

Everyone had witnessed Li Fan's depiction of the [Star] devouring everything. An invisible pressure welled up in their hearts.

"If you still don't believe me, you can try."

"We will save you before you are completely swallowed by the Void Realm," the Tai Yi phantom image said calmly.

Bai Xiao ultimately did not risk his life to verify his momentary feeling and remained silent, looking dejected.

After a round of discussion among the Saints, the Keeper of the Mound's phantom summarized the initial exploration.

"Except for Daoist Xuan Yin's slight mishap, the performance of the other Daoist friends was even better than we expected."

"With a few more times of adaptation, perhaps we can truly execute the plan to reconnect the Mountains and Seas."

The Keeper of the Mound paused and looked in Li Fan's direction, "Daoist Xuan Yin, there is no need to worry. The original plan was for thirteen Saints to connect with each other. Even if one of you is missing, with the current number of Saints in the Mountains and Seas and their performance this time, there should be no major issues."

Li Fan repeatedly said with shame, "Then, while I rest and recover, I will also observe if there are any more potential talents in the Mountains and Seas. If another Saint can be created to fill the gap, that would be for the best."

All the Saints agreed.

Regarding Li Fan, the "True Spirit Infuser," all the Saints were very tolerant.

As they were speaking, a stream of light suddenly arrived at high speed from the depths of the Mountains and Seas.

The Whirlwind Ring did not obstruct it; instead, it allowed it to fly to the front of all the Saints.

As the brilliance dissipated, all the Saints gazed intently and saw six pills emitting colorful streams of light, within which majestic Saintly court phantoms flickered continuously!

The grand aura of the Saintly court was like that of the Mountains and Seas. As the light and shadow flickered, it emitted a refreshing fragrance.

Upon hearing this, the six newly promoted Saints simultaneously felt an urge.

The Keeper of the Mound smiled, "The Grand Elixir of the Saintly Emperor has finally been refined. We exerted ourselves in the Void Realm, and he shouldn't be idle all the time."

"Esteemed elders, please take it quickly."

Without any doubt, the six newly promoted Saints very solemnly accepted the Grand Elixir of the Saintly court before them and swallowed it.

In an instant, the Saintly court flourished for countless years, with peace and prosperity, and the collective will of countless beings living in contentment transformed into a warm current. It was swallowed by all the Saints.

Because they had a home, they had a foundation to stand on.

Because they had a nation, they could avoid the chaos.

After swallowing the Grand Elixir of the Saintly court, all the Saints unconsciously felt that their resistance to the encroachment of the Void Realm had increased considerably.

And this was not their illusion.

As Duke Shou Qiu continued, "With the characteristics of this Grand Elixir protecting you, the time you can maintain your autonomous will in the Void Realm will at least double. The firmer your will, the better the effect."

"The Saintly Emperor will also send five more elixirs for each of you. After consuming a total of six, the effects of the Grand Elixir will disappear."

"It should barely solve the worry of maintaining order in the Void Realm."

The Saints, having tasted the effects of the Grand Elixir of the Saintly court, continuously praised it upon hearing this.

And Li Fan finally understood why the Saints of the Other Shore did not include that Saint Emperor in their plan to reconnect the Mountains and Seas.

It turned out that this individual, like himself, had a better "auxiliary" effect from the rear than in the Void Realm.

"However, the Grand Elixir of the Saintly court is still inferior to my [True Spirit Infusion] by a considerable margin."

Li Fan mused inwardly.

With the precedent set by the Saintly Emperor, he felt slightly more at ease.

After all, strictly speaking, his rapid loss of memory in the Void Realm was a significant flaw.

It was inconsistent with the strength of a true Saint.

But True Spirit Infusion was a divine ability that had never appeared in the Mountains and Seas before.

Li Fan used this as an excuse, even the Saints like the Keeper of the Mound found it difficult to discern the truth or falsehood for a time.

And this ability to create Saints could even make the Saints of the Other Shore overlook Li Fan's "flaws"!

However, Li Fan did not intend to stay in the Mountains and Seas indefinitely because of this.

Every time the Saints entered the Void Realm, he would accompany them.

After continuously consuming the Grand Elixir of the Saintly court, the time he could endure did indeed increase.

When the boundless cold darkness struck once more.

Li Fan's heart flashed with realization: "A Saint is as one with the Mountains and Seas. When the Void Realm devours the Mountains and Seas, none beneath it can escape. Although I am clad in the outer garment of the Mysterious Conception, I have ultimately not reached the Saint realm. Naturally, I cannot escape the Void Realm's encroachment."

"There is... a method."

"If the quality is insufficient, then make up for it with quantity."

Li Fan's knowledge was not limited to the Great Dao of [Mysterious Conception].

However, to prevent the Saints around him from suspecting, he did not deploy the other Saintly Daos he comprehended from the Whirlwind Ring.

Instead, he borrowed the Great Dao of [False Becomes True] from the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas!

Ever since he began cultivating, Li Fan had been comprehending the Transformation of True and False.

With [False Becomes True] in hand, his innate advantage allowed his comprehension in this area to surpass all beings in the Mountains and Seas.

Although Qiu Xin Hui had become a Saint through [False Becomes True], Li Fan's comprehension of [False Becomes True] had not yet reached the Saint realm.

However, it was sufficient to add more bricks and tiles to the Saintly outer garment he wore!

With a single thought, within the Profound Embryo Great Dao, a few more inexplicable and profound auras were added.

The Great Dao of [False Becomes True], difficult for mortals to perceive.

At this moment, Li Fan was within the Eternal Silence Void, making it even less likely to be discovered by other Saints.

With the superposition of two major Daos, Li Fan immediately felt the Void Realm's erosion of his memory weaken.

"As I thought!"

"Perhaps other Daos can still be added..."

As more insights were added, Li Fan finally emerged from the predicament of potentially losing his memories at any moment.

"True Saints do not need to add what is superfluous, unlike me. How can others' Daos compare to the solidity of one's own Great Dao? One only needs to adhere to their own heart to maintain their self in the vast darkness." Li Fan sighed inwardly.

"When the Profound Embryo outer garment approaches the normal Saint level, adding more will be useless."

With his thoughts able to function normally, Li Fan began to painstakingly discern auras in the darkness.

"There, it seems to be a phantom image I left behind."

"And ahead, there are the Saints of the Other Shore..."

Li Fan's expression gradually became serious.

Because he distinctly discovered that based on the proximity, Fang Cun and Tai Qi seemed to be closer to him.

But in reality, he sensed the auras of the three Saints, Keeper of the Mound, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi, to be far stronger!

Like blinding lighthouses standing in the darkness, pointing the way for the Saints in the Void Realm.

"This is the three Saints deliberately releasing their auras, allowing later arrivals, who have just entered the Void Realm, not to get lost in an instant. This way, they can proceed in an orderly fashion."

"Having stayed in the Void Realm for so long, they are still so powerful, showing no signs of weakening."

"..."

Li Fan truly felt the power of the three Saints, and thus became even more cautious.

With the three Saints setting the tone, theoretically speaking, later arrivals only needed to extend the rope in a straight line according to the established order.

But things were not that simple.

The Void Realm, with its collective consciousness, would naturally not stand idly by.

When Li Fan faintly sensed that after a long journey, the path of morality was about to connect with the nine Saints ahead.

Suddenly, dark currents surged in the darkness.

The rope built by the nine Saints, as if tempered through a thousand fires, remained unshaken.

But the connection of the six newly promoted Saints was instantly broken.

The former were behind, the latter in front. The direction was indistinguishable.

Fortunately, there were Saints standing in the past, and the phantom images of the Other Shore supporting in the present.

The Saints were able to avoid losing their sense of ancient and modern, and becoming lost in the Void Realm.

But after this incident, the connection they had painstakingly forged was broken.

Li Fan gradually felt the strain, and decisively withdrew from the Void Realm first.

Not long after, all the Saints reappeared, looking somewhat disheveled.

"The dark currents of the Void Realm are unpredictable and fierce. Even we need to deal with them with all our might."

"There are no other methods; you can only adapt slowly."

"Besides, strengthening each other's connection is also beneficial for adaptation," the Keeper of the Mound's phantom said.

The Keeper of the Mound also smiled and said, "You all need not be anxious. Reconnecting the Mountains and Seas is not a matter of one or two days. Forming a connection is only the first step."

"Once the rope is formed and the Mountains and Seas are re-manifested, it will also require our assistance."

Bai Xiao asked curiously, "Assistance? What do you mean by that?"

The Keeper of the Mound said, "When the Mountains and Seas were destroyed, everything within them turned to nothingness. It is not easy to transform from nothingness to reality. Traveling to key nodes and facilitating changes will greatly increase efficiency."

"Otherwise, the speed of transformation from nothingness to reality might not even match the speed of the Void Realm's renewed encroachment. Even if we all bear the burden, we won't be able to hold on."

The Saints vaguely understood.

Li Fan asked, "What are these key nodes?"

"There is no definitive answer. Anything that significantly impacts the Mountains and Seas, or leaves memories within the Mountains and Seas, can be considered one."

"We will have to judge based on the situation at the time."

"However, the nodes chosen for the previous connection of the Mountains and Seas can serve as a reference."

Duke Shou Qiu said, displaying images one after another.

Li Fan was surprised to see the Xuanhuang Realm among them.

"I wonder where the fracture point of the previous Mountains and Seas was."

"And during which period was it reborn from nothingness."

Li Fan hid these questions in his heart and did not ask them.

"Reconnecting the Mountains and Seas, although arduous, will bring great benefits to us after its completion!"

As everyone fell silent, Tai Yi spoke again.

Chapter 1685: Re-deriving the Heavenly Decision

"When the two divided sections of the Mountains and Seas merged, it was as if myriad selves became one. True spirits multiplied, benefiting even those at the Saintly realm. The prerequisite was your existence within that past section of the Mountains and Seas."

"The current section of the Mountains and Seas has continued for a total of one hundred and ninety-three thousand, six hundred and forty-five years. The void beyond covers approximately fifty-eight thousand, six hundred years. If it were five thousand years ago, when many of you had not yet been born, you naturally would not have reaped such benefits. Otherwise, even in an infant state, you could have enjoyed the advantages of 'myriad selves becoming one.'"

The phantom image of Lian Shan swept its gaze across the newly promoted Saints present, finally settling on Li Fan. "Except for Xuan Pin, who hails from the end of the Mountains and Seas, the rest have no such worries. 'Myriad selves becoming one'—the stronger you become, the greater the benefit. Moreover, it's not limited to just the true spirit aspect. When the Mountains and Seas reconnect, you will naturally understand."

The phantom image of Lian Shan paused again. "Even for those like Xuan Pin, whose previous section of the Mountains and Seas does not have their presence, there is no need to worry about gaining nothing. We Saints are one with the Mountains and Seas. It is as if we stand upon them; the stronger the Mountains and Seas become, the more our strength naturally increases. If you are even luckier, and your chosen Dao path is not controlled by the previous section of the Mountains and Seas, then in an instant, you can transform it for your own use, creating fortune out of thin air..."

Li Fan nodded slightly, grateful for the explanation from Saint Lian Shan.

The principle was similar to the Great Dao Returns to Truth—once taken, it is forever taken.

Those who could become Saints would undoubtedly have reached the pinnacle of understanding their own Dao paths. If they encountered an equivalent Great Dao in a previous section of the Mountains and Seas, it would be natural to subdue it instantly.

When Li Fan heard Lian Shan say, "The stronger the Mountains and Seas become, the more our strength naturally increases," the words "Mountain Sitting Secret" flashed in his mind.

This ancient cultivation technique of the Divine Wood Sect had been iteratively deduced by Li Fan since he obtained it.

Mountain Sitting, Immortal Sitting, Heaven Sitting.

Unfortunately, its effects were limited to before transcendence.

Once the threshold of transcendence was crossed, and the path towards becoming a Saint began, the Mountain Sitting Secret had already become...

"Its target is the transcendent realm; it can no longer generate feedback for cultivation, let alone the Saintly realm."

"Otherwise, with my ability to infuse true spirits..."

"Having created so many Saints, even the three Saints of Lian Shan might not be my match."

No matter how miraculous, it was merely a mortal cultivation method.

It had already reached its limit in assisting Li Fan in transcending.

After Li Fan's transcendence, he had long ceased to hold any expectations for it.

But today, Saint Lian Shan's words opened up a new line of thought for Li Fan.

"The principle of 'sitting on the mountain to gain height,' in the context of the Mountains and Seas and Saints, still exists."

"If that's the case..."

"If Heaven Sitting were further evolved into Saint Sitting, perhaps its benefits could still be enjoyed!"

"However, how should it be improved?"

Although he had a vague idea, he had no immediate means of implementing it.

Firstly, Li Fan himself had not yet reached the Saintly realm.

Even if he did, successfully deducing the Saint Sitting Secret would be almost a pipe dream.

All Saints were one with the Mountains and Seas.

Especially the three Saints of Lian Shan, who were existences that had shaken the past and present.

What kind of cultivation method or Great Dao could encompass them without being detected?
