"Perhaps I am overthinking this. The goal of the Saint Sitting Secret is not to target Saints who have already achieved their Dao, but rather those transcendent cultivators who are moldable. Its effect is only covered before they achieve Sainthood."

"The qualitative feedback from transcendence to Sainthood, if it could be collected and utilized, would undoubtedly be a world-shattering energy."

Li Fan's thoughts raced, finding a potential breakthrough.

But it was merely a concept.

With Li Fan's current foundation, he was far from being able to deduce this ideal marvelous method.

However...

Li Fan now had a total of fourteen Saints by his side!

Without any reservations, he directly spoke, "Saint Lian Shan, your insights are profound. The concept of 'sitting on the mountain to gain height' is indeed logical when thought about carefully. I wonder, is there a Saint of '[Mountain Sitting]' among the Mountains and Seas? One whose benefits are not limited to the Mountains and Seas, but could potentially include all beings within the Mountains and Seas, and even us Saints."

"If such a being truly exists, and we continuously ascend, wouldn't we be able to push them further?"

As soon as Li Fan spoke, all the Saints revealed surprised expressions.

The pursuit of the Great Dao has no end.

Although they had all achieved Sainthood and were one with the Mountains and Seas, to be satisfied at this point was clearly impossible.

After all, they could see with their own eyes the existence of [Gods] and [Stars] above the Mountains and Seas.

Even if Gods existed at the beginning of the Mountains and Seas, and Stars were born at the end,

All the Saints had only heard of them, never seen them.

This did not hinder their aspiration.

The realm above Sainthood, at present, did not even have a name or definition. It could only be compared horizontally with powers of seemingly equivalent caliber.

The Saints knew very little about it.

No one could answer Li Fan's question, and the scene fell into a prolonged silence.

Finally, the phantom image of Lian Shan, in a rare display, showed a subtle fluctuation.

"At that time, I ascended to the summit of the sacred mountain, gazing upon countless possibilities within the Mountains and Seas."

"The myriad beings, their vitality surging upwards. Sacrificing their lives, relentlessly climbing."

"I deeply felt that surge of life force, boundless and continuous, capable of even shaking mountains and moving seas."

"But I also saw the hardships of the beings. After all, only a rare few, like myself, managed to reach the pinnacle of the Mountains and Seas."

"The vast majority, throughout their entire lives, couldn't even take the first step."

"At that time, two choices lay before me."

"One was to act as '[Mountain Sitting]' with the advantage of being first. Utilizing the surging power of the infinite beings within the Mountains and Seas to push myself forward. Perhaps I could have touched upon the Star."

"The other was to become a bridge, creating a path to the summit for all beings. Though the path would be arduous, as long as they possessed sufficient wisdom and strength, and climbed step by step, they would eventually see the scenery of the mountains..."

The phantom image of Lian Shan swayed, appearing to be lost in ancient memories.

The Nine Saints of the Other Shore seemed to be familiar with this past event and did not show surprise.

However, the six newly promoted Saints, hearing this for the first time, were all profoundly shaken.

The phantom image of Lian Shan's words, spoken so casually, conveyed a clear message: regardless of which choice Saint Lian Shan had made back then, it would have had a profound impact on subsequent generations.

He chose Lian Shan over Mountain Sitting.

Thus, the prosperous era of immortal cultivation in later generations came to be.

But what if, back then, he had chosen Mountain Sitting?

A trace of fear flickered in the hearts of all the Saints.

"Perhaps a being comparable to the Star would indeed have been born, but we would likely have had no chance of ever rising."

"Saint Lian Shan, although he addresses us as peers, he is undeniably our trailblazer."

With this thought, the Saints could not help but feel reverence and bowed towards the phantom image of Lian Shan.

After the ceremony, Li Fan looked up and suddenly asked, "Saint Lian Shan, do you regret your decision back then?"

"Although Lian Shan created the prosperous era of immortal cultivation in the Mountains and Seas, he also missed the opportunity to compete with the Star. Now, with the Mountains and Seas lost, the outcome is ultimately tied to the Star..."

"If he had chosen '[Mountain Sitting]' back then, perhaps the outcome would have been different."

Lian Shan chuckled silently. "Having made a decision, it was after much deliberation, so what is there to regret? Even if I were to return to that moment, my choice would not change."

"I would simply do it again."

Chapter 1686: The Mountains and Seas Reconnect

After a brief silence, the phantom image of Saint Lianshan continued, speaking of the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain.

"All beings and Dao laws in this realm originate from Mountains and Seas. Therefore, those who can harness Mountains and Seas should possess the highest form of all Dao laws. Lian Shan is thus, and so is Sitting Mountain. However, from its very inception, Mountains and Seas were destined to return to the Star, following a path from prosperity to decline. If one were to practice the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain during the early days of Mountains and Seas, instead of benefiting, they would only suffer a decline in cultivation concurrent with the fall of Mountains and Seas, losing self and harming others without benefit."

"Times change. As Mountains and Seas become submerged by Dao Annihilation, this Dao of Sitting on a Mountain has naturally undergone changes. To sit on a mountain requires the power of Mountains and Seas' vibrant growth. If Mountains and Seas were already at their peak at birth, how could they advance further? However, in this fragmented end of Mountains and Seas, the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain may yet achieve remarkable effects. Precisely by leveraging the immense power unleashed when the two fragmented Mountains and Seas merge during their reconnection..."

Saint Lianshan shared his insights without reservation, speaking eloquently. Li Fan listened intently, gradually coming to understand.

Mountains and Seas arose from Gods and returned to the Star, following a path from prosperity to decline. If one were to achieve Sainthood through Sitting on a Mountain at its peak, that Saint would inevitably decline along with Mountains and Seas. Only in the calamitous end of Mountains and Seas, using one fragment as a base to practice the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain, could one benefit after Mountains and Seas were reconnected.

"It seems that Saint Lianshan's choice of Lian Shan back then was not solely due to so-called morality. Lian Shan was inherently the optimal choice. No wonder he said he had no regrets. The Dao of Sitting on a Mountain, though seemingly defying heaven, has extremely harsh realization conditions. It requires emerging at the moment of Mountains and Seas' annihilation, making one inherently weaker than the ancient Saints. Furthermore, the moment of achieving Sainthood is almost the peak of one's power. Afterward, as Mountains and Seas are encroached upon by Dao Annihilation, one's own strength continuously declines. It is almost impossible to cultivate independently, one must solely rely on the power of Mountains and Seas' reconnection."

...

Saint Lianshan, with his profound wisdom, directly pointed out the various drawbacks of the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain to Li Fan. Coupled with the discussions of the other Saintly phantoms, a nascent idea began to form in Li Fan's mind.

"I once witnessed, at the end of time, Mountains and Seas returning to the Star. Afterward, the power of True Return repelled the Star and reversed everything, causing Mountains and Seas to reappear from Dao Annihilation. Are these Mountains and Seas before and after the same entity? If so..."

"Moments when Mountains and Seas reappear from nothingness, instantly expanding to their peak. If the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain could be applied..."

Whether the Mountains and Seas before and after True Return originated from the same source was a question Li Fan, wielding the Great Dao of Xuan Pin, might be able to investigate. After True Return had integrated the Great Dao of Xuan Pin from the old Mountains and Seas, the Xuan Pin of the new Mountains and Seas also fell under his control.

"Even if they are not entirely identical, there must be a corresponding connection. The probability of Sitting on a Mountain being effective is very high."

"However, the reappearance of Mountains and Seas was not due to my efforts, but to True Return. It is difficult to say how effective it will be."

Li Fan's thoughts churned, wishing to abandon Xuan Pin and embrace Sitting on a Mountain on the spot. Unfortunately, he had not even comprehended the Dao of Sitting on a Mountain below the Saintly level, let alone performing the true act of sitting on a mountain.

Within the Xuán Jī Ring, after the Saints rested, they once again ventured into the Void Realm. Their phantom images remained, observing and sensing the situation in the Void Realm while continuing their discussions.

The eternal Void Realm was fraught with danger. Even after venturing in and returning several times, its oppressive nature remained unchanged with each new entry, as if it were the first time. There was no sense of "habit" or "familiarity." The only thing the newly promoted Saints could hone was the duration they could withstand the encroaching currents of the Void Realm.

Fortunately, with the nine Saints leading the way and the Xuán Jī Ring's phantom images serving as anchors, their journey into the Void Realm, though startling, was not perilous. After countless attempts and the passage of immeasurable time, the newly promoted Saints finally reached a tacit understanding. They were able to connect the great chain of Saints from the previous segment of Mountains and Seas to the current segment.

Li Fan, who was supposed to be the final link in the chain, did not play a significant role, nor did Fang Cun. Thirteen Saints connected made the chain complete. The chain of Saints, like a long dragon, broke through the eternal Void Realm. Leveraging the connection between the Saints, Li Fan could even sense the aura from the previous segment of Mountains and Seas.

"Xuan Pin is stationed at the other shore and should not act rashly."

"Fang Cun will roam within the Void Realm to guard against any unforeseen events," the voice of Saint Lianshan echoed from afar. This time, it was not a phantom image, but Saint Lianshan himself. Li Fan naturally obeyed. Fang Cun roaming as a reserve force was also optimal.

Now that the chain of Saints was formed, within the Void Realm, the illusory landscape of Mountains and Seas slowly emerged. Like faint lights in the darkness, though still dim, they were distinctly different from before. With the help of this illusory Mountains and Seas, Fang Cun could traverse the Void Realm at high speed. Even if one of them encountered trouble, he could provide support at any time.

"We need to remain in the Void Realm until the illusory Mountains and Seas are completely stabilized."

"At that time, we must project our thoughts into the key nodes to hasten their transformation from虚to实."

"Remember, do not move your bodies!"

"Otherwise, the long chain will break, and all our efforts will be in vain!"

Over the prolonged attempts, the Saints had prepared various contingency plans. Now, following the established procedures, no accidents occurred. The time required for the illusory Mountains and Seas to stabilize was longer than Li Fan had anticipated. During this period, he had not been idle. Using the True Spirit Infusion technique, he recreated another Saint, adding more support, making the operation to reconnect Mountains and Seas seem even more secure.

One day, sensing that the submerged illusory Mountains and Seas were on the verge of a qualitative change under the combined efforts of the Saints, Emperor Tai Wei also manifested his form and arrived in the Void Realm. Compared to before, the Void Realm was no longer entirely dark. The area where the illusory Mountains and Seas resided resembled a beacon, dispelling the darkness. However, an illusion was still an illusion, and it was still one step away from becoming true Mountains and Seas.

"Everyone, according to the plan, project your thoughts into it."

"The transformation of Mountains and Seas will then be successfully established."

Li Fan also joined in this time, projecting a thought into the illusory Mountains and Seas.

Chapter 1687: Secretly Peeking at the Mountain Sea Secrets

The eternal Void Realm seemed to sense the Mountains and Seas reappearing from destruction. Dark currents suddenly surged, causing the chain of Saints to tremble. The image of Mountains and Seas flickered, like a candle in the wind, on the verge of extinguishing at any moment. The Saints stood firm, protecting the newly formed illusory Mountains and Seas like a dam. Amidst this stalemate, their projected thoughts had already reached various parts of the illusory Mountains and Seas. This segment of Mountains and Seas, submerged by the Void Realm, spanned over fifty-eight thousand six hundred years. Because Li Fan's main body remained at the other shore, his projected thought only roamed the end of the illusory Mountains and Seas closest to the real Mountains and Seas. "Even with the protection of the chain of Saints, we are still in the Void Realm, which is vastly different from the real Mountains and Seas." "In the real Mountains and Seas, countless possibilities flow together. But in this illusory segment, most possibilities have not yet recovered. Only a few are true veins, which can be called the 'main currents' of Mountains and Seas." Although it felt like looking at a reflection in a mirror, where everything was vague and difficult to discern, Li Fan immediately identified a primary vein. It was the Xuanhuang Realm, the Origin, which he was intimately familiar with. Without hesitation, Li Fan's projected thought entered it. The illusory projection emitted a faint light, integrating his thought. Li Fan's consciousness merged, becoming a state between reality and illusion.

...

Even though he was not a true Saint, Li Fan, who could wield the Great Dao of Xuan Pin, possessed a mental strength not much weaker than the Saints. Therefore, after spending a little more time, his consciousness quickly awakened. He slightly shook his head, dispelling the sense of unreality, and attempted to fully integrate into the current possibility. After a long while, the strange feeling of his body being incompatible with the surrounding world finally disappeared. Li Fan began to examine his own condition. "Because there is no 'me' at this point in time, I can only parasitize in someone else's body." "Xuanhuang Realm, Divine Wood Sect, Li Bufan. This name is quite interesting..."

"An era where sects flourished, and the immortal path is not yet severed." Li Fan looked at the colossal Divine Wood above his head, its shade covering over thirty thousand li. "Not long ago, the Desolate God Sect summoned twelve Desolate Gods simultaneously, shaking all the sects in the world." "Three Desolate Gods attacked, fortunately, the Divine Wood repelled them. However, the Divine Wood was injured." "The Divine Wood is the foundation of the Divine Wood Sect's everything, concerning the sect's rise and fall and future." "The elders of the sect exhausted all possible methods to heal the Divine Wood's injuries. Among them, Elder Qu Changchu heard that the Samsara Sect possessed a 'Ten Thousand Year Pearl,' which had miraculous effects on accelerating time. Thus, he went to request it." "Yet, he only brought back a painting." "Although it temporarily eased the Divine Wood's injuries, it did not address the root cause..."

Li Fan carefully reviewed all the memories in "Li Bufan's" mind, and his expression became somewhat subtle. "I have seen this time period before." In the core depths of the Lan Ke Dao Field, guided by the cryptic message left by Sun Piaomiao on a bronze-cast immortal crane, Li Fan had pinpointed and glimpsed a segment of time. "The 213th year of the Heavenly Net Era. Starting with Yuan Shang Da Yuan, followed by Yue E Feng, ending with Yong Chi Fen Ruo and Yan Mao Xuan Mo..." "This is precisely the time period I am currently in." "It is also an important vein of the illusory Mountains and Seas, the place where memories of Mountains and Seas are condensed." "It seems Sun Piaomiao's guidance was not without purpose."

Li Fan's thoughts flowed, slightly moving his somewhat stiff body. He recalled the instructions from the Saints of the other shore earlier. "To promote the illusory Mountains and Seas from 虛 to 实, to naturally generate, the most crucial thing is to let it proceed naturally, meaning to let what should have happened continue to happen along the historical trajectory." "But because this segment of Mountains and Seas only exists as an illusion, with the Void Realm lurking outside, it is necessary to compress the time for key events to occur." "In simple terms, without altering the original direction of history, promote the early occurrence of a series of key events." "If capable of employing Saintly means, it would naturally be effortless. But the illusory Mountains and Seas are too fragile. Saints themselves are beings equivalent to Mountains and Seas. If they detect external interference, they might instantly trigger repulsion, which would be counterproductive." "More critically, once the illusory Mountains and Seas discern the difference between themselves and these real Saints from the outside, they will awaken to the fact that they are already in 'destruction.' The truth maintained by the Saints will then shatter like a bubble, and everything will return to the beginning." "It will be necessary to laboriously reconnect the chain of Saints from the previous segment of Mountains and Seas and initiate the process again..." These were all lessons learned from the Saints of the other shore during their previous attempts to reconnect Mountains and Seas. Although the conditions seemed quite strict, the Saints, being the most gifted beings in Mountains and Seas, found it merely troublesome. "First, we need to understand what constitutes the 'key memories' of Mountains and Seas." "This is simple enough."

Li Fan sat down and communicated with his main body at the other shore. His main body looked towards the illusory Mountains and Seas shrouded in darkness, focusing on the Origin and Xuanhuang. He observed the situation after the current time point. The reappearance of the illusory Mountains and Seas depended on... Although somewhat blurry, it was clearly different from other lights and shadows, distinguishable at a glance. "A figure secretly descended from the Immortal Realm into Xuanhuang, from the Mountains and Seas fishing grounds, escaping to another place." "The Divine Wood is increasingly withered, attracting the covetousness of Ruomu, sparking a world-shattering battle." "The Desolate God Sect summoned the Desolate Gods again, but the Immortal Realm offered no response." "... " "No, these are not the key points."

Suddenly, Li Fan's heart stirred, and his gaze bypassed these peripheral scenes, reaching the true core of the illusory Mountains and Seas. The image was hazy, faintly showing a figure, suddenly stumbling out of the void in a distressed manner. He looked around, seemingly with joy. Muttering a few words in a low voice, he then performed a magic technique, concealing himself. In just a few moments, it became impossible to discern his specific appearance from the memories of Mountains and Seas. However, Mountains and Seas had already changed because of him. The Mountains and Seas fishing grounds, which had gradually closed due to figures descending from the lower realm, slowly reopened. The battle between the Divine Wood and Ruomu was originally evenly matched, but as if a gust of invisible wind blew, the green leaves of the Divine Wood suddenly withered, and the Divine Wood began to fall into a disadvantage. The tide of Dao Annihilation from beyond the realm was inexplicably affected, changing direction and lightly brushing against a corner of the Primal Origin Immortal Realm. Large swathes of immortal domains were subsequently erased. The Xuanhuang Realm lost contact with the upper realms and various sects.

...

As if an invisible hand were manipulating and altering Mountains and Seas centered around the Xuanhuang Realm, each change was like pulling an invisible thread. A vast net slowly took shape. The mysterious figure nodded slightly, presiding over the net. Seemingly waiting for something. After an unknown period, the figure suddenly looked up. Raising its hand high, it reached towards the sky, making a grasping motion. Mountains and Seas seemed to twist at this moment!

Chapter 1688: Primordial Fog Object

The mysterious figure seemed to have truly grabbed something and was struggling to control it. The entire perspective of Mountains and Seas focused on his hand at this moment.

Within Mountains and Seas, a great wind blew, bringing the gazes from the Infinite Sea. Outside Mountains and Seas, undercurrents surged, as if countless intentions were communicating. The treasure in his hand seemed like it would break free at any moment.

The figure trembled violently, almost losing control of himself. The images flickered, appearing and disappearing. The original possibility where he resided seemed precarious, on the verge of being destroyed by the confrontation between these two forces.

In the Xuanhuang Realm, the sun rose and set three times. This struggle finally concluded. The object in the mysterious figure's hand no longer struggled. He seemed to have completely subdued it, laughing heartily.

However, his smile froze the moment he released his hand. He had clearly been victorious just moments ago, but now his hand was empty!

Even from the memory images of Mountains and Seas from years later, Li Fan could discern the extreme rage of this mysterious figure. Yet, for some reason, he did not vent his anger by destroying the Xuanhuang Realm. Instead, he continued to search within the Xuanhuang Realm, unwilling to give up. But ultimately, he found nothing and returned with disappointment.

...

This incident happened silently back then, and no one in the Xuanhuang Realm could perceive it. Even the Lan Ke Dao Field did not record it. Only Mountains and Seas themselves, due to the struggle between the mysterious figure and the unknown entity, preserved its light and shadow memory. If Mountains and Seas were in a normal state, this memory would be hidden within the endless, continuous Mountains and Seas, unseen by the world. Even Saints might not be able to detect it. Only now, as Mountains and Seas were in an intermediate state between 虛 and 实, were ordinary memory light and shadows concealed, while only important scenes manifested. Thus, Li Fan witnessed it.

"Who was that person?"

"What was he trying to hunt?"

Li Fan replayed the scene he had just witnessed in his mind, suddenly experiencing a strange premonition. What that mysterious figure had tried to hunt... might have been True Return!

"Rewriting everything in secret was to weave a net to attract True Return."

"But why would True Return come here?"

"And did True Return already appear so early?"

In an instant, a myriad of thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind, and doubts arose. He was eager to contact True Return and ask for clarification. Unfortunately, his main body was stationed in the Xuán Jī Ring, surrounded by Saintly phantoms, and True Return was engrossed, making communication impossible.

"No need to rush."

"Regardless of where True Return came from or why it came, the fact that it is now under my control is the key."

"Moreover, given its nature, even if I asked, it probably wouldn't tell me."

Li Fan shook his head inwardly. "However, that figure... the Saints of the other shore probably know him..." Thinking that even when True Return inexplicably broke free and was extremely enraged, he did not destroy and vent his anger. Li Fan speculated that he was worried about other Saints detecting his whereabouts.

After pondering for a while, Li Fan spoke directly. "Everyone, please look."

"This memory of Mountains and Seas is quite interesting."

The Saints' gazes, originally focused on the areas where their projected thoughts were invested, all turned towards Li Fan when he spoke. Slowly, a wondrous atmosphere began to flow among the Saints.

"So that's how it is. Back then, when he disappeared without reason, I thought he had gone to an even more ancient time. I never expected he would come to this era..." Saint Lianshan was the first to speak. His phantom image, unchanged for ten thousand years, rippled.

"The object in his hand..." Saints Lianshan and Guihai looked at Tai Yi simultaneously. Tai Yi pondered for a long time, first nodding, then shaking his head slightly.

"It looks very similar, but whether it truly is..."

"It's hard to say."

"What are you two talking about? Stop speaking in riddles," Bai Xiao impatiently asked before Li Fan could.

Seeing Bai Xiao's eager demeanor, Tai Yi chuckled softly. "We are talking about the primordial creation prior to Mountains and Seas, the 'Misty Creation'."

"'Misty Creation'?" These four words immediately captured the attention of the newly promoted Saints.

Tai Yi no longer played coy and slowly explained: "Mountains and Seas originate from the Primordial God. However, in the beginning, was there something that coexisted with the God?"

"Before the advent of Mountains and Seas, no one knows for sure. However, from various clues, we can vaguely confirm some things."

"What do you mean?" Bai Xiao curiously asked.

"It is precisely the existence of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas."

"If, at the time of the God's demise, only Mountains and Seas existed, then Mountains and Seas, working together, should have divided all divine power. But..."

"In this world, there are Great Daos of the same caliber as Mountains and Seas that did not truly integrate into Mountains and Seas."

"For example, [Eternal Life], [Fate], and [Xuan Pin]." Tai Yi said, his gaze sweeping over Shou Qiu, Gui Ming, and Li Fan.

"It is as if, at the time of the God's demise, something shared the division and consumption with Mountains and Seas, causing divine power to scatter and not completely return to Mountains and Seas."

"Perhaps it is because of this deficiency that the [Star] eventually appeared."

"We speculate that that ancient existence, comparable to Mountains and Seas, is what is referred to as Misty Creation."

Hearing this, Bai Xiao nodded with disappointment. "So it's just a pure guess. I thought you had actually seen it!"

The voices of Lianshan and Guihai came together, "I have indeed never seen it. However, Tai Yi is different."

Tai Yi's phantom image flickered slightly, seemingly lost in recollection. "In the past, when Mountains and Seas first formed and myriad Daos began to manifest, I was merely one of the myriad Innate Profound Wonders derived. Like me, there were Tai Chu, Tai Shi, Tai Su, Tai Ji, and even Wu Ji, etc."

"However, the reason why only I could become a Saint..."

"Is because there was an existence that enlightened me."

Tai Yi's phantom image spoke frankly, harboring no secrets. As one of the strongest among the Saints, Tai Yi was actually enlightened by someone before achieving Sainthood. The newly promoted Saints were all astonished to hear such a secret. Li Fan, however, recalled the "Chapter of Mountains and Seas' Beginning" he had seen before. It was written by Tai Yi and annotated by Wu Ji, expounding his feelings after witnessing Lianshan and Guihai build the Immortal Realm. It had already subtly revealed Tai Yi's identity as an Innate Being.

The Saints were shaken, but Tai Yi remained unfazed and continued: "At that time, Mountains and Seas were not yet fully formed and were still in the process of gestation."

"In the Tai Chu Immortal Realm, all things competed, and some even consumed Dao as food."

"I was merely one among them."

"But one day, I looked towards Mountains and Seas and suddenly saw the clouds and winds churning, and a stream of light traversing through, falling into the Tai Chu Immortal Realm."

"My heart suddenly felt an inexplicable excitement, as if finding that stream of light would bring immense fortune. However, it seemed many others felt the same."

"Thus, even after desperately searching, I could not find it."

"Just as I was about to give up, one day, that stream of light appeared before me on its own."

Chapter 1689: Remodeling of Life's Pivot

"I originally thought that flowing light was my good fortune. But when it truly stood before me, I realized... I myself was its good fortune!"

Tai Yi's phantom image chuckled lightly. "The flowing light seemed to feed on Dao. Standing still, I was uncontrollably drawn to it, as if I had originated from the flowing light. Can you all comprehend the terror I felt then?"

The phantom images of all the Saints secretly nodded.

"At that time, although I hadn't yet become a Saint, my strength was close to the current transcendent realm. But under the overflowing flowing light, I was completely bound, unable to struggle. Like a desperate prey, I slowly fell."

"Within the dreamlike splendor, I vaguely saw myriad Dao paths laid out. Some had empty positions, some returned, and some were completely erased, leaving only a blank space. A few traces remained."

"All Daos stood side-by-side, within a grand hall."

"And above it, a phantom image sat enthroned."

"Like an emperor ruling, looking down with indifference..."

Tai Yi's phantom image waved its hand, attempting to recreate for the Saints the scene it had witnessed at that time.

However, the light and shadow flickered for a moment, then vanished like a bubble.

Even with Tai Yi's power, he could not maintain and replicate the specific appearance within the flowing light!

Tai Yi, accustomed to this, no longer tried and continued to describe, "I was suddenly struck by this shocking scene, my body and thoughts frozen. I drifted towards the position of [Tai Yi] within the hall. At the same time, I realized that if I truly fell in, I would never be able to leave for the rest of my life. Thus, I was alerted and struggled with all my might..."

"But how can a worm caught in a net escape?" Ultimately, I was getting closer and closer to the position of Tai Yi."

Although they already knew that Tai Yi would be safe, recalling the thrilling scene at the time, all the Saints couldn't help but break into a cold sweat. Just as they were waiting for what happened next, Tai Yi's phantom image fell silent.

"What happened later? How did you escape?" Bai Xiao couldn't help but ask.

"I don't know," Tai Yi suddenly smiled.

The newly promoted Saints were astonished.

But the Saints of the other shore clearly knew this and all shook their heads helplessly.

"It's not that I'm unwilling to reveal it, but I truly escaped from that Grand Dao Hall in a confused state. This has always been my greatest confusion. Until later, when the Mountains and Seas took shape, and the Primordial Immortal Realm disintegrated, and even after I achieved Sainthood..."

"I never encountered that flowing light again."

Tai Yi said with some emotion, and then looked at the Saints present. "If, one day, any of you encounter this flowing light again, perhaps you can help me ask what exactly happened back then, to resolve the confusion in my heart for countless years."

Having finally heard a rather exciting story, only to have it abruptly stop midway with no continuation, all the Saints naturally felt frustrated.

Bai Xiao wanted to speak but stopped, eventually just clearing his throat. "You have lived a long time, and naturally seen more. None of us have seen any Misty Creation. I'm afraid even if we did, we wouldn't be able to identify it."

"That won't happen. Just like this thing held in the hand of [Fate Hub], even if it has no form, you will surely sense its extraordinariness." Tai Yi's phantom image pointed at the flickering memory of Mountains and Seas in the void.

From this, Li Fan understood the identity of the mysterious figure who sat and wove a net in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Listening to Saint Lianshan's words, it seems he knows this Fate Hub?"

"He was a traveling companion on my path to the summit mountain. At that time, the pattern of Mountains and Seas was not yet fixed, and countless heroes and prodigies wanted to establish eternal foundations. Naturally, I wasn't the only one who wanted to ascend the summit mountain."

"Countless people ascended, but only this Fate Hub could follow closely behind me. Thus, I have a deep impression of him."

"It's just..."

"I ultimately stood on the mountain peak before him. As I was meditating with closed eyes, I suddenly saw a look of terror on his face, as if he foresaw something extremely dreadful. Then he gritted his teeth and fled, disappearing without a trace. From then on, he was nowhere to be found in Mountains and Seas, and I haven't seen him for many, many years." Saint Lianshan's voice was somewhat ethereal.

"Perhaps he thought Saint Lianshan would indeed ascend the mountain. He thought he would be suppressed by you forever, and that's why he fled in a hurry," Bai Xiao joked.

"That's what I thought at the time too," Saint Lianshan suddenly said, and Bai Xiao's smile instantly froze.

"Although the choice at that time was made after much deliberation, I had not yet made my decision before Fate Hub disappeared. It was precisely his terrified flight that made me finally make my decision. To practice Lian Shan, not Sitting Mountain."

Saint Lianshan's words seemed incomplete.

Li Fan and all the Saints could naturally understand the hidden meaning in his words.

Roughly, before achieving Dao, Lianshan was somewhat arrogant. Seeing Fate Hub flee in a panic before he had even made his decision, Lianshan couldn't help but feel thoughts like "You look down on me like this?" and "Am I that kind of person?"

Thus, his decision was influenced.

The newly promoted Saints chuckled inwardly. Inadvertently, this foremost immortal in the world became a more concrete figure in everyone's minds, no longer just an unfathomablely powerful being.

"So, Fate Hub found no hope of proving Dao, and thus sought a way to reverse it. This Misty Creation was targeted by him. If it truly is the origin of Mountains and Seas before their existence, perhaps it could indeed change everything."

"I don't know what he was tracking and pursuing. Judging by his joyful expression upon his initial entry, perhaps this wasn't his first attempt to lure it," Bai Xiao murmured.

The Saints remained silent, their gazes returning to the memory of Mountains and Seas.

Finally, Duke Shou Qiu spoke.

"The priority now is to reconnect Mountains and Seas. As for the clue of Misty Creation... after Mountains and Seas are connected, perhaps we can personally travel to the scene and investigate," the Saints nodded, then withdrew their gazms and returned their attention to the areas observed by their projected thoughts.

Li Fan silently noted Duke Shou Qiu's words.

"Mountains and Seas will be reconnected, and everything within Mountains and Seas will be restored to its original state."

"But True Return, which transcends Mountains and Seas and is already within me, will naturally not reappear out of thin air."

"That Fate Hub Saint is probably the same."

"The so-called scene is merely a more realistic trace than a memory projection."

Li Fan had no worries about this point.

"I just don't know if the flowing light that Tai Yi encountered back then was indeed True Return."

"The hall of Daos he described bears some resemblance to [Great Dao Returns to Truth], but we cannot be sure."

"If it wasn't True Return... are there other Misty Creations in Mountains and Seas?"

With countless thoughts swirling, Li Fan's attention gradually returned to "Li Bufan."

Since he had already identified the key memory nodes of Mountains and Seas, what Li Fan needed to do was to ensure that this illusory memory continued to flow according to its original trajectory.

"If Fate Hub is not here, I will be Fate Hub."

"If the entity being captured doesn't come, I will create its presence. Put on a show to deceive the Mountains and Seas that are transforming from illusory to real."

"But I need to carefully consider how to perform this play."

Firstly, he could not use the Saintly power of his main body from outside the projection.

Instead, he had to rely on the strength of this "Li Bufan" himself.

Otherwise, the illusory Mountains and Seas would surely detect external manipulation.

"However, his cultivation is only at the late stage of Foundation Establishment..." Li Fan frowned, then relaxed.

"Fortunately, he also cultivates the [Mountain Sitting Secret]."

The version passed down in later generations, compared to the one obtained by He Zhenghao, was indeed very different.

The later version, although still called Mountain Sitting, was actually "sitting on people."

After all, to truly find a mountain that could grow day by day and cultivate there…

Perhaps before finding the target, one would turn into withered bones.

But by sponsoring potential talents and forming good relationships everywhere, through a wide net, the efficiency wouldn't be particularly low.

However, the most ancient version of the Mountain Sitting Secret from the Divine Wood Sect was true mountain sitting!

This was because the Divine Wood Sect possessed a Divine Wood.

Li Fan examined the cultivation methods of the Divine Wood Sect disciples in Li Bufan's memories.

The Divine Wood Sect came from outside the heavens and was the foundation of the Divine Wood Sect.

Rooted in the earth, its shade covered over thirty thousand li.

As the wood grew, the earth expanded.

Originally, the location of the Divine Wood was an endless plain.

But as the Divine Wood grew upwards, the mountain Li Fan stood on had now transformed into a continuous and majestic mountain range.

The Divine Wood sat atop this mountain range.

And with the continued growth of the Divine Wood, the mountain beneath Li Fan's feet was also continuously increasing in height at an almost perceptible speed.

Those who cultivate the Mountain Sitting Secret in the Divine Wood Sect, by remaining seated and not moving, saw their cultivation progress at lightning speed.

The weaker the person, the better the effect.

After all, compared to the Divine Wood and the mountain range, even a slight increase in their size was an unimaginable amount of power for low-level cultivators.

"Once I reach a certain level of proficiency in the Mountain Sitting Secret, I can then switch to other cultivation techniques."

"With the help of the Divine Wood's rise among the mountains, the number of the Divine Wood Sect's low-level cultivators far surpasses other sects in the Xuanhuang Realm, filling the land everywhere!"

Li Fan swept his gaze across. Beneath the shade of the Divine Wood, courtyards were built on almost every mountain peak. Cultivators resided there.

"No wonder Ruomu wanted to fight this Divine Wood to the death. At this rate, after tens of thousands of years, it would completely occupy the Xuanhuang Realm."

"This Divine Wood came from outside the heavens, I don't know whose work it was. They must have also coveted the so-called opportunities..."

"It's a pity it was so crudely severed," Li Fan snorted inwardly.

"The battle between the Divine Wood and Ruomu should have been evenly matched. However, with Fate Hub's secret intervention, the Divine Wood Sect soon fell into defeat, the wood died, and the sect was destroyed..."

"This time, I will act as a disciple of the Divine Wood Sect and re-enact the past actions of Fate Hub."

Thinking this, Li Fan came to the outside of the sect's sacrificial hall on the highest peak of the Divine Wood Sect.

Looking down, he saw countless disciples of the Divine Wood Sect.

"My debt is not heavy when not weighed, but it is more than a thousand catties when weighed..."

"After a year of arduous travel, it is time to collect some interest."

"Consider it a pre-performance for my Saint Sitting Secret!"

The Heaven Sitting Secret circulated silently within him.

*Boom...*

All the Divine Wood Sect disciples who had received favors from Li Fan felt their bodies tremble slightly at this moment. The spiritual energy flow within their Dantian seemed to accelerate.

Unaware of the reason, they believed it was the Divine Wood's grace, further accelerating their cultivation speed.

They rejoiced greatly.

However, they did not know that as spiritual energy flowed within their bodies, nearly half of the cultivation generated was plundered.

It converged upon Li Fan.

However, Li Fan secretly used the Heaven Sitting Secret to urge the numerous Divine Wood disciples, at the cost of their life force, to temporarily increase their cultivation speed.

Therefore, in general, their cultivation progress did not decrease but rather increased.

All of this was done by Li Fan in extreme secrecy.

As expected of Saintly means, ordinary people could not detect it.

"Anyway, they will all die in the upcoming battle between the Divine Wood and Ruomu."

"Using up their potential in advance will not affect the trajectory of the Mountains and Seas'脉络."

Feeling the feedback cultivation constantly gathering within his body, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction.

With the power of one person, even if cultivating extremely fast.

How could it compare to the merit of Heaven Sitting?

In just three years, Li Fan had risen from the Foundation Establishment stage to the Harmonious Dao stage.

The limit of mortals!

Chapter 1690: Enlightenment Between Reality and Illusion

"At this point in time, the immortal path still exists. After Harmonizing with the Dao, one ascends to become an immortal."

Even though it was merely the Mountains and Seas in a state of mutual generation between the illusory and the real, those things that should exist would still persist.

Standing atop the Divine Wood, Li Fan vaguely sensed the aura of the Immortal Realm, as if within reach. It seemed that with just a little more effort, he could ascend.

"The restrictions are indeed not as strong as they are later; one can truly become an immortal."

"It's a pity that with the successive destruction of the Immortal Realm's immortal domains, the frightened immortals, in their pursuit of survival, placed increasingly greater hope on the lower realm's testing grounds."

"This resulted in all beings in the Lan Ke Dao Field, except for those with connections, those who inherently came from the Immortal Realm, or those who were chosen. For all others who Harmonized with the Dao, there was no possibility of ascending. Even if their strength and cultivation were sufficient, all they would face was endless heavenly tribulations."

"However, on second thought, the Lan Ke Dao Field, especially the Xuanhuang Realm, is a true treasure land sought after by countless nameless individuals. If those who painstakingly sought to ascend knew this truth, I wonder what their thoughts would be."

Li Fan stood on the Divine Wood, contemplating, and slowly inhaled.

The lives and cultivation of hundreds of thousands of Divine Wood Sect cultivators were once again mobilized, slowly transforming into feedback cultivation within Li Fan.

Even though he had reached the pinnacle of the mortal realm and could no longer advance in his cultivation, the interest that should be collected still had to be collected without pause. Every bit, in the form of a phantom body, was stored within Li Fan's dantian, ready for when it was needed.

"The so-called 'going with the flow' can only be manipulated using the power of the Mountains and Seas born within this illusory realm; only then will it not arouse suspicion."

"However... with only the cultivation of Harmonizing with the Dao, recreating what Fate Hub once did will be somewhat strenuous."

"It's time for my next move."

Although the Divine Wood Sect also had cultivators who Harmonized with the Dao, cultivators who Harmonized with the Dao were not all equal. Li Fan, under broad daylight, stood on the Divine Wood for a long time, yet no one discovered it.

Even the Divine Wood itself was unaware.

Li Fan's figure flashed, and in an instant, he took a hundred steps on the Divine Wood's crown.

As if forming an arcane formation.

Simultaneously, the auras of hundreds of thousands of Divine Wood cultivators below were also drawn, surging towards Li Fan like rolling waves.

Through the Divine Wood's trunk, they wound and intertwined.

Like countless ropes crisscrossing, they all converged into Li Fan's hands.

"Go!"

With a soft shout from Li Fan, these ropes then connected with the phantom images that had been left in the previous steps.

"Cultivators dwell upon the Divine Wood to benefit from the 'Sitting on a Mountain' technique."

"The strength of the Divine Wood is millions of times greater than that of the cultivators. Therefore, it can disregard the burden on the cultivators and even promote them while it grows. However..."

"This weight of the cultivators, channeled through me, may not be something you can bear."

Li Fan's gaze deepened as he used the hundreds of thousands of cultivators under his control as a lever, gently pressing down.

"Creak..."

An invisible colossal force was instantly applied to the Divine Wood's body.

To the outside world, everything appeared normal; not even the leaves of the Divine Wood stirred too much.

However, in reality, the Divine Wood, which overshadowed an area of thirty thousand li, along with the mountains beneath it,

were pushed down by an inch by Li Fan.

To damage the 'Sitting on a Mountain' merit was not Li Fan's intention, but merely to test the limit of the power he could currently mobilize.

Having achieved his objective, he quickly retracted his hand.

"In my view, without the need for ascension from the upper realm, one could naturally step into the Mountains and Seas and become an immortal on the spot."

"But in this era, no true immortals were born. If the illusory projection deviates too much from the former true Mountains and Seas, the illusory Mountains and Seas will not reappear."

"To achieve transcendence with mortal power is indeed fraught with limitations and troublesome. Perhaps only the Saints can accomplish it."

Li Fan's solution was simple.

Since external forces could not be used to create something out of nothing, he would instead utilize the immortal power that already existed within the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Regardless of the process in between, as long as the beginning remains unchanged and the ending remains unchanged, and no external forces intervene during this period."

"Then the illusory Mountains and Seas can be recreated."

The first thing Li Fan had to do was to intercept the wisp of immortal power that lingered around the Divine Wood.

The Divine Wood originated from outside the heavens and was a means implanted by a true immortal from the upper realm into the Xuanhuang Realm. This was beyond doubt.

It was just that the method employed by this unknown true immortal was extremely subtle.

This connection was almost non-existent, extremely faint.

Even with Li Fan's cultivation of Harmonizing with the Dao, he could not sense the slightest connection between the Divine Wood and the distant Immortal Realm.

But now, with the power of hundreds of thousands of cultivators, he achieved comprehensive suppression of the Divine Wood.

Upon closer inspection, he finally found a clue.

"This connection is not in the branches or the trunk, but within the roots."

Li Fan scanned with his divine sense. Amidst the extremely complex roots of the Divine Wood, which burrowed and spread across a million li of earth, he found traces of its connection to the Immortal Realm.

"The entity on the other side is also an unknown true immortal, extremely cautious, afraid of exposing his designs on the Xuanhuang Realm, hence the limited immortal power he could wield..."

"As a starting point, it's enough."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. He gently pressed his hands down, suppressing the Divine Wood again, and simultaneously reordered its roots.

Instantly, the myriad root tendrils danced like dragons in the earth's veins, being dismantled and reassembled.

Slowly, amidst the surging earth veins, a formation woven from the Divine Wood's roots took shape.

With a thought from Li Fan, he split off a phantom image of himself and stepped into it to preside over it.

At this point, the Divine Wood's power was completely intercepted.

The life and death of the Divine Wood were in Li Fan's thoughts. He could easily suppress it even without the power of the hundreds of thousands of cultivators he controlled.

The wisp of faint immortal power transmitted from the upper realm, though it allowed the Divine Wood to grow to a towering height,

was something that Li Fan could transform into something extraordinary.

Unleashing a thousandfold, a millionfold of power.

"Next are the immortal artifacts left behind by the various sects."

Having intercepted the immortal power, although Li Bufan only possessed the cultivation of Harmonizing with the Dao, he was in fact no different from a true immortal.

Silently, he suppressed and subdued all the immortal artifacts, which was an easy task.

Even though the immortal artifacts were still stored in their respective sects, they had already changed owners in secret.

After the Immortal Realm came the Xuanhuang Realm's guardian Great Formation.

At this point in time, the ancient immortal formation was perfectly preserved, and the power it could wield was even greater than the immortal artifacts left by the various sects.

After modifying the ancient immortal formation, Li Fan also stole its immortal power and turned it to his own use.

Following that, Li Fan meticulously searched the Xuanhuang continent.

He unhesitatingly incorporated everything that could be utilized into his own possession.

Although the Xuanhuang Realm appeared calm and peaceful on the surface, with no changes,

in reality, internally, it had already undergone a complete upheaval, with a new management.

Time flowed, and Li Fan finally greeted the first critical juncture of the Mountains and Seas' memories.

On this day, it was the day when Fate Hub suddenly appeared in the illusory memory.

Rolling black energy enveloped Li Fan.

Stepping out from the "Li Bufan" he was possessing, he arrived at the exact location where Fate Hub should have appeared.

His actions and demeanor were identical to what was recorded in the Mountains and Seas' memories.

Initially appearing somewhat disheveled, then surprised and delighted.

Subsequently, he sat down and laid out his plan, weaving his net.

"This location is still more suitable for me."

Sitting in the sky above the Xuanhuang Realm, looking down at the myriad beings below, Li Fan joyfully mused.

Although his current location was not the exact center of the Xuanhuang Realm,

the power he controlled had already densely occupied every corner of the Xuanhuang Realm.

With him sitting here, this place had already become the absolute center of the Xuanhuang Realm!

Every move he made caused the Xuanhuang Realm to change.

The situation was precisely as recorded in the Mountains and Seas' memory of Fate Hub.

Suddenly, an invisible net was woven!

Outside the illusory realm, on the other shore, Li Fan's main body observed. He discovered that at this moment, the illusory Mountains and Seas seemed to have become more solid.

The scene rendered by the memory projection had perfectly inherited what had happened in the actual Mountains and Seas.

It was as if they were re-experiencing everything that had happened before, and the transformation between the illusory and the real began to flow.

After a moment of freezing, the light and shadow flickered again, but undoubtedly, it had become much more stable.

This change naturally did not escape the attention of the Saints on the other shore.

"Fellow Daoist Profound Embryo, your progress is quite rapid," Fang Cun said with surprise. "I was originally thinking of keeping a closer eye on your side."

"Let me observe. Hmm... Fellow Daoist Profound Embryo seems to be using his methods with practiced ease?" Bai Xiao also examined Li Fan with surprise.

Li Fan's expression remained unchanged. "Every time we traverse against the current from the end of the Mountains and Seas, suffering heavy injuries, we must start anew. Practice makes perfect."

The Saints nodded slightly but made no further comment.

Regardless of anything else, Li Fan's actions were indeed beneficial to the reconnection of the Mountains and Seas.

"It seems I need to speed up my pace," Jin Gui chuckled, shifting his gaze away from Li Fan.

On the other shore, silence descended once more.

Within the illusory Mountains and Seas, in the Xuanhuang Realm.

With the establishment of the first critical memory node, the entire world seemed to have become more real.

At the very least, the immortal power controlled by Li Fan now flowed almost identically with what he had seen in the true Mountains and Seas.

"Truth and falsehood, illusion and reality, what exactly defines them?"

"After the Mountains and Seas were swallowed by the Star and then recreated by the 'True Return' thought, how exactly was this achieved?"

Being situated between the illusory and the real allowed for a better perception of the Dao of illusion and reality.

Though he sat still, Li Fan's comprehension grew daily.

Not long after, another critical juncture arrived.

In the southeast corner of the Xuanhuang Realm, a hidden radiance lit up.

A true immortal from the upper realm had stealthily descended.

The true immortal believed his movements were hidden, but he did not realize that every action, every word, was under Li Fan's control.

"Living a life of carefree freedom in a cage, how can one achieve true carefree freedom? Even when trapped in a catastrophe..."

The light and shadow gradually darkened, and the true immortal revealed his true appearance. He looked towards the Immortal Realm, shook his head slightly, and sighed.

Perhaps because a segment of memory had solidified, the scene rendered by the Mountains and Seas at this moment was clearer than Li Fan had observed from the other shore earlier.

The appearance that was originally impossible to discern could now be seen clearly.

This true immortal was someone Li Fan had also seen before.

It was none other than the Lord of Famine, [Wu Wei]!

At this moment, he leisurely headed towards the fishing pond.

Clearly, he already knew the location of this fishing ground within the Mountains and Seas.

He seemed to be enjoying the process of escape, not rushing his journey, but looking around as he traveled.

"Long dwelling in the cage, to return to nature once more..."

He chanted softly, content and at ease.

But slowly, the ease and contentment on his face gradually disappeared.

Replaced by extreme solemnity.

"This place..."

"Seems somewhat amiss."

He stopped chanting and his expression turned panicked. He no longer bothered to look around and frantically quickened his pace, arriving at the edge of the fishing pond.

As if prepared, he casually cast his fishing rod.

He did not even sit down, but merely stood, waiting for the bite.

Soon, the water of the fishing pond rippled slightly, and waves gradually formed. A powerful force surged from beneath the water.

Wu Wei remained unfazed and even rejoiced. Without any resistance, he went with the flow and fell into the pond.

And disappeared.

In the fishing grounds of the Mountains and Seas, the water surface gradually returned to calm.

On the other side, it was unknown what had happened,

causing the passage on the Xuanhuang Realm side to gradually close.

At this moment, just as in the true history, Fate Hub the second had done, Li Fan made his move.

Starlight flickered throughout the Xuanhuang Realm.

This was Li Fan exerting all the power he could mobilize to its limit.

Behind the fishing pond, there was implicitly a Saintly existence.

Although in the illusory Mountains and Seas, true Saints could not manifest, the Mountains and Seas would instinctively simulate the might of a Saint based on their memories. Li Fan dared not be careless.

As expected, when he tried to prevent the passage of the fishing grounds from closing, an unimaginable pulling force suddenly emanated from beneath the water.

Li Fan, who was sitting in the void, almost lost his footing.

Fortunately, he had made ample preparations.

The Divine Wood's roots were embedded in the Xuanhuang Realm's earth veins; the immortal artifacts of the world were entangled with the fate of various sects; the Primordial Immortal Formation was even integrated with the Xuanhuang.

At this moment, they all transformed into Li Fan's tendrils.

Intertwining and wrapping, they helped Li Fan stabilize his footing.

However, the pulling force from the fishing pond was somewhat beyond Li Fan's imagination.

After being obstructed, instead of weakening, it intensified.

It was as if it were determined to hook Li Fan, this great fish, if he didn't get hooked!

Since Li Fan was now deeply bound to the Xuanhuang Realm, in reality, he was pulling the entire Xuanhuang Realm, and even the original possibility, into the fishing pond!

No matter how much preparation he made, all of Li Fan's arrangements relied on various factors within the Xuanhuang Realm.

This was a limitation determined by the illusory memory itself.

How could it contend with such colossal force?

Unstoppably, inch by inch, he fell towards the fishing pond.

What happened in the illusory memory began to deviate from the true Mountains and Seas.

The entire world, in this instant, seemed to be covered with a different hue, becoming peculiar and strange.

The beings within the world could not perceive it.

But the Saints on the other shore saw the change happen immediately.

If Li Fan failed here, all the Saints' efforts to reconnect the Mountains and Seas would be in vain.

In this urgent situation, Saint Lianshan made a decisive move and transmitted guidance, saying, "Do not contend with it. Its momentum is weak; perhaps there is a turning point!"

Li Fan's heart was enlightened, and he instantly retracted some of his power.

But he did not completely cease resistance.

Because in this brief moment of stalemate, the Xuanhuang Realm itself seemed to have fallen partially into the pond. The pond's area remained unchanged, but it appeared even more profound.

Strangely, as Li Fan released his grip, the pulling force from the fishing grounds of the Mountains and Seas also diminished.

After a few more tugs, realizing that this was not the intended "great fish," it lost interest.

Then it completely abandoned the attempt to pull.

Chapter 1691: Willing to be idle, not to be holy

With neither side exerting force, the fishing pond water gradually calmed.

With Li Fan's power acting as a barrier, this Mountains and Seas fishing ground was not sealed off again. The trajectory of the Mountains and Seas projection finally realigned with history.

Everything that was on the verge of collapse returned to stability.

Li Fan secretly breathed a sigh of relief.

"I almost made a fool of myself," he said with a look of shame on the Other Shore.

"There won't be any Saints truly appearing in the Mountains and Seas projection, but the memories of Mountains and Seas will instinctively manifest everything as it originally was. This means that although this fishing ground is fake, the pulling force it just exerted is no different from a real Mountains and Seas fishing ground. To be able to wrestle and hold your ground with it for so long with just a single wisp of intent is already quite remarkable," Duke Shou Qiu said.

"The Mountains and Seas projection is likely imitating that Angler. The more the hooked fish struggle, the happier he himself becomes. But if the prey is truly ordinary, he will lose interest. He might even give up directly," the phantom image of Saint Lianshan explained.

"It sounds like this 'Mountains and Seas Angler' is a true fishing enthusiast. But with Mountains and Seas on the brink of destruction, he still has the leisure to fish across the heavens," Bai Xiao said, staring at the Mountains and Seas fishing ground with an unreadable tone.

Saint Tai Yi chuckled upon hearing this, "Everyone has their own aspirations. In the Angler's heart, there is only fishing. He doesn't care about anything else, even if Mountains and Seas collapse. Not to mention saving Mountains and Seas from the reverse current."

Bai Xiao snorted, "If Mountains and Seas were truly annihilated, and this fishing ground ceased to exist, where else could he fish?"

"He did mention this. The Mountains and Seas fishing grounds connect different segments of Mountains and Seas. If he can still fish without end, it means the situation of the entire segment of Mountains and Seas is far from as dire as it appears. If, one day, he can't catch any more fish from anywhere in Mountains and Seas, then he will naturally take action," Saint Tai Yi shook his head.

"What kind of twisted logic is that..."

Bai Xiao, upon hearing this, was about to retort, but was interrupted by the phantom image of Saint Lianshan, "Not to mention that the Mountains and Seas Angler is of equal strength to us, even if he were a mortal, it would be inappropriate for us to impose our will under the guise of saving the world. Just like you, if you hadn't intended to 'connect the stars,' we wouldn't have forcibly intervened even if you spied on the secrets of all beings."

"This is what is meant by, 'all beings have their own karmic affinities. They cannot be forced.'"

Bai Xiao's expression froze instantly. He shut his mouth sheepishly.

Saint Tai Yi then chuckled and tried to smooth things over, "Do you still remember the Great Sage of the Tomb of Scriptures from the Immortal Realm you were in before?"

"How could I forget? That fellow is incredibly petty. He chased me all over the world just because I exposed his true form? After I became a Saint, I was so focused on saving the world that I forgot to go back and settle the score with him..." Bai Xiao said with a half-joking tone.

"The Great Sage of the Tomb of Scriptures had the potential to become a Saint back then. However, he was naturally free-spirited and unwilling to bear too much. Even the affairs of a realm were already beyond his capacity. So, over the years, his realm has remained stagnant. Originally, we occasionally persuaded him, but after finding it useless, we stopped interfering. If you truly wish to hunt him down, it's not impossible. Perhaps it could even put pressure on him and help him take that final step."

"He is hiding in the real Mountains and Seas, living a carefree life. If you search seriously, you should be able to find him," Saint Tai Yi said indifferently.

"Uh... let's forget it then." For some reason, a flicker of apprehension crossed Bai Xiao's eyes, and he said sheepishly.

...

After a brief commotion, peace returned to the Other Shore.

It turned out that Li Fan's progress in controlling the memory projection was among the best of the Saints.

After he stabilized the situation, substantive light beams began to arrive consecutively from the Void Realm. These were signs that the Saints had completed the main memory pathways of Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan's consciousness returned.

In the Xuanhuang Realm projection, he would now be leading the destruction of the Divine Wood Sect.

For Li Fan, who had already subdued the Divine Wood, this was naturally a simple matter.

"It's a good opportunity to transform the Divine Wood's power from manifest to hidden, and to completely harness it for my use."

"As for the people of the Divine Wood Sect..."

"Those who deserve to die, will eventually die."

Li Fan's expression was indifferent, having already decided the fate of the magnificent sect and millions of cultivators.

Everything unfolded as it had happened in the historical Mountains and Seas.

The news of the Divine Wood being gravely injured by the Desolate God and the Divine Wood Sect being forced to search everywhere for methods to heal it spread throughout the Xuanhuang Realm.

Some hearts began to stir.

Among them, Ruomu was the most prominent.

As the source of life in Xuanhuang and the progenitor of a hundred trees, the arrival and growth of the Outer Heavenly Divine Wood was the first true threat to it.

It was a pity that it had not paid attention in the beginning. By the time it realized its threat, it was already too late.

After lying in wait for so many years, an opportunity finally presented itself.

Thus, it no longer hesitated.

Countless mountain spirits and wood spirits, obscuring the sun and shielding the earth, arrived from all realms of Xuanhuang, surrounding the Divine Wood Sect.

Interspersed among them were many Harmonious Dao cultivators enticed by Ruomu's promise of "increased lifespan," as well as rogue cultivators with the intention of profiting from the chaos.

The cultivators of the Divine Wood Sect stood united, defending against the enemy.

Although they did not have many top-tier combatants, the total number of Golden Core to Nascent Soul cultivators far surpassed the invading forces.

Moreover, with the Divine Wood as their support, as long as they were not killed on the spot, they could quickly recover under the nourishment of the continuous life force.

For a time, this great battle was evenly matched, with neither side gaining an advantage.

Seeing no opportunity to profit, many cultivators on Ruomu's side began to retreat.

"As long as I can uproot this Divine Wood, I will surely reward all of you with the Fruit of Longevity.

This is a true divine medicine, capable of granting eternal life with just one bite." Ruomu manifested in human form and continued to offer temptations.

A phantom image of a crystal-clear fruit appeared in Ruomu's hand.

At this time, Ruomu was not yet the hunched and terrifying old man of later generations, but a graceful jade-like young man.

He wore green robes, his appearance was as if chiseled by the heavens, perfect and flawless. Coupled with the crystal-clear fruit exuding an aura of longevity in his hand,

The Harmonious Dao cultivators present were all moved and agreed to fight one last desperate battle.

Thus, the final bloody battle commenced.

Because Ruomu had completely withdrawn the life force of the Xuanhuang Realm to attack the Divine Wood Sect, all other regions fell into a sterile winter, frozen for tens of thousands of miles.

Even the flow of heaven and earth spiritual energy became sluggish.

Normal flight for cultivators was affected.

With the harsh weather conditions, except for the battlefield of the Divine Wood Sect, cultivators from other sects mostly chose to remain in seclusion,

Waiting for the outcome of this great battle.

"My son truly has foresight! He has bestowed favors upon others throughout the years, so even though battles are raging now, and he is not on the front lines, people are hesitant to say anything out of past kindness!" the father of Li Bufan exclaimed.

"Unlike the descendants of other elders, who have stayed in the rear for too long and can no longer suppress themselves. To quell public anger, they are forced to go out and fight. How can this terrifying meat grinder be something they can endure? They are basically sending themselves to their deaths."

"He can delay it for a while, but not forever. No, Old Li, you need to think of something. If things continue like this, even if Bufan can still hide in the back, what if the Divine Wood Sect falls..."

"Silence! How can you speak such womanly nonsense!" Li Bufan's father interrupted his wife rudely.

But he looked at Li Bufan, his eyelids gently lowered. He had already made a firm decision in his heart.

The next day, Li Bufan received a talisman from his father. And

Following his instructions, he quietly went to a cave deep in the back mountains of the sect.

After presenting the talisman, he was allowed to enter. He discovered that quite a few people had already gathered inside.

They were all acquaintances.

The elders of the Divine Wood Sect, though most were willing to fight to the death, all wanted to secure a way out for their descendants.

This was only natural for parents.

"Truly, the hearts of parents worldwide are pitiful," Li Fan sneered inwardly, his gaze sweeping over everyone present.

In real history, these second-generation disciples of the Divine Wood Sect naturally could not escape the pursuit.

In the memory projection, Li Fan did not find it troublesome to send them on their way.

With the group assembled, the cave entrance was sealed.

With a slight tremor, the Divine Wood's roots broke through the ground.

Everyone followed the Divine Wood's roots deep underground, quietly leaving the Divine Wood Sect's territory.

"Hm, that's not right? Why isn't the Divine Wood's root stopping even after reaching its destination?" the leading cultivator's expression changed drastically.

But it was already too late.

Unbeknownst to them, underground, the Divine Wood's roots, as if possessing their own will, instantly split into a million, deeply embedding themselves into the bodies of the disciple disciples present.

At this moment, their life force remained, but they were no different from the dead.

And the sect-leading cultivators of the Divine Wood Sect, sensing that their descendants were safely moving away, had no further worries.

They engaged in a desperate battle with the invading enemy.

They even resorted to depleting the original power of the Divine Wood.

Both sides fought for survival, regardless of right or wrong.

Blood energy surged, reaching the heavens.

The entire Xuanhuang Realm sky was stained crimson.

Too many lives were lost. If this continued, even if a victor emerged, other sects would likely benefit.

Thus, both sides began to feel a desire to retreat.

At this moment, Li Fan, who had been observing silently from the sidelines, finally made his move.

With his current cultivation, even without using the power of the Divine Wood disciples' "Sit Mountain Art," he could easily subdue the Divine Wood.

Under his manipulation, the Divine Wood suddenly began to show signs of decay.

A gust of wind blew, and countless withered yellow leaves fell like a torrential rain.

This scene caused both sides, who were locked in fierce combat, to be stunned.

The Divine Wood Sect's hearts went cold.

Ruomu's side, on the other hand, was invigorated.

With victory imminent, their eyes turned blood red, and they swarmed forward like they were injected with chicken blood.

Under the influence of Li Fan's mysterious hand, the scales of the battle tipped.

The Divine Wood Sect's defenses crumbled like an avalanche.

The battlefield transformed from a clash between two forces into a one-sided slaughter.

"Good, good, good!"

Seeing victory within reach, Ruomu was overwhelmed with emotion and exclaimed "good" three times.

Behind it, its true form projection could even be faintly seen.

Beneath the earth's veins, Ruomu's roots, coming from all directions,

Tightly entwined the independently standing mountains and rivers, the Divine Wood.

Then, it broke through the tree trunk and burrowed in.

"If I can be nourished by this wood, not only will all past injuries be restored, but I might even be able to advance further!"

Ruomu was leisurely fantasizing about the future, completely unaware that wisps of bizarre power were already entering its body along with the Divine Wood it was absorbing.

Finally, with the thunderous collapse of the towering Divine Wood, turning into rotten wood and ashes, signifying the end of this great battle.

Ruomu did not break its promise and distributed the Fruits of Longevity to several cultivators.

After this...

Ruomu returned to its original domain, smugly assessing its gains from absorbing the Divine Wood.

To its horror, it discovered that a figure was sitting on its head, who had appeared there at some unknown time!

"Since the Divine Wood is gone, I'll take you as a substitute," Li Fan said calmly.

"Who are you..." Ruomu attempted to speak, only to find that it could no longer move!

From Ruomu's body, roots began to sprout, piercing through its trunk and growing wildly.

In the blink of an eye, Ruomu was replaced.

The Divine Wood Sect was destroyed, and Ruomu regained control of the Xuanhuang spiritual脉.

Another predetermined event was completed, and the Mountains and Seas memory projection became even more stable.

Li Fan sat atop Ruomu's head, using its power to completely control the overall situation.

"At this point, Ruomu is far from comparable to its withered state in later generations."

"It is the central nexus of life flow in the Xuanhuang experimental field, capable of even reversing the states of the four seasons of the Xuanhuang Realm at a foundational level with a single thought."

"It's a pity that, whether willingly or unwillingly, too many Fruits of Longevity were distributed, leading to its tragic end in the future."

"But it doesn't matter."

With a single thought, Li Fan detected the whereabouts of the numerous longevity fruits Ruomu had bestowed.

"The opportunity for longevity should not be easily given to others."

"Although I cannot alter your fate..."

"I can turn you into my pawns."

Under Li Fan's profound energy infusion, the fruits that could grant eternal life with the heavens turned into puppet-like poisons without anyone noticing.

The eaters, though unaware, had their every word, action, and even thoughts influenced by Li Fan.

Although Li Fan previously had immense power, he still needed to intervene directly to manipulate and alter the Xuanhuang Realm.

However, with the implantation of these "longevity realm" pawns, outward intervention was no longer necessary.

With just a thought, the Xuanhuang Realm's situation could be subtly altered.

With absolute influence, the overall situation was decided.

The chessboard of the Xuanhuang Realm did not require Li Fan to personally move the pieces; the game would proceed according to his thoughts.

Effortless and efficient, the next step was the final and most crucial one.

To reproduce the scene of the Fate Pillar capturing the unknown divine object.

"Simply recreating the scene is not difficult. What's difficult is recreating the mysterious fluctuation generated during the struggle between both sides," Li Fan frowned slightly.

Even the Saints observing from the Other Shore, when witnessing the fluctuation, would instantly feel its extraordinary nature.

"To achieve the realm of 'real is imitation,' and even deceive Mountains and Seas themselves..."

Li Fan slowly recalled what he had seen.

At the same time, outside the projected realm, on the Other Shore, his main body once again cast its gaze.

He did not ask the Saints for help but instead focused on comprehending it himself.

He thought of the traction force from the self-simulated Mountains and Seas fishing ground by the Mountains and Seas projection earlier.

"It doesn't have to exist in reality. It just needs to make Mountains and Seas believe it exists."

"I can play the role of the Fate Pillar. And as for the other..."

Just as Li Fan was contemplating, a faint ripple emanated from the deepest part of his heart.

It was incredibly subtle, less than Li Fan's own mental fluctuations.

But it was clearly not Li Fan's own.

"Is this... True Return?"

Li Fan maintained an outwardly calm expression, but inwardly suppressed his shock, guessing True Return's intentions.

The ripple from True Return was fleeting, but it was certainly not without purpose.

"It must have sensed my thoughts just now."

"Just now..."

"I wanted to perfectly reproduce the fluctuation of that time."

"True Return means that doing so is dangerous?"

Chapter 1692: Virtual World's Great Counterattack

"Ever since I came to the Other Shore and came into contact with the Saints, True Return has remained hidden. Yet now, it suddenly appears, risking discovery by the Saints..."

"This indicates that if I truly act according to my thoughts, my situation might be even more perilous."

Having been with True Return for a long time, even though it didn't explicitly state anything, but only transmitted faint ripples, Li Fan instantly understood its intent.

"Before True Return's reminder, I intended to..."

"Replicate the fluctuation of the two sides' struggle as much as possible, in order to deceive the projected Mountains and Seas."

After careful consideration, Li Fan gradually understood.

The Misty Creation, with no duality in Mountains and Seas. The fluctuation caused by its struggle with the Fate Pillar was, theoretically, impossible to replicate. Even Mountains and Seas themselves could not truly restore that scene.

"Only through the transformation of true and false might it be possible to achieve a perfect replication. I was deeply immersed in it, desperately wanting to recreate that scene, and instinctively wanted to invoke the transformation of true and false."

"If it truly came to that, perhaps the fluctuation I fabricated would even be more real than what the Mountains and Seas memories displayed. Because that Misty Creation is very likely True Return itself."

Having figured this out, Li Fan inwardly lamented his close call.

In fact, Li Fan's identity as a time-traveler from the end of time already had minor flaws. However, due to his unique ability of True Spirit Infusion, the Saints chose to overlook them. But Li Fan believed that if he were to reveal that he possessed the Misty Creation, the outcome might be different.

"I only need to restore it to the best of my ability with the strength expected of the 'Profound Embryo' Great Dao. As for whether I can truly deceive the projected Mountains and Seas, and achieve the successful reconnection..."

"I am merely here to probe the Saints' strengths and find a path for further advancement. What does the well-being of Mountains and Seas matter to me?"

Li Fan snorted inwardly.

Then, his thoughts subtly shifted. Recalling his previous thoughts, he felt a slight sinking feeling.

"Now that I think about it, it's rather strange. After staying in the Zuan Ji Ring for so long, I've gradually started to genuinely desire to save Mountains and Seas."

"My own main body's influence hasn't been that significant yet, but the wisp of intent I projected into the Mountains and Seas projection..."

"Although its methods are still similar to mine, its objective is truly to reconnect Mountains and Seas, and it spares no effort."

"These old fellows are indeed not to be trifled with. No wonder they insisted that the newly promoted Saints sit in the Zuan Ji Ring, allowing them to subtly alter the Saints' thoughts."
