"Although I have awakened now, I cannot guarantee that I won't be influenced again at some point. I must return to True Return before I am completely changed..."

True Return's reminder was like a sudden enlightenment, allowing Li Fan to temporarily break free from the influence of the Saints in the Zuan Ji Ring.

Li Bufan in the projected Xuanhuang Realm also became less zealous.

"This preparation should be sufficient."

"If I can deceive the projected Mountains and Seas, all the better. If not..."

"I've done my best."

He sat on Ruomu and thought this.

Time flowed, and the day of the struggle between the Fate Pillar and the Misty Creation, as recorded in historical Mountains and Seas memories, arrived.

Although Li Fan had now mastered almost all the power of the Xuanhuang Realm, he still could not perfectly replicate the profound fluctuation of that time.

There were deviations from the memories, and subtle tremors began to emanate from the depths of the Mountains and Seas pathways.

Although the virtual projection had become more solid than before due to the establishment of the first two memory points, the instability at the end began to affect the entire projection of that segment of Mountains and Seas in the virtual realm.

It was almost predictable that it would become precarious, facing imminent overall destruction.

"Not good!" Li Fan's main body on the Other Shore cried out in alarm.

The anomaly in the projection had already attracted the attention of the other Saints.

Although the Three Saints of Lianshan intended to help, their main bodies were too far ahead in the virtual realm to intervene.

The newly promoted Saints, who were closer to Li Fan, were powerless to simulate the profound fluctuation.

Even though the phantom image of Saint Lianshan transmitted instructions in time, it was still somewhat late.

The collapse of Mountains and Seas began from the smallest of details.

The virtual projection, which had already been built to nine-tenths completion, began to collapse instantly.

Countless lights and shadows shattered like bubbles in an instant.

As if stirring up a colossal wave, the icy Void Realm unleashed a backlash.

"Return!"

In the Zuan Ji Ring, the phantoms of the Three Saints Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi simultaneously uttered a low cry.

The white circle also emitted an unprecedented radiance, as if reflecting through the boundless Void Realm, reaching the main bodies of the Saints.

Li Fan clearly saw invisible ropes extending from the Zuan Ji Ring, connecting to the Saints in the Void Realm.

At this moment, the ropes were instantly pulled, yanking the Saints, who were trapped in the Void Realm's backlash, back.

The Saints' phantom images instantly solidified, and all of them vomited large mouthfuls of blood.

Only Li Fan, who was already in the Zuan Ji Ring, was an exception.

Li Fan seemed stunned by the scene, freezing on the spot.

Before he could speak, Saint Lianshan sternly said, "The Void Realm backlash and the Dao Annihilation tide will consume at least eight hundred years. There's no point in defending, give up."

The newly promoted Saints did not yet understand what was happening, but the Nine Saints on the Other Shore sighed softly, preparing themselves.

The light circle on the Other Shore seemed to suddenly shrink.

The area it covered visibly shortened.

After adjusting the protective range, Li Fan saw the black tide silently approaching from the end of this segment of Mountains and Seas.

It felt even more suffocating than when he had personally experienced it.

Everywhere it passed, it was razed to the ground.

All things in Mountains and Seas were instantly swallowed.

Countless possibilities, countless beings, perished as a result.

It continued forward, devouring for more than eight hundred years of time, and only stopped when it encountered the white light of the Other Shore.

Although the Dao Annihilation tide was temporarily contained, the cost was...

The Saints in the Zuan Ji Ring vomited blood collectively again.

The Other Shore was still in violent tremors, seemingly on the verge of collapse at any moment.

The assault and backlash of the Dao Annihilation tide did not only come from the direction of the Void Realm.

Instead, it surged from all parts of this segment of Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan personally witnessed countless possibilities, which had been in a state of stalemate, instantly lose their balance and fall into Dao Annihilation.

Mountains and Seas were originally relatively healthy, but now, after a round of backlash from the Void Realm, they appeared to be riddled with holes!

This scene was like a roof suddenly being blown off by a fierce wind during a storm, and torrential rain flooding the house. It was chaotic and precarious.

"It's my fault!" Li Fan slapped his thigh, filled with regret.

"It's just the failure of reconstructing the memory projection, why did it turn out like this?" Bai Xiao coughed lightly, feeling a trace of dread.

"In the struggle with the Void Realm, it's either advance or retreat. If the initial construction had failed, it would have been better. The backlash wouldn't be so terrifying," Saint Lianshan said, abruptly getting up.

He took a step forward.

At this moment, it was as if countless versions of himself emerged from the Zuan Ji Ring and moved towards various parts of Mountains and Seas.

Each Lianshan figure was like a dam,

Forcefully plugging the loopholes in Mountains and Seas.

Not long after, the continuous tremors of Mountains and Seas gradually subsided.

Having escaped this earth-shattering upheaval, Saint Lianshan then looked at Li Fan.

*Buzz...*

The pressure from the main body was incomparable to that of the phantom image.

Even with True Return as protection, Li Fan suddenly felt as if endless Mountains and Seas were pressing down on his shoulders!

He seemed to hear the roars of mountains and seas, growing louder and louder, echoing incessantly!

Although Saint Lianshan remained silent, the invisible pressure in the air was palpable.

The Saints were silent, all looking at Li Fan.

Li Fan seized the opportunity, bowing his head and continuing to express his remorse, "It is my fault! Everything was perfect before. I thought this final step would also be a piece of cake. I never expected..."

"Enough," Saint Lianshan suddenly waved his hand, interrupting Li Fan's self-reproach.

He sat back down and said softly, "It is also my fault. I also thought that Fellow Daoist Xuan Pin could have succeeded."

There seemed to be a hidden meaning in his words, but the Saints present observed their own nostrils and hearts, showing no unusual reactions.

Li Fan continued to bow his head in silence.

Saint Tai Yi stepped in to ease the tension, "Victory and defeat are common in warfare. Our previous attempt to reconnect Mountains and Seas was not smooth sailing either. We can rest and recuperate, and try again. Why be so disheartened?"

As soon as these words were spoken, the frozen atmosphere in the room gradually thawed.

At this moment, as if sensing what had happened to the Saints on the Other Shore, the phantom image of Emperor Tai Wei appeared.

And he also delivered nine large elixirs.

"That's all for now."

"The next batch will take a thousand years to refine."

Emperor Tai Wei came and left like the wind, but before departing, his gaze seemed to sweep over Li Fan.

There were sixteen Saints present.

However, there were only nine Great Saintly Dynasty elixirs.

Lianshan, Shou Qiu, and Tai Yi were the first to speak, "We do not need them."

Li Fan then said tactfully, "Please, fellow Daoists, go ahead."

Afterwards, Shou Qiu, Prying Opportunity, and Guiming also spoke.

The distribution of the elixirs was thus decided.

After consuming the elixirs and recuperating for a period, the Saints' auras finally stabilized completely.

"Rise from where you fell."

"Today, let's first discuss the Fate Pillar and the Misty Creation."

Saint Lianshan spoke again.

In the Zuan Ji Ring, the scene remembered by Mountains and Seas reappeared.

It was vivid, even "more real" than what Li Fan had perceived from afar on the Other Shore.

"The person known as the Fate Pillar, governs the Dao of writing destiny."

"The destinies of all beings in Mountains and Seas are like strings, all within its manipulation."

"It can gather them into a net, or scatter them into a chessboard."

...

Saint Lianshan's voice was exceptionally calm as he expounded the principles of the Fate Pillar.

Li Fan listened intently, gradually becoming engrossed.

Unconsciously, he seemed to have grasped the Saintly Dao of the Fate Pillar.

"This is definitely not due to my own innate talent."

"It is the assistance of the other Saints who are comprehending the Dao in the Zuan Ji Ring."

"The mutual influence is even stronger than when the Saints were merely phantom images."

Li Fan thought this, and a sense of guilt gradually arose in his heart.

Because of his own dereliction of duty, the reconnection of Mountains and Seas had failed.

Although he quickly recoiled from this thought, this trend of "awakening conscience" was like an unstoppable tide.

It was difficult to suppress.

"After the Fate Pillar, let's talk about the Misty Creation."

"Although I do not know its true form, since Mountains and Seas retain its memory, it can be reproduced to some extent."

Saint Lianshan gently pointed towards the center of the hall where the Saints were gathered.

A pinpoint of light emerged,

It was the fluctuation of the Mountains and Seas memory projection, stripped of the Fate Pillar's influence.

The Saints stared at the pinpoint of light in the hall, lost in thought.

"This wisp of Dao intent is quite peculiar. It bears some resemblance to what I saw..." Saint Tai Yi said after observing it, frowning.

"I don't know if it's my imagination, but I seem to sense an aura of [Morality] from it?" Saint Morality said with surprise.

"It seems to encompass all things in Mountains and Seas, possessing everything. It is also like a mirror, reflecting us," Saint Guihai said softly.

...

The Saints each voiced their opinions, and Li Fan also chimed in, "Indeed, one can faintly sense the aura of the [Profound Embryo] Great Dao from it."

Although he appeared calm, his heart was churning like a stormy sea. He was merely forcing himself to maintain composure.

Because the moment the pinpoint of light appeared, he distinctly sensed the aura of [True Return] within it.

However, since True Return was still within him, Li Fan quickly reacted, and Saint Lianshan's simulated projection of True Return's aura was indeed remarkable.

"Transformation of True and False. Those who do not know will not understand."

"But Saint Lianshan can restore it to such an extent..."

As if unaware of Li Fan's thoughts,

Saint Lianshan continued to expound to the Saints, "Saint Guihai's words are brilliant. This Misty Creation, although we do not know its true form, is precisely like a mirror!"

"It can reflect all things in Mountains and Seas..."

"We can observe this mirror by comprehending Mountains and Seas."

As he spoke, without Saint Lianshan's signal, Saint Guihai cooperated, and they both projected images of Mountains and Seas simultaneously.

Mountains and Seas stretched out, faintly visible.

Corresponding to the pinpoint of light, there seemed to be scenes of Mountains and Seas within it.

And the boundless projection of Mountains and Seas slowly contracted, transforming into another pinpoint of light.

Like two suns hanging in the sky, suspended before the Saints.

Regarding the Misty Creation, the Saints had no knowledge of its origins.

But regarding the various aspects of Mountains and Seas, the Saints knew a great deal.

The Saints first looked at the pinpoint of light representing Mountains and Seas, then at the other one.

By extension.

An existence that was previously untouchable now, when viewed again, faintly evoked a sense of familiarity.

Saint Lianshan then looked at Li Fan and asked, "Now that it's reproduced, what's your confidence level?"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and did not answer immediately.

After pondering for a while longer, he extended his hand and revealed another pinpoint of light.

Although it was clearly different from the other two pinpoints of light present, it bore about seventy to eighty percent similarity.

Saint Lianshan nodded and said, "With another thousand years of refinement, it should be fine."

"Let's wait until the Dao Annihilation backlash tide recedes."

After speaking, Saint Lianshan closed his eyes and remained silent.

Only the two pinpoints of light remained in the hall for the Saints to comprehend.

The Void Realm, having gained the advantage of counterattack, did not cease its advance but continued to encroach.

The white circle on the Other Shore did not confront it directly but retreated repeatedly.

Until a thousand years later, when time had passed into the eternal void within which everything was silent, did the two sides finally reach a balance.

The Saints' injuries had long since healed, but they did not act rashly.

Instead, they waited for Emperor Tai Wei to finish refining the Great Elixirs.

During this period, Li Fan also searched for individuals with the potential to become Saints, but unfortunately, he found none after searching all of Mountains and Seas.

In the Zuan Ji Ring, the number of Saints remained as before.

Chapter 1693: The Mountains and Seas Finally Connect

"I fear I will fail again and trouble you all," Li Fan said with a worried expression before the reconnection of Mountains and Seas, "I fear I will fail again and trouble you all."

"Just do your best. Even if you fail again, it will only be another thousand years. Fellow Daoist Xuan Pin need not worry so much," Duke Shou Qiu said with a smile.

"Moreover, I see that you have already grasped nine-tenths of the essence. Deceiving the projected Mountains and Seas should not be a problem."

What Duke Shou Qiu was referring to was Saint Lianshan's explanation of the Fate Pillar and the Misty Creation to the Saints.

Not to mention Li Fan's innate comprehension was already exceptional. With the added benefit of all the Saints present in the Zuan Ji Ring, even a mortal who meditated there for a thousand years would be able to fully grasp its profound essence.

"Last time, we encountered almost no unexpected issues. As long as you can secure this final hurdle, Fellow Daoist Xuan Pin, the reconnection of Mountains and Seas will be within sight."

Li Fan's expression became solemn, "I will do my utmost and not fail the trust placed in me!"

When Emperor Tai Wei delivered the next batch of refined Saintly elixirs, the Saints consumed them, bringing themselves to their peak condition, and then they successively leaped into the Eternal Void Realm.

Naturally, they followed the previous order.

The Three Saints Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi led the way, followed by Prying Opportunity, Guiming, and others.

Tai Qi was last, and Fang Cun roamed.

As for Li Fan, his main body remained seated on the Other Shore, only needing to send a wisp of his intent to guide when the Mountains and Seas projection reappeared.

Repeating the process, with the Saints' talents and methods, no disturbances occurred.

Even though the Void Realm seemed to sense the Saints' return, and the tide became more turbulent and intense, it ultimately had no significant impact.

Specks of light gradually lit up in the darkness. The shattered projection of Mountains and Seas reappeared!

"Go!"

The Saints acted with great tacit understanding, simultaneously channeling their divine senses into it.

As if injecting vitality into it, flowing through the veins of Mountains and Seas, reawakling life.

This time, Li Fan made no further mistakes.

With the power that [Profound Embryo] could manifest, and guided by Saint Lianshan, he finally managed to simulate the struggle between the Fate Pillar and the Misty Creation.

The entire projected Mountains and Seas fell into stillness in an instant.

Then, as if the sky was falling, a rumbling sound came from all directions.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, about to seek the source of the sound.

However, a powerful repulsive force suddenly erupted from "Li Bufan's" body, expelling his intent.

Like ice melting into water, it vanished into Dao Annihilation.

Li Fan paid no mind to the demise of his wisp of intent and stared blankly at the Void Realm.

As far as the eye could see, the Mountains and Seas projection blazed with light.

As if boundless light and heat were constantly erupting, repelling the surrounding Void Realm, inch by inch.

The darkness receded, and the scene of continuous Mountains and Seas gradually rose from the darkness.

This scene was astonishingly similar to what Li Fan had witnessed in his previous life, the descent of the [Star]!

Li Fan stared intently at this wondrous scene. He knew that although the current projection of Mountains and Seas appeared incredibly powerful, it was still not the true Mountains and Seas.

It was merely an illusion.

Like water without a source or a tree without roots, even if they gained a temporary advantage, without subsequent support, they would inevitably be swallowed by Dao Annihilation.

But soon, the supporting power arrived.

From an even more ancient section of Mountains and Seas!

When this gap, severed by the Void Realm, was temporarily filled by the reconstructed projection, Mountains and Seas themselves seemed to sense the changes occurring within them.

An unfathomable great power suddenly descended.

Infinite life-giving and creative power flowed down from the ancient Mountains and Seas.

Wherever it passed, the illusion turned into reality!

Li Fan's eyes seemed to see a broken branch regrowing, sprouting anew, and reattaching itself to the main trunk of the great tree. In just a moment, it became lush and verdant!

"This is the true power of Mountains and Seas..."

Li Fan, at the end of time, had witnessed the pitiful sight of ancient Mountains and Seas, battered and broken by Dao Annihilation and the Void Realm.

And now, standing within Mountains and Seas himself, and possessing the cultivation of a Profound Embryo Saint, his shoulders were level with Mountains and Seas.

Therefore, he had somewhat underestimated the [Infinite Sea] and the [Upper Mountain].

Only today, after witnessing the magnificent scene of Mountains and Seas reconnecting, its grandeur no less than the Star's return, did Li Fan finally realize: "What I saw was merely a small segment of Mountains and Seas."

"Even spanning hundreds of thousands of years, it is only an insignificant part of the complete Mountains and Seas. The true Mountains and Seas inherited most of the power of the [Gods]..."

"In the past, what I saw of Mountains and Seas was not Mountains and Seas."

"It was merely an illusion of Mountains and Seas."

Lost in thought, Li Fan felt the life force flowing down surge towards him.

It collided violently with the current Mountains and Seas!

The white circle on the Other Shore suddenly retracted its radiance, no longer covering Mountains and Seas, but shrinking as much as possible.

Li Fan personally witnessed countless changes occur within the current Mountains and Seas.

Those possibilities that had already been destroyed, because they still existed in the previous time period, now seemed to be infused with life and began to grow again, repelling Dao Annihilation from Mountains and Seas.

As for those possibilities that could not find their origin upstream, they did not disappear out of thin air due to the fusion of the two sections of Mountains and Seas. As if by instinct, they found the closest possibilities and slowly attached themselves.

It was like a new branch growing on a branch.

Though newly formed and fragile, it was ultimately connected to the main trunk of the tree, and would no longer be easily destroyed.

The Saints on the Other Shore had expressions of daze.

Countless images seemed to surface in their minds.

These were the memories of "themselves" in the previous segment of Mountains and Seas.

Their auras fluctuated, as if erupting like a volcano, ready to burst forth at any moment.

Among them, the Three Saints Lianshan were the most prominent.

In the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, they were already Saints.

Now that Mountains and Seas were reconnected, it was as if they had doubled their fortune out of nowhere.

However, their strength was already unfathomable, and at this moment, during the brief period of fusion, it manifested as a fierce explosion of power, like a supernova, emitting blinding light.

It was so dazzling that others could not bear to look directly.

But it lasted only for a fleeting moment before returning to calm.

As for the other Saints, their individual gains were not mentioned, but it took them longer to subdue them.

As for Li Fan...

His mind was empty, with no new memories being implanted.

Because he was still too young, there was no "Li Fan" in the previous segment of Mountains and Seas.

However, this coincided with his identity as a time-traveler from the end of time.

Without acting rashly, he sat quietly, waiting for the changes in the Saints to conclude.

In fact, even though he had achieved the successful reconnection of Mountains and Seas, he had not gained much.

As Saint Lianshan had said before.

The Saints seemed to stand upon Mountains and Seas; the stronger Mountains and Seas became, the more their own strength would naturally increase. And if the Dao they wielded was not controlled by the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, then they could instantly turn it to their own use, creating fortune out of thin air!

This was precisely what Li Fan was experiencing now.

Great Dao Returns to Truth, First Profound Embryo.

No matter where the Profound Embryo Great Dao was located, it was already marked by Li Fan.

Therefore, the moment Mountains and Seas were connected, Li Fan had already sensed the aura belonging to the Profound Embryo.

However, unfortunately, in the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, the Profound Embryo already had a master.

And that master had already reached the Saintly realm!

Thus, a bizarre situation occurred.

There were now two Profound Embryo Saints in one segment of Mountains and Seas.

"In a sense, the other party is the true [Profound Embryo]. However..."

"Having obtained the Great Dao, how can it be easily given to others?"

With the control over the Profound Embryo through [Great Dao Returns to Truth], Li Fan believed that even if they fought, he would be the ultimate victor, and win easily.

With a winning hand, Li Fan decided not to act rashly for the time being.

He continued to wait for the changes on the Other Shore.

When Mountains and Seas were reconnected, and the life force pathways were successfully infused and finally stabilized.

The Other Shore no longer retracted.

Instead, it rapidly expanded and connected with another Other Shore in the upper reaches of time.

There was no earth-shattering collision sound.

Because they were originally one.

The blinding white light converged into a single point.

The same images overlapped.

At the same time, three more figures inexplicably appeared in the Zuan Ji Ring.

"Let me first introduce the current situation."

"Mountains and Seas have been successfully reconnected, plus the 58,600-plus years previously lost in the Eternal Void Realm, the total time span is now 339,800 years."

"Flowing backward to reconnect, the Saints from the latter segment of Mountains and Seas are: Myself, Guihai, Tai Yi... Xuan Pin."

"And the Saints from the former segment of Mountains and Seas are different."

"Yuán Mò, Guāng Yī, and..."

"Xuan Pin."

Saint Lianshan spoke slowly, but two "Xuan Pins" appeared in the list of Saints!

Theoretically, this was possible, but the probability was very low, unlike what everyone encountered today.

After all, a separated segment of Mountains and Seas was usually only a little over a hundred thousand years.

To be born in it and cultivate from scratch to Sainthood, without past accumulation,

It was basically impossible.

However, Xuan Pin was a time-traveler from the end of Mountains and Seas, so that was another matter.

Amidst the eerie silence in the Zuan Ji Ring, Saint Lianshan spoke again, "As to who Xuan Pin truly belongs to, it is a private matter between the two of you, and we cannot interfere. However..."

"The Mountains and Seas Walker possesses the method of True Spirit Infusion..."

The Saints from the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, Yuán Mò and Guāng Yī, did not know what True Spirit Infusion was.

Saint Lianshan then explained it.

Hearing that Li Fan had the ability to create Saints, the two Saints could not help but show surprise.

"No wonder there are so many new faces all of a sudden."

"Even though the time span of the two segments of Mountains and Seas is not far apart."

Yuán Mò and Guāng Yī exchanged glances and then looked at the Xuan Pin they were familiar with, sighing inwardly.

From a big picture perspective, even if Li Fan was not their opponent, the victory must go to Li Fan.

After all, the ability to create Saints was truly terrifying.

If not for Li Fan infusing the new five Saints, the reconnection of Mountains and Seas would not have been so smooth.

In comparison, just a mere [Profound Embryo]...

The Zuan Ji Ring was silent.

[Xuan Pin] slowly stood up, surveying the Saints.

Saint Lianshan's voice, as calm as an ancient well, spoke again, "If you are willing to give up the Dao of Xuan Pin, we promise to find another way to help you embark on the path of Sainthood. If you are unwilling..."

Xuan Pin's expression turned as dark as water, and the aura emanating from him could no longer be contained, as if he might erupt at any moment.

Although he was no match for the Saints present, he would never allow himself to be manipulated so easily!

"Wait a moment!"

Just then, Li Fan suddenly spoke.

"Actually, I am not necessarily Xuan Pin."

As soon as these words were spoken, all the Saints, including Lianshan, showed surprise.

"It is not easy for Saints to be born in Mountains and Seas. It is truly a pity to lose even one. Moreover, we are all committed to saving the world; starting an infighting amongst ourselves..."

"Although it is understandable, it is bound to create discord."

"So, does Fellow Daoist Xuan Pin have a better solution?" Saint Tai Yi asked.

Li Fan slowly nodded, "As I said before, I have risen from humble beginnings multiple times. Becoming a Saint through the Profound Embryo Dao is what I am most familiar with. If there are other viable paths..."

"I can also pursue them."

Upon hearing this, all the Saints' expressions became somewhat subtle.

Becoming a Saint was inherently difficult. Destiny, talent, opportunity, and hard work—all were indispensable.

Even among those present, few could guarantee that they could easily rise again after changing their Dao path.

But Li Fan seemed utterly confident.

"Since there is still room for negotiation, let us discuss it further for now," Saint Lianshan said.

Xuan Pin's suppressed aura slowly subsided. Before sitting down, he bowed slightly to Li Fan.

Li Fan nodded in response.

After Saint Gui Hai pondered for a moment, he said to Li Fan, "In this segment of Mountains and Seas, the latter 190,000 years have no potential for excavation. However, the former 150,000 years might offer an opportunity to achieve the Dao."

Saint Guiming deduced with his fingers, and images flickered before him.

Finally, they settled on one image.

It was a peculiar land within Mountains and Seas. Countless possibilities gathered there, but did not flow downwards.

As if sensing the destructive crisis downstream, it coiled and meandered within Mountains and Seas,

Gradually forming a self-contained cycle.

"This place was originally at the end of the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, near the Void Realm. To avoid falling into the Void Realm, it generated this peculiar change on its own. We had vaguely sensed it before, but it was of no help in saving Mountains and Seas, so we did not pay much attention. However, now..."

As Guiming was about to act, he was interrupted by Saint Lianshan.

Saint Lianshan looked at Li Fan and said slowly, "If you wish to achieve Sainthood through this opportunity, you will likely need to make the journey yourself. While we can offer assistance,..."

"On one hand, this opportunity is naturally wary of beings of equivalent aura. Forceful intervention might scare it away. Secondly, being tainted by our Dao might be even more disadvantageous for your cultivation."

Li Fan nodded slightly, "I understand this principle. It's fine, it's just another trip."

"Everyone, please wait for me for a while."

"This Profound Embryo Dao, I shall entrust to you, Fellow Daoist."

Li Fan said, a sharp glint flashing in his eyes.

Then, the Profound Embryo Great Dao he controlled, like an outer garment, was slowly shed!

After being abandoned, the masterless Profound Embryo instinctively sought to escape.

But it was immediately controlled by the other [Profound Embryo] Saint.

As for Li Fan...

Without the blessing of the Mountains and Seas Great Dao, his cultivation should have regressed to the Transcendent realm.

However, a hazy brilliance still emanated from him.

Even under the Saints' gaze, it was difficult to discern the truth or falsehood!

Chapter 1694: The Hungry Huan Zhen

Li Fan, who had always been hesitant before the All Saints, suddenly dared to shed the veil of the Profound Embryo Great Dao, naturally because he had something to rely on.

That was the transformation of True Return!

This time, the reconnection of Mountains and Seas yielded meager gains for Li Fan. But True Return was not so.

As if its vision had suddenly broadened and become much clearer. The span of time covered by the Mountains and Seas almost doubled, seemingly allowing True Return to act more freely.

Although it did not manifest in specific text on the True Return panel, it could be glimpsed in an inconspicuous corner.

For example, in the Divine Blessing section.

The words "Illusion Becomes Truth" suddenly shone with a dreamlike, ethereal seven-colored radiance, just like "Great Dao Returns to Truth."

When Li Fan's thoughts touched upon it, the magnificent radiance suddenly exploded, and then tightly enveloped the words "Li Fan" in the name column of the True Return panel.

As the colors shifted, the words "Li Fan" disappeared, replaced by an indiscernible halo.

And Li Fan himself felt as if a dark cloud had drifted over his head, or as if he had inexplicably donned a thick kasaya. Even before the All Saints, he felt much safer in his heart.

The sense of crisis, where he felt he could be seen through at any moment, was gone.

"Compared to the past, maintaining 'Illusion Becomes Truth' no longer consumes any energy and can be passively maintained at all times."

"More importantly, the effect has been greatly enhanced. Even when standing right before the All Saints and under their protection, one need not worry about their inner self being seen through."

"However, the price is..."

Li Fan glanced again at the "Great Dao Returns to Truth" section.

The seven-colored radiance on the words "First Profound Embryo" seemed to be suppressed, becoming dim.

Comparing the two, Li Fan gradually understood: "Profound Embryo and Illusion Becomes Truth both possess the power of Saints. With my current strength, I might, with the help of True Return, temporarily ascend to the Saintly realm. However, I can only choose one, not both."

"Perhaps in the future, when I truly ascend to Sainthood, I will be able to ignore such limitations. But for now..."

The reason Li Fan chose to temporarily cede the Profound Embryo Great Dao was not out of true kindness, unwilling to see a Saint perish.

The real reason stemmed from the intense hunger that surged from True Return.

It was as if after a long slumber, it was finally slowly awakening.

The first sensation was an almost unbearable, urgent desire to feed.

It was similar to the first time he saw Su Bai's skull, but hundreds of times more intense!

If Li Fan's will had not been tempered too much through reincarnation, he might have lost control under True Return's influence on the spot.

And thus exposed himself.

But to constantly suppress it was not a long-term solution. He needed to help True Return finish feeding as soon as possible to quell its gluttonous desires.

As for True Return's food...

While urging him, it had already conveyed through a faint fluctuation that there existed something that could satisfy its hunger in this segment of Mountains and Seas.

This was also why Li Fan feigned noble integrity.

Although he could not find it himself for the moment, he believed that the All Saints, in order to stabilize him, the "True Spirit Infuser," would definitely offer assistance.

Unexpectedly, the result came so quickly.

Li Fan stared at the location in the Mountains and Seas pointed to by the Sundial.

Indeed, as far as his gaze could reach, True Return's anomaly became even stronger.

"Esteemed Saints, I shall depart now."

"Await my good news!"

With that, he turned and transformed into a streak of light, vanishing into it without looking back.

On the Other Shore, the All Saints watched Li Fan leave, falling into a strange silence for a moment.

"This Mountains and Seas Walker is truly mysterious," Tai Yi chuckled.

"It matters not. Although we are called peers with Mountains and Seas, Mountains and Seas are boundless, and we dare not claim to comprehend all its mysteries. As long as he can truly create Saints..."

"Everything will be discussed after the reconnection of Mountains and Seas and our strength is fully restored."

The Saints nodded in agreement, their expressions varied.

As for Li Fan...

In just a moment, he had plunged into the currents of myriad possibilities.

Following True Return's subtle guidance, he sped towards the direction of the "food."

Only when he gradually separated from the Xuán Jī Ring did Li Fan feel the changes within himself more clearly.

"It was indeed not my illusion, but a real change. Fortunately, the time I spent there was not too long, and my nature is resilient. If I had stayed longer, I might have truly become one with them forever."

Li Fan inwardly felt a sense of dread.

"Even if I have temporarily escaped now, and have the protection of 'Illusion Becomes Truth,' I cannot be careless."

"After all, the All Saints are certainly still watching me from the Other Shore. If all else fails, then I will use True Return to escape!"

The reason Li Fan wanted to temporarily leave the Other Shore also considered this.

Being far from the All Saints at least allowed for some room for error when activating True Return.

If True Return were activated in front of the All Saints, there might be a risk of being stopped.

After all, the strength of the Three Saints of Lianshan was indeed formidable and awe-inspiring.

Recalling his thoughts, as he descended into this possibility, Li Fan first sensed the surroundings.

As he had spied earlier on the Other Shore.

The river of time did not flow straight forward but formed a loop, like a circle.

Most beings in this possibility could not realize their true situation.

Only a very few possessed the ability to temporarily leap out of the flow of possibilities.

"Specifically, it manifests as being able to exist briefly in the future at a certain moment and through a certain method. It appears as a dream, but it is a real existence. Whether in the present or the future, every action will affect this possibility."

"Although it forms a loop, it is always in flux."

Li Fan's eyes swept across the countless currents of possibility, trying to identify the so-called opportunity for enlightenment.

But it seemed to sense the approach of True Return, the predator, and quickly concealed itself.

Li Fan searched for a long time, but found nothing.

"The cyclical nature of this possibility must be related to the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas."

After pondering for a moment, Li Fan made up his mind.

He formed his fingers into a sword and chose one possibility, severing it from the rest!

Originally, the ends were connected, winding and existing within Mountains and Seas.

Now, it was broken by Li Fan.

The separated possibility could no longer integrate into Mountains and Seas.

It was like a lone boat, drifting in isolation.

Having lost its cyclical characteristic, the beings within this possibility lost their "future."

Their lives were all frozen at the last moment.

As if Dao Annihilation had descended, they would vanish without a trace in the next instant.

The change did not stop there.

The beginning of the possibility also began to wither, having lost its "source" from the future.

Like a plucked flower, although it could sustain itself for a short time.

Withered, it was inevitable.

"The key to maintaining the cyclical possibility is the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan silently observed the passing of a brilliant civilization within this possibility, lost in thought.

Then, he looked again at the countless intact winding possibilities.

If it were his true nature, he would simply and brutally sever all possibilities. Then the Mountains and Seas Great Dao, hidden behind them and maintaining their cyclical nature, would naturally be exposed.

However...

Doing so would cause countless beings to perish.

His actions, witnessed by the All Saints on the Other Shore, would be drastically different from his previous performance, raising suspicion and making things difficult.

"Let the All Saints see my ingenious methods as well!"

With this thought, Li Fan put away his crude intentions.

His form transformed into a streak of light, completely merging into the most prominent possibility within this loop.

Li Fan had once existed in a temporal state of "line" during his traversal against the current of time.

Unlike his normal state, which existed at a single point in time.

He simultaneously encompassed an entire period of time.

Now, as Li Fan merged, the stream of light spread throughout the loop.

Finally, encompassing the entire cycle.

Li Fan was thus able to witness the history of this possibility from the perspective of an indigenous being.

The civilization of this world was born from the ruins after a great war.

With ferocious beasts and calamities rampant, humans struggled to survive in the crevices.

On the vast wilderness, they gradually built cities like stars.

From the ruins of ancient relics, they searched for wondrous objects and rediscovered knowledge.

Due to the differences in the ancient records they found, they gradually divided into two completely different factions.

The first type focused on strengthening oneself, using everything available on the wilderness to modify and enhance the physical body.

The second type followed the path of "control," being extremely fragile themselves, but they could cultivate special mental powers to achieve the manipulation of ferocious beasts and even machinery.

Originally, there was no irreconcilable conflict between the two.

But when both sides cultivated to their highest realm, everything changed.

The path of "control" could actually control cultivators who strengthened their bodies.

And the mental power of cultivators practicing "control" was a great supplement to physical cultivators. Once ingested, it was almost equivalent to a hundred years of hard cultivation.

Thus, a world-shattering war erupted.

In the end, the civilization that both sides had painstakingly rebuilt from the ruins was once again destroyed.

No one was spared, only a few records remained.

Until, after a long period of deathly silence, new life was born.

Repeating the old events.

In this possibility, there were indeed beings who saw through this tragic cycle and tried to stand out and save the world multiple times, to reverse it.

However, the conflict between the two major cultivation methods was almost irreconcilable.

Individual power was, after all, like a drop in the bucket, unable to withstand the overwhelming trend.

This possibility, thus, fell into an endless cycle.

"The past can influence the future, and the future can also change the past."

"However, due to the outbreak of that world-ending war, the influence of all variables has been minimized. Perhaps after billions of reincarnations, it will produce a change great enough to alter civilization..."

Li Fan's consciousness, covering the entire timeline, pondered for a moment, then began to look for the crux.

"The root of everything lies in the fundamental contradiction between the two cultivation methods. If this can be resolved..."

"Perhaps this loop will be broken."

"And to maintain this state, the hidden Mountains and Seas Great Dao will inevitably intervene to reverse it."

Two figures then appeared in the city, reborn from the ruins.

They joined different factions respectively.

After decades of cultivation, both reached the peak of their respective cultivation methods.

"Indeed, whether it's 'control' or 'body,' in this world, they have already reached the limit of cultivation."

"To advance further, one must devour the other side."

"This is the limitation of this world, or rather, the limitation of the 'Dao'."

"But it is no match for me."

Li Fan's two created avatars, with their astonishing attainments in their respective schools, deservedly became the leaders of each faction.

With iron-fisted methods, they temporarily suppressed the momentum of the war.

Then, they focused their efforts on reforming their respective cultivation methods.

In the eyes of the masses, this was purely a meaningless delay, but unexpectedly, within less than three years, effective improved methods emerged.

"The way of 'control' can indeed control all things, and naturally can control one's own body. The stronger the physical body, the more easily it can be controlled."

"All things in the world can be a nutrient for the physical body. One's own spirit is also the same. A spirit tempered a thousand times, when consumed by oneself, is like a Golden Core. Once ingested, it reveals all the flaws of the physical body."

...

Initially, people did not believe it, but there were always curious ones willing to try.

After unremitting practice, they discovered that the two methods could indeed be cultivated together, even complementing each other!

Thus, the shadow of war gradually receded.

Exchange and prosperity began to take root and sprout on the land.

Li Fan, having completed his mission and retreated, looked up and sensed the subtle changes gradually re-emerging in the world.

Under the influence of a strange power, the prosperity of the civilization did not last long.

After a brief period of peaceful coexistence, the seeds of war began to sprout again.

This was because some cultivators discovered that combined cultivation was truly too slow!

The world was inherently filled with mediocre talents, and cultivating one method alone was already exhausting. What about cultivating both?

The strength was actually inferior to solely cultivating one method.

More crucially, the previous method of devouring cultivators from the other sect and converting them into one's own cultivation resources was still effective!

Human greed was hard to eradicate.

Amidst the calm, ripples began to arise.

Increasing amounts of slaughter began to emerge.

...

Li Fan captured that wisp of power that was altering the world, but he was not confident of striking it accurately.

He did not act rashly but continued to engage it.

The two leaders cooperated once again, improving the new methods.

This increased the efficiency of cultivation severalfold.

And those who dared to use cultivators for their practice were killed without mercy.

Another bloody slaughter forcibly suppressed the greed in people's hearts.

Moreover, it did not completely eliminate the path of cultivation; there were still acceptable cultivation methods.

Thus, people slowly began to accept this slower cultivation method.

Li Fan used human intervention to transform the world. The land and sky changed anew.

Cultivating both spirit and body simultaneously sometimes resulted in qi deviation.

Either the physical body transformed into a ferocious beast on the wilderness, but the spirit remained normal.

Or the spirit became chaotic, but the physical body remained in its original state.

Regardless of which type, when it erupted suddenly, it was enough to pose a great threat to civilization.

At first, people could still tolerate it, but as the outbreaks became more frequent, cultivators began to doubt the rationality of dual cultivation.

Of course.

Once again, it was resolved by Li Fan.

As the land and sky were about to undergo a third change, Li Fan, who had been observing silently from the sidelines, suddenly opened his eyes.

"Still dare to be mischievous, I've found you!"

His form leaped out of the cyclic possibility, manifesting a figure that could reach the heavens and tread the earth.

With a light step, he trod upon the myriad cyclic possibilities of this place.

Clasping his hands in the air!

Chapter 1695: Breaking the Game to Prove the Profound Mystery

The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, in its essence, was incorporeal.

Yet, under Li Fan's forceful drag, a vibrant, serpentine creature seemed to leap into existence from nothingness!

The serpent, in its natural state, maintained a perfect balance of intertwined head and tail.

This equilibrium, now disrupted by Li Fan's external force, instinctively triggered a counterattack.

A seven-colored light instantly enveloped Li Fan, and amidst the torrent of myriad possibilities, the light and shadow flickered and shifted, as if an acceleration button had been pressed.

The following scenes unfolded in rapid succession:

After the serpent was captured by Li Fan, it still struggled. However, as vibrant radiance surged and it strained with all its might, it ultimately couldn't escape the grasp of its captor. Li Fan's expression showed satisfaction as he looked at the seven-colored serpent, which had now turned into mist, and inhaled deeply.

The seven-colored profound energy, an endless stream, flowed into his belly.

As if gaining enlightenment, Li Fan sat cross-legged amidst the flowing torrent of countless possibilities. The aura that originally belonged to the seven-colored serpent gradually manifested around him.

Beneath him, the myriad possibilities, which had been slowly losing their cyclical nature due to the serpent's suppression, now became stable again.

Li Fan was immersed in this state, utterly lost, as if petrified, his original aura seemingly vanishing.

Uncountable years passed. As Li Fan's figure solidified within this time and space, seemingly belonging to this place, his presence as "Li Fan" gradually disappeared, becoming one with the surroundings.

The light and shadow continued to flicker rapidly, each moment representing the passage of hundreds of thousands of years.

The last trace of Li Fan's existence in this world finally vanished, transforming into wisps of colorful, misty energy. These energies converged from all directions, ultimately forming a seven-colored serpent!

As if newborn, it acted instinctively, its body slowly coiling, eventually reconnecting its head and tail, returning to its original form.

Like the countless possibilities below it, it was trapped in an eternal cycle.

As if a wisp of mist had drifted by, the serpent vanished into it, its trace lost.

The light warped and continued to accelerate.

Thus, after an unknown number of years and countless cycles, the seven-colored serpent materialized again from nowhere.

It was as if something inside its belly was struggling, increasingly violently.

*Boom!*

The serpent exploded into countless fragments of dust, and a figure leaped out from within. It was Li Fan, who had been lost in this realm for an immeasurable number of years.

As if having forgotten his bewildering experience, he had returned to the moment of his initial arrival.

Li Fan observed the hidden mysteries within the myriad looping possibilities. His final choice was the same as before.

He entered one of the possibilities, chose to break through the predicament with his own body, and forced the seven-colored serpent, which dominated the cyclical changes of this place, to reveal its true form.

The action proceeded smoothly as before.

After the seven-colored serpent was captured, it struggled incessantly. Ultimately, it could not escape Li Fan's refinement.

The misty energy entered his body, and Li Fan sat in contemplation.

After an unknown number of years, his body and this realm finally became one.

One cycle was like this, and countless cycles were no different.

Li Fan, the hunter of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, had instead become trapped within it.

Like falling into an eternal loop!

...

On the Other Shore.

Gazing at this scene from afar, Tai Yi chuckled and said, "It seems our Mountains and Seas Walker has encountered some trouble. Shall we lend a hand?"

"Time is like a wheel, constantly turning between creation and destruction. This [Cosmic Cycle] was not present from the beginning of Mountains and Seas, but rather a desperate measure for survival under the pressure of Dao Annihilation. Although the Mountains and Seas Walker's talent is extraordinary, after shedding the guise of a Saint, he is ultimately only at the Transcendent level. Being trapped within it… is understandable." Duke Shou Qiu nodded.

"Those inside are confused, but those outside are clear. If we were in his shoes, we might not fare any better," Morality said, as he was enlightened into Sainthood by Li Fan, and could not help but defend him.

The Saints remained silent, neither refuting nor agreeing.

However, Saint Lianshan, breaking the silence, suddenly said, "Perhaps we should wait a little longer. In my view, even within this unchanging cycle, there are variables. This Mountains and Seas Walker is not as simple as we imagine. You all seem to have underestimated him."

Saint Lianshan actually smiled rarely and silently.

The other Saints were all surprised by his words and turned their gaze back.

With the reunion of Mountains and Seas, the Other Shore now encompassed the entire current segment of Mountains and Seas.

Under the white light, time flowed, but it had no practical meaning.

Furthermore, where Li Fan was located, the cycle had formed its own unique system. Even if billions of years passed within it, it would not affect the overall situation of Mountains and Seas.

It was understandable for the Saints to wait.

...

As Saint Lianshan had said, there was indeed a variable hidden within the seemingly endless cycle.

And that variable was Li Fan's opportunity to escape!

Everything originated from the sword Li Fan wielded when he first descended, in his attempt to find the trace of the [Cosmic Cycle].

That sword had severed one of the possibilities in that realm. Time froze, and then it withered and perished.

When the Cosmic Cycle evolved and trapped Li Fan within its own loop, in order not to alert him, it also incorporated Li Fan's instinctive action into the cycle.

As a result, in every reincarnation, one possibility was destroyed by Li Fan's fingertips.

Although there were countless flowing possibilities in this realm, and although new possibilities were born in addition to destruction,

As Li Fan became completely integrated into the [Cosmic Cycle], each cycle became smoother.

The speed of reincarnation accelerated, and the speed at which Li Fan destroyed possibilities began to exceed the speed of their regeneration.

Even if the power of the Cosmic Cycle tried its best, it could no longer maintain balance.

If this continued, the outcome was already predetermined: all the myriad flowing possibilities in this realm would ultimately be annihilated by Li Fan.

And if the Cosmic Cycle chose to persist...

The outcome would be the same.

It would only be a matter of Li Fan being trapped for a longer time.

Ultimately, everything would lead to destruction.

Gradually understanding his situation, the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle made its choice.

At the beginning of yet another cycle, Li Fan captured the seven-colored serpent and absorbed its misty energy, about to enter enlightenment.

However, another, smaller beam of seven-colored light, fleetingly appeared.

It intended to stealthily escape.

In the next moment, it was about to leap out of the cyclical possibility stream and hide within the boundless Mountains and Seas.

At this very moment, Li Fan, who should have been immersed in enlightenment, suddenly opened his eyes.

With a calm expression, he brought his fingers together.

His two fingers acted like a lock, firmly capturing the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle.

The small, colorful serpent was suddenly trapped, shocked and enraged.

It tried to manifest the cyclical light and shadow again, to trap Li Fan within it.

But having already broken out of the grand cycle, how could Li Fan fall into the same trap again?

"If you had been more decisive and chosen to flee when I arrived, perhaps I truly wouldn't have been able to do anything to you."

"After exhausting countless cycles with me, you finally chose to sever your arm to save yourself..."

"Hmph! It's too late!"

Holding the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle in his palm, Li Fan lowered his gaze and slowly began to refine it.

Beneath him, the myriad looping possibilities, having lost their source of cyclical power, gradually fell into a frozen state.

Soon, they would face complete annihilation.

Having experienced this countless times in his reincarnation, Li Fan, now familiar with the process, took only a dozen breaths to completely integrate this Great Dao of Mountains and Seas into himself.

A mysterious and profound aura slowly emanated from Li Fan.

At this moment, Li Fan had once again reached the Saintly realm!

He opened his eyes and saw the myriad possibilities below him on the verge of disintegration. Li Fan lightly gestured with a finger.

With the infusion of the power of the Cosmic Cycle, the frozen possibilities began to surge again.

However, this cycle would not last indefinitely as before.

Instead, through repeated cycles, it would gradually find its ultimate direction and usher in its final destiny.

This, however, was no longer Li Fan's concern.

Having regained the mantle of a Saint, Li Fan looked up, faintly glimpsing the Saints on the Other Shore smiling at him.

Li Fan took a deep breath, forcibly clearing away the sense of staleness that had accumulated from being trapped in endless reincarnation. With a leap, he traversed the boundless Mountains and Seas and returned to the Other Shore.

He had been gone for countless years, but within the Xuanji Ring, there was no change.

"My apologies for keeping you all waiting," Li Fan said apologetically.

The Saints observed Li Fan, who had once again attained the Saintly realm, their expressions varied.

"It seems Saint Lianshan was right, we all underestimated you. Hehehe…" Tai Yi said with a smile.

Li Fan did not understand the meaning behind his words, so Shou Qiu explained in detail what had happened on the Other Shore after he left.

"It was merely a stroke of luck," Li Fan said with shame.

"There's no need for humility. To escape from this endless cycle and to bind the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle, even we might not be able to do it so easily. Mountains and Seas Walker, indeed, is worthy of the name," Guihai said, speaking out for the first time, offering praise.

Li Fan did not argue further.

He knew his own situation best.

This time, capturing the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle, though it appeared effortless, was in fact extremely perilous.

In the beginning, when Li Fan's consciousness was clouded and he was trapped in the endless cycle, he truly hadn't noticed his predicament.

It could be said that the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas was truly overwhelming for those at the Transcendent level.

Because of that unintentional sword strike that severed a possibility, Li Fan was destined not to be trapped forever. Therefore, from beginning to end, he had not been in any real danger.

It was only when the Cosmic Dao chose to escape, akin to a golden cicada shedding its shell, that Li Fan launched his attack.

He suppressed and refined it in one go.

Of course, it seemed as if Li Fan had absorbed the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle and attained Sainthood.

In reality, this Great Dao of Mountains and Seas had entered True Return's belly.

On True Return's panel, after [First Profound Embryo], a new line of characters appeared.

[Second Cosmic Cycle.]

Radiant streams of light intertwined with it, and faintly, one could even see a seven-colored coiling dragon above.

For Li Fan, feeding the Cosmic Cycle to True Return was clearly a better choice.

Firstly, although he had suppressed and refined the Cosmic Cycle, with his current aptitude, it would not be quick for him to truly become a Saint through this. It would still require a long period of tempering and practice. This didn't align with the persona of the "Mountains and Seas Walker," who could quickly rise from humble beginnings every time he traversed to a new Mountains and Seas.

Secondly…

In a sense, True Return consuming it was no different from Li Fan comprehending and becoming a Saint himself. After the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle returned to truth, Li Fan could now choose to impersonate a Saint, whether as [Profound Embryo] or [Cosmic Cycle].

Even with the aid of [From the Heart's Transformation], he could seamlessly switch. One moment he was a [Profound Embryo] Saint, and the next, an unfathomable [Cosmic Cycle] Saint.

This divine ability was already beyond the reach of ordinary Saints.

As for Li Fan's desire to have both…

With his current strength, it seemed impossible to achieve.

However, Li Fan had a vague premonition that as he grew stronger in the future, wielding the power of two Saints might not be unattainable.

Ultimately, it came down to the same principle.

Everything was Li Fan's limit, not True Return's.

"Subduing the Great Dao of the Cosmic Cycle is a trivial matter," Li Fan said.

"As I ascend to the Saintly realm, the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas will inevitably be brought under my control."

"It is not worth mentioning."

"However, that intuition…" Li Fan's mind drifted back to the moment he awoke from the endless cycle.

"Initially, I truly believed that the premonition was my own intuition, because the two feelings were too similar, almost indistinguishable."

"But later, it proved that the so-called intuition was merely residual memories from my cycles. However…"

"In the endless cycles, it was like this. But what about the real Mountains and Seas?"

Endless doubts churned within Li Fan's mind.

Ever since he embarked on the path of cultivation, Li Fan had benefited greatly from his keen intuition.

Under its guidance, he had repeatedly turned peril into safety and avoided danger.

Previously, Li Fan instinctively believed that this was his own intuition, a trait of his own, like [True Spirit Infinite].

But after this experience, he couldn't help but wonder.

"Could it also be my residual memories?"

"It's just that I haven't reincarnated enough times, so my intuition only appears intermittently and only functions at critical moments, when my memory is particularly vivid?"

"Mountains and Seas, Star, True Return…" Li Fan's eyes seemed to once again see the scene of True Return repelling the [Star] and resetting Mountains and Seas in an instant.

Chapter 1696: The Three Saints Ignored

"Xuan... Heh, it is now [Universe Cycle]."

"Now that Universe Cycle has returned to its rightful place, the next step is to look forward to the next segment of Mountains and Seas," the voice of Saint Tai Yi interrupted Li Fan's thoughts.

For Saints, there was no concept of rest.

To traverse the Void Realm, acting as a bridge, and reconnecting Mountains and Seas. This was what They pursued with unwavering dedication.

"As mentioned before, after two reconnecting efforts, we are now in this segment of Mountains and Seas, spanning a total of three hundred and thirty-nine thousand eight hundred years. However, the next journey may not be as easy."

All the Saints understood that Tai Yi would not speak without reason, and immediately listened intently.

"According to my investigations, the time occupied by the Void Realm ahead is already approaching one hundred thousand years. If the Void Realm were to encroach further and break this limit..."

"The connection of Mountains and Seas would be completely severed, and a complete reconnection might become hopeless."

"Firstly, We must guard Mountains and Seas, facing the invasion of Dao Annihilation, and cannot retreat any further."

"Secondly, this time, there is no room for error in the reconnection. It must succeed in one attempt. Otherwise, under the backlash of the Void Realm, even if We work together wholeheartedly, We may not be able to withstand that monstrous wave."

Saint Lianshan waved his hand, displaying the scene of the continuous Void Realm ahead to the Saints.

Distant and profound, the pressure it brought was even greater than the Void Realms they had encountered before.

As if personally experiencing it, the Saints' bodies seemed to be stained by darkness, and they all fell silent.

"Of course, there is also good news. After two reconnecting efforts, Our strength has also increased to a certain extent. And..."

"With over a hundred thousand more years of foundation in Mountains and Seas, and with our Mountains and Seas Walker here, perhaps several more Saints can be created to aid us," Tai Yi said. Just as he was speaking, a brilliant golden light rose from within Mountains and Seas and shot straight towards the Other Shore.

It was Saint Tai Wei.

This time, there were no pleasantries, and he went straight to the point: "With the True Spirit Infusion technique, I have not refined any more Saint Pill of Transcendence. This time, it has all been changed to Saintly Fortune Pills. Two segments of Mountains and Seas, plus the transformation from void to reality, the accumulation of thirty thousand years has been depleted by me."

"Nine more pills."

Saint Tai Wei scanned the group and took out nine orbs of light that emitted a crystal-clear radiance, as if possessing their own life.

"Benefiting from the reconnection of Mountains and Seas, the efficacy of the Saintly Fortune Pills refined this time is even better than before. Consuming them may trigger the devout thoughts of billions upon billions of beings in the Saintly Dynasty. I myself stopped after consuming two pills. Newly promoted Saints, act according to your capacity."

"The next batch will be in thirty thousand years."

After speaking, without waiting for the Saints to respond, Saint Tai Wei departed in a hurry.

"So many of us sharing nine pills, and he alone consumed two," Bai Xiao muttered to himself.

Tai Yi chuckled, "Tai Wei's main body needs to suppress the fate of the majestic Saintly Dynasty. He cannot move easily. Therefore, each trip is very hasty. As for this Saintly Fortune Pill..."

"Universe Cycle, you can take one first."

Li Fan was slightly stunned.

Last time he didn't get to eat this Saintly Fortune Pill, but this time, with more people sharing and the efficacy of the Saintly Pill being stronger, he actually got a share?

The Three Saints Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi were of one heart and mind.

Since Tai Yi had spoken, the other Saints naturally had no objections.

Seeing Li Fan's hesitation, Tai Yi explained, "Although you have already attained the Great Dao of Universe Cycle, during the process of subduing it, this Dao itself has suffered some damage. Furthermore, you will be responsible for True Spirit Infusion in the future..."

Tai Yi lightly gestured, and one of the light orbs slowly flew to Li Fan's side.

Li Fan inwardly felt ashamed, but still consumed the Saintly Fortune Pill.

He closed his eyes to digest it.

Li Fan received one pill alone, and the remaining eight were shared among the Saints.

The three Saints Lianshan did not need them. The newly promoted Saints received one each, while those with stronger power like Prying Opportunity and Guiming received half.

In a short while, the treasures delivered by Tai Wei had entered the Saints' stomachs.

As Saint Tai Wei had said, the efficacy was even greater than before.

As the light orbs entered their stomachs, Li Fan's sea of consciousness was engulfed by immeasurable light and shadows.

His perspective swept rapidly, as if traversing across an boundless land.

As far as the eye could see, there were only prosperous lands.

Beings lived and worked in peace, enjoying prosperity. In their leisure time, every household silently recited the Saint Emperor's virtues in their hearts.

In the Saintly Dynasty, there were no famines or disasters.

Everyone had enough to eat and a place to live.

The Saint Emperor's image reigned supreme, observing everything. All corruption and evil were instantly erased the moment they occurred.

This was undoubtedly a prosperous era.

Only in such a prosperous era could a Great Pill that even Saints could benefit from be condensed.

Li Fan had also had a Saintly avatar.

He naturally knew that such a glorious and prosperous era was built upon the powerful strength of Saint Tai Wei.

Without the Saint Emperor's suppression, it was likely that all the beauty would decay and collapse in an instant.

"No wonder Saint Tai Wei cannot leave for long."

"It is precisely because he is constantly rectifying injustice that the Saintly Dynasty can be called Saint."

A Saintly Fortune Pill seemed to condense the thoughts of countless citizens of the Saintly Dynasty.

Their life experiences, even their thoughts and desires.

After their deaths, they all flowed like streams, being refined and extracted by the Saint Emperor, turning into usable Great Pills.

Li Fan carefully savored it.

With his willpower, even though the Saintly Pill was extraordinary, it was impossible to truly influence him. To make him feel genuine admiration for Saint Tai Wei.

Instead, within the myriad converging thoughts, he discovered something interesting.

Even in the Saintly Dynasty, this seemingly utopian paradise, not all citizens felt satisfied.

Some even secretly complained in their hearts that the Saint Emperor's authority was too pervasive and his control too strict.

In his mind, fleeting and unrealistic dangerous thoughts flashed from time to time.

Of course, with their abilities, they naturally could not resist Saint Tai Wei.

But it did not prevent them from indulging in such fantasies from time to time.

All beings in the Saintly Dynasty were unaware that every thought in their minds was actually under Saint Tai Wei's control.

But Tai Wei intentionally allowed these discordant elements to exist.

And perhaps it was because of these "evil thoughts" that the Saintly Fortune Pill was not so "sweet."

It could be safely consumed.

"This Saint Tai Wei is quite an interesting person."

"It's a pity, he's too tired."

Li Fan's heart was like a rock. Whether it was praise or criticism from the myriad converging thoughts, none could shake his original intention.

He simply browsed and absorbed the life experiences, turning them into his own use.

On the Other Shore, time passed without notice.

When Li Fan had completely absorbed the effects of the Great Pill, he suddenly opened his eyes.

He realized that among all the Saints, he was the first to wake up.

"It seems that the experience in the endless cycle has allowed Universe Cycle to improve significantly," Tai Yi nodded.

Li Fan bowed slightly, and then realized that the main bodies of the Three Saints Lianshan were nowhere to be seen. They had already gone to the Void Realm.

Only their phantom images remained seated.

"We will proceed first. The ninety thousand years of continuous Void Realm are not to be trifled with."

"Before Mountains and Seas were reconnected, we could not advance further. Besides the fact that this Void Realm is extremely long, there are other reasons. With Our strength now doubled, We will go and test it again. If it can be resolved, that would be best. If not, We will discuss another method."

Li Fan was curious about the crisis in the Void Realm that even the Three Saints found difficult. However, Tai Yi's phantom image did not elaborate further. Instead, he changed the subject.

Pointing again towards Mountains and Seas, "Universe Cycle, you might as well return to that endless cycle of possibilities once more. While We were digesting the Great Pill, We looked back and discovered a detail that was almost overlooked."

This statement was transmitted privately, only to Li Fan, and not made public.

Li Fan was greatly astonished.

Even though he had already subdued the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, what else had he missed?

However, the Three Saints Lianshan would not jest with him about such matters. Li Fan's expression became solemn, and he looked back at the endless cycle of possibilities.

Because his residual power of Universe Cycle was suppressing it, the cycle had not yet collapsed.

Compared to his personal experience, there seemed to be no change.

Li Fan swept over this small area multiple times with his Saint-level intent, but still could not find the place that the Three Saints had mentioned.

He did not give up easily and seek guidance from Tai Yi's phantom image, but instead began to contemplate it himself.

Scenes from the past resurfaced in his mind, as if he were reliving them.

However, this time, it was from an outsider's perspective.

This time, Li Fan finally discovered a slight clue.

"The Great Dao of Universe Cycle should not have detected the presence of the Saints outside the Other Shore. When I was lost in the cycle, They had ample opportunity to flee."

"Why did They deliberately delay, even pulling me into the cycle, to guard this place?"

"Even in the end, resorting to severing an arm to survive, They only took away a relatively small portion of Their essence, leaving behind a considerably large husk to maintain the operation of the cyclical possibilities."

"Without external interference, as long as the Great Dao of Universe Cycle still exists within Mountains and Seas, those cycles can still continue."

"Was it an escape, or a diversionary tactic?"

"What is it that Universe Cycle is watching for, or rather, valuing!"

Li Fan suddenly understood, a sharp glint flashing in his eyes as he scanned the cyclical possibilities again.

It was so deeply hidden that even the Three Saints almost overlooked it.

But since Li Fan now knew its value, he became very patient.

He explored each of the countless possibilities one by one, no longer scanning them hastily.

He immersed his mind in them.

During this period, when other Saints awoke and saw Li Fan still with his eyes closed, they thought he was still digesting the Great Pill and paid no mind.

Instead, they paid more attention to the Three Saints' expedition into the Void Realm.

Silently, Li Fan spent a time period similar to his previous period of being lost, thoroughly investigating all the endless possibilities of the cycle.

Finally, he found his target.

It could be said that the existence of all cyclical possibilities was a maze built by the Great Dao of Universe Cycle to conceal it.

And the reason why the Great Dao of Universe Cycle only reluctantly left at the last moment was precisely because of the existence of this item.

In a seemingly sparse and ordinary cyclical possibility, where everything in the world revolved through the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter.

An infinite grassland stretched out, with a single stone monument standing in isolation.

On it, some blurry inscriptions seemed to be carved.

Li Fan's figure flickered and appeared before the stone monument, wanting to reach out and touch it.

But it was like passing through a bubble, his hand passing through empty air, unable to touch it.

"Even with my divine sense scanning from above in the sky, I cannot see its existence."

"Only by coming here in person can I see its form."

"This stone monument..."

Li Fan was certain that the Three Saints had been here before.

Even if he couldn't sense the aura left by the Three Saints, this stone monument reflected the shadows of the Three Saints!

Or, more accurately, lines.

Li Fan's gaze swept over the dozens of mottled marks on the stone monument, searching for the marks belonging to the Three Saints Lianshan.

"This one, this one..."

Two new marks represented Lianshan and Guihai.

"And..."

"Here."

An old mark, which was now accompanied by a new addition, represented Tai Yi's aura.

It was merely a faint stroke, yet it was enough to summarize the image of the Three Saints.

Lines were etched onto the stone monument, like the imprinted images of the Three Saints, as if the Saints themselves had personally visited.

"The other dozens of marks on the stone monument..."

Li Fan was momentarily stunned.

However, he quickly regained his composure.

As Mountains and Seas were devoured by Dao Annihilation, the current Three Saints were far from their peak state and strength.

They could only represent themselves from a certain period of time.

"However, those who could leave an imprint on this stone monument must also not be weak. At the very least, they would have the strength of a Saint of Mountains and Seas."

"Perhaps even before the separation of Mountains and Seas..."

Li Fan faintly sensed the auras of other Saints from the other mottled lines on the stone monument.

Surprisingly, most of them were Saints who had achieved their Dao through the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas!

"This stone monument has certainly existed for a long time. Because even Lianshan and Guihai did not leave any marks on it before."

"That was, before Saint Lianshan was even born, in an ancient time."

"Only Tai Yi existed."

"But at that time, Tai Yi was far from reaching his peak."

Li Fan reached out again, wanting to touch the lines of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas etched on the stone monument.

"It seems there are more Great Daos of Mountains and Seas than I thought."

"It's just that the ancient Saints had already occupied them, so those who came later could only find another way to achieve Sainthood, either through the unification of myriad selves or by creating a new world."

"..."

Thinking of this, Li Fan's thoughts paused slightly.

He suddenly realized something was amiss.

There were so many Saints in the original Mountains and Seas, why were there only a few like Lianshan now?

Where did those who left imprints on the stone monument go?

"Either they perished in the current time and space."

"Or they disappeared before Mountains and Seas were divided by Dao Annihilation, and thus do not exist in the current time and space."

"..."

"It should be the second scenario."

Given the current state of Mountains and Seas, where all Saints worked together with one heart to save the world, it was almost impossible for them to kill each other.

And if they perished in Dao Annihilation, the Saints on the Other Shore would definitely have mentioned it.

But they had never mentioned it.

This indicated that these Saints did not exist in the current Mountains and Seas to begin with.

In simple terms, those who left imprints on the stone monument did not live to see the time of Li Fan's birth.

They had perished long before the catastrophe of Mountains and Seas occurred.

Why did they perish? What power could kill a Saint?

Many questions arose in Li Fan's mind.

However, the Three Saints Lianshan only pointed out the existence of the stone monument and did not reveal the information behind it to Li Fan.

Regarding that ancient time and space, Li Fan knew almost nothing.

It was difficult to speculate.

"Even Saints cannot live forever."

Just as Li Fan sighed, True Return within his body stirred again.

Chapter 1697: Boundless Boundary Monument of Mountains and Seas

It seemed that after the True bodies of the Three Saints Lianshan went to the Void Realm, True Return had let down its guard considerably.

Li Fan could clearly sense the fluctuations from True Return within his body, which spread out and enveloped the many ancient marks on the stone monument before him.

It was as if a faint shadow was being imprinted from the stone monument.

Correspondingly, the "Return to Truth" panel on True Return changed.

Black lines appeared out of nowhere, but they did not display the name of their respective Dao paths, but were simply arranged in sequence, each occupying its position.

Originally only the first and second, almost empty, [Return to Truth] was now suddenly spacious and even full.

All sorts of Great Daos were solemnly listed. Although not yet in place, their ultimate fate was already determined.

Li Fan's mind roamed within it, and he gradually felt a sense of belonging.

Even though this place was still empty and formless, with only two Great Daos and several unformed lines, he felt as if he were at home and reluctant to leave.

It wasn't until he was forcibly expelled by True Return that he suddenly awakened.

The line of [Return to Truth] behind it, where the absorbed lines had disappeared, seemed to have been intentionally hidden by True Return, leaving only [First Profound Embryo] and [Second Universe Cycle]. This was to prevent Li Fan from being lost in contemplation again.

"Although there is no active seduction, it surpasses all temptations in the world."

"It's as if it is everyone's homeland."

Li Fan, gradually regaining his senses, secretly marveled.

At the same time, he reminisced with some reluctance about the scene he had just witnessed in [Return to Truth].

"I didn't see any marks representing the Three Saints. It seems that True Return is still somewhat wary of them."

"Or rather, what has been absorbed by True Return are all the Masterless Great Daos of Mountains and Seas, the future hunting list."

Li Fan refocused his attention on the [Return to Truth] panel.

He discovered that although the Dao marks had been intentionally hidden by True Return, as long as he focused more attention, he could still faintly sense their existence.

But the solemn listing, like a feeling of home, was gone, and he would no longer get lost in it.

"When my intent locks onto a line, it is like looking at the stone monument."

"Even..."

Li Fan had a premonition that he could follow the unseen guidance and find the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas represented by these lines!

Of course, this presupposed that these Great Daos still existed in the current segment of Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan's heart suddenly pounded. He scanned all the targets, but unfortunately, the Dao marks recorded on the stone monument were too ancient. None of them could find any corresponding traces in the current Mountains and Seas.

"However, since True Return has recorded them, it means that in True Return's view, sooner or later, I will encounter them and devour them. They have not truly disappeared, but still exist somewhere in Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan raised his gaze slightly, as if looking past the endless Void Realm, directly at the beginning of Mountains and Seas.
