"But why did the Three Saints specifically point out this stone monument to me?"

Although the stone monument had no further use, Li Fan did not leave directly.

"Either it is a test, or this stone monument is of great help to the newly promoted [Universe Cycle]..."

The previous creation belonged to True Return.

Next, Li Fan needed to find something beneficial to the Saint of [Universe Cycle].

After pondering for a long time, his heart suddenly moved.

He attempted to emulate the Three Saints Lianshan and leave his own imprint on the stone monument.

The power of temporal loops and cycles swirled around Li Fan. He stood before the stone monument motionless, like a statue, wanting to engrave the power of Universe Cycle on it.

But the stone monument seemed uninterested in the power Li Fan displayed.

No matter how Li Fan maneuvered, it did not react in the slightest.

"Is it because my current strength is still too low?"

"No. Even if I haven't reached the realm of the Three Saints, I am definitely not weaker than some of the lines on the stone monument."

"..."

After observing for a long time, Li Fan gained some insight.

"I am, after all, wearing the guise of [Universe Cycle], not the true Saint of Universe Cycle."

"If the place ahead were a blank sheet of paper, with my understanding of this Dao, I might be able to leave a mark. But if it is this ancient stone monument..."

"Let alone three inches into the stone, even three inches into the wood would be difficult to achieve."

"In short, I haven't put in enough effort."

"For Saints like the Three Saints, merely standing before this stone monument without any action would leave an imprint. The essence lies in their accumulated understanding of the Dao."

Understanding this, he did not feel discouraged.

Since Universe Cycle had entered [Return to Truth], his comprehension would naturally be more than twice as effective!

As Li Fan's thoughts evolved, on the True Return panel, the words [Second Universe Cycle] gradually radiated with a dazzling, multicolored light.

With the enhancement of True Return's profound energy, the Dao of Universe Cycle peeled away its outer layers, revealing all its secrets to Li Fan without reservation.

Others were comprehending the Dao. For him, the Dao itself was actively leaning in.

It revealed everything clearly.

Every second, Li Fan's understanding of the Dao of Universe Cycle increased exponentially.

Theoretically, True Return's control meant Li Fan's control.

He could use True Return's absolute manipulation power to leave an imprint on the stone monument.

However, for some reason, Li Fan was willing to try and comprehend the Dao of Universe Cycle on his own.

On the empty plain, the wind seemed to gradually pick up.

The aura of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas emanating from Li Fan's body grew stronger.

Like gusts of mountain wind, like crashing ocean waves.

It continuously blew and struck the ancient stone monument before him.

Slowly, a mark did appear as time flowed!

The stone monument was like a mirror, reflecting everything around it.

And those who could be reflected in the mirror...

*Boom!*

Li Fan instantly felt as if he had fallen into the stone monument.

He returned to the primordial past, surrounded by blurry figures, all of whom were peerless powerhouses comparable to Mountains and Seas.

At that time, Mountains and Seas were still undifferentiated.

The sea was still just the sea, and the mountains were still just mountains.

Outside of Mountains and Seas lay a misty, unknown realm, a place where creation was difficult to manifest.

Suddenly, a stone monument seemed to leap out of nowhere from within Mountains and Seas. Or perhaps it came from outside Mountains and Seas.

It fell into Mountains and Seas.

The mountains trembled, and the great waves churned.

Mountains and Seas merged, thus becoming boundless!

...

Li Fan suddenly retreated from the boundless illusion.

He was still standing before the stone monument. The scene he had just seen felt like an illusion.

But the ancient imagery and aura from before the separation of Mountains and Seas...

Were undeniably real!

"What is the origin of this stone?"

Li Fan tried to look back into the previous scene from the stone monument again, but no matter how hard he tried, he could not succeed.

Recalling what he had just seen, Li Fan remained silent for a long time.

"This monument is called the Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas."

"Because of the existence of this monument, Mountains and Seas are boundless."

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the cryptic message left by Sun Piaomiao.

"Judging from its description, at the time of the birth of Mountains and Seas, it seemed indeed more 'independent' than it is now."

"There was once a record, that something born in the sea wished to reach the mountains. After great hardship, although it succeeded in the end, it still died."

"Unlike now, where Immortals and Saints, stand within Mountains and Seas as if it were a common occurrence. Although the Three Saints Lianshan and Guihai made contributions, looking at it now..."

"It seems this Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas also played an indispensable role."

"Or rather, it was even more important."

"If not for this monument making Mountains and Seas boundless, the birth of beings within Mountains and Seas might have been extremely difficult."

Li Fan tentatively reached out to touch this ancient object, trying to explore its origin.

But it was still the same as before, his hand passed through it, unable to touch it.

"Besides the scene of the monument fixing Mountains and Seas, there are other benefits to inscribing the Dao onto it."

After Li Fan examined himself, he discovered that the aura of Universe Cycle had become more "fitting," not like an outer garment but like his own skin, integrated as one. Even if the Three Saints investigated deeply, they would not be able to find any flaws.

This change was partly due to Li Fan's comprehension of the Dao, and partly due to the assistance of the stone monument!

"The Dao is inscribed on the monument, as if it were a form of recognition."

"I, am now indeed a Saint worthy of the Great Dao of [Universe Cycle]."

"Although I could comprehend it so quickly thanks to True Return's assistance, the path leads to the same destination..."

"Even if I were to lose True Return now and return to the mortal realm. I could still reach the Saintly realm step by step through my own efforts!"

Like thunderclaps, they continuously exploded in Li Fan's sea of consciousness.

The greatest hidden worry in Li Fan's heart for a long time, "What if one day I lose True Return, or True Return leaves me, what should I do?", was first revealed.

Then it shattered like a bubble.

Li Fan's expression was stunned, and instead of the expected joy, he felt a sense of loss.

It was as if something had changed between him and True Return, yet also as if nothing had changed.

Even if he now had the potential to become a Saint, to give up True Return...

What was the point of being a Saint?

At the end of Mountains and Seas, at the end of time, even with all-powerful abilities, he could only be helplessly swallowed by the Star.

Without True Return's help, it was ultimately a dead end.

And to make True Return abandon him...

Looking at the entire Mountains and Seas, could a second being with infinite True Spirit be found?

Although he didn't know why True Return needed infinite True Spirit, Li Fan was certain that he was also irreplaceable to True Return!

"The path of ordinary Saints is ultimately not suitable for me."

"Carrying True Return, I am destined to possess more."

"However..."

"It's good to have a fallback plan."

Li Fan silently stared at the faint mark he had left on the Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas, thinking to himself.

Despite the immense changes he had undergone, True Return remained silent.

Li Fan was used to it and couldn't be bothered to dwell on it.

His consciousness returned to the Other Shore, and his main body suddenly opened his eyes and bowed slightly to the Three Saints Lianshan.

"To actually be able to leave an imprint so quickly..."

"I originally thought that after changing your Dao path from Profound Embryo, it would take you longer to consolidate it?" Tai Yi's phantom image said with some surprise.

"It's just a matter of talent. The imprint you left is faint and cannot compare to the Three Saints," Li Fan said, shaking his head.

With this conversation, the other Saints finally discovered the stone monument hidden within the endless cycle.

"I thought Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle was still consuming the Saintly Fortune Pill and didn't expect another opportunity?" Bai Xiao asked curiously, taking the lead and arriving beside the Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas.

However, after fumbling for a long time, he couldn't leave his own Dao imprint.

Naturally, he couldn't see the scene of the monument fixing Mountains and Seas.

The other Saints tried individually, and only Shou Qiu, Prying Opportunity, Guiming, and Profound Embryo succeeded.

And when their Dao entered the stone monument, they all saw the ancient scene of Mountains and Seas before their separation.

Returning to the Other Shore, the Three Saints Lianshan explained to everyone.

"The Great Dao of Universe Cycle lingered and was unwilling to leave, precisely because of the existence of this monument."

"It was hidden so deeply that even We almost missed it."

"With the imprint left on the monument, Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle can consolidate his Dao path and ensure his future safety. Even if there are any mishaps during True Spirit Infusion or the reconnection of Mountains and Seas, his foundation will not be affected. That is why We let him go first."

Saint Guihai finished speaking, and Saint Tai Yi added, "When this monument appeared, I had not yet been born. However, I heard some fragments about it from older beings."

Bai Xiao, unable to leave an imprint on the stone monument, was dispirited and couldn't help but ask, "What is the origin of this stone monument? How could it have determined the pattern of Mountains and Seas in one go? Mountains and Seas originated from [God]. Could this stone monument be..."

"Perhaps it is the so-called Misty Creation?"

"It can be called that." Tai Yi nodded, then shook his head slightly.

"We speculate that Misty Creation is the remnant of the division of God's power in Mountains and Seas. Judging from the various mystical abilities displayed by this stone monument, it indeed fits the origin from God. However..."

"Before the Primordial Era, who can truly know? Perhaps there was also someone comparable to God," Tai Yi said meaningfully.

The Saints all fell silent upon hearing this.

Li Fan, however, suddenly spoke, "I don't think so. This stone monument... is not found at the end of Mountains and Seas, which means it cannot escape Dao Annihilation."

"Rather than being a creation of God, it is more like an evolution born from the will of Mountains and Seas itself."

A silence fell upon the Saints present.

Lianshan's phantom image chuckled lightly and said, "This is where Universe Cycle is mistaken. This monument is different from other things in Mountains and Seas. It does not exist within Mountains and Seas like Us, but only exists in this moment, this instant."

"Before this, and after this, on that grassland, there is no other Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan was suddenly startled.

The other Saints had not noticed this detail before, but now, looking back at the existence of the Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas, they gradually saw some clues.

"Indeed, it seems to be self-contained in space-time, independent of Mountains and Seas."

"This is also why Universe Cycle was able to conceal it by creating various cyclical possibilities earlier. The cycle revolved around that central point, which was the location of the Boundless Monument. So that's how it is..."

"This means that this Boundless Monument is likely a divine artifact. It is unique in the entire segment of Mountains and Seas, and We were fortunate enough to encounter it. What great fortune!"

"It's all thanks to Saint Universe Cycle. If it weren't for him seeking an opportunity to re-establish his Sainthood, We might have missed this chance."

"However... besides leaving a Dao imprint, does this Boundless Monument have any other uses?"

...

Next, the Saints continued their discussion.

However, regarding this ancient creation, they could not come to any conclusion.

Through this incident, Li Fan also realized that the Three Saints Lianshan were not omniscient and omnipotent.

They were just stronger and lived longer than ordinary Saints.

They also encountered things beyond their knowledge.

Chapter 1698: The Three Saints Fall Together

The white light of the Other Shore shone brightly, enveloping the endless cycle.

The Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas was incredibly divine, standing firm and untouchable. It was even less likely to be moved.

However, by expanding the coverage of the Other Shore, it could be brought under the protection of the Xuán Jī Ring.

"Good and bad come hand in hand. Next, We must discuss some bad news."

"As We traversed the ninety thousand years of the Void Realm and were about to reach the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, We discovered that the Dao Annihilation tide was surging and churning, creating chaos and making it impossible to discern the direction. Based on past experience, this indicates that Mountains and Seas are in imminent danger and on the verge of collapse," the phantom image of Saint Lianshan's words interrupted the Saints' gazes.

Everyone was shocked to hear this.

"If the Mountains and Seas ahead are destroyed, causing the Void Realm to exceed the ten-thousand-year limit, Our plan to reconnect Mountains and Seas will fail."

"The priority is to go and assist, stabilize the situation, and then discuss the reconnection."

As he spoke, the phantom images of the Three Saints Lianshan looked towards Li Fan.

Li Fan's heart felt strange, but the Three Saints had already explained the reason, leaving everyone stunned.

"Our senses of the area ahead have been cut off. Either the [Lianshan, Guihai, Tai Yi] from the previous segment of Mountains and Seas have already crossed over, perhaps even leaving no phantom images behind. Or..."

"We have all perished."

"We have all perished." These four words reverberated like thunderclaps in the Xuán Jī Ring.

All the Saints showed expressions of disbelief, staring at the Three Saints Lianshan, their mouths agape, as if filled with endless doubts.

But in the end, it all turned into a single sentence: "How is that possible?"

"Life and death are ordinary matters. Even the Creator God perished and transformed into Mountains and Seas. Our falling is not impossible," Tai Yi chuckled lightly.

"This also indirectly proves the abnormality of the previous segment of Mountains and Seas. If We were all still here, Mountains and Seas would never have fallen into such a crisis of destruction," Guihai analyzed calmly.

Facing the "death of themselves," the Three Saints Lianshan could still maintain their composure.

But the other Saints on the Other Shore could not remain calm.

The strength of the Three Saints Lianshan was evident to all.

When traversing the Void Realm, they led the way, opening paths. Then, using their bodies as bridges, they illuminated the path for those who followed.

If not for the Three Saints, the plan to reconnect Mountains and Seas would have been mere empty talk.

But now, they were being told that the Three Saints had collectively perished?

What could possibly kill powerhouses like Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi?

"This is also related to the [Trouble] that I informed you of earlier."

"The trouble originates from the Void Realm."

"Have you all ever wondered if Our action to reconnect Mountains and Seas was perhaps too smooth?"

"As long as there are enough Saints to act as a link, connecting Mountains and Seas. Then, after some effort, Mountains and Seas can be reborn. The Void Realm, which devours everything, actually did not react too strongly to this, allowing Us to proceed."

Saint Lianshan's words caused the Saints' expressions to gradually become solemn.

"The Void Realm devours Mountains and Seas, a grand battlefield stretching from the beginning of Mountains and Seas to the end of time."

"Since it is a battlefield, there are priorities. The gains and losses of a single moment or place are ultimately insignificant. Today, Mountains and Seas reappear, and Dao Annihilation is repelled. Tomorrow, the Void Realm can return, and Dao Annihilation will devour everything again."

"What is truly important..."

"Is [Saints]."

"The Void Realm was originally slightly superior to Mountains and Seas. With a slight advantage, over time, it could eventually devour Mountains and Seas."

"But because there are beings comparable to Mountains and Seas, the existence of Saints. This battle situation has added several variables. We are naturally thorns in the eyes of the Void Realm, the very flesh and blood, the sharpest thorns." Saint Lianshan spoke calmly, as if stating facts unrelated to himself.

"But even with the Void Realm's intervention, it is hard to imagine what means could have killed all three of you simultaneously?"

Bai Xiao voiced the question in everyone's mind.

After all, with the strength of the Three Saints, they were practically fearless of Dao Annihilation.

Could it be that the Void Realm had some other special means?

Saint Lianshan no longer played coy and said calmly, "What could have killed Us..."

"Is only Ourselves."

At first, everyone did not understand the meaning, but when they looked at the unfathomably deep Void Realm, they seemed to finally understand something.

A chill slowly crept into their hearts.

"Yes, the ones who attacked should be the [Three Saints] from the destroyed Mountains and Seas."

"After being swallowed by the Void Realm and disappearing from the world, they reappeared in some form, becoming the claws and teeth of the Void Realm." Guihai nodded, confirming everyone's guess.

"When the calamity suddenly struck and Mountains and Seas were swallowed by the Void Realm, We were not killed. Instead, We perished with Mountains and Seas. Even though We stood shoulder to shoulder with Mountains and Seas, if the surrounding foundation was completely lost and We were surrounded by the Void Realm, unable to distinguish past from present. Even with a thousand divine abilities, the final solution could only be to be trapped to death."

"But the previous segment of Mountains and Seas still exists, yet We have already perished..."

"This situation should only have one explanation."

Lianshan finished speaking, and a complete silence fell in the Xuán Jī Ring.

All the Saints looked at each other, not knowing how to respond.

Lianshan continued, "We have not yet fought with ourselves in that state, but based on Our experience fighting against the Void Realm. The strength of Our resurrected selves from the Void Realm should be comparable to Our main bodies, or rather, it is Us ourselves. However..."

"They chose to side with the Void Realm."

"Not only Us. All beings in the swallowed Mountains and Seas could be resurrected by the Void Realm to deal with themselves. Using their own methods against them. This is the Void Realm's method specifically targeting the Saints of Mountains and Seas."

"A long time ago, We met an old friend with a completely different temperament. We argued over the slightest disagreement, and later, things escalated into a fight. At first, We did not understand why. Until the end, when We killed him..."

"It was as if a passage to the Void Realm was opened in Mountains and Seas. Endless waves of Dao Annihilation surged, their momentum almost comparable to the initial outbreak of the calamity. Even though We tried Our best to maintain it, We were still unable to stabilize Ourselves under the impact. Mountains and Seas perished in an instant, and We could only flee in a hurry."

"Afterward, reflecting on it, We realized that was the Void Realm's resurrection technique."

...

Hearing the narration of the Three Saints Lianshan, Li Fan gradually understood.

If the confrontation between Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm was a continuous war, then the Void Realm they traversed to reconnect Mountains and Seas was merely the battlefield where the two armies clashed.

With the power of the Three Saints, even if they could fight their way in and out, they would still perish if they were truly surrounded by the endless armies of the Void Realm.

It was precisely because of this that Mountains and Seas were lost and Saints annihilated under the concentrated attack of the Void Realm.

This point, Li Fan could understand.

After all, he had personally witnessed the desolation of Mountains and Seas at the end of time, and the powerlessness of the last few Saints as they were swallowed by Dao Annihilation.

But he never expected that the Void Realm could actually resurrect the swallowed Saints!

The thought of facing an opponent with the full strength of the Three Saints, who acted recklessly, with the sole aim of destroying Mountains and Seas, made Li Fan somewhat apprehensive.

"However, there is no need to worry too much. The Void Realm's resurrection of Saints also requires the mobilization of its own power, which is not inexhaustible."

"Otherwise, these creations alone would be enough to destroy Mountains and Seas."

"Therefore, I suspect that the purpose of these resurrected creations is to eliminate the Saints who pose a threat to the Void Realm."

"We have not encountered them yet, but it is only because We are lucky."

"But since We have already discovered their possible whereabouts, We must be vigilant."

"The action to reconnect Mountains and Seas must not stop. As the saying goes, 'What is lost can be regained.' If Mountains and Seas are completely doomed to failure... We might only be able to sit and wait for death."

Li Fan finally asked, "The Three Saints were just looking at me..."

"The Mountains and Seas ahead have no one to guard them and are in danger of destruction at any moment. Someone needs to be sent to stabilize the situation. If We were to descend, it might attract the resurrected [Void Realm Resurrected] to return. Their strength is comparable, and the outcome of a fight is uncertain. Although We are not afraid of them, it might lead to the complete destruction of Mountains and Seas."

"Therefore, the person sent should ideally not be in the Void Realm's memory. That is, someone who never existed in those swallowed Mountains and Seas."

Saint Lianshan's words caused all the Saints to look at Li Fan.

Among everyone present, only he seemed to fit the criteria.

"This..."

Li Fan instinctively hesitated.

Was he kidding? He was being asked to go and save a dangerous place where even the Three Saints had perished?

As if seeing Li Fan's thoughts, the Three Saints added, "The [Void Realm Resurrected] only targets the main body. You are not on the Void Realm's memory list, so even if you descend, you will not attract the Void Realm's attention."

"Your task is only to stabilize the crumbling state of Mountains and Seas. While you are going, We will also be working on reconnecting Mountains and Seas in the Void Realm. We will not keep you waiting too long."

"To prevent any accidents, We will each give you a protective treasure. Even if you truly encounter the [Void Realm Resurrected], you can still escape with ease."

"You possess the ability of True Spirit Infusion. If the situation becomes truly desperate, We will not force you to go."

...

With things said to this point, under the gaze of all the Saints, Li Fan could only nod silently.

Otherwise, it would not fit the persona of a "Mountains and Seas Walker."

However, Li Fan naturally had no intention of fighting against any [Void Realm Resurrected] beings. If anything went wrong, he would immediately use True Return to return to his anchor point.

"The previous segment of Mountains and Seas may collapse at any time. We must act immediately."

"However, We must also note..."

"Those who can provoke the Void Realm Resurrected attack must be in a place important enough. The continuous time span may even surpass the three reconnecting attempts and where We are now. With the Three Saints perished and no leader, it is bound to be a scene of unimaginable destruction. Stabilizing the situation may not be easy. Fellow Daoist must be careful." Shou Qiu's expression was solemn as he reminded him.

"I will be mindful." Li Fan nodded slightly and then looked at the Three Saints.

He was waiting for the promised protective treasures.

The Three Saints would not go back on their word. Each of them emitted a stream of light, which flew to Li Fan's front.

The moment the light and shadow appeared, one could feel their extraordinary nature.

Lianshan's gift was a wooden staff.

Its surface was rough, as if casually plucked from a tree.

But the ancient aura that occasionally appeared on the staff indicated that it was far from being as simple as it looked.

Indeed, Lianshan explained with a hint of nostalgia, "This staff was used by me when I first ascended Mount Shang in the past. Although it has accompanied me all these years, I have not used it again. Now that you bear the burden of everyone and are heading into a dangerous situation, I present it to you."

Li Fan gently stroked it. The moment he touched it, it was as if he felt the path Lianshan had once walked through this hiking staff.

The continuous, vast mountains that had not yet been devoured by Dao Annihilation.

Li Fan was overjoyed and put the hiking staff into his storage.

Lianshan's gift was so precious, and Guihai's was no less.

It was still a seemingly ordinary iron shovel.

But it seemed to gather an infinite source of power. Just by being near it, Li Fan felt his entire body being nourished, and he relaxed unconsciously.

"It was with this iron shovel that I forged the path from infinity to the Infinite Sea. With the merging of Mountains and Seas, this shovel has lost its use. Keeping it with me would be a waste. You take it." Saint Guihai said calmly.

Li Fan suppressed his excitement and also accepted the item.

Next, it was Tai Yi's turn.

"Those two were quite generous. I don't have anything noteworthy to give..."

"I'll give you this little thing."

Tai Yi said nonchalantly, but from the fleeting expression on his face, the gift was definitely not a mere trifle.

"Don't disgrace it." Indeed, after seeing Li Fan put it away, Tai Yi couldn't help but say.

It was a stone club.

It looked good externally, appearing crystal clear as if cast from jade. But the moment Li Fan touched it with his hands, he sensed a terrifying aura of blood and gore.

To describe it as a mountain of corpses and a sea of blood would not even be enough to describe a fraction of it.

It was as if countless beings had met their end under this club.

Even with Li Fan's experience, seeing such a bloody scene, he couldn't help but change his expression slightly.

But fortunately, he did not flinch in fear and drop the stone club.

"I never expected that the seemingly amiable and easy-to-talk-to Saint Tai Yi would have walked such a path of terrifying slaughter." Li Fan observed. Even after hundreds of millions of years, the countless resentful spirits that still lingered at the top of the club made Li Fan secretly astonished.

Wooden staff, iron shovel, stone club.

The gifts from the Three Saints, though seemingly ordinary and even crude, were undoubtedly supreme treasures of Mountains and Seas.

Holding the wooden staff, with the iron shovel at his waist.

The stone club on his back.

Li Fan cupped his hands in farewell to everyone on the Other Shore and was about to depart to traverse the Void Realm.

"Be careful."

Naturally, everyone did not want Li Fan to be harmed and warned him.

"Come here."

Before Li Fan could bid farewell to everyone, the three phantom images exerted force simultaneously.

Li Fan felt himself being enveloped by a great force and was hurled into the boundless Void Realm.

Fortunately, he did not lose his direction.

Instead, he was propelled at high speed towards a predetermined location.

It was like riding the wind and waves, breaking through thorns and brambles.

Occasionally, Void Realm tides would rise, but they could not stop him in the slightest.

In the Void Realm, ninety thousand years of time passed in an instant.

In the blink of an eye, Li Fan saw the main bodies of the Three Saints ahead.

They stood like lighthouses in the darkness, repelling all the surrounding storms.

But...

Even with the protection of the Three Saints' treasures, Li Fan keenly sensed that the activity of Dao Annihilation in the vicinity was far greater than in the previous Mountains and Seas.

"It's almost similar to the ferocity at the end of time."

Chapter 1699: The Saints Fight in the Apocalypse

"Although We have the treasures to protect you, do not overexert yourself. If it is impossible..."

"Prioritize your own safety. With True Spirit Infusion, there are infinite possibilities. Even if Mountains and Seas cannot be reconnected, there may still be a way to salvage the situation."

The Three Saints were present, yet they spoke differently from those on the Other Shore.

"Remember, after descending to the Mountains and Seas ahead, do not trust anyone, even familiar individuals."

"There is only one ultimate goal: to preserve Mountains and Seas amidst the rampant Dao Annihilation. As for other matters..."

"Be unrestrained, and act according to your judgment."

As if seeing the chaos of the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints Lianshan solemnly instructed.

Without waiting for Li Fan's reply, three streams of power enveloped his body.

They forcefully broke through the surging Dao Annihilation tide and shot towards the precarious Mountains and Seas in the Void Realm.

The Void Realm's reaction was unexpectedly fierce, quickly reclaiming the passage Li Fan had created. As if determined to completely conquer the Mountains and Seas ahead, the faint light representing Li Fan only lasted for a few moments before being submerged in the endless darkness.

And the Three Saints, under the impact of the Void Realm, their figures trembled slightly.

"We should also start making preparations."

The majestic figures suddenly grew larger, pushing back the surrounding darkness.

The Three Saints stood like interconnected mountains, illuminating the epochs of the Void Realm.

...

Even with the help of the Three Saints to send him off, the experience of forcefully traversing the Void Realm under its backlash was extremely unpleasant.

It was as if ten thousand steel knives were constantly shaving at the foundation of one's existence, each blow almost shattering the Dao foundation.

If not for Li Fan's enlightenment of Universe Cycle at the Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas, leaving his unique imprint.

If not for Li Fan possessing Infinite True Spirit, completely unafraid of the Void Realm's erosion.

He would likely be heavily injured by now.

"Heh heh..."

His figure finally stabilized, Li Fan coughed lightly, calming his blood and Qi.

He paid no mind to the dozens of possibilities that had been shattered by his impact.

After all, the Mountains and Seas here, as far as the eye could see, were already a scene of shattered land, withered and decaying!

The moment he descended, Li Fan sensed the abnormality of this place.

Chaos, madness, hysteria.

Even Mountains and Seas themselves had undergone inexplicable changes due to the demise of the Three Saints.

"Even ants cling to life, let alone Mountains and Seas."

"As it is about to be devoured by the Void Realm, various distorted phenomena will manifest."

Li Fan frowned slightly, dispelling the mountain and sea roars that sounded like ghostly wails reaching his ears.

He had also witnessed the end of Mountains and Seas before.

But that was at the twilight of time.

Now, Mountains and Seas were still managing to hold on in their middle age.

Therefore, the desperate struggle of Mountains and Seas before their demise was also terrifying.

All beings within the countless possibilities of Mountains and Seas originated from Mountains and Seas. Now that Mountains and Seas were about to collapse, in their struggle for survival, Mountains and Seas intended to reclaim everything.

In order to prolong their existence for a little longer.

Without the arrival of Dao Annihilation, the possibilities collapsed like landslides, burying all life within them.

The Immortal Realm, built by the Three Saints upon the continuous Mountains and Seas, began to collapse entirely.

Even...

Li Fan looked towards where the Other Shore should have been.

The radiant white light that enveloped Mountains and Seas was no longer present.

Instead, it had turned into a strange black, dim light.

It trembled from time to time, as if a fierce battle was underway within it.

"This mess..."

"Preserve Mountains and Seas." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, observed for a moment, and then shook his head slightly.

"Let's observe first. If it's really impossible, then I'll use True Return to go back. Anyway, this life has yielded enough gains..."

Just as Li Fan was thinking this, his expression suddenly changed.

Because just now, he sensed an invisible hand slowly brushing over the top of his head. The cold and smooth touch made him instinctively shudder. At the same time, Li Fan felt as if something had been "scraped off" him!

"Who!"

Before Li Fan could react, the bamboo staff in his hand spontaneously struck out towards the empty space.

It seemed silent at first.

Then, ripples gradually spread, growing louder and louder, finally turning into continuous, earth-shattering roars that shook Mountains and Seas.

A figure was forced out in a sorry state.

And far behind him, Li Fan clearly saw that the Mountains and Seas, which were in a state of self-collapse due to the impending apocalypse, had actually temporarily stabilized their situation.

It was as if an invisible force was forcefully condensing the collapsing Mountains and Seas.

It looked as if the mountains that had collapsed were rising again!

With the wooden staff's strike, the Mountains and Seas instantly fell silent.

Only the roars of the mountains reappearing and rising echoed.

Li Fan himself was stunned, and then he felt the gazes from all parts of Mountains and Seas!

And as the sneak attacker was exposed, the object that had been "scraped off" by the invisible hand returned to its owner.

"Lian... Shan... Staff."

The Saint opposite him spoke word by word, as if encountering something utterly incredible.

Li Fan also recognized the opponent's identity in an instant.

Prying Opportunity.

He thought that after recognizing the Saint Lianshan's token, the opponent's attitude would change.

However, he did not expect that Saint Prying Opportunity would only freeze for a moment before launching another attack on Li Fan.

The target was no longer Li Fan, but the Lianshan Staff in Li Fan's hand!

Not only that, but Li Fan could also feel several familiar auras instantly approaching from all directions of Mountains and Seas.

Their target was clearly Li Fan.

Li Fan's scalp tingled. Only now did he understand why, before his departure, the Three Saints had suddenly instructed him to "act with impunity, and proceed as you see fit."

There was no need for Li Fan to control it. The Lianshan Staff automatically waved, creating layers of mountain shadows all around, blocking the sight of all the Saints.

Even so, it could not completely block Prying Opportunity's frenzied actions.

"Cough, cough, cough..."

Li Fan sensed that his "luck" seemed to be draining away at an alarming rate. Even the normal circulation of his own blood and Qi was affected, as if he had gone mad and was unable to regulate himself!

More importantly, the outer layer of Universe Cycle he wore had begun to fit loosely!

And besides Prying Opportunity, a second Saint had already attacked.

Starlight paved the way, and a wooden boat drifted.

A small boat broke through the infinite mountain shadows created by the Lianshan Staff and forcibly rammed towards Li Fan.

Li Fan vaguely discerned Saint Xingcha standing on the boat.

Compared to the Xingcha Saint they were familiar with on the Other Shore in later generations, the Xingcha Saint here was enveloped in an extremely dense, murderous aura.

The target was also clear: the Lianshan Staff in Li Fan's hand.

Every speck of starlight seemed to contain an infinite amount of energy, continuously crashing against the rising mountain shadows, scattering starlight. The situation of Mountains and Seas, which had just been stabilized by the Lianshan Staff, became unstable again.

Just then, the iron shovel at Li Fan's waist also moved.

Like the Lianshan Staff, it acted on its own.

With a casual thrust into the Mountains and Seas,

The starlight, the invisible icy hand, and even the rising mountain shadows were all repelled by a mysterious great vibration.

The great sound was silent.

All sounds disappeared, and in the Mountains and Seas, only the sound of gurgling spring water echoed.

The sound of flowing water grew louder and louder, and in just a moment, it turned into a roaring torrent, resounding in the ears of all the Saints.

The chaotic and depleted Infinite Sea had another spring dug out.

The madness of Mountains and Seas weakened.

Li Fan looked at the actions of the two divine artifacts and suddenly understood.

"This is the act of the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai, recreating the merging of Lianshan and Guihai."

"Further excavating the potential of the dying Mountains and Seas, making it like a dying man's last burst of vitality, regenerating life."

"However, this is not a long-term solution. If it cannot be stabilized as soon as possible..."

"This segment of Mountains and Seas will collapse even faster!"

Li Fan's thoughts raced, already considering using True Return to go back.

And with the advent of the iron shovel, the expressions of all the Saints looking at Li Fan changed again.

But they only hesitated for a moment.

They still did not give up their attempts to seize the treasures!

No one knew what had happened in this segment of Mountains and Seas after the death of the Three Saints.

The dispositions of the Saints on the Other Shore had all changed drastically.

"The items opened up by the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai should belong to the virtuous. Fellow Daoist cultivating is insufficient, and holding them instead will bring disaster."

A faint voice echoed from the depths of Mountains and Seas.

As if to confirm his words, the Lianshan Staff and Guihai Shovel, which had been inspiring unparalleled protection, actually showed signs of losing control at this moment!

"Oracle Prediction." Li Fan's expression changed slightly as he recognized the owner of the voice.

One word, and the prophecy could be broken or fulfilled.

"Quickly let go. Delay will bring self-destruction!"

As Oracle Prediction spoke, the Lianshan Staff that was being wielded actually swung towards Li Fan, summoning a mountain shadow.

*Bang!*

Li Fan, caught off guard, collided head-on with it.

As a Saint, he naturally would not be so easily injured, but his body vibrated, and his blood and Qi became turbulent.

More importantly, the Lianshan Staff and Guihai Shovel in his hands became increasingly difficult to control.

The protective mountain and sea shadows inspired by the two divine artifacts were no longer stable.

The Saints became more aggressive.

"I came from the Mountains and Seas of the future, to save..."

Li Fan's voice was deep, but he was horrified to find that what he said had unknowingly changed.

"What bullshit Saints, they are nothing but dogs and chickens."

"First kill the Three Saints, then slay all of you. Mountains and Seas will perish, and all will return to the Void Realm!"

"Hahahaha!"

His laughter was maniacal.

Even more terrifying, as these words were spoken, Li Fan's thoughts actually began to change accordingly.

It was as if a pen in the background was rewriting his fate!

"Guiming..."

Li Fan gritted his teeth, forcefully resisting the distorted invasion in his mind.

Because if he could not resist this distortion, he would act like a puppet. He would fight the Saints until death, and would not activate True Return.

As Li Fan devoted most of his willpower to fighting against Guiming, the signs of the Lianshan Staff and Guihai Shovel losing control became even more apparent.

Oracle Prediction, Divination, Prying Opportunity, Karmic Judgment, Xingcha...

These familiar Saints on the Other Shore, completely disregarding Li Fan's identity as an envoy of the Three Saints, displayed their divine abilities, all trying to capture Li Fan.

The Dao paths of the Saints had not changed, but their actions were like completely different people.

Even with the protective treasures bestowed by the Three Saints, under their siege, Li Fan was gradually struggling to hold on.

At this critical moment, the stone club that had been hanging on Li Fan's back.

Finally moved.

"Now that the Three Saints have perished, we naturally live and die by our own fate. Fellow Daoist, why must you..."

Oracle Prediction's words were cut short by a muffled groan.

Then, a series of muffled thuds followed.

In just a few moments, Li Fan felt the pressure on him greatly reduced.

And the stone club that had disappeared reappeared before Li Fan.

However, at some unknown time, it had become stained with blood of varying degrees.

"All Beings Club... Hehehe."

Prying Opportunity, having suffered a hidden loss, let out a cold laugh.

Although the siege on Li Fan had stopped, they did not disperse.

Instead, they stared intently.

The other Saints did the same.

"Live and die by our own fate." Li Fan tightly gripped the All Beings Club, recalling Prying Opportunity's words just now.

And thinking of the subtle changes occurring in the Xuán Jī Ring, he finally began to understand.

"The dispositions of all the Saints have changed drastically."

"The special instructions from the Three Saints before their departure."

"And..."

"Prying Opportunity, Oracle Prediction, Divination..."

"The so-called Saints on the Other Shore were probably not the good and righteous people I saw."

"They were merely subdued by the Three Saints and then transformed by the Xuán Jī Ring over a long period, allowing all the Saints to work together with one heart for the salvation of Mountains and Seas."

"As long as the Three Saints were present, everything was manageable. Even if the Saints harbored dissatisfaction in their hearts, they could not turn the tide."

"But in this segment of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints were killed by [Void Realm Resurrected]. The Saints on the Other Shore have, however, returned to their original nature..."

The Saints' ill intentions permeated the air, encircling Li Fan tightly.

However, the All Beings Club in his hand remained fearless, as if it hadn't tasted blood in a long time and was even eager to try.

The current situation, although Li Fan could use True Return to return to his designated anchor point.

But even a clay figurine has some temper.

After being teleported and then besieged by all the Saints, Li Fan was extremely stifled.

"Although you have numbers, I possess the divine artifacts of the Three Saints."

Li Fan casually weighed the All Beings Club in his hand, a dangerous glint in his eyes.

"Act with impunity."

He repeatedly muttered the Four Words instructed by the Three Saints, and then, without any warning, swung a blow towards Oracle Prediction in the distance.

There was no need for him to target the opponent.

As long as he thought about who he wanted to hit, the All Beings Club in his hand would naturally strike the target.

Ignoring space and time, it hit accurately upon release.

And it was unavoidable.

"All beings are under the club."

Another muffled sound was heard. Li Fan felt the feedback force from the hand in his grasp and understood the origin of the name [All Beings Club].

His gaze swept over the Saints surrounding him, and Li Fan did not hold back, swinging repeatedly.

He could not kill the Saints, but each strike landed squarely on their heads.

However, the Saints present were not lambs to the slaughter.

Although Li Fan had gained a temporary advantage with the divine artifacts, the Saints, working together, endured the attacks of the All Beings Club and collaborated to interfere with Li Fan's actions.

His movements, his thoughts, all began to be uncontrollably affected.

After having his fun, Li Fan was about to use True Return to leave.

But suddenly, his thoughts stirred, and he shouted in a deep voice, "Duke Shou Qiu, if you don't help me now, Mountains and Seas may have no hope of recovery!"

"Alas..."

A sigh echoed from the middle of Mountains and Seas.

As if a continuous great tide was arriving, obscuring the sight of all the Saints.

"Follow me."

A faint whisper sounded, and Li Fan did not resist. He was swept away by this force and safely escaped from the encirclement of all the Saints.

Chapter 1700: Natural Recovery

"So, is it truly possible for Mountains and Seas to be reconnected after being severed?"

In the chaotic currents of possibilities amidst the shattered Mountains and Seas, Duke Shou Qiu listened to Li Fan's explanation of the cause and effect, his doubt tinged with belief.

A Walker from the end of Mountains and Seas, who had reconnected Mountains and Seas twice.

If this were said before, he might have believed it implicitly, but now...

After the calamity of the Three Saints' inexplicable demise, even Duke Shou Qiu's state of mind had undergone a subtle change.

"The Three Saints knew of the danger of my journey, hence they each bestowed protective treasures. The Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Club. All are treasures of the Three Saints, and all can serve as tokens."

"Moreover..."

Li Fan reached out, his divine sense touching the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas. As if sensing something with his eyes closed, he then grasped it firmly and presented it to Duke Shou Qiu.

Facts speak louder than words.

With the True Spirit silt from the Void Realm as proof, Duke Shou Qiu immediately believed seven-tenths of Li Fan's words.

"There is truly such a divine technique, it is truly to the fortune of Mountains and Seas!"

Duke Shou Qiu was overcome with emotion, but after a moment, his expression dimmed: "Unfortunately, it has come a little late."

Li Fan knew that Duke Shou Qiu was referring to the matter of the Three Saints' demise in this segment of Mountains and Seas. He was also somewhat curious about the Void Realm Resurrected that could kill the Three Saints, so he inquired.

Duke Shou Qiu seemed to still be in lingering fear. After a period of silence, he slowly said, "That day, just like usual, the Three Saints' main bodies were carving out a path in the Void Realm ahead. We attempted to use ourselves as bridges to connect the Mountains and Seas before and after. Who would have thought..."

"The Void Realm erupted with wind and waves!"

"That was a Dao Annihilation tide I had never seen before, its ferocity was a thousand times greater than what is raging here!"

Duke Shou Qiu pointed to the Dao Annihilation torrents outside the shattered Mountains and Seas, his expression solemn.

"It was as if the entire Void Realm had concentrated its power here. Caught off guard, our formation was instantly scattered. In our haste, we could only quickly withdraw to the Xuanji Ring, but we discovered..."

"The Three Saints had not returned!"

"Even their phantom images left behind had vanished. If this were to happen, it means either the Three Saints had already perished in that storm, or they had encountered an extremely dangerous situation. They needed to exert all their strength to deal with it, hence they had to recall all their outward-shining power. Regardless of the cause, this was something unprecedented for us."

"At that time, we only then realized in hindsight. The terrifying turmoil in the Void Realm was precisely because the Three Saints were locked in battle."

Duke Shou Qiu took a deep breath: "Previously, we only knew that the strength of the Three Saints was far superior to that of the other Saints. But how strong they truly were, no one knew. It was only at that moment that we understood the vast difference. However, even such Three Saints..."

"Have perished." Duke Shou Qiu's body trembled slightly, as if he still found it hard to accept this fact.

Li Fan frowned slightly: "Did Duke Shou Qiu personally witness the demise of the Three Saints?"

Duke Shou Qiu shook his head: "No need to see it personally. The shattering of the Xuanji Ring is the best proof. The Xuanji Ring was a divine artifact jointly built by the Three Saints. Even the most malevolent beings, once fallen into the ring, would be easily subdued. Only through this method could we all work together with one heart and save Mountains and Seas. It's just..."

"Jiangshan is easy to change, but human nature is hard to shift. Originally, I thought they had truly changed their ways. Who would have expected that once the Xuanji Ring shattered, they couldn't maintain it for long before revealing their true colors."

"Coupled with the chaotic situation of Mountains and Seas, although I wished to salvage the situation, I was powerless. I could only hide first and think of a plan later. Who would have thought I would encounter the scene of your rash arrival."

Li Fan also felt a little helpless: "The Three Saints sensed the drastic changes in the Mountains and Seas ahead, so they sent me. The Saints on the Other Shore are not the biggest problem. The most crucial thing is the Void Realm Resurrected. It is precisely they who killed the Three Saints in this segment of Mountains and Seas."

"Void Realm Resurrected... So it is this thing." Duke Shou Qiu's expression turned solemn.

Li Fan continued: "Precisely because I come from the end of Mountains and Seas, and do not exist in the Void Realm's memory, I am not in danger of being invaded by the Void Realm Resurrected, so the Three Saints decided to send me. However, as you saw just now, with only me, I am probably no match for them."

Li Fan stopped halfway through his sentence.

Duke Shou Qiu naturally understood his meaning and said sternly: "Whether it is for the sake of the Three Saints, or for the sake of all beings in Mountains and Seas, I have no responsibility to shirk. It's just..."

Suddenly, Duke Shou Qiu's expression changed, and he grabbed Li Fan.

"We've been discovered, quickly go!"

Amidst the bursting starlight, Duke Shou Qiu, bringing Li Fan, escaped from the encirclement of the Saints once more.

They found another place in the chaotic currents of Mountains and Seas and temporarily hid themselves.

Li Fan was a little puzzled: "Why did they go madly trying to snatch the Three Saints' treasures the moment they saw me holding them? Isn't the priority to survive in this collapsing Mountains and Seas?"

Duke Shou Qiu was slightly stunned, then sighed: "It seems you still don't understand the weight of the Three Treasures in your hands. It's no wonder. Perhaps only then did the Three Saints hand them over to you."

"What do you mean?"

"Never mind the wooden staff, iron shovel, and stone club; they all look like ordinary mortal items. But they are all objects through which the Three Saints attained their Dao. Saint Lianshan ascended Mount Shang with his staff. Saint Guihai opened springs with his shovel. Saint Tai Yi suppressed all beings with his club. In the ancient Mountains and Seas, these three items all had formidable reputations. After the Three Saints attained their Dao, with their strength, they didn't need to use their treasures. They kept them by their side to nurture them. They would rarely use them, only in truly critical moments..."

"Once, we personally witnessed the Three Saints joining forces to save Mountains and Seas that were on the verge of collapse. It can be said that these three items already possess the power comparable to that of Saints!"

Li Fan looked at the staff, shovel, and club on his person, which had returned to their dormant state, and felt somewhat surprised.

He naturally knew these three items were extraordinary, but he never expected them to hold such great significance for the Three Saints.

"If their power can be fully unleashed, the current encroaching enemies can be subdued in an instant." Duke Shou Qiu asserted with certainty.

"But I can't truly use them right now. They are acting entirely on their own." Li Fan said.

Duke Shou Qiu was not surprised: "The Three Treasures have their own spirituality. They followed the Three Saints for a long time and developed their own tempers. They were subservient to the Three Saints, but..."

"Your strength might not be weak enough yet, hence it's understandable that they are unwilling to fully submit." Duke Shou Qiu said tactfully.

Li Fan chuckled: "It's fine. As long as the situation of Mountains and Seas can be stabilized, that's good."

"My arrival with the treasures has attracted their attention. If not for this, letting them fight among themselves would have led to the destruction of Mountains and Seas soon."

"However, it cannot last long. If they search for you for a long time and cannot find you... knowing their temperament, they might threaten us by destroying Mountains and Seas to force us to appear," Duke Shou Qiu warned sternly.

Li Fan was astonished: "Such dignified Saints are actually so despicable?"

Duke Shou Qiu sighed: "Saints are merely divisions of strength; they have no actual relation to moral integrity. Before they attained Dao, many were already unscrupulous individuals. However, they were suppressed by the Three Saints in the Xuanji Ring, and their rough edges were smoothed out. Now that they are free..."

"They will likely become even more unrestrained."

Duke Shou Qiu's expression was worried.

"Before I came, the Void Realm had already extended for nearly a hundred thousand years. If this segment of Mountains and Seas collapses further, the grand plan of reconnection will fail."

Li Fan clarified the seriousness of the situation and then asked, "In Duke Shou Qiu's opinion, among the Saints on the Other Shore, who can be the first breakthrough point?"

"Although I am not talented, I am willing to sacrifice my life to reverse the tide."

Li Fan's righteousness contrasted sharply with the rampant Saints on the Other Shore.

Duke Shou Qiu couldn't help but feel respect upon hearing this.

After pondering for a moment, he said solemnly: "The strength of the Saints has long been classified. From strongest to weakest, they are Prying Opportunity, Fate Script, Divination, Karmic Judgment, Star Ferry..."

Li Fan declared loudly: "Then let's start with Prying Opportunity!"

Duke Shou Qiu seemed a little puzzled.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes: "To deal with such individuals, we need to use lightning-fast methods to intimidate them. If we attack the weaker ones first, it would seem like we are faltering. Conversely..."

"If we can take down the strongest among them in one fell swoop, the rest will be nothing to fear. They will be like scattered sand, allowing us to defeat them one by one," Li Fan said with great confidence.

Duke Shou Qiu listened, and it did seem to make sense.

"However, Saint Prying Opportunity is extraordinarily powerful. All beings in the world, and even the destiny of Mountains and Seas, can be stolen by him. To be his enemy is like standing on the opposite side of Mountains and Seas..."

Li Fan snorted coldly, weighing the wooden staff in his hand: "Mountains and Seas are already in such a dire state, unable to save themselves. What if we become his enemy? Will he really dare to oppose us? Duke Shou Qiu, you must know that we are here to save Mountains and Seas."

"In the desperate situation of collapsing Mountains and Seas, opportunities, destinies, and fates are all in chaos. Only by living, by surviving, is truly the only effective measure."

Li Fan gazed into the distance, taking in the chaotic scene of the collapsing Mountains and Seas and the turbulent possibilities, all within his sight.

In such a doomsday scenario, he not only felt no discomfort or sense of crisis.

Instead, he felt unprecedented freedom, as if all the shackles that had been atop his head were removed.

"In the past, when I was in the Xuanhuang Realm, I had the guidance of a teacher."

"Outside the Xuanhuang Realm, I had the Hunger Immortal."

"Beyond the tall walls, there were the Black Heaven Physician and Black Su Bai from beyond the possibilities."

"And after leaping out of the Primordial Chaos, there were the Saints on the Other Shore sitting in command."

"Truly, I felt uneasy everywhere."

"Until now..."

A hint of inexplicable light flickered in Li Fan's eyes.

"The Three Saints. This greatest threat has already died."

"And their treasures are now in my hands."

"Act with impunity, and do as you see fit. Hehehe..."

The reason Li Fan still had no reason to leave with True Return even now was simple and pure.

To kill Saints.

And to do so under the guise of righteousness.

A once-in-a-lifetime opportunity, how could he bear to miss it?

Li Fan had not forgotten the time when he was seen through by the Saints on the Other Shore in the True Return simulation.

"The matter with the Three Saints can be settled later. For now, let's collect some interest from the others."

"Moreover..."

Li Fan's heart stirred, and the True Return panel instantly appeared before his eyes.

"Great Dao Returns to Truth. I wonder if their names can be left in it after killing the Saints on the Other Shore."

Although his thoughts were grand, he still needed to discuss the specific actions carefully.

"Saint Prying Opportunity is extremely cautious. Given his nature, he will likely remain in the background, reaping the benefits." Duke Shou Qiu said solemnly.

"No matter. To conquer an enemy, one must first strike."

Li Fan was confident and secretly transmitted his thoughts.

"This..." Duke Shou Qiu showed hesitation.

"Trust me, Duke Shou Qiu, and we will surely succeed in this battle."

Duke Shou Qiu's expression shifted, and finally, he gritted his teeth and agreed.

*Boom, boom, boom...*

Not long after, enormous explosions sounded from the chaotic currents of Mountains and Seas.

In the collision of light and shadow, countless possibilities that were originally in a state of chaos and disorder instantly turned to dust.

The already precarious Mountains and Seas became even more perilous in an instant.

As if a chain reaction had occurred, large swathes of Mountains and Seas collapsed and fell into Dao Annihilation.

The Void Realm tides surged continuously, as if celebrating their imminent victory.

And a roar, both shocked and enraged, echoed through the heavens: "Good for you, Duke Shou Qiu! I thought you were a man of virtue, but you turned out to be an utter hypocrite!"

"I entrusted my life to you, yet you, like other beasts, covet the treasures in my hands!"

The speaker was none other than Li Fan. At this moment, his face was ashen, and his clothes were tattered, as if he had suffered heavy injuries.

And facing him, Duke Shou Qiu's expression was more gloomy than ever before.

Before Li Fan could continue speaking, he thrust a finger at him.

Amidst the collapsing mountains and seas, Duke Shou Qiu's presence was even more imposing.

He stood motionless, with the turmoil caused by the collapsing Mountains and Seas trampled beneath his feet. Instead, he could subdue and utilize it.

This casual finger thrust seemed to carry the might of collapsing mountains and surging seas.

It was like a thousand-zhang wave crashing down, intending to crush Li Fan completely.

At the critical moment, an iron shovel cleaved through the giant wave, rescuing Li Fan from its grasp.

"Go!"

Li Fan roared.

The Lianshan Staff transformed into a stream of light, enveloping Li Fan and charging directly towards the outside of Mountains and Seas.

He abandoned the collapsing Mountains and Seas and escaped directly.

Duke Shou Qiu naturally would not let the prey he had in hand escape so easily and closely pursued him.

In Mountains and Seas, the other Saints witnessed this bizarre scene and did not easily follow.

But as the two streams of light, one in front and one behind, flew out of Mountains and Seas.

Into the Void Realm, it seemed they would never return. Only then did they break their silence.

"Hmph, I thought Duke Shou Qiu was truly a gentleman of virtue. Turns out he was just wearing a mask to deceive the world."

"This is the common sense of the world. In this world, where are there any true Saints or perfect beings? Even the Three Saints Lianshan are merely bullies who rely on their position!"

"Excellent, excellent. Originally, I had some reservations about Duke Shou Qiu, but now I see he has revealed his true colors. This is more to my liking. Worthy of deep friendship, hahahaha!"

"Duke Shou Qiu's change from before to now is too drastic, be careful of a trap."

"Trap? I don't think so, he's just revealed his true nature!"

"No matter what, Mountains and Seas are about to collapse. This Dao Annihilation is more ferocious than ever before. Our only chance of survival lies in the Three Saints' treasures. We must catch up to that brat..."

"He actually dared to call us beasts."

...

Seemingly unburdened for a long time, the Saints transformed into streams of light and flew towards the direction Li Fan had disappeared.

Without these fierce gods causing trouble, Mountains and Seas temporarily regained their peace.

After all, with countless years of accumulation, it had managed to temporarily stabilize itself amidst the relentless onslaught of Dao Annihilation.

Of course, it was only temporary.

The battle outside the Void Realm would determine its fate.

Chapter 1701: The Void Realm Sets a Killing Trap

In the Void Realm, which flowed towards the "future," the figures of the Three Saints still stood tall.

Therefore, Duke Shou Qiu and Li Fan were heading towards the direction of the "past" Mountains and Seas.

Without the guidance of the Three Saints standing tall, and without the positioning of the phantom images of the Xuanji Ring.

As soon as they entered the Void Realm, everything became chaotic, making it difficult to distinguish between ancient and modern.

It was as if they were in a surging tide, with the danger of being swallowed at any moment.

"A dark and windy night, a time for murder and arson. This place, isolated from the outside world, is perfect for slaying Saints!"

Li Fan entered the Void Realm first.

Although Duke Shou Qiu followed closely behind, the moment he entered the Void Realm, he almost lost his direction.

If Li Fan had not deliberately released the aura of the Lian Shan Staff, Duke Shou Qiu would have had difficulty finding Li Fan.

The two quickly merged and, while the Envious Saints were unaware, they discussed again.

"Although the performance was a bit exaggerated, they should definitely chase after them."

"The plan remains the same, first slay the leader..."

While communicating, they deliberately engaged in combat, releasing bursts of fluctuations to lure the Saints deeper.

"This place should be about right."

"Ahead, it should be the place where the Three Saints perished. Do not proceed further."

As Duke Shou Qiu reminded him, Li Fan gradually sensed the abnormality of the surrounding Void Realm.

The Void Realm should be an absolute void where the foundation of all existence is absent.

But now, under Li Fan's careful observation, he clearly felt "auras" faintly floating and emanating from the surroundings.

Like ice melting into water, like a stone mill turning into sand.

The foundation of the former Three Saints had already vanished, and most of it disappeared. Only a small residue flowed, as evidence of the former existence of the Three Saints.

It was thought that it was originally not so thin, and as the Void Realm encroached, only a faint, almost imperceptible aura remained.

Li Fan tried to collect these residues.

It was a pity that its divine power had already been erased at the level of "Dao," and the truth and reality were completely unmoved.

"Deep in the Void Realm, no matter how big the commotion, it will not affect Mountains and Seas."

"Let's subdue all evils and pay tribute to all Saints here."

The two continued to maintain the fluctuation of combat, while Li Fan quietly handed the Lian Shan Staff and the Gui Hai Shovel to Duke Shou Qiu.

When he sensed the approaching Envious Saints, Li Fan waved the Myriad Beings Cudgel and forced Duke Shou Qiu back.

"Shou Qiu! Why relentlessly pursue me! You have obtained the Lian Shan Staff and Gui Hai Shovel, isn't that enough!"

"Give me a way to live, how about it? I am willing to exchange it with the secrets of the Mountains and Seas' rare fortune. You originally obtained the longevity of Mountains and Seas, and if you can also possess the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas, perhaps you can reproduce the divine might of the Three Saints!"

Li Fan's indignant roar echoed in the Void Realm, following the residue after the Three Saints' demise.

Duke Shou Qiu remained silent.

The Lian Shan Staff and Gui Hai Shovel danced non-stop, as if determined to kill Li Fan.

Although Li Fan was still protected by the Myriad Beings Cudgel, he was ultimately no match for them.

He was hit squarely on his chest and back with a cudgel and a shovel.

The Envious Saints who tracked them saw clearly that Li Fan was severely injured this time, his body shattered, and his true spirit was uncontrollably dissipating, unsettling the Void Realm even more.

But Duke Shou Qiu still did not hold back, appearing determined to kill Li Fan.

"I didn't expect Shou Qiu, who has always been known for his benevolence, to be so fierce in reality." The Envious Saints who witnessed this scene were all surprised.

"It seems Shou Qiu is afraid that the boy will escape, and his true form will be known by the other Three Saints of Mountains and Seas. That's why he's doing this." Xingcha judged.

"We must not let him take all the benefits!"

Before Xingcha finished speaking, he transformed into a beam of starlight, enveloping Duke Shou Qiu and Li Fan.

Duke Shou Qiu, like the Lian Shan and Gui Hai Saints, holding a bamboo staff and an iron shovel, easily scattered the surrounding starlight.

In the Void Realm, it seemed as if phantom images of Mountains and Seas were rising, howling incessantly.

And Duke Shou Qiu stood on the Mountains and Seas, confronting the Saints who had arrived later.

Taking advantage of this rare opportunity, Li Fan, who was already in a near-death state, suddenly unleashed his final strength.

He threw the Myriad Beings Cudgel upwards.

In an instant, it transformed into two, then four, then eight.

Endless phantom images of stone clubs fell upon the heads of all the Saints.

Everyone present, without exception, was hit by this blow.

However, from the power contained in this blow, all the Saints knew that Li Fan was definitely at the end of his rope.

Even the Myriad Beings Cudgel, a treasure of slaughter, seemed light and frivolous when he wielded it.

It had the appearance, but no real threat.

The Saints looked and saw that, as expected, Li Fan's true spirit was further shattered, like a flickering candle flame, about to extinguish at any moment.

He no longer cared about the Myriad Beings Cudgel, supporting his broken body, he fled rapidly.

"The true spirit is completely shattered, where can he escape to? He will probably die in the Void Realm."

"He thought that by taking the Three Saints' treasures, he could turn the tide and command us? He's too young."

"The Three Saints themselves dared not come, but they sent this boy to test and die. Indeed, there is no morality in Mountains and Seas."

...

The dying had no need for the Saints to pursue.

Instead, they turned their attention to the ownerless Myriad Beings Cudgel in the field, and Duke Shou Qiu, who possessed two treasures.

Following the combat just now, the residue of the Three Saints' demise was about to completely dissipate.

The Void Realm would reveal its true ferocious fangs.

"Brother Shou Qiu, we have been brothers in the Xuanji Ring for who knows how many tens of thousands of years. It's not very good for you to swallow the supreme treasure alone." Ye Pan said slowly.

"If I kill all of you, then there will be no problem." Duke Shou Qiu replied indifferently.

Ye Pan was slightly stunned, then laughed angrily: "Good, good, good. I'd like to see what abilities the virtuous Duke Shou Qiu, who has been hiding his true face for so long, really has!"

Gui Ming, Jian Ji, Ye Pan, Xing Cha, four Saints slowly revealed their figures.

Surrounding Duke Shou Qiu in the center.

Duke Shou Qiu scanned the Saints present, his expression freezing like ice.

But a flicker of fluctuation flashed deep in his heart.

"Not good!"

It wasn't worry for his own safety.

But unexpectedly, two Saints had disappeared simultaneously.

Jian Ji, and...

Sui Jun.

During his previous exchange with Li Fan, Duke Shou Qiu had learned that Sui Jun did not exist in the *next* segment of Mountains and Seas.

Because in that period of forty thousand continuous years, which had now been swallowed by the Void Realm, he had perished due to some reason.

The original plan was for Li Fan to abandon all three Saints' treasures, and only escape with his broken body.

The Saints present should have only been interested in Jian Ji, continuing to pursue Li Fan.

But he never expected that Sui Jun would also ignore the Three Saints' treasures and chase after Li Fan!

"He said there were other Three Saints' treasures that could deal with Jian Ji."

"But if we add one more Saint..."

Duke Shou Qiu's heart sank.

But now he had no good solution, he could only try his best to stall the Saints present.

...

Deeper in the Void Realm.

Where the residue of the Three Saints completely disappeared, a figure rapidly fled.

It seemed impossible to distinguish direction, and the target was not any ancient or modern Mountains and Seas. Instead, it darted about in the Void Realm like a headless fly.

Initially, he could still move by relying on the last burst of power.

But gradually, perhaps due to his bad luck. Wherever he passed, the Void Realm tides were noticeably stronger. The wind and waves blocked him, and Li Fan's aura became weaker and weaker, until he could no longer escape.

He stopped.

The Void Realm tides surged, as if they would swallow him completely in the next moment.

Li Fan's face was ashen, but he still did not give up hope of survival. He sat cross-legged in the Void Realm, trying his best to recover from his injuries.

But his luck seemed to have declined to the extreme.

The more he tried to heal his luck, the worse his injuries became. He suddenly spat out a mouthful of

blood, accompanied by a large amount of dissipating true spirit. He seemed truly close to death.

"Heh heh. All thanks to Jian Ji."

Li Fan muttered to himself, looking around.

He had practiced the Heavenly Luck Sutra before, and even devoured a remnant of the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas. He could now clearly feel the loss of his own luck.

Not just luck.

It was the relentless shattering of the countless possible futures that represented his future life.

As the saying goes, when the heavens block all paths, there is always a glimmer of hope.

But now, under Jian Ji's pressure, Li Fan, from any aspect, seemed to have reached a dead end.

Nowhere to go!

With a bitter smile, he seemed to accept his fate and gave up struggling.

No longer resisting, he let the surrounding Dao annihilation swallow him.

His body slowly dissipated, and his true spirit dissolved like melting snow.

At this moment, a mysterious force protected Li Fan, who was about to disintegrate.

"Tell me where the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas is, and I will save your life, how about it?" A faint, illusory voice sounded in Li Fan's ear.

Li Fan ignored it, acting as if he hadn't heard it.

Until Jian Ji's words, like a demonic sound, echoed continuously, as if he wouldn't give up until Li Fan answered.

Li Fan snorted lightly and shook his head slightly: "Do you believe me if I tell you? It was just a pretense to deceive Shou Qiu."

Jian Ji chuckled: "I have been searching for the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas for many years. If I can't even sense its scent, then I am unworthy of the name Jian Ji."

"The scent is truly nostalgic..." Jian Ji deeply inhaled and sighed with emotion.

"Say it again. Tell me about the news of the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas, and I will spare your life. I, never go back on my word." Jian Ji said proudly.

"If you kill me, or if you find it from my mind, isn't it the same?" Li Fan retorted.

Jian Ji heard this and fell into silence.

He seemed to be considering Li Fan's suggestion.

But then, he shook his head and denied it.

Even involuntarily, he moved a little further away from Li Fan.

The illusions surrounded Li Fan, and facing this dying person, he still examined him cautiously: "No, no, no. I can sense that although you appear to be at your wit's end, there is still a sliver of life.

"And this sliver of life..."

"Corresponds to my dead end!"

"It's definitely correct."

Jian Ji muttered to himself, suspicious and looking around.

But he could never figure it out.

"I know you must have a contingency plan."

"Although the play with Duke Shou Qiu was brilliant, it couldn't fool the fate and fortune."

"The seemingly weak fate, in reality, has the opportunity to counter-kill at any time. Those fools, caught in the game, are still unaware."

"However... as long as I stay out of it, you can't hurt me."

Jian Ji's voice was like a ghost, coming from all directions.

Making Li Fan unable to determine his exact location.

Thus, he believed Duke Shou Qiu's words. This Saint Jian Ji was indeed extremely cautious.

Coupled with his Dao that could pry into the fate and fortune of all beings, it was truly difficult to scheme against him!

"Fine!" Li Fan sighed deeply, "Although the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas is my close friend. But ultimately, it's not as important as my own life."

"He transformed twice to avoid covetousness, becoming an ordinary person and hiding in the mortal world of Mountains and Seas. But after all, he is the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas, and he cannot truly be buried like an ordinary person. Even though he knows nothing of his past, relying on his purely mortal background, he ascended to immortality in the Age of Dharma Decline. However, when he returned to Mountains and Seas, he was discovered by his adversary..."

"Speaking of which, is the existence that has been chasing him you?" Li Fan asked suspiciously.

Jian Ji shook his head and denied: "I was trapped in the Xuanji Ring before and was unable to act. With the divine nature of the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas, many people are envious. I am just one of them."

Li Fan continued: "At a critical moment, a Mountains and Seas Angler appeared and rescued him, drawing him out of Mountains and Seas and avoiding the calamity. This... is what happened in our segment of Mountains and Seas. As for this segment of Mountains and Seas, I have only just arrived and do not know."

"Mountains and Seas Angler? As expected, he is blessed with immense luck."

Jian Ji looked back in the direction of Mountains and Seas, pondered for a moment. Then, as if talking to himself, "After the Three Saints perished, I searched the shattered Mountains and Seas in secret long ago, but I couldn't find the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas."

"He should have sensed his other self's fortune and gone there as well. Only the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas, under the condition of being isolated from all senses by the Void Realm, could act according to its instincts."

With the answer to his question obtained, Jian Ji lost interest in Li Fan.

He immediately withdrew his protective power and gracefully fled.

The gravely injured Li Fan exclaimed in shock: "You said you would save my life, what about it?"

Jian Ji chuckled: "Didn't I save you just now? I said I never go back on my word."

"However..."

"Saving you for a moment is not the same as saving you for a lifetime. Whether you can survive in this storm of the Void Realm depends on your own fortune."

Jian Ji's voice faded away.

Li Fan's panicked expression suddenly calmed down.

"Then there's nothing we can do."

"I hope you can really find the rare fortune of Mountains and Seas."

"Hmm? What do you mean by that?" Jian Ji's voice suddenly drew closer.

"Just a sincere blessing." Li Fan said with a smile.

As soon as these words were spoken, Li Fan could feel Jian Ji's gaze fixated on him as if it had solidified.

"Trying to trick me. Heh heh..."

Then, ignoring the procrastinating Li Fan, he gracefully fled.

Li Fan did not stop him, but took a deep breath.

In the Void Realm, as if something had been triggered. After a moment, Li Fan's shattered true spirit actually began to recover at a visible speed!

So Jian Ji returned.

"This is..."

Li Fan completely ignored the other party and focused on absorbing the accumulated true spirit and recovering from his injuries.

The Dao annihilation tide surged, as if lurking like a tiger, threatening to swallow Li Fan at any moment.

As he absorbed more and more true spirit, Li Fan's complexion gradually became ruddy. His aura recovered its former strength, nearing its peak.

At this moment...

A powerful force suddenly descended upon Li Fan's surroundings.

It was not simply weight, but the crystallization of time, rushing and flowing!

Saints were not immortal, they merely lived for a very long time.

But under such terrifying acceleration of time, Li Fan, the Saint of the Cycle of Eons, was also tainted with a trace of old age in an instant.

Even if he desperately circulated the Dao of the Cycle of Eons, dividing the incoming long years through endless reincarnation.

But this instant flow of time, with billions of years, could even annihilate reincarnation.

In the battle, being at a disadvantage, Li Fan inevitably became more and more frail.

"Sui Jun the Saint? He came too?"

Sui Jun's appearance was indeed unexpected for Li Fan.

Although he appeared disheveled on the surface, he had not yet reached his limit. More importantly, Li Fan was certain that Jian Ji had not gone far, but was hiding in the dark, waiting to reap the benefits of others' hard work.

"Discerning fate and fortune, this person is truly hard to scheme against."

"Perhaps only when I am truly in a desperate situation, using myself as bait, can I lure him in."

A flash of enlightenment crossed Li Fan's mind.

He no longer diverted any attention to Huán Zhēn, as if he had forgotten his ability to restart at any time.

Instead, he resolutely engaged in combat with the suddenly attacking Sui Jun.

When Li Fan came to this Mountains and Seas, although Sui Jun was not present.

But Li Fan had heard about his deeds from the Saints' conversations.
