He embraced all time and returned it to himself, then "lent" it to the beings of Mountains and Seas, calling it "Jun."

The countless possibilities and endless beings of Mountains and Seas, although they inexplicably gained seemingly inexhaustible lifespans.

But this was not what they desired, but was forcibly imposed upon them.

In the endless life ahead, beings had to work diligently their entire lives to repay their debt of time.

Even if they couldn't help Sui Jun in their cultivation, their thoughts, words, actions, and even themselves were valuable.

Sui Jun comprehended the Dao through the beings of Mountains and Seas, and his strength was definitely not weak.

The pressure Li Fan felt at this moment was evident.

As if he had vaguely experienced several complete life cycles of Mountains and Seas, a trace of paleness slowly crept onto Li Fan's hair.

It had been a long time since he had tasted aging, and now, under the pressure of endless time, Li Fan was helpless and gradually became senile!

What followed was a worsening situation.

The older he got, the weaker he became. The protective effect of the endless reincarnation of time became increasingly negligible.

Li Fan's body became completely hunched, curled up.

His hair turned completely white, then withered and fell off.

His flesh and skin shriveled, hanging loosely on his fragile, aging bones.

In a short while, Li Fan transformed from a graceful young man into a dying old man!

And Sui Jun, as if only here to kill Li Fan, showed no mercy until this moment.

The endless torrent of time continued to roar and surge, determined to crush Li Fan.

Far away, Jian Ji, who was hiding and watching secretly, hesitated for a moment, and ultimately chose not to intervene.

He was confident that Li Fan still had a trump card and would not die just like this.

"Although it seems like a dead end, there is always a way out. On the contrary, Sui Jun, although he has been suppressing from beginning to end..."

"His fierce aspect is fully revealed."

What happened next in the Void Realm confirmed Jian Ji's guess.

As if at the end of one's rope, when one encounters a new beginning.

Li Fan, who had been sitting with his eyes closed, on the verge of death, suddenly opened his turbid eyes.

He opened his mouth slightly and said something.

The next moment...

As if a fantasy, it shattered with a bang.

What about senility, what about the appearance of near death. All vanished.

For no reason, Li Fan, who had been near death, returned to his initial state. With a calm and relaxed expression, as if Sui Jun's billions of years of torment had been completely useless!

"What?"

Sui Jun's surprise was evident.

The surging torrent of time also paused because of this.

But Saint Sui Jun was not one to give up easily, and only paused for a moment.

The next moment, endless time surged towards Li Fan again.

From youth to old age, from old age to decay.

Li Fan went through this process again.

But...

Just like before. When Li Fan was on the verge of death, a flash of light appeared, as if nothing had happened, and his condition returned to the starting point of the battle.

Causing Sui Jun's every effort to be in vain.

This time, the period of stagnation caused by the suppression of time was even longer.

But Sui Jun did not give up.

Time roared, and the speed at which it flowed over Li Fan increased.

In just a few breaths, Li Fan became extremely old.

But the story repeated itself.

With a flash of light, Li Fan returned to his original state!

Sui Jun seemed to be utterly enraged, constantly increasing the power of time's torment.

The flow of time reached a certain limit, even attracting the attention of the Void Realm tides.

As if something in the depths of darkness was about to open its eyes.

With every breath, Li Fan repeatedly switched between youth and old age dozens of times.

But in the end, he always returned to his original form.

In this battle, Li Fan remained calm and composed.

Conversely, Sui Jun gradually panicked.

He considered himself knowledgeable, but he had never seen such a bizarre event.

Even during the battle with the Three Saints, the Three Saints crushed him with their absolute power gap.

But at that time, they couldn't make him ignore the passage of time like Li Fan.

He had truly experienced a portion of the passage of time.

However, the Three Saints were too powerful and quickly suppressed him.

And those lost years were almost negligible to them.

"How did this person manage to ignore my divine ability?"

For the unknown, even Saints cannot help but feel fear and curiosity.

At this moment, the situation in the field had quietly changed.

When Saints battle, it's either the east wind prevails over the west wind, or the west wind prevails over the east wind.

As time's torment gradually showed signs of fatigue,

It was Li Fan's turn to counterattack.

Li Fan, who had been trapped in the endless cycle of reincarnation, broke free from the torrent of time.

With fierce eyes, he inflicted the repeated cycles of aging he had experienced onto Sui Jun!

Previously, endless reincarnation could not resist the impact of time, but now, various cycles formed shackles.

Trapping the long passage of time within them.

Even though Sui Jun had the power to control the flow of time, he could not escape the carefully woven cage of reincarnation that Li Fan had created for him.

And with each aging, Sui Jun was far less calm than Li Fan appeared.

Each near-death aging was a heavy blow to him.

Because he could not predict when death would truly come.

Physically and mentally, he suffered endless torment.

After a long battle, Sui Jun finally lost his composure.

Fear gradually crept onto his face, and he no longer thought about fighting Li Fan.

Instead, he tried to escape from this endless cage of reincarnation.

Even though Li Fan had gained an absolute advantage, it had to be said that killing a Saint was by no means easy.

As Sui Jun frantically counterattacked, the cage of reincarnation woven by Li Fan was constantly subjected to violent impacts.

It seemed on the verge of collapse.

Li Fan, however, had a determined expression and fierce eyes: "I must kill you!"

Ignoring everything else, he exhausted his own origin, reinforcing the cage of reincarnation.

The injuries he had just recovered from worsened due to the excessive use of power.

His body began to disintegrate, and his true spirit once again drifted outwards.

But Li Fan paid no heed, continuing to weave reincarnation while absorbing scattered true spirits from the surrounding Void Realm.

He was actually trying to kill Saint Sui Jun here!

At this moment, the situation had changed from a simple battle to a fight to the death.

Sui Jun did not beg for mercy, and even the fear on his face disappeared.

In the endlessly aging reincarnation, he silently accumulated strength, attempting to make a final desperate effort.

And Li Fan sensed the approaching storm, his expression becoming increasingly serious.

...

"The struggle for the Great Dao should be like this!" Saint Jian Ji, who was watching from afar, was extremely excited.

The changes in the fate and fortune of the two Saints fighting in the field fascinated him.

Even at this point, it was still uncertain who would be the Saint victorious in this battle between Li Fan and Sui Jun.

"Originally, Sui Jun was in a desperate situation. But as the saying goes, when one is in a dead end, one finds a way out. Now that Sui Jun has nowhere to escape and has forgotten everything, and is fighting desperately, the chance of survival for Zhou Hui has actually become slim. Wonderful, wonderful!"

Jian Ji watched and observed, not forgetting to use his divine abilities to steal the fate and fortune from the two Saints.

"All possible destinies belong to me."

"You all deserve to die!"

Jian Ji finally saw that the sliver of life force that had always surrounded Li Fan like a protective charm was gradually dimming.

And his own corresponding apocalyptic future had disappeared.

Jian Ji rejoiced in his heart but still did not choose to intervene, waiting for the outcome of the deadly battle.

Li Fan did not expect Sui Jun's final counterattack to be so ferocious.

His own Dao foundation was shattered inch by inch, and Sui Jun's figure seemed to melt into the billions of years of time's flow, launching a final impact on the cage of reincarnation.

Li Fan could not see Sui Jun's trace.

But he knew that if even a single wisp of this flow of time managed to escape, all his previous efforts would be in vain.

At this moment, Li Fan had forgotten all his schemes.

His mind had only one thought.

He must kill Sui Jun here!

Separate from grudges, separate from emotions.

It was a matter of life and death at the crucial juncture of battle!

To ensure that the cage of reincarnation could withstand this final impact, Li Fan divided himself into countless thoughts, all pouring into all the cycles.

Thus, beside Sui Jun's aging figure in every reincarnation, there was Li Fan silently watching.

Omnipresent, to the extreme.

No matter how Sui Jun's powerful torrent of billions of years impacted, the cage Li Fan constructed remained indestructible.

Not retreating an inch.

The momentum of the counterattack, strong to the extreme, eventually weakened.

When the greatest storm passed, Sui Jun's final blow became weaker and weaker.

The residual waves, ultimately, could no longer stir up any trouble.

In countless cycles, Li Fan's figure appeared before the Sui Jun he was guarding.

With a blank expression, he struck with a palm.

*Bang!*

In an instant, billions of Sui Jun phantoms shattered simultaneously.

And in reality, it was the fall of a Saint!

The fall of a Saint, if it happened in Mountains and Seas, would undoubtedly cause earth-shattering changes.

But this was the Void Realm!

Even when the Three Saints perished here, they did not cause much of a stir.

Sui Jun died so silently, without a ripple.

Not even the fluctuations of his own Dao dispersed.

And Li Fan, the victor, was not much better off.

He had exhausted himself in his desperate struggle.

Blood flowed uncontrollably from the corner of his mouth, and the true spirit he had forcibly absorbed also returned to the Void Realm uncontrollably.

There was no excitement of having won a great battle and slain a Saint on his face, but instead, with a worried expression, regardless of his own injuries.

He hurriedly tried to escape this place.

Even though the Void Realm tides were surging more fiercely, he could not afford to care.

In the distance, Jian Ji, who had been waiting for a long time, was still observing.

"The true spirit is shattered to this extent, even with the ability to absorb accumulated true spirits, it is a certain death situation."

"Now that I am the fisherman, it is foolproof!"

Jian Ji finally felt at ease.

He had already begun to plan how to use Li Fan.

"I don't know what kind of method he used to return to normal from Sui Jun's hands just now. But it doesn't matter, once I refine him into a divine artifact, everything will be at my disposal."

"With this treasure, this dangerous Void Realm will become an inexhaustible treasure trove for me! Even the Three Saints will no longer be able to trap me!"

"Moreover, I might even have a chance to glimpse the beginning of Mountains and Seas..."

Lost in his thoughts, Jian Ji had already caught up with Li Fan.

After all, he was severely injured, and even with his efforts to escape, he was no match for Jian Ji's speed.

"I wonder if he was just pretending to be weak against Duke Shou Qiu. But it doesn't matter, I will refine him into a treasure."

Without further ado, Jian Ji placed his hands on Li Fan's head.

At this very moment, Li Fan, who had been unable to move, suddenly opened his eyes.

In an instant, the fate and fortune of both parties, intertwined, were completely reversed!

Chapter 1702: The Three Sages Fight

Saint Prying Opportunity, who had initially decided to distance himself from Li Fan and cease all involvement, could not help but cast his gaze back upon witnessing Li Fan absorbing the accumulated nascent spirits in the Void Realm.

"I knew there had to be a reason why the Three Saints entrusted this burden to you. So, you possess such a miraculous ability."

After observing for a moment and confirming he wasn't mistaken, Prying Opportunity finally understood. His expression towards Li Fan also became somewhat nuanced.

"It's not entirely without merit," Prying Opportunity mused inwardly. Saints were not inherently immortal; they could still be wounded or perish. In the past, Prying Opportunity had been injured several times during his efforts to reconnect the Mountains and Seas. Once, his nascent spirit had even been harmed. Such injuries were resistant to ordinary methods of healing; recovery only came through lengthy periods of self-restoration or with the aid of the Saintly Fortune Pills refined by Emperor Tai Wei.

"But if... if an external force could constantly replenish the nascent spirit..." Saint Prying Opportunity's heart stirred, as if envisioning a living, inexhaustible elixir.

"However..." Prying Opportunity was not blinded by the superficial benefits. "This brat deliberately lured me here, he must have something he relies on. Moreover, I've observed that our intertwined destinies remain unchanged; his life force and my desperate situation are linked."

After contemplating for a while, Prying Opportunity, without revealing his thoughts, glanced at Sui Jun, who was hiding nearby, and a plan formed in his mind.

"If the Three Saints were still here, they would certainly not have let you die in the Void Realm like this. Unfortunately..." Prying Opportunity chuckled lightly and suddenly vanished, seemingly disappearing into the Void Realm.

Li Fan, ignoring him, focused on absorbing the nascent spirits and recovering from his injuries. Only the tides of Dao Annihilation surged, circling him like a lurking tiger, threatening to swallow him at any moment.

The injuries he had just recovered from worsened due to the excessive exertion of power. His body began to disintegrate, and his nascent spirit once again drifted outwards. But Li Fan paid no heed, continuing to weave reincarnation while absorbing scattered nascent spirits from the surrounding Void Realm. He was actually attempting to kill Saint Sui Jun right here! At this juncture, the situation had escalated from a simple battle to a fight to the death. Sui Jun did not beg for mercy, and even the fear on his face had vanished. Within the endlessly aging reincarnation, he silently accumulated strength, attempting a final desperate gamble. And Li Fan sensed the approaching storm, his expression growing increasingly serious.

...

"The struggle for the Great Dao should be like this!" Saint Prying Opportunity, observing from afar, was incredibly excited. The fluctuations in the destinies and fortunes of the two Saints battling in the field utterly captivated him. Even at this point, it was still uncertain who would emerge victorious in this battle between Li Fan and Sui Jun. "Originally, Sui Jun was in a desperate situation. But as the saying goes, when one is trapped in dire straits, they find a way out. Now that Sui Jun has nowhere to escape, has forgotten everything, and is fighting desperately, Zhou Hui's (Li Fan's) chances of survival have actually become slim. Wonderful, wonderful!" Prying Opportunity watched and observed, not forgetting to use his divine abilities to steal the fate and fortune from both Saints. "All possible destinies belong to me." "You all deserve to die!" Prying Opportunity finally saw that the sliver of life force that had always surrounded Li Fan like a protective charm was gradually dimming. And his own corresponding apocalyptic future had disappeared. Prying Opportunity rejoiced inwardly but still chose not to intervene, waiting for the outcome of the deadly battle. Li Fan had not expected Sui Jun's final counterattack to be so ferocious. His own Dao foundation was shattering inch by inch, and Sui Jun's figure seemed to melt into the flow of billions of years of time, launching a final assault on the cage of reincarnation. Li Fan could not see Sui Jun's trace. But he knew that if even a single wisp of this time flow managed to escape, all his previous efforts would be in vain. At this moment, Li Fan had forgotten all his schemes. His mind held only one thought: He must kill Sui Jun here! Separate from grudges and emotions. It was a matter of life and death at this critical juncture of the battle! To ensure the cage of reincarnation could withstand this final impact, Li Fan divided his consciousness into countless thoughts, all pouring into every cycle. Thus, beside Sui Jun's aging figure in every reincarnation, there was Li Fan silently watching. Omnipresent, to the extreme. No matter how Sui Jun's powerful torrent of billions of years impacted, the cage Li Fan constructed remained indestructible, not retreating an inch. The momentum of the counterattack, which was extreme, eventually weakened. When the greatest storm passed, Sui Jun's final blow became weaker and weaker. The residual waves, ultimately, could no longer stir up any trouble. In countless cycles, Li Fan's figure appeared before the Sui Jun he was guarding. With a blank expression, he struck with his palm. *Bang!* In an instant, billions of Sui Jun phantoms shattered simultaneously. And in reality, it was the fall of a Saint! The fall of a Saint, if it happened in Mountains and Seas, would undoubtedly cause earth-shattering changes. But this was the Void Realm! Even when the Three Saints perished here, they did not cause much of a stir. Sui Jun died so silently, without a ripple. Not even the fluctuations of his own Dao dispersed. And Li Fan, the victor, was not much better off. He had exhausted himself in his desperate struggle. Blood flowed uncontrollably from the corner of his mouth, and the nascent spirit he had forcibly absorbed also returned to the Void Realm uncontrollably. There was no excitement of having won a great battle and slain a Saint on his face, but instead, with a worried expression, regardless of his own injuries, he hurriedly tried to escape this place. Even as the Void Realm tides surged more fiercely, he could not afford to care. Far away, Prying Opportunity, who had been waiting for a long time, was still observing. "The nascent spirit is shattered to this extent; even with the ability to absorb accumulated nascent spirits, it's a certain death situation." "Now that I am the fisherman, it's foolproof!" Prying Opportunity finally felt at ease. He had already begun planning how to use Li Fan. "I don't know what method he used to return to normal from Sui Jun's hands just now. But it doesn't matter; once I refine him into a divine artifact, everything will be at my disposal." "With this treasure, this dangerous Void Realm will become an inexhaustible treasure trove for me! Even the Three Saints will no longer be able to trap me!" "Moreover, I might even have a chance to glimpse the beginning of Mountains and Seas..." Lost in his thoughts, Prying Opportunity had already caught up with Li Fan. After all, he was severely injured, and even with his efforts to escape, he was no match for Prying Opportunity's speed. "I wonder if he was just pretending to be weak against Duke Shou Qiu. But it doesn't matter; I will refine him into a treasure." Without further ado, Prying Opportunity placed his hands on Li Fan's head. At this very moment, Li Fan, who had been unable to move, suddenly opened his eyes. In an instant, the fates and fortunes of both parties, intertwined, were completely reversed!

Chapter 1703: Stealing the Opportunity and Recapturing the Truth

Though he was the one to play the hunter, appearing leisurely from the shadows, he now found himself on the brink of death, his life force utterly depleted, his future a dead end.

Meanwhile, Li Fan, whom he had considered a surefire prize, had inexplicably reversed the situation, now standing as the hunter. His aura was unfathomable, posing no threat to Li Fan's life.

All these changes occurred with such astonishing speed and incredulity.

Even witnessing it firsthand, Prying Opportunity was momentarily stunned.

He simply couldn't comprehend how Li Fan, who appeared near death, could possibly stage such a comeback.

But it didn't matter; Li Fan would soon reveal the answer.

"When truth becomes falsehood..."

"Falsehood too becomes truth."

A serene, ethereal chant, possessing a magical resonance that seemed to pierce through the void, suddenly echoed in Prying Opportunity's ears.

Though Prying Opportunity failed to grasp its full meaning, he instinctively recognized its extraordinary nature.

His heart tightened, and he desperately attempted to suppress Li Fan.

But...

Li Fan suddenly extended his hands, instantly locking Prying Opportunity in place, rendering him immobile.

"What?!"

Prying Opportunity was horrified to realize that his opponent's apparent grave injuries were merely a facade!

In fact, the power erupting from the Cycle of Eons was no less than his own.

Their forces clashed, locked in a stalemate.

"Could it be that the Cycle of Eons was hiding its strength all along?" Prying Opportunity's heart flashed with disbelief and anger.

But then, something even more terrifying occurred.

As he belatedly realized, it wasn't that Li Fan had concealed his cultivation. It was...

He himself had become weaker.

In an instant, a significant portion of his strength vanished, reducing him to the cultivation level of a newly promoted Saint.

How could such an absurd and bizarre event unfold in the world?

Fear began to fester in Prying Opportunity's heart, but he quickly suppressed it, desperately seeking a way out amidst the impossible.

He recalled the phrase Li Fan had just chanted.

"When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood too becomes truth..."

Abruptly, Prying Opportunity's body trembled slightly.

Recalling the previous confrontation between the Cycle of Eons and Sui Jun, he suddenly understood.

"It appears that not only have all the negative effects of the passage of time vanished, rendering them completely ineffective. In reality, it's about recreating a new self upon a decaying body. In a single thought, from falsehood to truth. Even Sui Jun's power, which even the Saints would fear, ultimately has its limitations."

"How could it possibly contend with this endless creation?"

"This is the transformation of 'Falsehood Becomes Truth'! And now..."

"My Saintly realm, cultivation, power, fortune, the accumulation of countless years, all lost in an instant. Such incredulity, such an unreasonable turn of events..."

"Truth Becomes Falsehood!"

From the very beginning, there was no Saint of the Cycle of Eons, but rather a Saint of 'Truth and Falsehood.'

Engaged in their struggle, Prying Opportunity, having grasped the profound mystery, felt not despair but an unprecedented brilliance surged in his eyes. His heart pounded with an intensity it hadn't felt in ages.

He truly saw a glimmer of hope for his survival!

"The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. I never imagined such an inconceivable Dao existed in Mountains and Seas."

"That ancient legend was actually true."

"Even in the face of certain death, there lies great opportunity. Even if 'Truth and Falsehood' is your path, I may still seize it!"

A greedy, murderous intent, like a blazing fire, burned in his eyes.

Prying Opportunity exhaled deeply, and instantly, myriad rays of light scattered from his body.

These were the accumulations of fortune he had gathered over countless years, from mortals, true immortals, and even Saints of Mountains and Seas.

It was precisely this foundation that had forged his formidable reputation.

But now, he cast it all aside!

He was making a final, desperate gamble, using the pure principle of 'prying' to seize the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood from his opponent.

"If I obtain Truth and Falsehood..."

"Then I shall obtain Mountains and Seas!"

The myriad fortunes, now free, scattered like dragons soaring through the sky, stirring up turmoil in the void.

And with the loss of all his accumulated fortunes, Prying Opportunity's power naturally declined further.

But...

Because of this, he could now fully employ the entirety of the 'Prying' Great Dao, to claim the transformation of Truth and Falsehood before him!

*Boom boom boom!*

"When falsehood becomes truth..."

As Li Fan chanted again, he suddenly felt a tremor in his soul.

It was as if something cold and intangible had forcefully inserted itself into his consciousness!

And it was attempting to violently tear itself outwards!

*Hum hum hum...*

A faint, sharp ringing began to sound, escalating into thunderous booms that exploded in Li Fan's heart!

Before Li Fan's eyes, a radiant screen materialized, then blurred and shook.

Intolerable pain radiated from every part of his body and soul.

Like countless needle pricks and knife cuts, indescribable by any earthly language.

The agony Li Fan was experiencing at this moment was beyond words.

Distracted, his casting of the "Falsehood Becomes Truth" transformation was interrupted!

Sensing that his act of prying was effective, Prying Opportunity's spirit jolted, seizing the moment.

He even ignited the very origin of the 'Prying' Great Dao, burning it away.

This was a move of "win or perish." Once the origin of Prying fled, it could not be stopped. Even if Li Fan managed to disrupt the weakening effect of "Falsehood Becomes Truth," Prying Opportunity would eventually devolve into a mere mortal, devoid of any cultivation, as his origin slowly dissipated.

But at this moment, Prying Opportunity showed no hesitation!

"Even if my 'prying' is extinguished, as long as I can seize the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, I can instantly turn the tables."

With this conviction, flames erupted from Prying Opportunity's body.

The invisible hand that had intruded into Li Fan's divine soul stirred with increasing intensity.

It was determined to find the trace of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood!

Extreme pain gave rise to rage, and rage to malice.

As Li Fan gradually adapted to the pain of 'prying,' he reorganized his thoughts.

"Falsehood... Becomes... Truth..."

He gritted his teeth and once again unleashed the transformation of Truth and Falsehood.

Fortunately, after years of reincarnation, the casting of "Truth and Falsehood" had become an ingrained instinct.

Though his consciousness was blurry, he could still perform it smoothly.

Another carving knife seemed to descend from above.

But perhaps because Prying Opportunity was already burning his origin and his realm was in decline, the effect this time was far less potent than the first.

Before him, the flames still burned brightly, almost blinding Li Fan.

"Almost... almost found it."

Prying Opportunity's senses were always keen, especially for treasures.

And the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was undoubtedly among the highest-tier treasures in Mountains and Seas.

"Legend has it that the Creator God, in His near-death state, left behind three contingency plans."

"Each possesses the power to overturn Mountains and Seas."

"After the Creator God perished, Mountains and Seas evolved independently, but these three contingency plans were never found."

"Until the advent of Dao Annihilation, heralding the arrival of the Star."

"The Creator God divided His power, the Star devoured Mountains and Seas. This is one of them."

"And this Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood before me..."

ωωω ..c ○

The closer he got, the more Prying Opportunity could sense its essence.

"Containing the foundation of all things, fostering the changes between reality and illusion, upholding the balance of all wonders..."

"It is like the lingering will of the Creator God, capable of shattering Mountains and Seas, and stabilizing the illusory Star..."

Even from afar, Prying Opportunity could perceive the immense profundity of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood.

Despite being engulfed in flames, his body trembled with excessive excitement.

As one of the foremost powerhouses in Mountains and Seas, Prying Opportunity had never imagined he would experience the sentiment of "hearing the Dao in the morning and dying contentedly in the evening."

Two tears suddenly streamed down his face, quickly dissipating into the flames of his origin.

Then, a greater greed surged in his heart.

"Such a wondrous item must be claimed as my own!"

Prying Opportunity went completely mad, leaving nothing behind. He ignited all his remaining essence, including his thoughts, desires, feelings, and even his body and soul.

All became bargaining chips for this desperate struggle.

Towards the location of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood he sensed, he struggled to grasp it!

*Boom!!*

An unprecedented tremor shook Li Fan's soul.

Li Fan's face registered horror, while Prying Opportunity was ecstatic.

"Found it!"

Disregarding everything else, Prying Opportunity, with only a wisp of his remaining essence after burning his origin, used his last ounce of strength.

He intended to rip the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood from Li Fan's body and claim it as his own.

But...

Prying Opportunity's expression slowly froze.

The intense brilliance in his eyes instantly dimmed.

Though he had touched the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, it remained unmoving.

"How... how could this be?"

Prying Opportunity stared blankly, in disbelief and incomprehension, and tried to exert himself again.

The result was still the same.

A third attempt yielded no different outcome.

Prying Opportunity finally resigned himself.

Because of his misjudgment, his life was nearing its end.

But his expression gradually calmed.

"To witness such a divine object before my death is enough to assuage my regrets."

"It is a pity, however..."

"That I cannot claim it as my own!"

He gently touched it one last time, but ultimately felt nothing.

Within Li Fan's body, normalcy was restored. The previously blurred screen of True Return became clear once more.

And Saint Prying Opportunity, amidst the roaring flames, turned into ashes!

Li Fan gently shook his head, trying to expel the alien sensation from his mind.

Looking at the flames of the Great Dao origin before him, he felt a sense of relief at having narrowly escaped death.

He truly hadn't anticipated that Saint Prying Opportunity's strength would be so terrifying.

Not only could he endure the "Falsehood Becomes Truth" transformation for so long, but he could even attempt to strip away Zhen Huan from his own body!

Though he ultimately failed, it still left Li Fan with lingering fear.

"I was perhaps too overconfident."

"The 'Truth and Falsehood' transformation is invincible against opponents below the Saint realm. In an instant, it can strip away the opponent's true spirit and turn them into mortals. But against a Saint of Mountains and Seas..."

"Their accumulation over countless years in Mountains and Seas is too vast. Even if they are unable to escape the influence of 'Truth and Falsehood,' they can still endure for a period. In a battle between Saints, during this time, anything can happen."

Li Fan took a deep breath.

If Saint Prying Opportunity was already like this, then, undoubtedly, the Three Saints Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi, who were even stronger, would be far more formidable.

"Fortunately, the Three Saints currently appear to uphold moral integrity. As long as I continue to maintain my identity as the 'True Spirit Infuser' and 'Walker of Mountains and Seas,' I should be safe."

Li Fan pondered this while not forgetting to absorb the residual essence of Saint Prying Opportunity before him.

Though Saint Prying Opportunity had self-immolated, the Great Dao of Prying in Mountains and Seas remained.

However, it appeared as if it had just recovered from a severe injury, appearing so weak compared to the formidable Saint Prying Opportunity.

With a thought from Li Fan, the scattered sparks of light vanished.

And on the "Return to Truth" panel of True Return, new characters suddenly appeared.

Representing Li Fan's gains from this encounter.

Sui Jun and Prying Opportunity.

As the light swirled and manifested, they were inscribed into truth.

The Third, Sui Jun, and the Fourth, Prying Opportunity.

Li Fan looked at the "Return to Truth" panel, which was gradually filling up, and felt overjoyed.

Suddenly, he sensed that this line of characters seemed to be undergoing a change.

Seven-colored light swirled, like flowing water, with a subtle shifting motion.

Prying Opportunity, ranked last, seemed to be moving forward, as if aiming for the first position.

"Prying Opportunity, Eon Return, Sui Jun, Profound Embryo..."

"Is this in order of strength?" Li Fan intuitively guessed.

However, he then pondered and frowned.

"Let's stick to the order of arrival."

"Naturally, there is a cosmic order."

"Order matters, profound principles are hidden within. As for strength..."

"Strength is not absolute. Today, I consecutively defeated Sui Jun and Prying Opportunity, which is proof of this!"

Li Fan declared proudly, adhering to his chosen principle.

As if sensing Li Fan's firm resolve, the seven-colored flowing light on "Return to Truth" paused for a moment before returning to its original state.

Everything reverted to Li Fan's will.

As the light settled, it stopped moving.

Li Fan, however, did not immediately leave the void. Instead, he began to recover from his injuries.

This battle had been truly brutal.

Though he had successfully acquired the Great Daos of Sui Jun and Prying Opportunity, the backlash he suffered was also quite severe.

Putting aside other matters, the few blows he endured from Duke Shou Qiu while acting were not light.

Not to mention the subsequent struggle with Sui Jun and Prying Opportunity, which had nearly depleted him.

"Even with my constitution, enduring the extreme shattering and absorption of nascent spirits was difficult. I could clearly feel symptoms akin to 'True Spirit Loss,' requiring time to fully recover."

"Furthermore..."

Li Fan extended his arms, observing them carefully, his expression solemn.

"Although it's not obvious, I can still sense it."

"As if existing between truth and falsehood, neither fully present nor absent."

"This is the price of forcefully using the 'Truth and Falsehood' transformation to deal with enemies."

"Originally, if everything had gone smoothly, I wouldn't have suffered such a strong backlash. However, Prying Opportunity's ferocity far exceeded my expectations."

"I can use the excuse of severe injuries to deceive Duke Shou Qiu and the other Saints on the Other Shore. But this trace... I fear it cannot be hidden from the Three Saints Lianshan."

"It seems I cannot return to my original Mountains and Seas this time."

Fortunately, Li Fan had no intention of returning to his previous Mountains and Seas to report to the Three Saints anyway.

"Then I'll just suppress and absorb the remaining Saints here."

Li Fan sat cross-legged in the void, using "Truth and Falsehood" to heal his severe injuries.

Perhaps due to the past interference of external forces, the repair process felt particularly strenuous, as if there were loopholes.

Li Fan's mind worked on multiple fronts, simultaneously sensing the Great Daos of Sui Jun and Prying Opportunity he had newly acquired.

Within their respective Dao paths, the lingering thoughts of their previous possessors seemed to remain.

While Li Fan had little to say about Sui Jun, he found Prying Opportunity particularly intriguing.

"Containing the foundation of all things, fostering the changes between reality and illusion, upholding the balance of all wonders..."

"This must be the 'Truth and Falsehood' transformation, right?" Li Fan mused after a moment of contemplation, his brow furrowed slightly.

"It's even more profound than my own understanding?"

Chapter 1704: The璇玑 Ring in the Heart

"Although I had the treasures to protect you, do not overexert yourself. If it is impossible..."

"Prioritize your own safety. With True Spirit Infusion, there are infinite possibilities. Even if Mountains and Seas cannot be reconnected, there may still be a way to salvage the situation."

The Three Saints were present, yet they spoke differently from those on the Other Shore.

"Remember, after descending to the Mountains and Seas ahead, do not trust anyone, even familiar individuals."

"There is only one ultimate goal: to preserve Mountains and Seas amidst the rampant Dao Annihilation. As for other matters..."

"Be unrestrained, and act according to your judgment."

As if seeing the chaos of the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints Lianshan solemnly instructed.

Without waiting for Li Fan's reply, three streams of power enveloped his body.

They forcefully broke through the surging Dao Annihilation tide and shot towards the precarious Mountains and Seas in the Void Realm.

The Void Realm's reaction was unexpectedly fierce, quickly reclaiming the passage Li Fan had created. As if determined to completely conquer the Mountains and Seas ahead, the faint light representing Li Fan only lasted for a few moments before being submerged in the endless darkness.

And the Three Saints, under the impact of the Void Realm, their figures trembled slightly.

"We should also start making preparations."

The majestic figures suddenly grew larger, pushing back the surrounding darkness.

The Three Saints stood like interconnected mountains, illuminating the epochs of the Void Realm.

...

Even with the help of the Three Saints to send him off, the experience of forcefully traversing the Void Realm under its backlash was extremely unpleasant.

It was as if ten thousand steel knives were constantly shaving at the foundation of one's existence, each blow almost shattering the Dao foundation.

If not for Li Fan's enlightenment of Universe Cycle at the Boundless Monument of Mountains and Seas, leaving his unique imprint.

If not for Li Fan possessing Infinite True Spirit, completely unafraid of the Void Realm's erosion.

He would likely be heavily injured by now.

"Heh heh..."

His figure finally stabilized, Li Fan coughed lightly, calming his blood and Qi.

He paid no mind to the dozens of possibilities that had been shattered by his impact.

After all, the Mountains and Seas here, as far as the eye could see, were already a scene of shattered land, withered and decaying!

The moment he descended, Li Fan sensed the abnormality of this place.

Chaos, madness, hysteria.

Even Mountains and Seas themselves had undergone inexplicable changes due to the demise of the Three Saints.

"Even ants cling to life, let alone Mountains and Seas."

"As it is about to be devoured by the Void Realm, various distorted phenomena will manifest."

Li Fan frowned slightly, dispelling the mountain and sea roars that sounded like ghostly wails reaching his ears.

He had also witnessed the end of Mountains and Seas before.

But that was at the twilight of time.

Now, Mountains and Seas were still managing to hold on in their middle age.

Therefore, the desperate struggle of Mountains and Seas before their demise was also terrifying.

All beings within the countless possibilities of Mountains and Seas originated from Mountains and Seas. Now that Mountains and Seas were about to collapse, in their struggle for survival, Mountains and Seas intended to reclaim everything.

In order to prolong their existence for a little longer.

Without the arrival of Dao Annihilation, the possibilities collapsed like landslides, burying all life within them.

The Immortal Realm, built by the Three Saints upon the continuous Mountains and Seas, began to collapse entirely.

Even...

Li Fan looked towards where the Other Shore should have been.

The radiant white light that enveloped Mountains and Seas was no longer present.

Instead, it had turned into a strange black, dim light.

It trembled from time to time, as if a fierce battle was underway within it.

"This mess..."

"Preserve Mountains and Seas." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, observed for a moment, and then shook his head slightly.

"Let's observe first. If it's really impossible, then I'll use True Return to go back. Anyway, this life has yielded enough gains..."

Just as Li Fan was thinking this, his expression suddenly changed.

Because just now, he sensed an invisible hand slowly brushing over the top of his head. The cold and smooth touch made him instinctively shudder. At the same time, Li Fan felt as if something had been "scraped off" him!

"Who!"

Before Li Fan could react, the bamboo staff in his hand spontaneously struck out towards the empty space.

It seemed silent at first.

Then, ripples gradually spread, growing louder and louder, finally turning into continuous, earth-shattering roars that shook Mountains and Seas.

A figure was forced out in a sorry state.

And far behind him, Li Fan clearly saw that the Mountains and Seas, which were in a state of self-collapse due to the impending apocalypse, had actually temporarily stabilized their situation.

It was as if an invisible force was forcefully condensing the collapsing Mountains and Seas.

It looked as if the mountains that had collapsed were rising again!

With the wooden staff's strike, the Mountains and Seas instantly fell silent.

Only the roars of the mountains reappearing and rising echoed.

Li Fan himself was stunned, and then he felt the gazes from all parts of Mountains and Seas!

And as the sneak attacker was exposed, the object that had been "scraped off" by the invisible hand returned to its owner.

"Lian... Shan... Staff."

The Saint opposite him spoke word by word, as if encountering something utterly incredible.

Li Fan also recognized the opponent's identity in an instant.

Prying Opportunity.

He thought that after recognizing the Saint Lianshan's token, the opponent's attitude would change.

However, he did not expect that Saint Prying Opportunity would only freeze for a moment before launching another attack on Li Fan.

The target was no longer Li Fan, but the Lianshan Staff in Li Fan's hand!

Not only that, but Li Fan could also feel several familiar auras instantly approaching from all directions of Mountains and Seas.

Their target was clearly Li Fan.

Li Fan's scalp tingled. Only now did he understand why, before his departure, the Three Saints had suddenly instructed him to "act with impunity, and proceed as you see fit."

There was no need for Li Fan to control it. The Lianshan Staff automatically waved, creating layers of mountain shadows all around, blocking the sight of all the Saints.

Even so, it could not completely block Prying Opportunity's frenzied actions.

"Cough, cough, cough..."

Li Fan sensed that his "luck" seemed to be draining away at an alarming rate. Even the normal circulation of his own blood and Qi was affected, as if he had gone mad and was unable to regulate himself!

More importantly, the outer layer of Universe Cycle he wore had begun to fit loosely!

And besides Prying Opportunity, a second Saint had already attacked.

Starlight paved the way, and a wooden boat drifted.

A small boat broke through the infinite mountain shadows created by the Lianshan Staff and forcibly rammed towards Li Fan.

Li Fan vaguely discerned Saint Xingcha standing on the boat.

Compared to the Xingcha Saint they were familiar with on the Other Shore in later generations, the Xingcha Saint here was enveloped in an extremely dense, murderous aura.

The target was also clear: the Lianshan Staff in Li Fan's hand.

Every speck of starlight seemed to contain an infinite amount of energy, continuously crashing against the rising mountain shadows, scattering starlight. The situation of Mountains and Seas, which had just been stabilized by the Lianshan Staff, became unstable again.

Just then, the iron shovel at Li Fan's waist also moved.

Like the Lianshan Staff, it acted on its own.

With a casual thrust into the Mountains and Seas,

The starlight, the invisible icy hand, and even the rising mountain shadows were all repelled by a mysterious great vibration.

The great sound was silent.

All sounds disappeared, and in the Mountains and Seas, only the sound of gurgling spring water echoed.

The sound of flowing water grew louder and louder, and in just a moment, it turned into a roaring torrent, resounding in the ears of all the Saints.

The chaotic and depleted Infinite Sea had another spring dug out.

The madness of Mountains and Seas weakened.

Li Fan looked at the actions of the two divine artifacts and suddenly understood.

"This is the act of the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai, recreating the merging of Lianshan and Guihai."

"Further excavating the potential of the dying Mountains and Seas, making it like a dying man's last burst of vitality, regenerating life."

"However, this is not a long-term solution. If it cannot be stabilized as soon as possible..."

"This segment of Mountains and Seas will collapse even faster!"

Li Fan's thoughts raced, already considering using True Return to go back.

And with the advent of the iron shovel, the expressions of all the Saints looking at Li Fan changed again.

But they only hesitated for a moment.

They still did not give up their attempts to seize the treasures!

No one knew what had happened in this segment of Mountains and Seas after the death of the Three Saints.

The dispositions of the Saints on the Other Shore had all changed drastically.

"The items opened up by the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai should belong to the virtuous. Fellow Daoist cultivating is insufficient, and holding them instead will bring disaster."

A faint voice echoed from the depths of Mountains and Seas.

As if to confirm his words, the Lianshan Staff and Guihai Shovel, which had been inspiring unparalleled protection, actually showed signs of losing control at this moment!

"Oracle Prediction." Li Fan's expression changed slightly as he recognized the owner of the voice.

One word, and the prophecy could be broken or fulfilled.

"Quickly let go. Delay will bring self-destruction!"

As Oracle Prediction spoke, the Lianshan Staff that was being wielded actually swung towards Li Fan, summoning a mountain shadow.

Bang!

Li Fan, caught off guard, collided head-on with it.

As a Saint, he naturally would not be so easily injured, but his body vibrated, and his blood and Qi became turbulent.

More importantly, the Lianshan Staff and Guihai Shovel in his hands became increasingly difficult to control.

The protective mountain and sea shadows inspired by the two divine artifacts were no longer stable.

The Saints became more aggressive.

"I came from the Mountains and Seas of the future, to save..."

Li Fan's voice was deep, but he was horrified to find that what he said had unknowingly changed.

"What bullshit Saints, they are nothing but dogs and chickens."

"First kill the Three Saints, then slay all of you. Mountains and Seas will perish, and all will return to the Void Realm!"

"Hahaha!"

His laughter was maniacal.

Even more terrifying, as these words were spoken, Li Fan's thoughts actually began to change accordingly.

It was as if a pen in the background was rewriting his fate!

"Guiming..."

Li Fan gritted his teeth, forcefully resisting the distorted invasion in his mind.

Because if he could not resist this distortion, he would act like a puppet. He would fight the Saints until death, and would not activate True Return.

As Li Fan devoted most of his willpower to fighting against Guiming, the signs of the Lianshan Staff and Guihai Shovel losing control became even more apparent.

Oracle Prediction, Divination, Prying Opportunity, Karmic Judgment, Xingcha...

These familiar Saints on the Other Shore, completely disregarding Li Fan's identity as an envoy of the Three Saints, displayed their divine abilities, all trying to capture Li Fan.

The Dao paths of the Saints had not changed, but their actions were like completely different people.

Even with the protective treasures bestowed by the Three Saints, under their siege, Li Fan was gradually struggling to hold on.

At this critical moment, the stone club that had been hanging on Li Fan's back.

Finally moved.

"Now that the Three Saints have perished, we naturally live and die by our own fate. Fellow Daoist, why must you..."

Oracle Prediction's words were cut short by a muffled groan.

Then, a series of muffled thuds followed.

In just a few moments, Li Fan felt the pressure on him greatly reduced.

And the stone club that had disappeared reappeared before Li Fan.

However, at some unknown time, it had become stained with blood of varying degrees.

"All Beings Club... Hehehe."

Prying Opportunity, having suffered a hidden loss, let out a cold laugh.

Although the siege on Li Fan had stopped, they did not disperse.

Instead, they stared intently.

The other Saints did the same.

"Live and die by our own fate." Li Fan tightly gripped the All Beings Club, recalling Prying Opportunity's words just now.

And thinking of the subtle changes occurring in the Xuanji Ring, he finally began to understand.

"The dispositions of all the Saints have changed drastically."

"The special instructions from the Three Saints before their departure."

"And..."

"Prying Opportunity, Oracle Prediction, Divination..."

"The so-called Saints on the Other Shore were probably not the good and righteous people I saw."

"They were merely subdued by the Three Saints and then transformed by the Xuanji Ring over a long period, allowing all the Saints to work together with one heart for the salvation of Mountains and Seas."

"As long as the Three Saints were present, everything was manageable. Even if the Saints harbored dissatisfaction in their hearts, they could not turn the tide."

"But in this segment of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints were killed by [Void Realm Resurrected]. The Saints on the Other Shore have, however, returned to their original nature..."

The Saints' ill intentions permeated the air, encircling Li Fan tightly.

However, the All Beings Club in his hand remained fearless, as if it hadn't tasted blood in a long time and was even eager to try.

The current situation, although Li Fan could use True Return to return to his designated anchor point.

But even a clay figurine has some temper.

After being teleported and then besieged by all the Saints, Li Fan was extremely stifled.

"Although you have numbers, I possess the divine artifacts of the Three Saints."

Li Fan casually weighed the All Beings Club in his hand, a dangerous glint in his eyes.

"Act with impunity."

He repeatedly muttered the Four Words instructed by the Three Saints, and then, without any warning, swung a blow towards Oracle Prediction in the distance.

There was no need for him to target the opponent.

As long as he thought about who he wanted to hit, the All Beings Club in his hand would naturally strike the target.

Ignoring space and time, it hit accurately upon release.

And it was unavoidable.

"All beings are under the club."

Another muffled sound was heard. Li Fan felt the feedback force from the hand in his grasp and understood the origin of the name [All Beings Club].

His gaze swept over the Saints surrounding him, and Li Fan did not hold back, swinging repeatedly.

He could not kill the Saints, but each strike landed squarely on their heads.

However, the Saints present were not lambs to the slaughter.

Although Li Fan had gained a temporary advantage with the divine artifacts, the Saints, working together, endured the attacks of the All Beings Club and collaborated to interfere with Li Fan's actions.

His movements, his thoughts, all began to be uncontrollably affected.

After having his fun, Li Fan was about to use True Return to leave.

But suddenly, his thoughts stirred, and he shouted in a deep voice, "Duke Shou Qiu, if you don't help me now, Mountains and Seas may have no hope of recovery!"

Alas...

A sigh echoed from the middle of Mountains and Seas.

As if a continuous great tide was arriving, obscuring the sight of all the Saints.

"Follow me."

A faint whisper sounded, and Li Fan did not resist. He was swept away by this force and safely escaped from the encirclement of all the Saints.

Chapter 1705: The Theory of Shan Hai's Potential

It was as if the tempering process of the Xuanji Ring was being replayed, or perhaps it was an emulation of the Three Saints reforging the Xuanji Ring. Amidst the floating phantom images of Mountains and Seas, time flowed and changed, and the shattered Xuanji Ring was mended piece by piece! After a long while, the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel retracted their divine radiance, appearing to have lost their sentience, almost falling from their floating state. Li Fan quickly stored the Three Treasures away and then looked at the seemingly perfectly restored Xuanji Ring. Shou Qiu, however, was the first to discern its true nature. "It is not truly restored, but rather the method to recast it has been etched into it. Like a mold, we only need to infuse it with materials and power." "Although it cannot be compared to the true Xuanji Ring, it possesses a third of its power. This should be more than enough to momentarily deceive Guiming and the others." Duke Shou Qiu said with pleasant surprise. "Perhaps when the Three Saints delivered the supreme treasures to me, they had already considered the shattering of the Xuanji Ring and my need to rebuild it," Li Fan mused thoughtfully. Shou Qiu nodded in agreement. Li Fan once again carefully examined the Xuanji Ring before him. Or perhaps, calling it a mold for the Xuanji Ring would be more appropriate. Intertwining reality and illusion, it revealed the profound principles of Mountains and Seas. It began and ended in a cycle, forming its own distinct lineage. While mirroring and containing Mountains and Seas, it also used the power of "Xuanji" to restrain everything within this small circle, thus fostering unity and adherence to rules. "This method is exquisitely crafted, displaying kingly and overbearing might. It is infinitely more brilliant than forcibly distorting thoughts!" Li Fan praised repeatedly after studying it. All the Saints were seated within the Xuanji Ring, and their personalities and temperaments did not truly change. The Saints remained Saints. However, under the influence of the Xuanji power, their thoughts and considerations would first prioritize the overall situation of Mountains and Seas. Simultaneously, they would regard the Saints seated together in the Xuanji Ring as fellow travelers. Coupled with the suppression by the Three Saints, they appeared so peaceful and benevolent. But once the Xuanji Ring shattered, this collective community would instantly be broken. When facing outsiders, the Saints would naturally reveal their true abilities and show no mercy. Li Fan savored the wonders of the Xuanji Ring, while Duke Shou Qiu's expression gradually turned solemn. "The Xuanji Ring was forged by the combined efforts of the Three Saints. Although it appears as a unified whole, it is actually composed of three coexisting powers. Therefore, if we want to restore it using this mold, it is best to have three individuals do so. Otherwise, its efficacy will be greatly diminished." After speaking, Li Fan and Duke Shou Qiu exchanged glances. "If Tai Wei had not perished, perhaps we could have sought his cooperation. But now..." "With Mountains and Seas about to wither, where can we find a third Saint?" Shou Qiu was troubled. Li Fan also frowned: "Although I possess the supreme technique of True Spirit Infusion, it still requires suitable seeds. I wonder if there are still such individuals in this segment of Mountains and Seas?" After discussing for a while, they decided to partially complete the Xuanji Ring mold while simultaneously searching for suitable materials for Sainthood within Mountains and Seas. At the same time, to deter the four Saints of Guiming, Li Fan occasionally manipulated the accumulated True Spirits in the Void Realm, creating significant disturbances. The four Saints, filled with suspicion, believed Li Fan was plotting something in the Void Realm, and their attention was temporarily diverted. "As the saying goes, 'Amidst the vast currents, true heroes emerge.' In times of crisis and downfall, there will always be those who can turn the tide. In the past, Duke Shou Qiu, you were such a person, and in today's Mountains and Seas, there is also someone like that." Li Fan observed, pointing at a figure in a surviving possibility. "This child, a hundred years ago, during the shattering of Mountains and Seas, was merely an unknown True Immortal. With the descent of the end times and the impending disintegration of Mountains and Seas, the intertwined bonds between possibilities weakened. He finally broke through his long-standing shackles and achieved the realm of transcendence." "It is a pity that after leaping beyond the possibilities, all he saw was a fractured and precarious vision of Mountains and Seas. He even encountered the tide of Dao Annihilation several times, nearly perishing. If not for your intervention, I would have felt compelled to save him." Li Fan said calmly, "I observe that this child's destiny is not yet exhausted. In the face of life and death, he repeatedly encounters great opportunities hidden within. If I had saved him, it would have caused him to miss these opportunities." Shou Qiu nodded: "The art of seizing opportunities is indeed profound. He has indeed survived peril multiple times, even... finding a Saint Pill scattered during Tai Wei's demise amidst the chaotic currents of Mountains and Seas." "With the aid of this Saintly Destiny Pill, he has completely stabilized his transcendent realm. If Mountains and Seas were still stable, he might have had the chance to aspire to Sainthood through his own efforts. But now..." Li Fan chuckled: "Aren't we still here?" "After observing for so long in secret, this child truly meets all our requirements in every aspect." "Indeed. After his strength increased, feeling the chaotic and apocalyptic state of Mountains and Seas, he returned to his hometown alone. He led the immortals to resist Dao Annihilation. He even imparted all his insights without reservation. In this single possibility, thirteen transcendent experts were born in a short period. Although it has almost exhausted the potential of this possibility, it has also formed a solid defense force. Now that the wind of Dao Annihilation is rising, they can still be considered safe. Even if Mountains and Seas collapse, their location will be the last to perish." Duke Shou Qiu praised him without reservation. "Speaking of potential, after my recent observations, I find that here, the potential seems to have increased even as it was being depleted. I wonder if it is my imagination." "It is not your imagination; it is indeed the case." Shou Qiu explained to Li Fan. "The potential of possibilities originates from Mountains and Seas. Under normal circumstances, from the day it is born, it is fixed. How much namelessness, how many transcended beings, or even whether Saints will be born, are all predetermined. Only in extremely special circumstances can destiny be altered..." Shou Qiu paused slightly, as if recalling something. Then he pointed to the possibility they were observing: "Now that Mountains and Seas are shattered and order is lost, this is an opportunity to change destiny. To put it plainly, the potential of possibilities is like nutrients in soil. Although not absolutely fixed in quantity, the rate of replenishment is extremely slow. From our perspective as living beings, it will always seem 'limited.' Moreover, Mountains and Seas are already in a state of self-preservation, unable to divert power to nourish the beings within." "The increase in potential now is due to the shattering of Mountains and Seas and the self-loss of potential." Li Fan immediately understood: "This surplus potential comes from other extinguished possibilities." Originally, Li Fan found it difficult to perceive the potential contained within possibilities. However, in the process of searching for suitable candidates for Sainthood, he noticed that Shou Qiu could often judge at a glance whether a possibility contained their target, and his accuracy rate was very high. Thus, he inquired. As fellow saviors of the world, Duke Shou Qiu naturally did not begrudge sharing this small method of discerning the potential of possibilities. He meticulously taught it to Li Fan. This method was called [Observing Mountains and Seas], and it allowed one to perceive the脈絡 radiating from Mountains and Seas within possibilities. Then, by synthesizing various forms, one could determine the magnitude of its potential. Li Fan had already cultivated it to near-perfection in his years of searching for suitable helpers. "Logically speaking, if the method is proper, it is possible to drain the potential of several possibilities and supply it to one." Li Fan suddenly had a realization while observing and contemplating. Shou Qiu was slightly taken aback, then nodded: "Indeed, it is possible. However..." "It is not of much significance." "To us, although they originate from different possibilities, they are all born within Mountains and Seas. There is no difference." "Moreover, the potential of possibilities involves the fundamental power of Mountains and Seas. Forcibly summoning it might provoke a backlash from Mountains and Seas. Although we Saints are not afraid, we must also worry about further damaging the already fragile Mountains and Seas." The topic ended here, and they returned to the topic of the transcendent cultivator they had their eyes on. This individual cultivated the path of [Indestructibility], following the method of unifying myriad selves. In the apocalyptic era of Mountains and Seas, while fraught with crisis, it also presented unprecedented opportunities. Numerous possibilities were extinguished, and the number of [Indestructible] beings in the entire Mountains and Seas requiring unification was few. In just a hundred years, [Indestructible] traversed a path that ordinary transcendent beings could not achieve in a lifetime. "Like Morality, special circumstances have created a kind of unique entity in Mountains and Seas." "Although there is no self-nourishment from other possibilities, it inevitably leads to the weakness of his True Spirit." "But with my intervention, all worries are gone!" They had waited long enough. It was time to act. Duke Shou Qiu nodded slightly, and then the two of them, with remarkable tacit understanding, split up. Li Fan's figure flickered and appeared beside [Indestructible] within the possibility. Looking down from above, he revealed an unfathomable smile: "Young friend, today I have a great fortune for you!" With that, he gently swept his hand downwards. Facing this sudden development, [Indestructible] revealed a look of panic. He instinctively tried to resist, but under Li Fan's restraint, he was completely unable to move. He could only obediently allow Li Fan to imbue him. Gradually, the fear on [Indestructible]'s face disappeared, replaced by immense joy. He closed his eyes to comprehend the Dao, awaiting the final step. Meanwhile, outside Mountains and Seas, to attract the attention of the four Saints of Guiming, Shou Qiu had already flown out. Wielding the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel, he engaged in combat with the four Saints. The Three Treasures had recuperated for many years and had regained some combat effectiveness, but ultimately had not returned to their peak state. Shou Qiu was destined to be at a disadvantage. As long as he could stall the four Saints for a period, the birth of a new Saint would be achieved. Li Fan's creation of Saints was already a familiar process. And [Indestructible] was an absolute prodigy who emerged from the end of Mountains and Seas. Without any accidents, soon, a flicker of extraordinary fluctuation descended upon Mountains and Seas. A new Saint was born. "Not good!" As if realizing something, the four Saints of Guiming immediately intended to abandon Shou Qiu and rush over to slay this newly born Saint. In an instant, Li Fan and [Indestructible] had completed their exchange of information. [Indestructible], deeply grateful to the senior who had enlightened him to Sainthood, naturally stood by Li Fan's side. Conversely, the four Saints of Guiming, who sought his life without a word, were obvious enemies. "Can Shou Qiu return?" Li Fan's voice boomed, resonating throughout the shattered Mountains and Seas and reaching the Void Realm. The Lianshan Staff and the Three Treasures shone brightly, protecting Shou Qiu's return. "Request the Xuanji Ring!" Li Fan and Shou Qiu said solemnly and in unison. Then, under the watchful eyes of the four Saints, a familiar white circle suddenly appeared on the scene. The four Saints, who were originally rushing towards Mountains and Seas with great speed, instantly halted. They looked at the shattered yet reappearing Xuanji Ring with astonishment. They knew the power of the Xuanji Ring, having been suppressed within it for countless years. Therefore, they instinctively felt fear. Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and the newly promoted Saint [Indestructible] took their seats within the Xuanji Ring. In an instant, they became of one mind, their thoughts as if unified. "So, even the Three Saints who first took their seats in the Xuanji Ring had such a profound secret." Under the illumination of the Xuanji Ring's white light, Li Fan revealed a complex and unfathomable expression. Beside him, Shou Qiu and [Indestructible], whose attention should have been focused on repairing the Xuanji Ring and resisting the impending onslaught of the four Saints, were now staring at Li Fan. "Refine the four Saints of Guiming entirely. The Great Dao Returns to Truth, and there will be even more to add. Perhaps it will bring inexplicable benefits to True Return." These words were not spoken by Li Fan. It was Duke Shou Qiu! [Indestructible] also nodded in agreement: "It turns out that it is not suitable to return to Mountains and Seas. By absorbing other Saints, even Shou Qiu can vaguely sense the changes in your aura. Let alone the Three Saints. The ancient Mountains and Seas, with their situation unclear, it is best not to go alone. It is better to return to True Return and infiltrate the Saints' ranks to investigate their true intentions. "The Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel are also considered top-tier treasures in Mountains and Seas. After refining the four Saints of Guiming, we will help each other to comprehend them. If we can subdue them and store them within True Return, perhaps in the next life, they can be our surprise forces." "And this Xuanji Ring. After all this is done, there is no need to rush back to True Return immediately. Let us comprehend it together. If in the next life, the Three Treasures of the Lianshan Staff are no longer needed, you can reproduce it on your own..." "This will avoid many troubles." Shou Qiu pondered for a moment, then uttered a more astonishing statement. Although the secret of possessing True Return had been inadvertently revealed, Li Fan showed no signs of panic. Instead, he was overjoyed. "Xuanji, Xuanji, true to its name." "I finally understand why the Three Saints of Lianshan always had unified opinions and acted as one." "Wonderful, truly wonderful!" "Indeed wonderful." Duke Shou Qiu and [Indestructible] both nodded in agreement. The moment the three of them took their seats within the Xuanji Ring, countless unforeseen events occurred for Li Fan. Li Fan had far underestimated the power of the Xuanji Ring's [Unity of Mind and Purpose]. Especially in this situation, where the three of them joined forces to forge it and were the first to be seated within. The so-called unity of mind and purpose meant that all the memories and emotions of the three of them were intertwined, as if they had become a single entity. All future decisions and thoughts of the three would be made from the perspective of the collective interest. If Li Fan had not possessed True Return, and merely pretended to conceal his inner villainy, there would inevitably be intense conflicts between his views and the virtuous Duke Shou Qiu's. A self-struggle would be necessary before discussing unity of mind and purpose. But... Li Fan happened to possess the power of True Return! Shou Qiu's goal was to save Mountains and Seas. From a strategic perspective, the stronger Li Fan became, the more beneficial it would be to saving Mountains and Seas. As for the current state of Mountains and Seas... What about Saints, or even Mountains and Seas themselves? They were all usable materials!

Chapter 1706: Four Saints Together

Within the Xuanji Ring, Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Bu Jue were momentarily one, their identities indistinguishable.

"In the past, by chance, you once comprehended a fragment of the Great Dao of Longevity. Destiny truly works in mysterious ways! I had underestimated you. Even knowing you possessed 'Return to Truth,' I never expected you to engage in such forceful acquisitions. Treasures of Mountains and Seas belong to those who can seize them, not necessarily those who are virtuous. Just as I obtained the Great Dao of Longevity – it was fate. It's not so easy for others to simply snatch it away."

"Times have changed. With 'Return to Truth' in hand, one must be cautious. Even if I understand Shou Qiu's temperament now, I might not dare to easily reveal 'Return to Truth' in the next life."

"Perhaps the 'Inheritance of Memory' option can be utilized. From my perspective, this 'Inheritance of Memory' is more like utilizing the transformation between truth and falsehood to re-manifest beings who have already perished. Much like the cycles you have experienced."

As they communicated, witnessing the Four Saints of Gui Ming charging towards them to prevent the Xuanji Ring's reappearance, Li Fan chuckled, "Mites trying to shake a tree, how laughable and self-unaware. Today, let us use these four saints as a sacrifice to celebrate our newfound acquaintance."

"Excellent!" Shou Qiu nodded.

The wondrous utility of the Xuanji Ring was truly unfathomable. In the brief moments Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Bu Jue merged their memories, knowledge, and senses, it was as if Shou Qiu experienced Li Fan's transformations between truth and falsehood over countless eons simultaneously. Though the timing of their comprehension was limited to those few hundred moments when Li Fan had activated 'Return to Truth' in the past, Shou Qiu's gains were undoubtedly far superior to Li Fan's. As for Bu Jue, though slightly weaker than Li Fan, he too possessed his own unique insights.

Three intertwined, three united. In the mere moments Li Fan spent seated within the Xuanji Ring, his comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood had increased exponentially. The Xuanji Ring, which originally required the combined efforts of three individuals for decades to forge, was completed in mere breaths under the influence of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood.

As the white light erupted and enveloped Mountains and Seas, the Four Saints of Gui Ming arrived at that precise moment. Within that intensely familiar light, a primal fear surged in the hearts of all the Saints.

"How is this possible? The Xuanji Ring was clearly shattered!" Gui Ming exclaimed, unable to contain his shock.

Shou Qiu spoke loudly, "Without seeing its face, how can one comprehend its supreme mysteries? Cease your futile struggles. Enter the Great Dao of Return to Truth!"

As Shou Qiu spoke, rings of white light, like ropes, began to constrict the bodies of the Four Saints from the outside in, from large to small. The Four Saints of Gui Ming, relying on their Saintly divine abilities, might have managed to break one or two rings. But the Xuanji restraints were countless, just like their own ancient fates. In mere moments, they were suppressed by the Xuanji Ring. They had initially thought it was merely a matter of returning to the Other Shore and resuming their world-saving efforts. They never expected...

Compared to when the Three Saints presided, the atmosphere within the Xuanji Ring now felt exceedingly strange.

"Shou Qiu, what are you attempting to do?" The Four Saints of Gui Ming vaguely sensed unease from the phrase "Great Dao of Return to Truth."

"What am I doing? Naturally, I am doing what should be done." Shou Qiu chuckled again, his expression chillingly cold as he scanned the bound Saints. "You all possess Saintly realms, yet you are of no benefit to the salvation of Mountains and Seas. It would be better to contribute to Fellow Daoist Fan. Once the crisis of world destruction passes, perhaps you can at least be credited for your contributions."

"What Shou Qiu says resonates deeply with me," Li Fan chimed in.

"Stop your nonsensical talk! We were not mistaken; now that the Three Saints are gone, your true nature is fully exposed! Your talk of great virtue was all a pretense to deceive the world!" Duan Chan retorted coldly.

"Even if we are captured now, you are only relying on the power of the Xuanji Ring. The Xuanji Ring only has the power to suppress, not to harm. Killing us will not be so easy!" Ye Pan countered disdainfully, unfazed even while suppressed.

"Is that so..." Shou Qiu's expression was unreadable.

"Mortals, how can you comprehend the mysteries of the Xuanji? Today, I shall let you witness. To be able to glimpse the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, you can consider yourselves fortunate in your demise." With a faint remark, he pronounced the death sentence upon the Four Saints.

"Fellow Daoist Fan, watch carefully." Within the Xuanji Ring, scenes of endless Mountains and Seas instantly surged forth. It was not merely an illusion, as in the past. The Saints actually felt the aura of genuine Mountains and Seas. Above, mountains stretched endlessly; below, the sea was boundless. The pressure from Mountains and Seas alone caused the Saints' breaths to falter. Within the illusory Mountains and Seas, a solitary figure stood out. Seated on a mountain, gazing at the sea, his back to all beings.

"Do you hear the roars of mountains and seas?"

"Have you seen the might of collapsing mountains and engulfing seas?"

"Have you experienced the calamity of breaking mountains and sinking seas?"

"Have you faced the end of mountains vanishing and seas going silent?"

Surrounded by the illusory mountains and seas, the Saints could barely glimpse Shou Qiu's form. Only the pressure of Mountains and Seas, their collapse, their destruction – all these aspects pressed in like blades of wind and frost. This was not only Shou Qiu's past experience and comprehension but also a tangible manifestation after integrating the changes of truth and falsehood. The Four Saints of Gui Ming, though formidable, were naturally unable to escape this immense catastrophe. The illusory Mountains and Seas appeared and then shattered, returning all to tranquility. The Four Saints of Gui Ming, as if truly experiencing the annihilation of Mountains and Seas, were silently erased from existence! Thus, only four faint rays of light remained suspended within the Xuanji Ring – the Dao paths of the Four Saints. Although Li Fan was astonished by the destructive power displayed by Shou Qiu after mastering the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, he did not freeze. He immediately activated 'Return to Truth.' Under his gaze, the Dao paths of the Four Saints were instantly absorbed. On the 'Return to Truth' panel, several more characters appeared.

"To achieve Saintly Dao is already extraordinary. Yet, observing it now, it is merely an insignificant brick on the endless wall of truth and falsehood." Bu Jue remarked with a sigh, gazing at the hall of 'Return to Truth' through Li Fan's eyes.

Shou Qiu remained silent for a moment, then nodded in agreement. "Even the Great Dao of Longevity falls into this category."

"When this era ends, we too shall enter it." Shou Qiu's words implied that he might willingly dissipate himself into 'Return to Truth' before Li Fan's 'Return to Truth' activated, rather than returning to the Other Shore.

"This matter is not urgent for now. I observed Shou Qiu's divine ability just now, its power was truly terrifying. Even without the Xuanji Ring's suppression, ordinary Saints would likely be unable to withstand it."

"The method to perceive potential is called 'Observing Mountains and Seas.' This Saint-slaying divine ability could be named..."

"Leveling Mountains and Seas." Li Fan savored the entire process of the illusory Mountains and Seas appearing and disintegrating, feeling both shock and joy. Although, through the unified state of the Xuanji Ring, he now had a comprehensive understanding of this divine ability, without that state in the future, he might not grasp its true meaning. Noticing Li Fan's thoughts, Shou Qiu elaborated in detail.

"All sorts of phenomena are merely recreations of my past experiences, applied to the opponent through the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

"Without the enhancement of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, it would simply be a slightly more real illusion. However, under the effect of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, it can transform into the methods of Saints!"

"Even the Three Saints of Lianshan might pass through safely. But other Saints on the Other Shore... even the strongest, Prying Opportunity, would find it difficult to escape this calamity," Shou Qiu stated with great confidence. The comprehension of techniques, even with the enhancement of 'Return to Truth,' was faster than Li Fan's previous experiences. Even though 'Leveling Mountains and Seas' encompassed Shou Qiu's insights from countless eons, its core still revolved around the transformation of truth and falsehood. Within a hundred years, Li Fan had mastered it completely. During this period, the Xuanji Ring's white light only enveloped most of the remaining Mountains and Seas, maintaining its endangered state without truly resolving the crisis of annihilation. This was to create a facade of Li Fan still struggling, preventing the Three Saints of Lianshan from the future from crossing over.

"This method cannot be sustained for long. The wisdom of the Three Saints is beyond even my comprehension. Perhaps they have already vaguely sensed your possession of 'Return to Truth.' However, knowing that 'Return to Truth' cannot be taken or is useless, they allowed you to act freely." Shou Qiu said calmly.

"As long as this truth is not exposed, it's fine. I will continue to play the role of a 'True Spirit Infusion,' a 'Walker of Mountains and Seas.' For the sake of reconnecting Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints will eventually have to compromise, or even assist." Li Fan replied after some thought.

"Moving against the current, absorbing numerous Saints to fill 'Return to Truth.' I have a premonition that if the magnificent hall reappears from the void, even if the plan to reconnect Mountains and Seas fails, Mountains and Seas can still be saved. As for the Three Saints..."

"We can neither fully believe nor entirely disbelieve them." Shou Qiu offered this advice.

"What is the reason for this?"
