"Before the reconnection of Mountains and Seas, their motives might have been different. But after the reconnection, who knows what they will do? It is still uncertain. Moreover, the ultimate goal of the Three Saints is to return to the time when God separated the seas. Otherwise, even if Mountains and Seas return to their peak, they would still be no match for the Stars." Within the Xuanji Forest, Li Fan and Shou Qiu exchanged many insights. Shou Qiu's experiences over countless eons, especially his interactions with the Three Saints, were an unimaginably valuable asset to Li Fan. He also made general plans for future reincarnations.

"You can travel upstream against the current until the time I reach the Other Shore. It should be safe then. However, further ahead..."

"Perhaps I can no longer assist you."

"It's alright. I have grown accustomed to traveling alone. Moreover, perhaps we can still journey together." Li Fan said calmly. Suddenly, three unusual fluctuations within the Xuanji Ring interrupted their conversation. Shou Qiu glanced and chuckled lightly. "The Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, the All Beings Cudgel – these three treasures have fully recovered and are desperately trying to break free."

"Although they do not know our recent fortune, they can sense the unusual events from the act of slaying the Four Saints. Their actions are contrary to the mission of the Three Saints, and they naturally intend to depart. However, for now, it is beyond their control." Shou Qiu effortlessly suppressed the three treasures with a wave of his hand. Before comprehending the transformation of truth and falsehood, Shou Qiu might not have been the Three Treasures' match. But having mastered the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, the three treasures, no matter how miraculous, were ultimately not the Three Saints themselves. With the assistance of the Xuanji Ring, they naturally could not escape Shou Qiu's suppression.

"We are running out of time. Since we have captured the Four Saints, let us now dismantle the Xuanji Ring."

"Although we have reforged the Xuanji Ring, most of it was due to the role of the Three Treasures in providing the mold. If we lose the mold in the next life, it will not be as easy to create a Xuanji Ring again." Shou Qiu said, his gaze sweeping over the white light of the Xuanji Ring enveloping Mountains and Seas.

"Indeed. Moreover, without the Xuanji Ring's protection, Fellow Daoist Fan might not feel at ease." Bu Jue nodded in agreement. Li Fan did not retort to Bu Jue's teasing but frowned instead. "The Xuanji Ring is a supreme treasure crafted by the Three Saints. Even if I can recreate it from scratch in the next life, it will be difficult to escape the Three Saints' detection. I need to fully comprehend its principles, to create not *the* Xuanji Ring, but *my* Xuanji Ring." Li Fan's words were somewhat convoluted, but Shou Qiu and Bu Jue immediately understood his meaning.

"I do not have absolute confidence either, but I will try my best." Shou Qiu said. The difficulty in analyzing the Xuanji Ring was somewhat beyond Li Fan's expectations. Even with the combined wisdom of the three, progress was agonizingly slow. After all, it was the 'tool' the Three Saints used to unite the hearts of others, and it was not easily deciphered. As they reached an impasse, Li Fan suddenly had a flash of inspiration.

"With the strength of a mere three individuals, our efforts might be insufficient."

"What about incorporating the beings of Mountains and Seas? How about that?" Shou Qiu nodded in agreement after pondering for a moment. Bu Jue also concurred. "The wisdom of the beings of Mountains and Seas is not necessarily inferior to that of Saints. It is merely a matter of opportunity and fate. Once they attain enlightenment, perhaps they can find an alternative path, something we have overlooked." With their agreement, the Xuanji Ring's light suddenly expanded again, illuminating the entirety of Mountains and Seas. At this moment, all beings within the remnants of Mountains and Seas glimpsed the brilliant white circle above them. Though their physical bodies had not entered, their spirits and consciousness were drawn within. Within the Xuanji Ring, where initially only the three majestic figures of Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Bu Jue stood alone, there now appeared countless points of light resembling a sea of stars. Upon arrival, some were startled, some fearful, some excited. A cacophony of noises arose. Bu Jue frowned slightly, Li Fan's eyes turned cold, and Shou Qiu simply sneered.

"Silence!" Bu Jue's voice echoed, clarifying their mission to all the boundless beings. Those who were receptive to the Dao, without needing to be asked, spontaneously began to explore the mysteries of the Xuanji. As for those who were not interested, Li Fan was not worried about them remaining idle. After all, with the influence of the Xuanji Ring's 'Concentric Unity,' unwillingness would eventually turn into willingness. Gradually, the Xuanji Ring quieted down. Countless star-like points floated everywhere, permeating every corner of the Xuanji Ring. Their knowledge, thoughts, feelings, and insights all converged like streams, eventually forming a vast ocean.

Eight hundred years passed uneventfully. The research on the Xuanji Ring had reached a critical juncture. "Fellow Daoist Fan's ingenious idea has proven effective. The collective exploration by the boundless beings of Mountains and Seas is far more effective than our solitary research." Shou Qiu's voice echoed within the Xuanji Ring. Compared to eight hundred years prior, the Xuanji Ring now appeared much brighter and more transparent. Where previously there were many obscure areas, now, to Li Fan and the others, it was as clear as glass.

"So this is what the Xuanji Ring looked like in the eyes of the Three Saints."

"However, there is still one crucial core aspect that remains unsolved."

"That is..."

"The secret of 'Concentric Unity.'"

Chapter 1707: Marvelous Solution for the Three Saints' Abilities

Li Fan and the other two looked towards the heavens. The three sat in the center, as if bound by some mysterious force. It was this connection that initially granted the Xuanji Ring its 'Concentric Unity' property. Concentricity, unity, like one entity – this was the ultimate secret of the Xuanji Ring. The subtle influence exerted on the other beings seated within the ring all derived from this.

Shou Qiu gazed intently for a long time, then mused, "There is no need to rush to unravel this final step. After all, it is a supreme treasure crafted by the Three Saints. If this secret were to be uncovered instantly by another, the Three Saints might sense it. Even across the Void Realm, we cannot rule out such a possibility."

Li Fan nodded upon hearing this. Shou Qiu had been seated within the Xuanji Ring for many years. Although he did not share the same synchronized thoughts and memories as the Three Saints, through prolonged interaction, he had gleaned some details about the Three Saints' true strength. For instance, the Three Saints' 'Premonition' divine ability was terrifyingly potent. They could often foresee events long before they occurred, allowing them to prepare accordingly. And the success rate of this premonition... countless times over countless years, it had never failed.

"Even when the 'Void Realm Incarnations' attacked, the Three Saints seemed to have foreseen it. However, for reasons unknown, they chose not to evade but to face the onslaught resolutely."

"This premonition differs somewhat from Fellow Daoist Fan's intuition, yet it is not entirely the same. The Three Saints' premonitions do not occur only when an event is imminent. They could foresee events far in advance, possibly even proactively activating their divine abilities to perceive them. Thus, the Three Saints' minds are profound, and their true intentions are difficult to fathom."

"In addition to premonition, the Three Saints displayed another divine ability during their public appearances."

"That is 'Boundless Indestructibility.'"

Through their shared divine sense, Li Fan instantly understood what 'Boundless Indestructibility' meant. Shou Qiu continued his detailed explanation. "This is a divine ability the Three Saints derived in the instant before Mountains and Seas were divided. Although on a historical and present timeline, the Three Saints, like Mountains and Seas, were fragmented into individual entities. Yet, with unfathomable divine power, the Three Saints maintained their collective integrity."

"To put it simply, considering the Three Saints existing in Mountains and Seas across different time periods as a unified whole. The demise of any single individual would not affect the overall strength of the collective. The collective strength maintained a constant lower limit relative to the moment Mountains and Seas were divided, while the upper limit could increase accordingly."

"If an individual were to perish in the current time and space of Mountains and Seas, the collective strength would remain unchanged. The result would be a certain degree of growth in the strength of the remaining Three Saints. In an extreme scenario, if all Three Saints across all time and space were annihilated, with only one surviving in a particular region, then this final surviving Saint would return to their peak state."

"'Boundless Unity, Eternal Indestructibility' – this was a contingency measure created by the Three Saints to deal with the crisis of the Void Realm dividing Mountains and Seas. It was intended to allow them to turn the tide even in the worst-case scenario, retaining at least one last strike."

"Besides this, the Three Saints might have possessed other divine abilities, but I am unaware of them. It is regrettable that I did not witness the battle between the Three Saints and the Void Realm Incarnations in the Void Realm; otherwise, I might have been able to glean more about their true capabilities."

Li Fan frowned deeply. "In that case, the Three Saints are indeed incredibly formidable. I can hardly imagine any method that could truly kill them."

Shou Qiu nodded. "However, at the very least, for a considerable period, you will not have to contend with the Three Saints. As for the future..."

Shou Qiu smiled. "Even though the Three Saints are mysterious and unfathomable, they are ultimately no match for the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. If you can truly master the transformation of truth and falsehood, you will not only surpass the Three Saints but will hold the fate of Mountains and Seas in your hands."

Li Fan shook his head. "To fully comprehend the transformation of truth and falsehood is exceedingly difficult!"

"In the past, with my understanding, even after experiencing a hundred reincarnations, I felt I had only scratched the surface. Yet, now, with Shou Qiu's insights from countless eons added, I realize there is so much more unknown. It is astonishing. What I thought I knew was merely the superficial layer."

Within the Xuanji Ring, the three fell into silence. Even though Shou Qiu could provide details about the mysterious Three Saints, when faced with the vastness of the transformation between truth and falsehood, he appeared as a novice. It was indeed a difficult task for Master Fan.

As time passed and the myriad beings of Mountains and Seas continued their analysis, the Xuanji Ring grew brighter and brighter. Finally, when all other secrets were unraveled, only the secret of 'Concentric Unity' remained.

Li Fan's current life's journey was finally reaching its end. "We must make thorough preparations in advance."

"Whether it succeeds or fails, it is not advisable to linger in this life for too long." Shou Qiu glanced towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas, his expression grave. "The Three Saints might descend upon Mountains and Seas at any moment..."

Sensing the crisis Shou Qiu perceived, Li Fan nodded slightly. "As mentioned before, before your 'Return to Truth,' I will merge into 'Great Dao of Return to Truth.' However, unforeseen circumstances might arise. If the return fails, do not cling to it, and leave as soon as possible."

"Shou Qiu means..." Bu Jue's expression sharpened.

"The Longevity I obtained from the Infinite Sea in the past was merely a fragment. Although it shares the same level as Mountains and Seas, and allowed me to cultivate to the Saint realm. However..." Shou Qiu's tone became wistful. "Beyond the boundless void, there may be other 'Longevity' existences. Though I am willing to return to 'Return to Truth,' they might not be. At that time, conflict and collision may erupt."

"This is merely my premonition. It might not actually happen," Shou Qiu added with a smile, temporarily easing the tension in the atmosphere. "The Three Saints, Mountains and Seas, the Void Realm, the Stars, and other unknown existences. Even at the Saint realm, the path is fraught with peril and arduous."

Bu Jue sighed.

After final deliberations and rehearsing all potential scenarios, Li Fan and the other two finally extended their consciousness towards the mysterious point above their heads. As if touching the Xuanji Ring's forbidden area, the once bright and clear Xuanji Ring instantly dimmed. Like dark clouds pressing down, with the imminent arrival of a storm. Streaks of light flashed like lightning, causing the Xuanji Ring to appear on the verge of disintegration.

Li Fan and the others, however, ignored these signs. Under their mental manipulation, the countless points of light, formed from the beings of Mountains and Seas, fearlessly charged towards the final hidden secret. Like a meteor shower flying against the current, majestic and breathtaking.

The moment the points of light touched the Xuanji's mysteries, they withered and vanished like flowers. Every instant, billions of beings disappeared. But under the influence of 'Concentric Unity,' the concepts of life and death were utterly irrelevant to these points of light. At the cost of their lives, they slowly peeled back a corner of the Xuanji Ring's ultimate secret.

"This is..." Even Shou Qiu, after observing for a long time, showed a slight change in expression.

Li Fan, though shocked, suddenly understood. "All beings in Mountains and Seas originated from 'God.' They were inherently united, thus achieving unity of heart. But who would have thought the Three Saints could already glimpse the form of 'God'?"

At this moment, before their eyes, floating above the three of them, maintaining the secret of the Xuanji Ring's 'Concentric Unity,' was an indescribable figure. It resembled the "human" form, with a similar face. Yet, it seemed to have three heads and six arms, as if formed from the fusion of three beings. It was even like a shadow without a fixed shape, elusive and unpredictable. Although Li Fan and the two shared 'Concentric Unity,' in this instant, their perceptions of the figure's appearance varied. But without exception, the moment they witnessed this shadow, a single word appeared in their minds.

"God."

The profound principles condensed upon this shadow were as if they were on par with the Great Dao of 'Return to Truth,' not inferior in any way. Even with Li Fan's current understanding, comparing the two, he could only conclude they were "evenly matched."

"This is the Three Saints' deconstruction of 'God.'"

"Although it might have arisen from the Three Saints' comprehension, yet..."

"It must have had a foundation!" Shou Qiu realized and sternly reminded them. "To explore further."

However, a roaring sound had already begun to echo from beyond Mountains and Seas. It was not only from the direction Li Fan had come but also from the ancient Mountains and Seas, as if something was rapidly approaching. Li Fan and the two were trying to analyze the divine shadow within the Xuanji Ring, but they had inadvertently touched the Three Saints' forbidden zone. Disregarding everything else, they were about to descend. With each passing moment, the immense roar intensified, like the tide recedes before a tsunami. The Dao Annihilation outside Mountains and Seas also vanished at this moment.

"There's no time. We'll have to wait for the next life!" Li Fan was still somewhat reluctant, his gaze deeply fixed on the unfathomably deep divine shadow. This was the first time he had seen something that could rival 'Return to Truth.'

But Shou Qiu had already regained his composure. With a low cry, immense vitality erupted from his body. It was the Great Dao of Longevity! With the manifestation of Longevity, all things were born. Mountains and Seas, which were precarious under the pressure of Dao Annihilation, received a surge of vitality. Instantly, they revived as if from a winter slumber, returning to their peak. Countless possibilities rapidly evolved, presenting a scene of flourishing life.

However, all these illusions of vitality collapsed the moment the Great Dao of Longevity vanished. In fact, due to this immense stimulus, it had a counterproductive effect. After the spectacular final surge, an even faster demise followed. Amidst the backlash of Dao Annihilation waves, Mountains and Seas disintegrated.

And within the 'Return to Truth' panel, a line of colorful characters representing the Great Dao of Longevity of Mountains and Seas quietly appeared. As Shou Qiu had predicted, this absorption by 'Return to Truth' was not as smooth as before! It seemed there was an invisible pulling force from without. The characters flickered in and out of existence, unstable.

In the real Mountains and Seas, Shou Qiu's form gradually became illusory. He vanished first. Seeing this, Bu Jue did not hesitate and immediately dissipated himself, merging into 'Return to Truth.' Compared to the Great Dao of Longevity, his own comprehended 'Endless' Dao assimilated more smoothly. Without any complications, several more lines appeared on the 'Return to Truth' panel.

However, without the assistance of Shou Qiu and Bu Jue, they felt as if they had lost their two brains, becoming sluggish and disoriented. Even their once clear thoughts were affected. But the palpable warning of imminent danger made Li Fan quickly shake off the side effects of losing the 'Concentric Unity.'

At this moment, as if time had stood still, Li Fan clarified the critical situation. Mountains and Seas were on the verge of destruction, and outside in the Void Realm, two timelines of Three Saints were rushing towards them. Without the external interference, the divine shadow of 'God' had already concealed itself. But similarly, without anyone presiding over it, the Xuanji Ring was gradually losing its power of suppression. The Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel were becoming restless. And within the 'Return to Truth' panel, Shou Qiu's transformed Great Dao of Longevity was still under some form of strain. It had not fully entered 'Return to Truth.'

...

"Fortunately, apart from the divine shadow of 'God,' we had foreseen all other eventualities." Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp glint. "We will proceed according to the plan."

He then used the Xuanji Ring's remaining suppression power to seize the Three Treasures. Afterward, he gathered all the remaining beings of Mountains and Seas and silently chanted the 'True Spirit Burning Great Technique.' Ordinary lives possessed weak true spirits, but their numbers were infinite. When piled together, they were equivalent to Saints. Now, ignited by Li Fan, they resembled a blazing fire, illuminating the near-extinguished Mountains and Seas. The already fragile and nearing destruction Mountains and Seas could no longer withstand this inferno. Within moments, flames erupted, and fire spread relentlessly.

Li Fan, hidden within the raging inferno, wielding the Three Treasures like torches, aimed them at the center of the Xuanji Ring, where the divine shadow of 'God' resided. With a cold gaze, he hurled them forward with all his might. Carrying the intensely burning true spirit flames, the myriad lights fiercely collided with the concealed divine shadow of 'God.'

Yet, Li Fan still felt it was insufficient. He took a deep breath and beckoned towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas. "Come!" With all his strength, he summoned the accumulated true spirits from the Void Realm. Like fuel to the flames, the expansive fires of Mountains and Seas suddenly surged several times over. And this fire continued to grow and grow!

However, the arsonist could not escape. As the instigator of the burning of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan was engulfed by the flames. Inevitably, he himself was ignited. "Ahhh..." The pain of the true spirit fire's combustion was beyond any earthly description. Every part of his soul felt as if it were undergoing the most brutal torture. But Li Fan endured all the pain. His gaze was focused intently on the center of the Xuanji Ring, scorched by the true spirit flames.

Without 'Concentric Unity,' relying only on his own judgment, Li Fan's choices began to change. "Steady progress, while seemingly good."

"If I hadn't glimpsed the shadow of 'God,' I might have followed Shou Qiu's advice. But..."

"This shadow of 'God' cannot be truly unraveled by conventional means. Only through a desperate struggle can its secret be unlocked!"

"No matter how many reincarnations, the outcome remains the same."

"It's better to act sooner!"

With his body and soul ignited, merging into the vast true spirit flames, his own infinite spiritual essence dissipating as fuel. Supporting this immense fire. Mountains and Seas were consumed, and even the Void Realm was temporarily repelled. Under the scorching of the true fire, the Lianshan Staff and the other two treasures turned to ash. And the Xuanji Ring, unable to endure any longer, its outer layers shattered.

Within... the divine shadow of 'God' reappeared! Without the Xuanji Ring's containment, the divine shadow revealed its true form. It resembled Mountains and Seas, and also resembled the beings of Mountains and Seas. Even the true spirit flames could not harm it in the slightest.

Chapter 1708: The God Has Appeared

The raging inferno across Mountains and Seas paused the moment the divine shadow of 'God' manifested. Under an invisible pressure, the once fervent flames rapidly subsided.

Not only the true spirit flame but also Mountains and Seas, and everything within perception, vanished. The area around the divine shadow of 'God' became an absolute void, drawing everything towards it.

Perhaps because the swallowed Mountains and Seas were insignificant in quantity compared to 'God,' the unfathomable divine shadow did not change despite the consumption. It remained its silent posture.

Outside the shattered Mountains and Seas, the immense roaring that had been rapidly approaching ceased with the true manifestation of the divine shadow. Within the observable range, everything was dead silent.

Only Li Fan, in a state of true spirit dissipation, retained some consciousness. He was powerless to act further, drifting involuntarily towards the abyss of the divine shadow.

"This..."

"Is this 'God'?"

Li Fan's thoughts were exceptionally calm. As he plunged into the abyss, he felt no fear, as if the divine shadow before him was his homeland and returning was his destined fate.

His tranquil state allowed Li Fan to observe the manifested divine shadow of 'God' in its entirety. Insights flooded his mind.

"Even facing 'God,' ordinary individuals cannot comprehend it."

"'God' is like being high in the heavens, too distant from the world for ordinary people to see clearly."

"But I, through the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, am as if positioned in the sky."

"Extremely close to 'God,' within reach, hence I can gain some understanding."

Time seemed to have stopped for Li Fan at this moment. Fearless, without joy or sorrow, without anger or despair. Not contemplating the saying "If one hears the Dao in the morning, death in the evening is acceptable," nor showing reverence for the unfathomable 'God.'

He simply observed instinctively, then began to think.

...

"Neither spirit nor matter, neither existence nor non-existence, neither pure nor impure, a calamity beyond calamities."

"Reflecting all phenomena without form, giving rise to all laws without thought."

"All beings are its children, and also its abyss."

"To know it as a boat is to drown in the boat; to see it as the Dao is to be lost in the Dao."

"Cannot be fathomed, cannot be measured, cannot be seen, cannot be heard..."

These whispers erupted from Li Fan's mind. It seemed as if, apart from the divine shadow of 'God' and Li Fan, nothing else existed in this realm.

As Li Fan observed the divine shadow of 'God,' the divine shadow also perceived him. They were in a state of subtle opposition.

The descent into the abyss suddenly accelerated. In the silent flow, whispers gradually arose. Upon closer listening, they were Li Fan's own insights from before his encounter with 'God'!

It was as if, within the abyss of the divine shadow, countless other versions of himself awaited Li Fan's arrival.

"Return, return..."

As he was about to plunge into the divine shadow of 'God,' Li Fan seemed to have accepted his fate and calmly submitted. 'Return to Truth' remained silent, allowing Li Fan to proceed as he willed.

As he stepped into the abyss, the shadows Li Fan felt gradually grew larger. But the instinctive insights rising in his mind diminished.

His body was stretched infinitely; the front half continued to fall towards the divine shadow, while the latter half continued to fall. Li Fan patiently waited for himself to be fully absorbed by the divine shadow. He waited and waited...

After an unknown period, the surrounding illusory void of Mountains and Seas had been completely swallowed.

But... Li Fan's descent was still not complete!

"What's going on?"

"Is it taking too long?"

His absolute inner peace did not mean the complete loss of his thoughts. Instinctively, Li Fan's mind conjured a question. Thus, he began to ponder again. And he easily found the answer.

"Ah... it turns out it's because my True Spirit is infinite."

As if a stone had stirred a thousand waves, Li Fan's state of "calmness" after encountering 'God' was shattered.

"It seems..."

" 'God' is nothing special?"

The moment this thought arose, the world turned upside down!

"The East Sea can swallow all the waters of the world, but what if there is an uncreated source of water from the heavens?"

"Even with all the power of the East Sea, it would be difficult to match."

"Alas! In the end..."

"It is merely a shadow of 'God.'"

Li Fan sighed deeply in his heart. His infinite true spirit, which was still external, transformed into a large hand and gently pushed, forcibly pulling his own true spirit out of the divine shadow's devourment!

Moreover, the return of these rebellious true spirits seemed to carry certain shadows unique to 'God.' Previously, only 'God' swallowed the world; today, 'God' was being 'fleeced.'

The abyssal darkness, after a moment of silence, began to churn. It had possessed the demeanor of 'God,' passively waiting for all things in the world to fall into its abyss. Now, it actively exerted force, intending to swallow Li Fan!

Although he relied on his infinite true spirit to escape the descent previously, Li Fan now felt he could barely hold on against the divine shadow's active devouring.

"Let's see how the mere shadow of 'God' fares against the transformation of truth and falsehood."

Li Fan finally whispered the words 'Return to Truth' in his heart. The churning shadowy abyss stilled once more.

The seven characters 'When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth' appeared out of thin air in Li Fan's vision. Subsequently, they exploded, enveloping the universe. Everything seemed to be covered in a layer of mist, becoming indistinct.

Even the unfathomable divine shadow of 'God' was the same! But unlike the mountains and seas and myriad things that had fallen into stillness, the divine shadow of 'God' became even more active as the mist covered it!

Almost visibly, it lunged towards Li Fan! This was the first time Li Fan had been directly threatened by an external force after activating 'Return to Truth.' His heart couldn't help but skip a beat.

Just as the divine shadow of 'God' was about to touch Li Fan... A ray of light rose from within the white mist. Like a sharp sword, it slashed towards the lunging shadow. The shadow was instantly split in two, then submerged by the white mist, becoming indistinct once more. The divine shadow's only chance of victory vanished.

Li Fan, as usual, was swept away by 'Return to Truth,' restarting the cycle of Mountains and Seas.

...

This time, it seemed he had slept exceptionally long. When Li Fan's consciousness cleared, his mind was blank for a moment, and he couldn't recall his final experiences from the previous life. Only after sitting in a daze for a long time did he recall everything.

"Hiss..."

"After encountering the divine shadow of 'God,' my actions were somewhat reckless. It's not like my usual self. Was I influenced by something?"

Li Fan frowned deeply, pondering for a long time but finding no answer.

Rows of small text kept scrolling before his eyes, seemingly urging Li Fan to make a choice.

"Could it be that 'Return to Truth' has changed again?"

Li Fan suppressed the chaotic thoughts in his heart and focused on observing. Unfortunately, there were no significant changes compared to the previous life.

【This simulation has concluded】

【You may choose one of the following options to retain:

1. Your cultivation, possessions, or your mastered Dao Path from this simulation.

2. The simulation results of any favored companion from this simulation. This result can be overwritten onto the current Mountains and Seas.

3. A summary of the changes in Mountains and Seas from this simulation.

4. The strategy for the Star Splendor Rhythm from this simulation.

5. Forgo all choices and accelerate the recharge progress.】

...

"Logically speaking, the transformation between truth and falsehood is but a thought."

"Why can I only choose one out of four, and not all of them?"

Li Fan did not make a hasty decision but instead questioned 'Return to Truth.' Clearly, 'Return to Truth' would not answer Li Fan's question. The lines of text on the light screen continued to scroll, as if taunting Li Fan.

Li Fan, unfazed by the lack of response, did not rush to choose but first carefully examined the changes within 'Return to Truth.' His status had been reset to the anchor point, but 'Return to Truth' was different.

First, the 'Great Dao of Return to Truth' panel.

"Bu Jue has already entered."

"But the Great Dao of 'Longevity'..."

"Shou Qiu's premonition was indeed correct. There is indeed another 'Longevity' existence in some unknown place. Furthermore, the one who controls this 'Longevity' has reached an unfathomable realm, capable of resisting the influence of 'Great Dao of Return to Truth' to a certain extent."

The Great Dao of Longevity, though entered, was not fully assimilated. Other Dao characters were all in seven colors, and upon seeing them, Li Fan could comprehend the principles they expounded. But 'Longevity'... it was merely a transparent outline. Though it had the form of Longevity, it was clearly incomplete.

Witnessing this scene, Li Fan frowned slightly.

"It seems that 'Longevity' is not necessarily a good thing within the hall of 'Return to Truth.'"

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, the already transparent 'Longevity' characters suddenly disappeared, as if vanishing into thin air. Li Fan's heart stirred, and upon active recall, it reappeared.

"It exists between truth and falsehood, between reality and illusion, truly marvelous!" Li Fan couldn't help but exclaim.

"I wonder who the true master of Longevity is."

In the previous life, under the 'Concentric Unity' with Shou Qiu, Li Fan had learned some of Shou Qiu's speculations regarding this matter.

"It exists at the very beginning of Mountains and Seas, a time so ancient that Shou Qiu himself had not yet been born, possibly even during the initial separation of God's power in Mountains and Seas."

"Perhaps it suffered severe injuries during this conflict."

"The main body did not fall into the evolution of Mountains and Seas over time, but a fragment fell into Mountains and Seas..."

Li Fan suddenly became lost in thought. Although there was no concrete evidence, the fact that it could contend with the limitations of 'Great Dao of Return to Truth' already proved the extraordinary nature of the true master of Longevity.

"Perhaps it is not inferior to the Three Saints. Such a being is best not provoked for now."

Returning to the anchor point and starting anew, Li Fan regained his characteristic caution.

"Besides the two Great Daos, there is also the Xuanji Ring."

"And the divine shadow of 'God.'"

In the final moments of the previous life, Li Fan had stared at the divine shadow of 'God.' Moreover, he had used the great fire of True Spirit to break through its surface, directly confronting its core. Because he had a clear understanding of its nature.

"It is not the true shadow of the Creator God who has already perished."

"Rather, it is an artifact created by the Three Saints using their unfathomable power to materialize the concept of 'God.'"

"Although not a physical entity, the Three Saints' creative prowess was so profound that this created shadow already possessed some of 'God's' power."

"If... if the Three Saints were to further their understanding of Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm, or even assimilate the transformation of truth and falsehood, perhaps they would create not a shadow of 'God,' but the body of 'God.'"

The divine shadow of 'God' represented the core of the Three Saints' comprehensions. Therefore, upon sensing that others were attempting to probe it, they had disregarded everything else and rushed to stop it. However, upon realizing that the core of the divine shadow had been exposed and the situation could no longer be salvaged, and possessing full knowledge of the destruction the divine shadow's manifestation would bring to Mountains and Seas, they abandoned their pursuit.

It was indeed worthy of its name. Once manifested, the divine shadow of 'God' drew everything in Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm into its abyss. It was as if the Creator 'God' sought to be reborn through its shadow. Only Li Fan, not only with his infinite true spirit but also by temporarily resisting the assimilation by the divine shadow of 'God,' managed to extract something from it.

"Gaining one is to gain all."

"This fragmented point is the divine shadow of 'God' itself."

"It is like the mold created by the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel. With this, and the assistance of the other two Saints, the Xuanji Ring can be recreated."

In the subsequent confrontation with 'Return to Truth,' the complete defeat of the divine shadow of 'God' undoubtedly proved that it was merely a shadow, incapable of rivaling 'Return to Truth.' Naturally, it could not be ignored by 'Return to Truth,' and it still existed within the reset Li Fan.

But... Li Fan closed his eyes slightly. The next moment, the infinite true spirit within him seemed to boil. As if re-experiencing the pull and descent into the abyss, his body and soul remained mortal. However, the infinite true spirit had silently dissipated outwards.

In the void, there seemed to be an invisible mold. After Li Fan's true spirit flowed quietly, a phantom image gradually stood erect. Compared to the divine shadow of 'God' created by the Three Saints, this one appeared much more ordinary.

"The divine shadow of 'God' is the Three Saints' deconstruction of 'God.'"

"But this phantom image is my deconstruction of the divine shadow of 'God,' shaped by my previous true spirit infusion."

"Although inferior in other aspects, it is blessed by the transformation of truth and falsehood..."

"It possesses a unique charm."

"Sufficient to create the Xuanji Ring!"

Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp glint, speaking with great confidence. This phantom image, unlike the oppressive divine shadow of 'God' created by the Three Saints, which sought to devour all things in Mountains and Seas, seemed to exist between reality and illusion, ethereal and unpredictable. It hovered above Li Fan's head like a phantom.

The Great Xuan, the Xuanhuang Realm, even the Primordial Era and the surrounding Mountains and Seas were all reflected within it. Like countless carving knives, they sculpted the phantom image, leaving imperceptible but profound marks.

As the creator of the phantom image, Li Fan could clearly observe the changes occurring within it moment by moment.

"This divine shadow of 'God' is the manifestation of my comprehension. But after its birth, it can also actively help me comprehend everything it comes into contact with."

"Although not comparable to the comprehension of 'Return to Truth'..."

"It is not far off."

The phantom image acted like a mirror, allowing Li Fan to observe Mountains and Seas. His comprehension seemed to have increased tenfold!

"This change is the touch of brilliance from the transformation of truth and falsehood."

"My comprehension of the transformation of truth and falsehood is like understanding all the principles of the world. However, in the past, I needed to actively convert them. Now, with the help of the divine shadow of 'God,' this trouble is eliminated."

"If I had obtained this at the beginning of my cultivation, I would have been overjoyed. Unfortunately..."

"At the Saint realm, innate talent and comprehension are no longer the deciding factors."

"Although it can temporarily bridge the gap between myself and the Three Saints, to truly contend with the Three Saints..."

"I still need the assistance of 'Return to Truth.'"

Li Fan was very clear-headed.

Chapter 1709: The Method of Becoming a Saint in Mountains and Seas

The perspective of a Saint is by no means comparable to that of ordinary beings.

Especially in the previous life, Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Bu Jue, the Three Saints, sat together within the Xuanji Ring, united in heart and mind, as if a single entity.

Li Fan's own strength had improved a thousandfold compared to before.

Although he was still a mortal in this life, having not yet chosen to inherit, he could now shape the divine shadow of 'God' merely by perceiving and utilizing his infinite true spirit.

This was the result of the combined efforts of the Three Saints.

"Therefore..."

"This life, there is no need to choose to inherit cultivation. Not to mention that my comprehension of the Great Dao of 'Universe Cycle' has reached perfection, even any single item within 'Great Dao of Return to Truth' could help me attain Sainthood."

"I will rely purely on myself, starting from a mortal, to reach the Saint realm step by step."

As Li Fan's thoughts flowed, the divine shadow of 'God' seemed to sense something, its radiance swirling and reflecting more scenes.

"The divine shadow of 'God' is currently observing the Mountains and Seas at the anchor point."

"In my previous life, I also sat within the Xuanji Ring on the Other Shore and witnessed the changes in Mountains and Seas over time."

"The difference between these two..."

Li Fan's eyes flickered, he did not immediately make a distinction but began to cultivate again, starting from the mortal realm.

What 'Xian Fan Zhang,' what 'Dharma Transmission Pressure,' what 'rules and restrictions' – all these seemed fragile as paper to the current Li Fan.

Easily shattered with a flick of his finger.

Li Fan re-cultivated from the mortal realm, transcending the Great Xuan, ascending the Xuanhuang Realm, breaking through high walls, and surpassing the Primordial Era.

He reached transcendence and re-entered Mountains and Seas in just over five hundred years.

Though his path was slow, his progress was steady.

Yet, as Li Fan re-cultivated, he frequently utilized Shou Qiu's 'Observing Mountains and Seas' technique to survey the potential of the Primordial possibilities, discovering a most interesting phenomenon, which indirectly confirmed his long-held suspicions.

Li Fan's transformation from mortal to transcendent, step by step, surprisingly did not deplete the potential of the Primordial Era!

"Over five hundred years, apart from me, no other powerful beings have emerged from the Primordial Era. The potential of the Primordial Era has only slightly diminished. Compared to other possibilities, it remains far superior!"

Merging his consciousness with Shou Qiu's, he also gained answers to many secrets.

For instance, the reason for the anomaly in the potential of the Primordial Era.

"It is indeed the merit of Emperor Tian Luo. However, the attempts of the Primordial Immortal Realm to transcend..."

"Are still unknown."

"The Saints on the Other Shore reside in the Xuanji Ring and can observe Mountains and Seas closely. But the Primordial Immortal Realm vanished from the sight of the Saints of Mountains and Seas in the past in one fell swoop."

"Perhaps destroyed by the Void Realm, or returned to the Stars. Or perhaps..."

"It truly transcended the system of Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm, reaching the height of 'God' in ancient times, achieving an alternative form of freedom, which is not impossible."

"Even the Three Saints are not omniscient and omnipotent. This is also the basis of my confidence in confronting them."

Returning to the anchor point and starting anew, Li Fan regained his characteristic caution.

"As for the infinite true spirit and intuition..."

"Shou Qiu believes it is not strongly related to my identity as a traverser but rather has a great connection to the cycles of 'Return to Truth' I have experienced."

Recalling this, Li Fan suddenly fell silent.

Even his steps, about to enter Mountains and Seas, involuntarily halted.

"In the endless cycles woven by 'Universe Cycle,' I experienced illusory premonitions that resonated with my intuition."

"Of course, this does not mean I have truly experienced all this. It is merely that during the momentary transformation between truth and falsehood in Mountains and Seas, countless possibilities have already unfolded. As the only being in Mountains and Seas who retains memories before and after the drastic changes, I may have unknowingly witnessed many things."

"This also explains why 'Return to Truth' specifically chose me. Even if Prying Opportunity tried to snatch it, he couldn't move it an inch."

"'Return to Truth' had already seen through endless possibilities long ago. Only I, only me."

"Can achieve 'Return to Truth's' desired goal together."

"It is not solely because I possess infinite true spirit."

...

Li Fan's thoughts churned, while 'Return to Truth' remained silent as ever.

Ultimately, the entire Mountains and Seas, apart from 'Return to Truth' itself, could only speculate.

However, Li Fan believed that the day he discovered the answer was not far off.

Where do I come from? Where do I go? Why do I live?

Without resolving these questions, how can one speak of freedom and longevity?

Suppressing his thoughts, Li Fan took his halted steps, re-entering Mountains and Seas.

There was the barrier of Dao Annihilation, but also the interconnected veins of Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan walked slowly, his destination not the Other Shore.

Instead, he decided to leisurely stroll through Mountains and Seas first.

In the past, in order to find the location of the Other Shore, Li Fan had divided his consciousness into countless streams, sailing to various parts of Mountains and Seas in search of possible traces.

This targeted search had made him overlook the scenery along the way.

Mountains and Seas themselves.

In this life, Li Fan temporarily set aside all distracting thoughts and observed the unfolding of everything in Mountains and Seas from a purely observational perspective.

At the same time, he mentally chanted, finally selecting the inheritance option he had contemplated for over five hundred years.

"Option three: A summary of the changes in Mountains and Seas from this simulation!"

Li Fan stated with certainty.

The flickering characters suddenly stopped.

Li Fan's 'Return to Truth' panel seemed to fall into a strange stillness, even the light dimmed.

Then, countless points of light floated from the darkness, converging like a sea of stars, composing a long scroll!

There were no words, no images.

Only constantly flashing starlight!

Each beam of light seemed to contain unimaginable, vast information.

This was a detailed record of the possibilities observed by 'Return to Truth.'

The entire sea of stars, with its countless lights combined, represented the changes in Mountains and Seas!

For a transcendent being to read the summary of changes in Mountains and Seas was akin to seeking their own humiliation.

Li Fan's form instantly shattered, and his spirit dissolved.

But Li Fan showed no panic.

Such an anomaly was within his expectations.

"It is precisely by using the changes in Mountains and Seas that I can seize the opportunity for sainthood in this life!"

Without a physical form, only his true spirit dissipated.

In the past, Li Fan would have certainly panicked and hastily activated 'Return to Truth.'

But having experienced the descent into the abyss and the encounter with the divine shadow of 'God' in the previous life, Li Fan was now remarkably calm.

"Even Saints cannot fully observe the entirety of Mountains and Seas."

"But I can use my infinite true spirit..."

"To sculpt Mountains and Seas!"

As the thought arose, the infinite true spirit, against the backdrop of the starlight displayed by 'Return to Truth,' slowly took shape.

It formed a 'Map of Mountains and Seas'!

Infinite True Spirit, Infinite Mountains and Seas.

The Map of Mountains and Seas was also infinite.

The infinite true spirit could bear the infinitude of Mountains and Seas.

Though the Map of Mountains and Seas was infinite, it originated from the infinite true spirit.

Therefore, Li Fan could comprehend it all at once.

"Attaining Sainthood, in reality, has another path."

Although he lacked power and only had wisps of consciousness lingering before this map, Li Fan felt an unprecedented sense of strength.

"Without external help, without other methods."

"Only through myself, becoming one with Mountains and Seas."

Instantly, like the clash of wind and thunder, immense waves of infinite true spirit surged.

From the infinite Map of Mountains and Seas, a figure slowly emerged.

It was Li Fan himself!

Simultaneously, in the real Mountains and Seas, something seemed to have been sensed.

All possibilities trembled in unison!

On the Other Shore, in the Grand Palace of Tai Xu.

All the Saints cast their gazes upon Li Fan at the same moment.

Even the usually stoic Three Saints showed a flicker of surprise in their eyes.

Because what they saw was another Mountains and Seas!

"This... did we see incorrectly?"

"Did a new Saint suddenly emerge in Mountains and Seas?"

"And He..."

"Esteemed colleagues, did I perhaps see incorrectly?"

...

Li Fan ignored the gazes from all directions and silently contemplated his current state.

Having returned to the Saint realm, and far more powerful than the Saints of Xuanpin and Zhou Hui in his previous life.

Even 'Return to Truth,' which had always remained silent, transmitted subtle fluctuations, as if in praise, or perhaps with some other special meaning hidden within.

Li Fan simply smiled faintly in response, then his expression turned solemn, and he began to expound the Dao!

His voice boomed like thunder, echoing throughout the universe.

All beings and all possibilities in Mountains and Seas could now hear him.

"The world has the Upper Mountain and the Infinite Sea, sustaining countless beings."

"Sainthood is to become one with Mountains and Seas."

"For beings of Mountains and Seas to aspire to Sainthood, one may unify all forms of self, seek the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, or establish a new lineage."

"Alternatively..."

"Become one with Mountains and Seas."

...

In Li Fan's words, a vast and boundless Map of Mountains and Seas slowly manifested.

Initially, the beings did not understand Li Fan's meaning, but upon seeing the Map of Mountains and Seas, they gradually comprehended.

Since Sainthood is to become one with Mountains and Seas, then as long as this standard is met, one naturally becomes a Saint!

The beings were enlightened, but then became confused again.

Was this not simply stating the obvious?

If it were that easy to become one with Mountains and Seas, everyone would have become a Saint long ago.

It was precisely because it was impossible that they sought other methods.

They initially thought this newly emerged Saint of Mountains and Seas had come to expound the Dao, but instead, he was outwardly showing off!

At this moment, countless thoughts of this nature arose among the beings.

Li Fan ignored them.

Indeed, this method of sanctification was unique to him in the entire Mountains and Seas.

Otherwise, he would not have shamelessly shared it so openly.

First, one needs the 'Summary of Mountains and Seas Changes,' which meticulously records all specific data and information within Mountains and Seas.

Then, a target vessel is needed to contain this massive data.

Even the Three Saints dared not claim to have fully comprehended the secrets of Mountains and Seas.

But 'Return to Truth' could achieve this.

And only infinite true spirit could bear the infinite changes of Mountains and Seas and transform them for one's own use.

'Return to Truth' and infinite true spirit.

Unified within one person, this gave rise to such an incredible method of achieving Sainthood!

To become one with Mountains and Seas, body and Mountains and Seas as one!

"Congratulations, Fellow Daoist, on attaining the Dao today."

Amidst the beings' thoughts, Li Fan's figure gradually faded.

On the Other Shore, the phantom image of Tai Yi actually left the Xuanji Ring to personally congratulate Li Fan.

After all, such a heaven-shattering method of attaining the Dao was witnessed for the first time even by the Three Saints.

They could not immediately discern how Li Fan had achieved it, so they used congratulating him as an opportunity to probe further.

But Li Fan was no longer the same as before.

In the past, he could be easily seen through by the Three Saints.

Even while wearing the guise of a Saint, he was constantly apprehensive, fearing his thoughts would be exposed.

But now...

Standing firm like a mountain, unfathomable and mysterious.

Tai Yi observed Li Fan, feeling as if he were the embodiment of Mountains and Seas.

Boundless and immeasurable, difficult to speculate.

He couldn't help but feel even more perplexed.

To achieve Sainthood through the Dao of Mountains and Seas, the world should only have Lianshan and Guihai as Saints.

Where did this new Saint of Mountains and Seas come from?

Tai Yi, who shared the same heart as Lianshan and Guihai, naturally felt the familiar aura of Mountains and Seas emanating from Li Fan.

It was undoubtedly genuine!

Amidst his shock, he heard Li Fan calmly reply.

"Attaining the Dao is a trivial matter..."

"What is there to celebrate?"

Even after living for countless years, very few things could stir Tai Yi's emotions.

But upon hearing Li Fan's words, Tai Yi could barely suppress the anger that surged within him.

"Moreover, Mountains and Seas are already in a precarious state. After becoming a Saint, the responsibilities will only increase."

"True freedom will be further out of reach!"

Li Fan sighed lightly.

This statement, however, slightly shifted Tai Yi's perception of Li Fan.

"Perhaps you would care to visit the Other Shore?"

Tai Yi's phantom image invited.

Before he finished speaking, Li Fan looked up towards the Other Shore within Mountains and Seas.

"That would be acceptable."

After a moment of silence, he nodded in agreement.

The radiance of the Other Shore illuminated Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan, having attained Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, naturally perceived the location of the Other Shore the moment he became a Saint.

Tai Yi harbored no suspicion about this.

With the strength of two Saints, the boundless Mountains and Seas were like bình địa.

They quickly arrived outside the Other Shore, but Li Fan suddenly stopped.

He inexplicably smiled at Tai Yi's phantom image.

"Within this ring, there seems to be a unique mystery."

Li Fan spoke meaningfully.

Tai Yi's phantom image was about to explain, but was surprised when Li Fan walked directly into the ring, momentarily stunned.

"This individual is indeed quite interesting..." he muttered to himself, following Li Fan in.

Within the Xuanji Ring, all the Saints on the Other Shore turned their gazes upon Li Fan.

Li Fan, no longer possessing the initial trepidation and fear he felt upon first meeting the Saints, calmly accepted their stares.

His form, sculpted from Mountains and Seas, and having achieved Sainthood, was difficult to assess in terms of combat power, but at the very least, none of the Saints present could see through him.

Even if the Three Saints themselves were present, it would be the same.

"It is fortunate for us that a new Saint has emerged within Mountains and Seas."

The phantom image of Lianshan was the first to break the silence.

"I have existed for an eternity, yet I never imagined someone could attain the Dao through 'Mountains and Seas.' May I ask how you accomplished this, Fellow Daoist? Could you enlighten us?"

The phantom image of Guihai, usually taciturn, spoke directly, asking the question.

"It is both difficult and easy. It is merely a matter of the four words, 'Comprehend Mountains and Seas.'"

Li Fan did not refuse, stating it simply.

"'Comprehend Mountains and Seas?'"

The phantom images of all the Saints froze slightly, their expressions varied as they pondered the meaning.

"'Comprehend Mountains and Seas,' well said. With all our efforts, and 'Heavenly Creation's Pillar,' we could only attain either Lianshan or Guihai. Yet, with a few casual words, you have surpassed us. What great power you possess!"

Guihai exclaimed loudly, his words carrying a hint of contention.

It was not unreasonable for Saint Guihai to have such a peculiar attitude.

The Three Saints had existed since the primordial era of Mountains and Seas, for an unimaginably long time, witnessing the birth and destruction of countless beings.

They believed they had thoroughly understood the limits of what beings in Mountains and Seas could achieve.

Achieving Sainthood from mortality was already difficult.

As for Li Fan's method of attaining the Dao...

It was simply unheard of, and more importantly, defied common sense.

Could there truly be such a monstrous talent in Mountains and Seas?

Or perhaps...

The Three Saints instinctively began to doubt.

As if sensing the doubts in the hearts of the Three Saints, Li Fan calmly and righteously stated, "It's not a matter of great power. Although I attained Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, I can only grasp the 'form' of Mountains and Seas, not its 'spirit' like the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai."

"Lianshan sculpts bones, Guihai cleanses hearts. Standing at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas, there might be potential for further advancement. As for me..."

Li Fan sighed regretfully, "My limit is merely to be as one with Mountains and Seas."

His tone was filled with heartbreak and regret.

Li Fan's attainment of Sainthood through Mountains and Seas indeed made it difficult to transcend Mountains and Seas and advance further.

But these were obvious words.

In the entire Mountains and Seas, aside from the legendary 'God,' who else dared claim to be above Mountains and Seas?

To stand at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas, was he still not satisfied?

Within the Xuanji Ring, a peculiar atmosphere began to brew.

The intentions of all the Saints towards this newly emerged Saint of Mountains and Seas, who displayed heaven-defying talent and suddenly attained the Dao, were varied.

But soon, their attention was completely captivated by the scene Li Fan subsequently presented.

It was a scroll depicting an endless Map of Mountains and Seas!

"Everyone, observe. This is the foundation of my Dao!"

Li Fan waved his hand gently, unfurling a scroll.

Light and shadow flowed incessantly, dreamlike and illusory, appearing both real and false, making it difficult to distinguish.

For a time, it even suppressed the Xuanji Ring's white light, making the assembled Saints feel as if they were truly within Mountains and Seas.

"This is..."

"The Mountains and Seas within my eyes!"

"What do you all think?"

Li Fan stood with his hands behind his back before the endless Map of Mountains and Seas.

His faint words echoed endlessly within the Xuanji Ring.

Yet, no one responded.

All the Saints' divine senses were already immersed in this endless landscape of light and shadow.

Sweeping their divine senses across it, the Saints were horrified to discover that the depicted Map of Mountains and Seas was indistinguishable from the real Mountains and Seas!

There might be minor differences, but Mountains and Seas themselves were in constant flux.

Regardless of scale or magnitude, Li Fan's Map of Mountains and Seas seemed to be a microcosm of the true Mountains and Seas.

Not only the current Mountains and Seas, but all observable Mountains and Seas, from ancient times to the present!

Though it was merely a shadow of Mountains and Seas, lacking specific details and divine essence, it was already incredibly miraculous.

"Fellow Daoist, who exactly are you?"

The phantom image of Lianshan slowly asked.

All the Saints' gazes converged, awaiting Li Fan's answer.

"Me?"

Under the collective pressure of the Saints' gazes, Li Fan remained unfazed.

"My name is Li Fan, merely a humble mortal from the Great Xuan Realm."

"I am even from the same possibility as Fellow Daoist Shou Qiu."

"As for why I can observe all of Mountains and Seas..."

"It's simply because I can see further than ordinary people."

Li Fan's ambiguous answer did not convince the Saints.

"'See further than ordinary people?'"

Saint Guihai snorted lightly.

Seeing that the Saints did not believe him, Li Fan feigned looking towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas.

Although he claimed to be looking, his eyes were tightly closed.

"The Void Realm is vast and can block Saints, but my gaze can occasionally penetrate the Void Realm, allowing me to see more of Mountains and Seas."

"For instance..."

After a brief silence, Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes, a sharp glint within them.

"Ahead in Mountains and Seas, the demise of your three forms!"

Extending his finger, he traced a line across the phantom images of Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi.

"The demise of the Three Saints!"

Upon hearing Li Fan utter such a world-shattering prophecy, everyone present was stunned.

The atmosphere within the Xuanji Ring suddenly dropped to freezing point.

Those who were unaware suspected Li Fan had come to deliberately provoke them.

The Three Saints of Lianshan, who had been named, were about to say something.

But suddenly, their expressions shifted.

Following the direction Li Fan had indicated, they all looked towards the same point.

Their expressions gradually became extremely grave.

"Fellow Daoist, have you seen how we met our demise?"

After a long pause, Lianshan asked.

His attitude had subtly changed.

"Void Realm Incarnation."

Li Fan enunciated each word, uttering this sentence.

"So that's how it is."

As if sighing, the phantom image of Lianshan instantly became substantial.

He had returned from the depths of the Void Realm.

Then came Guihai and Tai Yi.

The other Saints also returned one after another.

The demise of the Three Saints was a matter of great importance.

The operation to reconnect Mountains and Seas in the Void Realm had to be halted.

Because no one knew if another Void Realm Incarnation would descend upon the current Mountains and Seas, and kill the Three Saints!

"Could it be that what this Saint of Mountains and Seas said is actually true?"

On the Other Shore, the other Saints who had been brought back by the Three Saints looked at Li Fan with surprise in their eyes, tinged with hidden worry.

After all, the Three Saints were the strongest among them.

If even they could not guarantee their lives...

"Although we possess the divine ability of 'Boundless Indestructibility,' it is ultimately a last resort. Each time we 'lose' the fortune obtained from reconnecting Mountains and Seas, the potential peak strength we can achieve diminishes slightly. We should not perish unless absolutely necessary."

Tai Yi spoke slowly, setting the tone.

"We are about to perish, yet we have not. Even ants cling to life... We must save ourselves."

Saint Guihai also said gravely.

"But Mountains and Seas have not yet been reconnected. If we forcefully leave now, firstly, we will not gain the merit of reconnecting Mountains and Seas, and our strength will not improve significantly. We might fail to save the situation and lose our own lives. Secondly, traveling to ancient Mountains and Seas is blocked by the Void Realm. Perhaps even the phantom images of the Xuanji Ring cannot remain. If Mountains and Seas lack our presence now..."

Lianshan surveyed everyone present and shook his head slightly.

Li Fan seemed to understand the thoughts of the Three Saints and smiled.

"It matters not. I have a plan that can resolve your concerns."

"Oh?"

Under the confused gazes of the Three Saints, Li Fan calmly revealed his solution.

"We only need to reconnect Mountains and Seas before the Void Realm Incarnation descends."

Tai Yi frowned slightly.

"Even with your assistance, reconnecting Mountains and Seas is not something one person can achieve alone..."

Li Fan waved his hand.

"Allow me to inform you all, the reason my sight can penetrate the Void Realm is thanks to this!"

Saying this, as if plucking stars and moon, Li Fan beckoned towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas.

Like stars descending from the heavens, a vast river formed.

Under the public gaze, the endless accumulated true spirits within the Void Realm were summoned and gathered around Li Fan.

The once-hollow Map of Mountains and Seas, which lacked spirit but possessed form, became more vibrant with the appearance of these accumulated true spirits.

"Hmm?!"

The astonishment of all the Saints surpassed that of moments ago.

"Fellow Daoist can actually summon and control the accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm?"

The voice of Saint Lianshan grew several decibels louder.

Not to mention the other Saints within the Xuanji Ring.

Their expressions were a mixture of awe and disbelief.

After all, a Saint of Mountains and Seas was merely a stronger Saint.

To them, it was merely replacing three Saints with four.

But Li Fan's ability to summon and utilize accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm was entirely different.

"If it were only this, how could it demonstrate my divine abilities?"

Li Fan declared proudly.

"Accumulated true spirits are inexhaustible. Their usefulness to us is ordinary. Only when they become sustenance for Saints..."

"The more, the better!"

Saying this, Li Fan looked towards the real Mountains and Seas.

His gaze swept around as if searching for something.

"Could it be..."

Seeing Li Fan's actions, the Saints seemed to guess something.

But they could not believe it and remained silent, awaiting Li Fan's performance.

"I possess a method to infuse the accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm into Saints, using them to establish Sainthood!"

Saying this, Li Fan found Jin Gui.

Having existed in the transcendent realm for countless years and being only one step away from achieving Sainthood, he was unable to cross the final threshold of the great chasm.

Now, captured by Li Fan, he was initially terrified.

However, upon seeing the Saints on the Other Shore present, he immediately paid his respects.

Before he could finish his greetings, Li Fan placed a hand on his head.

"Everyone, witness this with peace of mind."

Boundless true spirits, as if alive, surged into Jin Gui's body under Li Fan's guidance!

Under the watchful eyes of the Saints, a stubborn stone gradually transformed into a fine jade!

In a short while, the new Saint Jin Gui was born within the Xuanji Ring.

"Thank you, Senior, for this creation!"

The newly appointed Saint Jin Gui was overwhelmed with gratitude.

The remaining Saints remained speechless for a long time.

In such a short period, Li Fan had delivered one shocking revelation after another.

Attaining Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, his sight penetrating the Void Realm to reach ancient Mountains and Seas, his ability to summon and utilize accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm.

Furthermore, his ability to transform them for his own use and enlighten Saints.

All these abilities were concentrated in one individual!

Even the Three Saints would need considerable time to accept and process this.

"Delay leads to change. The Three Saints ahead are nearing their end!"

Li Fan sighed softly, interrupting the Saints' contemplation.

The newly appointed Jin Gui was startled but unsure how to react, remaining silent.

The Three Saints had finally made a decision.

"Let us reconnect Mountains and Seas as soon as possible."

This time, after Li Fan achieved Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, his ability to summon and utilize accumulated true spirits became even more proficient.

Even after enlightening Jin Gui, he felt no strain.

Just like in the previous life, he found Daode and Bai Xiao separately and enlightened them.

With the combined strength of the Saints, Mountains and Seas were quickly reconnected.

Amidst roaring sounds, Mountains and Seas naturally began to recover their vitality.

All the Saints benefited greatly from this.

However, none of their expressions became relaxed.

All because of Li Fan's words.

"The demise of the Three Saints lies ahead."

Li Fan looked towards the more ancient segment of Mountains and Seas ahead and spoke softly.

Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi sensed for a moment and all nodded slightly.

"The Void Realm Incarnation should have descended. However, our deaths are not imminent. We must plan carefully."

Guihai stated after observing for a long time.

"Although we have gained the fortune of a segment of Mountains and Seas, we do not have a definitive advantage. Of course, if we could gain more assistance..."

Tai Yi looked at Li Fan.

Li Fan said, "I still have some capacity left. Those who can be enlightened in this place can all be illuminated by me. With our combined efforts, reconnecting Mountains and Seas would be a trivial matter. But..."

Li Fan paused before speaking sternly, "As Elder Guihai mentioned, the battle with the Void Realm Incarnation is not a matter of days. Six Saints in battle, if without protection, could even affect Mountains and Seas."

"Furthermore..."

"The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting the Three Saints ahead. If we were to offer our assistance and fail, who knows if the Void Realm would send even stronger Void Realm Incarnations? We may have the strength for one battle, but do we have the strength for a second or third?"

Facing Li Fan's questions, all the Saints fell silent.

After all, except for the Three Saints, none of them had truly encountered the so-called Void Realm Incarnations.

"Fellow Daoist Fan's considerations are indeed thorough. But please rest assured, if the Void Realm Incarnation is defeated swiftly, it will not reappear immediately. At the very least, it will give us some breathing room. And this 'breathing room,' in the timescale of the Void Realm, is an extremely long period from our perspective."

Guihai explained.

"As for affecting Mountains and Seas..."

The Three Saints exchanged glances and then looked at Li Fan, saying, "The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting us. Naturally, we shall deal with it ourselves."

"And with Fellow Daoist Fan presiding over Mountains and Seas, it should remain safe."

The Three Saints' answer was within Li Fan's expectations, but he shook his head slightly.

"I can enlighten Saints, but I cannot protect Mountains and Seas."

"Firstly, after continuous enlightenments, even Mountains and Seas have become somewhat depleted. Secondly, as you all saw earlier, the Map of Mountains and Seas only possesses the 'form' of Mountains and Seas, not its substance. To withstand the residual waves of battle..."

"I fear my strength is insufficient."

Li Fan said truthfully.

Chapter 1710: The Sage Appears Before the Mortal Saint

"Within this ring, there seems to be a different kind of wonder," Li Fan said with a profound implication.

Tai Yi's phantom image was about to explain, but Li Fan unexpectedly walked directly into it, leaving him stunned.

"This person is quite interesting indeed..." he muttered to himself, following Li Fan in.

Within the Xuanji Ring, the gazes of all the Saints on the Other Shore fell upon Li Fan.

Li Fan no longer possessed the apprehension and fear he felt upon first meeting the Saints, calmly accepting their stares.

With Mountains and Seas as his foundation, forging his saintly form. His true combat power was difficult to ascertain, but at the very least, none of the Saints present could see through him.

Even if the Three Saints themselves were present, it would be the same.

"It is fortunate for us that a new Saint has emerged within Mountains and Seas," the Lianshan phantom image was the first to break the silence in the hall.

"I have existed for an eternity, yet I never imagined someone could attain the Dao through 'Mountains and Seas.' May I ask how you accomplished this, Fellow Daoist? Could you enlighten us?" the Guihai phantom image, usually taciturn, spoke directly, asking the question.

"It is both difficult and easy. It is merely a matter of those four words, 'Comprehend Mountains and Seas.'" Li Fan did not refuse, stating it plainly.

"'Comprehend Mountains and Seas?'" The phantom images of all the Saints froze slightly, their expressions varied as they pondered the meaning within.

"'Comprehend Mountains and Seas,' well said. After exhausting all our efforts, along with the Pillar of Heavenly Creation, we could only achieve the attainment of Lianshan or Guihai. Yet, with a few casual words, you have surpassed us. What immense power you possess!" Guihai exclaimed loudly in admiration.

His words, however, carried a hint of contention.

The attitude of Saint Guihai was peculiar.

They believed they had thoroughly understood the limits of what beings in Mountains and Seas could achieve.

To ascend from mortal to Saint realm was already extremely difficult.

As for Li Fan's method of attestation...

It was simply unheard of, and more importantly, contrary to common sense!

Could there truly be such a monstrous talent in Mountains and Seas? Or perhaps...

The Three Saints instinctively began to doubt.

As if sensing the doubts in the hearts of the Three Saints, Li Fan calmly and righteously stated, "It is not a matter of immense power. Although I attained Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, I can only grasp the 'form' of Mountains and Seas, not its 'spirit,' unlike the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai."

"Lianshan sculpts bones, Guihai cleanses hearts. Standing at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas, there might be potential for further advancement. As for me..."

Li Fan sighed, shaking his head slightly. "My limit is merely to be as one with Mountains and Seas."

His tone was filled with heartbreak and regret.

Li Fan's attainment of Sainthood through Mountains and Seas indeed made it difficult to transcend Mountains and Seas and advance further.

But these were obvious words.

In the entire Mountains and Seas, aside from the legendary 'God,' who dared claim to be above Mountains and Seas?

To stand at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas, was he still not satisfied?

Within the Xuanji Ring, a peculiar atmosphere began to brew.

The intentions of all the Saints towards this newly emerged Saint of Mountains and Seas, who displayed heaven-defying talent and suddenly attained the Dao, were varied.

But soon, their attention was completely captivated by the scene Li Fan subsequently presented.

It was a scroll depicting an endless Map of Mountains and Seas!

"Everyone, observe. This is the foundation of my Dao!" Li Fan gently waved his hand, unfurling a scroll.

Light and shadow flowed incessantly, dreamlike and illusory, appearing both real and false, making it difficult to distinguish.

For a time, it even suppressed the Xuanji Ring's white light, making the assembled Saints feel as if they were truly within Mountains and Seas.

"This is..."

"The Mountains and Seas within my eyes!"

"What do you all think?"

Before the endless Map of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan stood with his hands behind his back.

His faint words echoed endlessly within the Xuanji Ring.

Yet, no one responded.

All the Saints' divine senses were already immersed in this endless landscape of light and shadow.

Sweeping their divine senses across it, the Saints were horrified to discover that the depicted Map of Mountains and Seas was indistinguishable from the real Mountains and Seas!

There might be minor differences, but Mountains and Seas themselves were in constant flux.

Regardless of scale or magnitude, Li Fan's Map of Mountains and Seas seemed to be a microcosm of the true Mountains and Seas.

Not only the current Mountains and Seas, but all observable Mountains and Seas, from ancient times to the present!

Though it was merely a shadow of Mountains and Seas, lacking specific details and divine essence, it was already incredibly miraculous.

"Fellow Daoist, who exactly are you?" the Lianshan phantom image slowly asked.

All the Saints' gazes converged, awaiting Li Fan's answer.

"Me?"

Under the collective pressure of the Saints' gazes, Li Fan remained unfazed.

"My name is Li Fan, merely a humble mortal from the Great Xuan Realm."

"I am even from the same possibility as Fellow Daoist Shou Qiu."

"As for why I can observe all of Mountains and Seas..."

"It's simply because I can see further than ordinary people."

Li Fan's ambiguous answer did not convince the Saints.

"'See further than ordinary people?'" Saint Guihai snorted lightly.

Seeing that the Saints did not believe him, Li Fan feigned looking towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas.

Although he claimed to be looking, his eyes were tightly closed.

"The Void Realm is vast and can block Saints, but my gaze can occasionally penetrate the Void Realm, allowing me to see more of Mountains and Seas."

"For instance..."

After a brief silence, Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes, a sharp glint within them.

"Ahead in Mountains and Seas, the demise of your three forms!"

Extending his finger, he traced a line across the phantom images of Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi.

"The demise of the Three Saints!"

Upon hearing Li Fan utter such a world-shattering prophecy, everyone present was stunned.

The atmosphere within the Xuanji Ring suddenly dropped to freezing point.

Those who were unaware suspected Li Fan had come to deliberately provoke them.

The Three Saints of Lianshan, who had been named, were about to say something.

But suddenly, their expressions shifted.

Following the direction Li Fan had indicated, they all looked towards the same point.

Their expressions gradually became extremely grave.

"Fellow Daoist, have you seen how we met our demise?" After a long pause, Lianshan asked.

His attitude had subtly changed.

"Void Realm Incarnation." Li Fan enunciated each word, uttering this sentence.

"So that's how it is."

As if sighing, the Lianshan phantom image instantly became substantial. He had returned from the depths of the Void Realm.

Then came Guihai and Tai Yi.

The other Saints also returned one after another.

The demise of the Three Saints was a matter of great importance.

The operation to reconnect Mountains and Seas in the Void Realm had to be halted.

Because no one knew if another Void Realm Incarnation would descend upon the current Mountains and Seas and kill the Three Saints!

"Could it be that what this Saint of Mountains and Seas said is actually true?" On the Other Shore, the other Saints who had been brought back by the Three Saints looked at Li Fan with surprise in their eyes, tinged with hidden worry.

After all, the Three Saints were the strongest among them. If even they could not guarantee their lives...

"Although we possess the divine ability of 'Boundless Indestructibility,' it is ultimately a last resort. Each time we 'lose' the fortune obtained from reconnecting Mountains and Seas, the potential peak strength we can achieve diminishes slightly. We should not perish unless absolutely necessary," Tai Yi spoke slowly, setting the tone.

"We are about to perish, yet we have not. Even ants cling to life... We must save ourselves," Saint Guihai also said gravely.

"But Mountains and Seas have not yet been reconnected. If we forcefully leave now, firstly, we will not gain the merit of reconnecting Mountains and Seas, and our strength will not improve significantly. We might fail to save the situation and lose our own lives. Secondly, traveling to ancient Mountains and Seas is blocked by the Void Realm. Perhaps even the phantom images of the Xuanji Ring cannot remain. If Mountains and Seas lack our presence now..." Lianshan surveyed everyone present and shook his head slightly.

Li Fan seemed to understand the thoughts of the Three Saints and smiled. "It matters not. I have a plan that can resolve your concerns."

"Oh?"

Under the confused gazes of the Three Saints, Li Fan calmly revealed his solution. "We only need to reconnect Mountains and Seas before the Void Realm Incarnation descends."

Tai Yi frowned slightly. "Even with your assistance, reconnecting Mountains and Seas is not something one person can achieve alone..."

Li Fan waved his hand. "Allow me to inform you all, the reason my sight can penetrate the Void Realm is thanks to this!"

Saying this, as if plucking stars and moon, Li Fan beckoned towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas.

Like stars descending from the heavens, a vast river formed.

Under the public gaze, the endless accumulated true spirits within the Void Realm were summoned and gathered around Li Fan.

The once-hollow Map of Mountains and Seas, which lacked spirit but possessed form, became more vibrant with the appearance of these accumulated true spirits.

"Hmm?!"

The astonishment of all the Saints surpassed that of moments ago.

"Fellow Daoist can actually summon and control the accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm?" The voice of Saint Lianshan grew several decibels louder.

Not to mention the other Saints within the Xuanji Ring. Their expressions were a mixture of awe and disbelief.

After all, a Saint of Mountains and Seas was merely a stronger Saint. To them, it was merely replacing three Saints with four. But Li Fan's ability to summon and utilize accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm was entirely different.

"If it were only this, how could it demonstrate my divine abilities?" Li Fan declared proudly.

"Accumulated true spirits are inexhaustible. Their usefulness to us is ordinary. Only when they become sustenance for Saints..."
