"The more, the better!"

Saying this, Li Fan looked towards the real Mountains and Seas. His gaze swept around as if searching for something.

"Could it be..." Seeing Li Fan's actions, the Saints seemed to guess something. But they could not believe it and remained silent, awaiting Li Fan's performance.

"I possess a method to infuse the accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm into Saints, using them to establish Sainthood!" Saying this, Li Fan found Jin Gui. Having existed in the transcendent realm for countless years and being only one step away from achieving Sainthood, he was unable to cross the final threshold of the great chasm. Now, captured by Li Fan, he was initially terrified. However, upon seeing the Saints on the Other Shore present, he immediately paid his respects. Before he could finish his greetings, Li Fan placed a hand on his head.

"Everyone, witness this with peace of mind." Boundless true spirits, as if alive, surged into Jin Gui's body under Li Fan's guidance! Under the watchful eyes of the Saints, a stubborn stone gradually transformed into a fine jade! In a short while, the new Saint Jin Gui was born within the Xuanji Ring.

"Thank you, Senior, for this creation!" The newly appointed Saint Jin Gui was overwhelmed with gratitude.

The remaining Saints remained speechless for a long time. In such a short period, Li Fan had delivered one shocking revelation after another. Attaining Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, his sight penetrating the Void Realm to reach ancient Mountains and Seas, his ability to summon and utilize accumulated true spirits of the Void Realm. Furthermore, his ability to transform them for his own use and enlighten Saints. All these abilities were concentrated in one individual! Even the Three Saints would need considerable time to accept and process this.

"Delay leads to change. The Three Saints ahead are nearing their end!" Li Fan sighed softly, interrupting the Saints' contemplation. The new Jin Gui was startled but unsure how to react, remaining silent.

The Three Saints had finally made a decision. "Let us reconnect Mountains and Seas as soon as possible." This time, after Li Fan achieved Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, his ability to summon and utilize accumulated true spirits became even more proficient. Even after enlightening Jin Gui, he felt no strain. Just like in the previous life, he found Daode and Bai Xiao separately and enlightened them. With the combined strength of the Saints, Mountains and Seas were quickly reconnected. Amidst roaring sounds, Mountains and Seas naturally began to recover their vitality. All the Saints benefited greatly from this. However, none of their expressions became relaxed. All because of Li Fan's words.

"The demise of the Three Saints lies ahead." Li Fan looked towards the more ancient segment of Mountains and Seas ahead and spoke softly. Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi sensed for a moment and all nodded slightly. "The Void Realm Incarnation should have descended. However, our deaths are not imminent. We must plan carefully," Guihai stated after observing for a long time. "Although we have gained the fortune of a segment of Mountains and Seas, we do not have a definitive advantage. Of course, if we could gain more assistance..." Tai Yi looked at Li Fan. Li Fan said, "I still have some capacity left. Those who can be enlightened in this place can all be illuminated by me. With our combined efforts, reconnecting Mountains and Seas would be a trivial matter. But..." Li Fan paused before speaking sternly, "As Elder Guihai mentioned, the battle with the Void Realm Incarnation is not a matter of days. Six Saints in battle, if without protection, could even affect Mountains and Seas." "Furthermore..." "The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting the Three Saints ahead. If we were to offer our assistance and fail, who knows if the Void Realm would send even stronger Void Realm Incarnations? We may have the strength for one battle, but do we have the strength for a second or third?" Facing Li Fan's questions, all the Saints fell silent. After all, except for the Three Saints, none of them had truly encountered the so-called Void Realm Incarnations. "Fellow Daoist Fan's considerations are indeed thorough. But please rest assured, if the Void Realm Incarnation is defeated swiftly, it will not reappear immediately. At the very least, it will give us some breathing room. And this breathing room, in the timescale of the Void Realm, is an extremely long period from our perspective," Guihai explained. "As for affecting Mountains and Seas..." The Three Saints exchanged glances and then looked at Li Fan, saying, "The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting us. Naturally, we shall deal with it ourselves." "And with Fellow Daoist Fan presiding over Mountains and Seas, it should remain safe." The Three Saints' answer was within Li Fan's expectations, but he shook his head slightly. "I can enlighten Saints, but I cannot protect Mountains and Seas." "Firstly, after continuous enlightenments, even Mountains and Seas have become somewhat depleted. Secondly, as you all saw earlier, the Map of Mountains and Seas only possesses the 'form' of Mountains and Seas, not its substance. To withstand the residual waves of battle..." "I fear my strength is insufficient," Li Fan said truthfully.

Chapter 1711: Li Fan Fights the Three Sages

"The danger that could cause the Three Saints to perish, the Mountains and Seas themselves might shatter under its impact.

'Other matters aside, even if I were to sacrifice my life, I could protect the Mountains and Seas. But if at a critical moment...'

'The Xuanji Ring here is shattered, what then?'

Li Fan's gaze swept across the assembled Saints, 'How many of you can guarantee you won't suddenly turn your coats?'

Under this cold questioning, no one responded for a time.

Li Fan had paused slightly the moment he first entered the Other Shore.

It was not strange that he could discern the profound mystery of the Xuanji Ring's concentricity.

It was just that he hadn't expected that at such a critical juncture, he would highlight it. Even under the influence of concentricity, the Saints couldn't help but feel a little awkward.

'We have been seated in the Xuanji Ring for countless years, we've long been like brothers. I believe even without the Xuanji Ring, there wouldn't be much change,' Prying Opportunity asserted with certainty.

'That's right. In the face of such critical matters as the survival of Mountains and Seas, we can distinguish right from wrong. If Mountains and Seas cease to exist, where would I go?'

Oracle Prediction, Divination, and other Saints nodded in agreement subsequently.

They swore oaths with conviction.

Clearly, they did not have a clear understanding of their original temperaments.

In the previous life, Li Fan had personally witnessed the actions of Prying Opportunity and other Saints after they lost their restraints; he merely chuckled and remained silent.

The Three Saints, however, fell into silence for a time, pondering something.

After a long while, interrupting the Saints' words: 'What Daoist Fan worries about is not unreasonable. If we manage to survive this calamity, yet cause Mountains and Seas to be ravaged...'

'That would be putting the cart before the horse.'

'Since that is the case...'

As the Three Saints spoke, they each took out the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel, placing them before Li Fan.

'Daoist Fan, you may wield these three items. Firstly, they can help protect Mountains and Seas and regulate the Saints. Secondly...'

'If the Xuanji Ring truly has the power to shatter, you can recreate the Xuanji with these three items.'

'At that time, you can invite Shou Qiu and Dao De to also take their seats. It should be without worry,' Saint Lianshan personally nominated.

Shou Qiu, having been named, remained expressionless, as if he had long anticipated it.

The newly appointed Saint Dao De, however, was clearly taken aback and repeatedly refused.

'If we do not pass this calamity, and still perish in the Void Realm. The matter of reconnecting Mountains and Seas will then rely on you, Daoist Fan.' Saint Tai Yi looked at Li Fan and spoke softly.

Li Fan looked at the three treasures before him, hesitating to respond for a long time.

Instead, he closed his eyes and began to ponder.

After a while, he suddenly spoke, 'I do have a thought.'

Under the gaze of all the Saints, Li Fan slowly opened his mouth: 'The Void Realm Incarnations originate from the Mountains and Seas devoured by the Void Realm. As for me, since the beginning of my cultivation, it has only been a little over five hundred years. The Mountains and Seas where I am located are safe and sound, thus there is no danger of Void Realm Incarnations.'

'Originally, with my strength, I was indeed not qualified to participate in the six-Saint battle. But...'

Li Fan pointed at the three treasures in front of him, then swept his gaze across the Xuanji Ring that illuminated the entire Other Shore: 'Why don't I, Dao De, and Shou Qiu, represent them and go to the Void Realm to assist the Three Saints through their calamity!'

These words were like a thunderclap.

Even the Three Saints of Lianshan had not anticipated Li Fan's decision, and were slightly stunned.

As for the other Saints in the Other Shore, they looked at Li Fan with great astonishment.

After all, the Three Saints were in danger of perishing and lacked the confidence to safely pass through the calamity. Ordinary Saints had even less ability to get involved. Perhaps they wouldn't even withstand the aftermath of the battle. They would most likely fail to rescue them and would be buried in the Void Realm instead.

In the eyes of all the Saints, Li Fan's actions were simply no different from suicidal!

Within the Xuanji Ring, the Saints had various expressions. Li Fan, however, calmly explained, 'The Three Saints have already said before that they would not gain the merit of reconnecting Mountains and Seas, so even if they went to support them in traversing the Void Realm, their strength would not increase significantly. It would still be three Saints against three Saints, not six Saints against three Saints.'

'At most, it would change from being at a disadvantage to being evenly matched. As for the final outcome, who wins and who loses, is still unknown.'

'But if it were us three going to support, it would be different.'

Li Fan continued, 'Although my combat strength is weak, relying on my True Spirit Infusion divine ability, I can actually perform better in the Void Realm. Not only can I divert the Void Realm Incarnations, but I can also help the Three Saints recover from their injuries. The situation would then become a true six Saints against three Saints.'

'Perhaps it would be more beneficial than the Three Saints going personally.'

'Furthermore, with the Three Saints guarding Mountains and Seas, no matter how great the disturbance in the Void Realm, I believe they can successfully quell it...'

After Li Fan's explanation, the Saints actually found some truth in it.

'I achieved Sainthood through Mountains and Seas. Although weaker than the Three Saints of Lianshan, I am certainly not weaker than the rest of you here. Therefore, who else but I should go?' Li Fan said proudly, not being modest at all at this moment.

The Saints witnessed Li Fan's bold declaration, their expressions varying.

Saint Lianshan was the first to speak, expressing his opposition.

'Daoist Fan, we appreciate your good intentions. However, the 'True Spirit Infusion' divine ability is unique to Mountains and Seas. It is of too great importance for reconnecting Mountains and Seas. Your safety cannot be compromised! We can perish inch by inch, but you must not meet with an accident.'

'In the worst-case scenario, we would lose the fortune of reconnecting several segments of Mountains and Seas. But if you continue to preside over the overall situation, and Mountains and Seas are fully reconnected, we can accept that.' Saint Guihai also did not agree with Li Fan's self-endangerment.

Li Fan chuckled, 'The Three Saints underestimate me. Moreover, the Void Realm Incarnations' target is the Three Saints, not me. Even if my support fails, escaping should not be difficult. I naturally understand my own importance. If the situation becomes unmanageable, I will naturally retreat early.'

Upon hearing this, the Three Saints truly began to consider the feasibility.

Li Fan saw this and added, 'Why don't we, within the Xuanji Ring, each send out an avatar and have a spar first? This way, the Three Saints will know our capabilities. How about it?'

Inside the Xuanji Ring, there was a sudden silence.

All the Saints looked at the Three Saints and Li Fan, their eyes filled with anticipation.

After all, it had been an unknown number of years since they had seen the Three Saints truly make a move.

And they were indeed quite curious about the strength of this 'Saint of Mountains and Seas.'

'Agreed!'

After a brief silence, the Three Saints agreed.

Just like the ordered competition in the previous life.

The Xuanji Ring shone brightly, and the Three Saints and Li Fan each flicked out a virtual particle, entering it.

Within the Xuanji Ring, obtaining one meant obtaining all.

Although they were merely virtual projections, they represented a large part of their full strength.

The Saints watched intently, afraid of missing any detail.

'It's not appropriate for us to bully the young. You go first,' the voice of Saint Lianshan came from afar in the projection.

The Three Saints, after all, had their reputation to maintain; they wouldn't attack Li Fan simultaneously.

And they even let Li Fan attack first.

Li Fan did not hold back either. From the start, he unleashed his strongest move, excluding the manipulation of truth and falsehood.

It was inspired by his observation of the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes' and his contemplation of Shou Qiu's 'Leveling Mountains and Seas' divine ability in his previous life.

Although the destructive power of the move was greatly reduced due to the absence of truth and falsehood manipulation, the ripples and impact it caused, amplified by countless realistic details within the Mountains and Seas, were even more profound!

In the Xuanji light circle, scenes of continuous Mountains and Seas surrounded Li Fan, rising into the air.

He roared, 'That won't be necessary. The situation is urgent, we need to finish this quickly. Three Saints...'

'Attack together!'

These words were uttered, and all the Saints watching in the Xuanji Ring couldn't help but look at Li Fan.

Some were surprised, some found it laughable, some frowned.

The Three Saints, however, chucked and said, 'Since Daoist Fan is so confident...'

'Finishing quickly is also good.'

They flicked their fingers towards the Xuanji light, and a gentle touch.

The three light spots of the Three Saints then moved.

Originally, Saints Guihai and Tai Yi were just observing, but now they both joined the battlefield.

Li Fan was instantly surrounded by the Three Saints.

But his expression remained unchanged, and he became even more excited.

His form flickered again, disappearing from sight.

Only endless phantom images of Mountains and Seas roared and surged forth.

They transformed into Li Fan's arms, intending to capture the Three Saints.

But such tricks naturally couldn't harm the opponents. The Three Saints remained motionless, as if separated by an invisible chasm, and the endless phantom images of Mountains and Seas, although always close, could never touch them.

They merely formed a circle around the Three Saints.

'Since I proved my Dao, I have witnessed the birth and destruction of countless Mountains and Seas. To injure you with the Dao of Mountains and Seas...' Saint Lianshan chuckled as he beheld the familiar scenes of Mountains and Seas in the Xuanji light.

But very quickly, his expression changed.

'The Three Saints do not know. This move of mine has a miraculous effect against you!'

Amidst the roaring of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan coldly uttered.

'Collapse!'

And then...

The mountains instantly collapsed, and the boundless seas boiled.

It was as if the calamity of Mountains and Seas' destruction had suddenly descended upon this place!

It was truly a great disaster. The endless Mountains and Seas were all affected at this moment, unable to escape.

This was not caused by the erosion of the Void Realm's Dao Annihilation.

This momentum of collapsing mountains and surging seas was, in fact, an internal change of the Mountains and Seas themselves.

From a logical standpoint, Mountains and Seas at such prosperity would never be destroyed without reason.

But now, Li Fan, as the Saint of Mountains and Seas, the master of this piece of Mountains and Seas, had, as if destroying his own Dao path, deliberately created this world-ending catastrophe!

Mountains and Seas divided their spirits, nurturing endless possibilities and endless beings.

And if it were to collapse during its full prosperity...

Then how terrifying would this catastrophe be?

At this moment, all the Saints within the Xuanji Ring were fortunate enough to witness it.

Although it was only a partial preview, it already allowed them to glimpse such unimaginably terrifying scenes.

Even the Three Saints could not escape!

Or rather, it was precisely because they were the Three Saints that they could not escape!

Saint Lianshan, ascended Mount Tai, the first immortal in the world. Always stood at the peak of the mountains, looking down on all living beings.

Saint Guihai, understood the infinite principle, opened the infinite spring. Majestic and unfathomable, immeasurable.

Saint Tai Yi, comprehended the Dao from innate spiritual beings, primordial to all things.

The divine power of the Three Saints was immeasurable.

But all their cultivation originated from Mountains and Seas.

Therefore, when Li Fan summoned the endless phantom images of Mountains and Seas, they instinctively sought to counter it.

The powers of both sides, originating from the same source, met at that moment.

Li Fan only had the phantom image of Mountains and Seas.

While the Three Saints possessed the spirit of Mountains and Seas.

Under normal circumstances, Li Fan would certainly not be the opponent of the Three Saints, and could not harm them in the slightest.

But now, he had deliberately triggered the self-destructive momentum of Mountains and Seas.

And once this world-ending catastrophe appeared, it would be impossible to stop!

The chain reaction ran through Mountains and Seas, coming from afar and arriving in an instant.

Mountains collapsed and seas surged, along with everything within Mountains and Seas, all perished.

The Xuanji Ring's light dimmed instantly and shattered inch by inch!

The competition between Li Fan and the Three Saints also came to an abrupt halt.

On the Other Shore, there was silence.

'Who won or lost?'

Finally, Bai Xiao couldn't help but break the silence and ask.

Shou Qiu sighed, 'Mountains and Seas are lost, so where is the victor? Daoist Fan's move was a bit too much against heavenly harmony.'

Inside the Xuanji Ring, similar to the real world.

Since Li Fan could use it within the Xuanji Ring, it meant he could also use this move in the real Mountains and Seas.

The implication was such that all the Saints' hearts skipped a beat.

Li Fan, however, chuckled and broke the stalemate.

'This method of sacrificing a thousand to injure eight hundred, how could I easily use it?'

'Furthermore, Mountains and Seas are now separated by Dao Annihilation. Even if I exert all my strength, I may not be able to induce its collapse. Moreover...'

'My ambition is to save Mountains and Seas, how could I truly use this move?'

'It was merely to prove to the Three Saints that I have the power to fight.'

'The events in the Void Realm will not affect the current Mountains and Seas. This move can serve as a surprise tactic, perhaps having the effect of stabilizing the situation.' Li Fan said solemnly.

In the Xuanji Ring competition, the Three Saints were brought to mutual destruction by Li Fan's 'Collapsing Mountains and Seas.'

But they did not lose their composure because of this.

Instead, they shook their heads and smiled, 'Daoist Fan's move can be used once, but not twice. It can indeed serve as a surprise tactic, but it can only be a surprise tactic.'

Bai Xiao curiously asked, 'What do Saint Lianshan mean by this?'

Without waiting for the Three Saints to speak, Li Fan explained himself, 'The Mountains and Seas I saw were actually not the Three Saints' Mountains and Seas. Merely by taking advantage of the Three Saints' instinctive counter-attack when facing the phantom images of Mountains and Seas, I unleashed my divine ability at lightning speed and caused Mountains and Seas to fall. If the Three Saints had been prepared, or knew I had this connection...'

'The boundaries are clear. If my Mountains and Seas were destroyed, it would not affect them in the slightest.'

'As Saint Lianshan said, it can only be used as a surprise tactic, only once.'

'I see...' After Li Fan's explanation, all the Saints secretly breathed a sigh of relief.

'Once is enough. Since it can deal with us, it will naturally be effective against the Void Realm Incarnations.'

The Three Saints seemed to have reached a decision, and finally agreed to Li Fan's plan.

'If I go alone, it is inevitable that I will be like a single leaf struggling against a strong current. Therefore, I need Shou Qiu and Dao De to accompany me.'

'As for why I chose them...' Li Fan looked at the other Saints within the Xuanji Ring, including Prying Opportunity.

He smiled slightly and did not elaborate further.

The Three Saints could understand Li Fan's thoughts and did not dwell on this matter.

'Even with ultimate skills, more preparations are needed before the actual journey.'

As the Three Saints spoke, Saint Tai Wei, as if sensing something, arrived like a rainbow.

Because there was no mistake in reconnecting Mountains and Seas, Saint Tai Wei this time produced a total of eighteen great elixirs.

Half of them were given to Li Fan.

Chapter 1712: Three People Reunite

'Daoist Fan's sermon on Mountains and Seas upon achieving Sainthood caused quite a stir in the Saint Dynasty, requiring considerable effort to quell it.' Before Saint Tai Wei departed, he suddenly uttered this.

Li Fan instantly understood the reason behind this.

The subjects of the Saint Dynasty lived forever under the protection of Saint Tai Wei, without disasters or misfortunes. Although it could be called happiness, they were completely unaware of anything outside the Saint Dynasty.

Beings like True Immortals, Nameless Ones, Transcended Ones, and even Mountains and Seas, were all unheard of to the subjects of the Saint Dynasty.

Li Fan's attainment of the Dao in one fell swoop revealed the secrets of the Saints of Mountains and Seas.

This led countless subjects of the Saint Dynasty to glimpse a world they should not have seen.

They learned that the Saint Emperor was not the greatest existence in all of Mountains and Seas, and that they too could become as strong as the Saint Emperor.

Even surpass him!

The hearts of the people were stirred, and the stability of the peaceful Saint Dynasty was disrupted.

Although it was decisively suppressed by the Saint Emperor Tai Wei, it still caused considerable loss. It wasn't a fatal blow, but it was a severe injury.

This had never happened in the history of the Saint Dynasty, which was why Saint Tai Wei made such a remark.

'What is bound to come, will eventually come. I merely brought it forward. Perhaps it is even more beneficial for you,' Li Fan said meaningfully.

With his hand, he beckoned towards the Void Realm, drawing a mass of accumulated True Spirit and infusing it into a Saintly Fortune Elixir in his hand.

'This elixir is compensation and can make up for Daoist's loss. Also, if there truly are individuals among the countless subjects of the Saint Dynasty who are exceptionally talented, what harm is there in opening a path for them?'

Saint Tai Wei knew that Li Fan's sight could penetrate the Void Realm's obstruction, thus being far-sighted.

'Does he perhaps see something in the future?'

'For instance, my demise?'

Li Fan's attitude made Saint Tai Wei secretly ponder, as he took the Saintly Fortune Elixir infused with True Spirit and pondered Li Fan's words.

'Perhaps Daoist Fan is right. If there truly are those with the potential to become Saints, what harm is there in letting them prove their Dao? Emerging from the Saint Dynasty, they would naturally be our allies in the future. Perhaps they could even assist me in refining Saintly Fortune Elixirs, so I wouldn't have to work so hard in the future...'

Saint Tai Wei's heart stirred, and his beliefs were unknowingly rewritten.

The Saint Emperor took his leave and departed.

Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De were also about to set off for the Void Realm ahead.

'Looking forward to your good news.'

Under the gaze of all the Saints, the three figures successively entered the Void Realm.

Initially, they could still sense some traces of the three individuals' auras. But soon, the vast and boundless Void Realm obscured everything.

'Hope it is indeed good news.'

'This Saint of Mountains and Seas, his thoughts are unfathomable!'

'No matter. The outcome... should be favorable to us.'

In the eyes of Saint Lianshan, countless scenes flashed by in an instant, and he made his judgment.

Saint Guihai paused slightly and then nodded in agreement.

'Favorable in the moment, but not necessarily for a lifetime. It's a pity we are trapped and cannot see the full picture,' Saint Tai Yi sighed softly, his gaze deep as he vanished into the depths of the Void Realm.

...

Spanning nearly a hundred thousand years, this journey was extremely long.

Even with the Three Saints' assistance at the beginning, by the time they reached halfway, all their power had been exhausted.

Li Fan and Shou Qiu were fine; one was a Saint of Mountains and Seas who wielded the manipulation of truth and falsehood, with unfathomable profundity. The other possessed the Great Dao of Longevity, and simply observing Mountains and Seas was an easy task.

But for Dao De, who was merely a newly appointed Saint, and ranked only in the middle among the Saints, he was gradually showing signs of exhaustion.

'Let's take a break for now.'

Resting in the Void Realm was initially a fantasy. However, with Li Fan's True Spirit Infusion, it became possible.

Dao De and Shou Qiu felt the erosion of their existence in the Void Realm gradually being replenished, and even showing signs of improvement. Both lamented, 'Daoist Fan's divine ability is truly incredible! It is indeed the good fortune of Mountains and Seas!'

'Being able to summon and utilize the accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm has immense significance for reconnecting Mountains and Seas,' Shou Qiu said with great excitement, personally feeling the benefits of True Spirit Infusion.

And as the two were lamenting, they suddenly discovered that a figure had suddenly descended in the Void Realm.

It was Li Fan himself.

This phantom image possessed an unfathomable aura. Even in the Void Realm, it attracted the attention of Shou Qiu and Dao De the moment it appeared.

'Daoist Fan... what is this?' Dao De stammered.

He could see everything in Mountains and Seas within this blurry and distorted phantom image.

Not just the superficial appearances of Mountains and Seas, but even all possible principles within Mountains and Seas!

Crucially, Li Fan had never revealed the existence of this phantom image before the Saints in Mountains and Seas.

'This is the Shadow of God.'

'It was obtained by imitating the mystery of the Three Saints' Xuanji Ring.'

'The Mountains and Seas ahead face the Void Realm Incarnations; not a single misstep is allowed.'

'Please, the two of you, join me in the Xuanji!'

With that said, a dazzling yet familiar white light erupted from the phantom image.

The phantom image vanished, replaced by a white circle extremely similar to the Xuanji Ring on the Other Shore.

However, this white circle flickered intermittently, not very stable. In the Void Realm, it seemed on the verge of disappearing at any moment.

Li Fan had already taken his seat within it, smiling and waiting for Shou Qiu and Dao De.

'This...'

Shou Qiu and Dao De were immediately filled with doubt.

It wasn't that they doubted the authenticity of the Xuanji Ring before them, as they had been seated within it for countless years. The aura was almost identical, and they could clearly distinguish it.

It was just that... when did Li Fan become capable of creating the Xuanji Ring like the Three Saints?

After all, although the Three Saints had indeed expressed their intention to entrust the secret of the Xuanji Ring to Li Fan in their words, they still needed the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel to forge the Xuanji Ring again.

But now, Li Fan had recreated the Xuanji Ring entirely on his own, without relying on the Three Treasures!

'Could it be that in this short time he spent within the Xuanji Ring, he has actually deciphered its mysteries?'

'How is this possible?'

The two knew Li Fan could see further, but they couldn't imagine he could see so far!

Li Fan, seeing the subtle changes in Shou Qiu and Dao De's expressions, chuckled and said, 'You two need not hesitate. All your doubts will be resolved once you are seated within the Xuanji. Everything will become clear.'

'Isn't it said that only those who are the first three to take their seats truly share the same heart and mind?'

The Xuanji Ring's light fluctuated unstably, and Li Fan's voice sounded like a ghost, 'Only those who are the first three to take their seats truly share the same heart and mind.'

Shou Qiu and Dao De exchanged glances, and finally, it was Shou Qiu who, undeterred, strode into it.

'I can see that Daoist Fan harbors no ill intentions.'

'This journey is perilous; only by sharing the same heart and mind can we better face the crisis.'

Dao De saw this and could only grit his teeth and follow closely behind.

With the Three Saints seated, the originally flickering light circle of the Xuanji Ring instantly stabilized.

Li Fan's insights into the Shadow of God truly surfaced like a spring, appearing in their minds.

Even for Saints, such insights were an extremely valuable treasure.

However, they had no time to pay attention to it now, focusing solely on stabilizing the Xuanji Ring.

There were no disturbances.

After an unknown period, a new Xuanji Ring, independent of the Three Saints, was born in the Void Realm.

And Shou Qiu and Dao De's expressions changed drastically during this time.

'So that's how it is! Indeed, Daoist Fan's gains from this 'Return to Truth' are far beyond my imagination.'

'As expected, only those who wield the manipulation of truth and falsehood can truly comprehend its mighty power. Who would have thought that a mere regression could elevate an ordinary Saint to a level comparable to the Three Saints?' Shou Qiu sighed softly.

'The Three Saints cultivated for countless years to achieve their current divine abilities. Yet, Daoist Fan achieved it in just five hundred cycles... The gap between them is truly astonishing.'

Li Fan smiled and replied, 'Shou Qiu's assistance was also indispensable. Otherwise, how could I have understood the Shadow of Mountains and Seas in such a short time?'

Compared to Shou Qiu, who had cooperated once before, Dao De seemed somewhat dejected.

'Daoist Fan, you indeed toyed with me several times in the past by relying on the benefits of reincarnation.'

'But my enlightenment of you as a Saint is an undeniable fact,' Li Fan said nonchalantly.

'Alas...' Dao De was rendered speechless.

Shou Qiu chuckled and said, 'If being toyed with like this could lead to proving the Dao as a Saint, I think countless people in Mountains and Seas would be willing.'

Dao De had to admit that Shou Qiu's words were indeed the truth.

All the past events were dismissed with a laugh.

Next, it was time for concentricity and trinity!

'So, Daoist Fan's plan is truly to save the Three Saints?' Shou Qiu asked, surprised upon learning Li Fan's true intentions.

Li Fan nodded slightly, 'I have observed the complete 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.' Although I have grasped the overall changes in Mountains and Seas, there are still many details lacking. Thus, I only have the Shadow of Mountains and Seas, not the Spirit of Mountains and Seas.'

'Therefore, I plan to use the variables of the Three Saints to observe the changes in this segment of Mountains and Seas.' Li Fan pointed ahead and said proudly.

'By gaining one, one can gain all. If we can gain some enlightenment, we can then deduce the entire segment of Mountains and Seas.'

'Moreover...'

'We can hide in the shadows and observe all the methods of the Three Saints. Facing the crisis of life and death, they will surely reveal everything without reservation. Perhaps we can discover their trump cards.'

...

Li Fan explained the reasons for his actions.

Shou Qiu, after pondering, offered a different opinion.

'Why not try to reverse the situation and eliminate the Three Saints?'

'If we can absorb the Great Daos of Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi into the Hall of Return to Truth, we might be able to settle everything in one go and save a lot of trouble.'

Dao De sensed the situation and narrowed his eyes slightly, speaking for Li Fan, 'Daoist Fan is afraid.'

'Not only because of the unfathomable divine abilities of the Three Saints, but also because...'

'Tai Yi Saint aside, Lianshan and Guihai, these two are quite hard to fathom.'

Li Fan continued slowly, 'This is also something I vaguely sensed after observing the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.' The so-called Lianshan and Guihai, there are no such Dao paths within Mountains and Seas. The two of them became Saints because of Lianshan and Guihai, rather than proving their Dao through Lianshan and Guihai.'

'Why Lianshan? By what means Guihai?'

'The greatest trump cards of these two, we have never seen clearly.'

Shou Qiu nodded in agreement, 'Indeed.'

Li Fan said, 'The Three Saints are from the very beginning of the separation of Mountains and Seas, difficult to fathom by common sense. Perhaps they gained the creation of some primordial ancient artifact, who knows. If we rashly expose Return to Truth...'

'It seems Prying Opportunity's attempt to seize Return to Truth, although unsuccessful, has left you with quite a shadow,' Dao De chuckled.

Shou Qiu defended Li Fan, 'This is only natural for a person.'

After a moment of contemplation, Shou Qiu added, 'Steady progress has its merits. For now, our wings are not yet fully grown, and it is indeed not suitable to confront the Three Saints head-on. Especially since you said the Three Saints might have gained the creation of primordial ancient artifacts...'

'I believe it is true!'

With their minds aligned, Li Fan quickly reacted, 'Shou Qiu's suspicion stems from the Shadow of God?'

Shou Qiu nodded, 'In my previous life, when I saw the Shadow of God, I merely thought the Three Saints had reached the pinnacle of their cultivation and could actually glimpse the existence of 'God.' However, after reading the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes' through Return to Truth, I have a new idea.'

'With the power of Return to Truth, I finally obtained this scroll that only recorded the shadow, not the spirit of God. How did the Three Saints obtain the spirit of Mountains and Seas? Was it truly just through their peerless talent?'

Upon hearing this, Li Fan and Dao De both fell silent.

'There are countless beings in the world, and some may indeed be extraordinary, but there is always a limit. And some things clearly transcend this limit. The Three Saints, from nothingness to creation, are indeed divinely talented. But I believe...'

'Beings of Mountains and Seas, after all, are born from Mountains and Seas. To see the true God, one can only rely on external means.'

Shou Qiu gazed at the Shadow of God floating above Li Fan's head, feeling inspired and sighing.

Li Fan could faintly empathize with Shou Qiu's thoughts.

Although Shou Qiu often modestly claimed his cultivation was mediocre, he had, after all, cultivated from being a mere Warden of the Sea to a Saint. He definitely possessed his own pride.

But all of this was instantly smoothed away upon truly witnessing the power of Return to Truth.

Talent and effort were all irrelevant before Return to Truth.

Even after cultivating diligently for billions of years, the scenery that was still hard to glimpse was now clearly visible under the guidance of Return to Truth.

'This is not a matter of talent, but a limitation of our origin.'

'The creations of Mountains and Seas are destined to be confined within these Mountains and Seas. To aspire to see the True God, one must rely on external objects.'

Shou Qiu said slowly, 'Daoist Fan, since you started as a mortal and had the treasure of Return to Truth by your side, perhaps you don't empathize deeply with this. Dao De should have a more profound experience.'

After a long period of silence, Li Fan finally agreed with Shou Qiu's conjecture.

His estimation of the Three Saints' strength, unknowingly, rose another level.

'Taking advantage of this opportune moment, perhaps we can use the Void Realm Incarnations to thoroughly investigate the secrets of the Three Saints.'

After resting, the three set off again towards their destination.

However, this time, Li Fan and Dao De would provide protection, while Shou Qiu immersed himself in seclusion.

Li Fan, having obtained the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes,' could comprehend the Shadow of God.

Shou Qiu, naturally, also gained something.

Moreover, over the years, he had personally witnessed the changes in Mountains and Seas.

The detailed entries in the manual were as if everything he had experienced.

Everything was vivid.

As if going through another cycle of Mountains and Seas' changes, Shou Qiu's aura became increasingly ethereal.

'In the previous life, after comprehending the manipulation of truth and falsehood, Shou Qiu could instantly kill four Saints.'

'In this life, after obtaining the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes' through Return to Truth, who knows how much stronger he has become.' Li Fan looked at the meditating Shou Qiu, as if he had gained a sense of confidence out of thin air.

Even if the six Saints were in a fierce battle ahead, there was no longer any need to be so timid.

Chapter 1713: The Six Saints Battle Each Other

If traversing the Void Realm was a long ocean voyage, then True Spirit Infusion meant infinite supplies.

This made an extremely dangerous endeavor seem mundane.

The journey was smooth and uneventful, and soon, the first segment of Mountains and Seas was within sight.

'Currently, the Mountains and Seas ahead appear intact, so the Three Saints should not have perished yet.'

'However, I can already feel the atmosphere of an impending storm. They must be locked in battle. It's just the right time for us to arrive.'

Li Fan and Dao De concealed themselves in the Void Realm and observed the Mountains and Seas for a while, exchanging words.

At this moment, Shou Qiu had also awakened from his enlightenment.

His aura was deep and profound, making him unfathomable, as if seeing the Three Saints.

'I will go first and merge with my other self.'

'If the Three Saints' main bodies are too preoccupied to care about the Other Shore's Xuanji, I will suppress the other Saints first.' With that said, Shou Qiu transformed into a white streak, heading straight for the Mountains and Seas ahead.

Li Fan did not doubt Shou Qiu's ability to do so.

In this life, while Shou Qiu was enlightened, he also had some insights.

He could only lament that the stronger one's power became, the greater the amplification brought by Return to Truth.

With Shou Qiu's abilities and countless years of observing Mountains and Seas, after awakening his Dao, he had already reached a level comparable to the Three Saints.

'If Shou Qiu had obtained Return to Truth, Mountains and Seas would have been turned upside down long ago,' Dao De marveled.

Li Fan felt a slight sense of helplessness but could not deny it.

Fortunately, the three were united in heart and mind at this moment, indistinguishable from each other. There was no strangeness in their hearts.

Shou Qiu's actions were extremely swift.

There were no earth-shattering sounds, but in just over half a day, the Other Shore had been silently taken over.

Sensing Shou Qiu's communication, Li Fan and Dao De then descended upon Mountains and Seas at a leisurely pace.

Inside the Xuanji Ring, a miraculous sight appeared.

As if two suns filled the sky, besides the initial white circle, another ring appeared.

This newborn ring was extremely domineering and took the lead without politeness, not only that but it also captured all the Saints within the original ring under its command.

Shou Qiu had already secured the core position and was waiting for Li Fan and Dao De.

'It seems the battle in the Void Realm has reached a critical juncture. The Three Saints have even summoned their remaining phantom powers. Otherwise, it would not have been so easy for me.'

'After I merged with my other self in these Mountains and Seas, I launched a surprise attack. The Saints like Prying Opportunity hadn't even reacted before I instantly subdued them.'

'For now, I have spared their lives. On one hand, it is to stabilize Mountains and Seas. On the other hand...'

'Perhaps I can borrow their strength to absorb nutrients from the Xuanji Ring.'

In an instant, Li Fan and the other two had communicated mentally.

Following Shou Qiu's words, Li Fan looked at the miraculous scene of the two rings coexisting.

Both were Xuanji Rings, but their fates were now vastly different.

The old ring, though still magnificent, had lost its Saints, and more importantly, with the departure of the core sovereign Three Saints, it had begun to show signs of decline.

The new ring, though newly formed, possessed a vibrant life force.

Like a newborn calf, it was challenging the status of the old ring.

Li Fan was quite surprised that the new and old rings could coexist without mutual exclusion.

'The core of the Xuanji Ring is the Shadow of God.'

'Whether it is our comprehension or the Three Saints' comprehension, it is merely a crude imitation of the true Shadow of God. In a sense, we are of the same origin and one entity. Naturally, there will be no exclusion.'

'Conversely, just like when we from different time periods of Mountains and Seas meet, we merge. The new and old Xuanji Rings will gradually merge into one through this contact.'

'Of course, this is also because the old ring has lost the dominance of the Three Saints, becoming a leaderless entity,' explained Shou Qiu.

Li Fan squinted his eyes and slowly understood, 'In my previous life, I observed the Xuanji Ring to comprehend the Shadow of God, but in this life, it's the opposite; through the merging of the Xuanji Rings, it feeds back the Three Saints' comprehension of the Shadow of God.'

'Undoubtedly more pure and specific.'

Shou Qiu also reminded him, 'Beneath the True God, each has their own understanding. The Three Saints' thoughts and ideas may not necessarily be superior to ours. They can only serve as reference. We still need to maintain our own unique characteristics.'

'Shou Qiu is absolutely right,' Dao De nodded in agreement.

Although he was the weakest among the three and had the least experience, he was capable of devising the method of 'splitting family' for Dao De and becoming a Saint through an alternative path. Dao De's comprehension was undoubtedly among the top in Mountains and Seas.

Now, with Shou Qiu's lifelong experiences and his comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, his strength was advancing by leaps and bounds every moment, even growing the most among the three.

Especially in the process of mutual consumption after splitting families, he had gained considerable experience. At this moment, he was handling the merging of the Xuanji Rings with ease.

Under the watchful eyes of Prying Opportunity and other Saints, the two rings gradually merged.

The familiar white circle representing the Three Saints' past glory was gradually suppressed by the light and shadow of the newborn ring.

Even though the Saints were still seated in the Xuanji True Return, they knew that something had changed.

'Apart from the initial three main seats, although the rest can still be influenced by 'Concentric Unity,' the effect is greatly reduced.'

'Of course, it is more than enough to achieve our plan.'

'Dao De will preside over Mountains and Seas, while you and I will infiltrate the Void Realm and act according to the situation.'

From the more ancient Void Realm, bursts of heart-pounding fluctuations became more frequent.

It seemed the battle of the six Saints was nearing its climax.

Li Fan and the others no longer delayed. Only two phantom images were left behind; their true bodies entered the Void Realm together, cautiously moving towards the direction of the fluctuations.

'I only have the power of the 'Collapsing Mountains and Seas' attack, which can be used at the critical moment. The rest will likely depend on you, Shou Qiu.' Li Fan said with great certainty.

At the same time, he summoned countless accumulated True Spirits in the Void Realm, covering their surroundings as a disguise.

The accumulated True Spirits surrounded them layer by layer, completely concealing their auras.

They silently moved through the Void Realm.

'Your 'Collapsing Mountains and Seas' move can only be used at the most critical moment to achieve its greatest effect.'

'Just wait patiently. For other times...'

'Leave it to me.'

Shou Qiu's words revealed an innate confidence.

While communicating, they were already getting closer and closer to the scene of the six Saints' fierce battle.

The accumulated True Spirits seemed to be stirred into waves, fluctuating unstably.

It seemed as if a colossal creature was causing trouble in the Void Realm, leading to widespread turmoil.

Li Fan and Shou Qiu proceeded with increasing caution. In their sight, they finally saw the Three Saints.

To be precise, it was Tai Yi and his Void Realm Incarnation!

Tai Yi's expression was solemn, no different from Li Fan's usual observations. However, his clothes were slightly wrinkled, as if he had been forced into a somewhat disheveled state.

As for the Void Realm Incarnation...

Its form, appearance, and aura were identical to the main body. However, outside its body, it was covered by a layer of dim mask, and the entire person seemed to be shrouded in shadows.

Its face was icy cold, devoid of any expression.

Its eyes only contained the main body Tai Yi, vowing to kill him.

The battle between Tai Yi and his Void Realm Incarnation was quite profound.

Not only the two of them, but also two boundless worlds, and the innumerable beings within them, were all participating.

The two great worlds merged, and the junction was the most brutal battlefield.

'Could Shou Qiu discern the mystery?' Li Fan asked.

'That should be... the Primordial Immortal Realm,' Shou Qiu said after observing for a while.

'The Primordial Immortal Realm?'

'Of course, it's not the one that once existed in Mountains and Seas. More accurately, it is a replica of the Primordial Immortal Realm that evolved within Tai Yi, almost identical to the original. With Tai Yi's power, he recreated the Primordial Creation of Mountains and Seas...'

'And the beings manifested in this world should be those previously killed by Tai Yi, who have long since disappeared from the river of history in Mountains and Seas, but precisely because Tai Yi slew them, a trace of their imprint remained.'

Li Fan's gaze suddenly sharpened upon hearing this, and he couldn't help but think of Tai Yi's Saint-proving treasure, the All Beings Cudgel.

'Among the Three Saints, indeed, this one has the most heavy killing intent.'

Li Fan looked at the scene of the Primordial Immortal Realm, which was locked in battle, and saw many innate beings emitting strange auras, essentially manifestations of Great Daos.

Among them, the four leading figures with the strongest strength radiated auras of 'Primordial Beginning,' 'Primordial Origin,' 'Primordial Essence,' and 'Primordial Ultimate.'

'The true face of Saint Tai Yi is indeed extraordinary.'

Although the real Saint Tai Yi was extraordinary, his Void Realm Incarnation perfectly replicated everything about him.

The manifested scene of the Primordial Immortal Realm was identical to the original.

Furthermore, being in the boundless Void Realm, fighting on home ground, with an inexhaustible source of power, it was subtly gaining the upper hand in the battle.

However, it was still in a stalemate, and Tai Yi's defeat was far from imminent.

Li Fan began to search for the figures of Lianshan and Guihai.

'I can clearly sense the aftermath of the battle, why can't I see them?' Li Fan pondered carefully, feeling somewhat puzzled.

Shou Qiu looked towards the distance, his expression becoming increasingly solemn.

'Being within Mountains and Seas, it is naturally difficult to see Mountains and Seas. These two have already revealed their true forms.'

Under Shou Qiu's guidance, Li Fan's vision instantly changed the scene in the Void Realm!

In the seemingly empty darkness, countless turbulent currents surged.

Sometimes they collided and intertwined, sometimes they remained distinct.

The surface was chaotic, but it revolved around four core points.

It was Lianshan, Guihai, and their Void Realm Incarnations.

If Tai Yi's battle was the 'movement' of an endless chaotic battlefield.

Then, Lianshan and Guihai's battle represented the word 'stillness.'

The four figures stood opposite each other, each motionless.

Yet, countless undercurrents swirled, transforming into competing killing intent.

Tai Yi's battle was still in a stalemate.

But the confrontation between the two Saints had reached a critical juncture.

Sensing Li Fan's confusion, Shou Qiu explained, 'The battle between the two Saints and their Void Realm Incarnations can be seen as a battle of their Dao lineages.'

'Why Lianshan? Why Guihai? These are the reasons the two Saints reached their peak. And now, this authority has been tainted by the Void Realm Incarnations.'

'It involves the foundation of their own power's existence. Compared to ordinary battles, it is far more dangerous!'

'Look there!'

Li Fan followed Shou Qiu's pointing finger and saw that in the competition, several turbulent currents were being swallowed by other vortices.

Although it was just a minor change in a corner of the battlefield, it caused a hundred changes, ten thousand changes, leading to a drastic transformation of the entire war, making Li Fan feel slightly dizzy from what he saw.

'Every subtle change can be seen as a possible evolution of Mountains and Seas as they surge through time.'

'Tai Yi used the Primordial Immortal Realm as the core of his Dao derivation, while Saints Lianshan and Guihai, on the other hand, are treating the entire Mountains and Seas as their own dojo!' Shou Qiu exclaimed with sincere emotion, mixed with inexplicable excitement.

'However, this is still superficial!'

'The changes in the infinite Mountains and Seas are merely the specific manifestations of the two Saints' powers. The origin of these changes...'

Shou Qiu did his best to find the true core amidst the immeasurable turbulent currents in the battlefield.

Although Li Fan could not fully comprehend the true nature of the battle, he could tell from the increasingly frequent superficial phenomena of merging and competing that the battle was becoming fiercer.

He occasionally heard the lament of Mountains and Seas.

'The foundation of the two Saints in Mountains and Seas has begun to suffer damage.'

'It's like wearing armor that is gradually breaking. If one concentrates, one might be able to see the true faces of Lianshan and Guihai!'

Under Shou Qiu's reminder, Li Fan's heart calmed down.

Time seemed to stand still at this moment. His consciousness rapidly scanned the countless interwoven lines before his eyes.

Slowly, whether it was Li Fan's illusion or not, he felt as if these turbulent lines had all come to life.

Every change in a line seemed to represent... civilizations that had once existed in Mountains and Seas!

In the immensely ancient and vast years of Mountains and Seas, countless civilizations were born and then destroyed.

Every time a civilization appeared and disappeared, although it seemed to leave no trace.

Yet, it was like countless invisible knives, leaving ripples on the sea and wrinkles on the mountains.

Mountains and Seas each had their own vague consciousness.

Regarding these civilizations born within them, they could naturally perceive them vaguely.

'Mountains and Seas are formless, divided and transformed.'

Li Fan suddenly had an epiphany.

'After Mountains and Seas were divided and transformed, they took on their current appearance. Although it is due to their own powerful creation, who knows if it is not influenced by these born civilizations?'

'A drop of water pierces a stone, a rope saws wood. Although the impact of each civilization is small, when infinitely superimposed, it is enough to affect the overall trend of Mountains and Seas!'

'But what is the source of all these changes?'

Li Fan, like Shou Qiu, felt an inexplicable question arise in his heart.

Amidst these billions of turbulent lines, he searched endlessly.

Vaguely, he seemed to forget his own situation, existing only as a pure seeker of knowledge.

Constantly bathed in the vast and ancient aura of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan seemed to have truly returned to the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

What he had seen before, the fairy tales of Mountains and Seas left by Sun Piao Miao, every word and sentence came to mind.

'In the beginning, Mountains and Seas were not merged but separated.'

'There were beings born in the sea, yearning for the mountains, hence the endeavor to ascend.'

'Although such an act of transgression was quickly killed by the mountains, but...'

'The exploration from the sea was incessant.'

'Leading to the Mountains and Seas of today.'

'Why Lianshan? Why Guihai...'

Li Fan's heart stirred, and he seemed to faintly glimpse the true origins of Saints Lianshan and Guihai!

Chapter 1714: Method of Cutting Off the Future

Previously, Li Fan had encountered the remnants of a peculiar civilization in Mountains and Seas.

[Mo] Dynasty, Sacrificing to Mountains and Seas, Xiao Wangsheng.

Although that ancient dynasty had long since vanished into the river of history, Xiao Wangsheng had miraculously survived and had a chance encounter with Li Fan.

Through him, Li Fan glimpsed a corner of ancient Mountains and Seas.

Now, to confirm his guess, Li Fan seemed to transform into a member of the Mo Dynasty's sacrifice, searching for his familiar aura amidst the countless vast lines in the Void Realm.

From its creation to the present, Mountains and Seas had experienced countless years.

But the Mo Dynasty had also persisted for countless eons. If not for the calamity of Mountains and Seas merging into Dao Annihilation, this group of beings dependent on Mountains and Seas would not have been so easily annihilated.

Mo, ultimately, left its own mark in the history of Mountains and Seas.

And now...

As if transformed into Li Fan of the Mo Dynasty's sacrifice, he truly sensed the familiar aura of "homeland" from the surrounding countless lines!

His familiar fellow sacrificial members, the countless subjects of the Mo Dynasty, seemed not to have died, but were still gathered there, calling for his return!

Li Fan followed the trace, but ultimately did not see the already destroyed remnants.

What he saw was merely an endless ray of light formed by the existence of Mo in Mountains and Seas.

This ray of light represented the mark left by the Mo Dynasty civilization in Mountains and Seas!

Li Fan's consciousness returned to his own body, withdrawing from the scene of the Mo Dynasty's light. He looked around.

Like this, countless threads of civilization...

Endless, boundless!

Li Fan was greatly shaken.

'When I first emerged from the Primordial, I saw countless possibilities flowing concurrently in Mountains and Seas, and I thought I understood the vastness of Mountains and Seas.'

'However, seeing all this today, I finally realized...'

'The vertical lifespan of Mountains and Seas on the timeline is not inferior to the 'infinite' on the horizontal scale.'

'Incomprehensible, an immeasurably long time!'

Li Fan also recalled a strange black box he had once fished up while fishing in Dao Annihilation.

It was an ancient artifact of Mountains and Seas, the manifestation of its state after turning black from green.

'Initially, it was a member of the abundant algal life forms in Mountains and Seas during the period when Mountains and Seas swallowed God. After countless years of accumulation, it evolved into that appearance.'

'Even the period after Mountains and Seas swallowed God might have been much longer than I imagined.'

Algal life forms had no subjective consciousness, only the instinct for survival.

But even it had an impression of "extremely long ago" for its experiences, indicating the ancient nature of Mountains and Seas.

'Originally heading towards the mountain, hence called Lianshan.'

'Originally coming from the sea, hence became Guihai.'

'The answer was in the question itself.'

Amidst the turbulent lines of countless civilizations, Li Fan seemed to see the true source of power of Saints Lianshan and Guihai.

'Every attempt by the ancient civilization of Mountains and Seas to 'Lian Shan' pushed forward the birth of Saint Lianshan.'

'And every process of civilization disappearing and returning to the Infinite Sea was the cause of Saint Guihai's appearance.'

'Not the effort of one person or one moment to reach the peak, but the collective push of countless eons and countless civilizations, leading to that astonishing leap out of nowhere!'

Li Fan then recalled Saint Lianshan's past account of meeting Ming Shu when he first ascended.

After Lianshan ascended, Ming Shu seemed to have encountered something terrifying and fled in a panic.

'Thinking about it now, perhaps at the moment Lianshan succeeded, Ming Shu also glimpsed his true face, just like me.'

'The source of Saint Lianshan's power is the sum total of all those who attempted 'Lian Shan' but failed. This means that all those who attempted to ascend could be his nourishment.'

'The scene Ming Shu saw at that moment was probably a terrifying monster standing on countless piles of corpses. It is not surprising that he fled in fear.'

Although he understood the method of Dao Proving for the two Saints, Li Fan still had many doubts in his heart.

For example, how did abstract concepts like the civilization's 'Lian Shan' attempts and the inertia of returning to the Infinite Sea after demise influence Mountains and Seas? And how did they materialize into real beings?

'Mountains and Seas are divided into spirits, then life and civilization are born. Is this inevitable, or accidental?'

In the Void Realm, Li Fan had an epiphany.

Shou Qiu, sharing the same thoughts, also understood something.

'Daoist Fan, do you still remember the true master of the Great Dao of Longevity? In your previous life, after you used Return to Truth, the Great Dao of Longevity actually resisted returning to the Hall of Return to Truth.'

'I also vaguely glimpsed traces of His existence amidst these countless civilization threads!'

'He only existed before the ancient period of Mountains and Seas, perhaps even before the initial separation of God's power in Mountains and Seas.'

'Perhaps He suffered severe injuries during this conflict.'

'The main body did not fall into the evolution of Mountains and Seas over time, but a fragment fell into Mountains and Seas...'

Li Fan suddenly fell into thought.

Although there was no concrete evidence, the fact that it could contend with the limitations of the Great Dao of Return to Truth already proved the extraordinary nature of the true master of Longevity.

'Perhaps He is not inferior to the Three Saints. Such a being is best not provoked for now.'

Returning to the anchor point and starting anew, Li Fan regained his characteristic caution.

'As for the infinite True Spirit and intuition...'

'Shou Qiu believes it is not strongly related to my identity as a traverser but rather has a great connection to the cycles of 'Return to Truth' I have experienced.'

Recalling this, Li Fan suddenly fell silent. Even his steps, about to enter Mountains and Seas, involuntarily halted.

'In the endless cycles woven by 'Universe Cycle,' I experienced illusory premonitions that resonated with my intuition.'

'Of course, this does not mean I have truly experienced all of this. It is merely that during the momentary transformation between truth and falsehood in Mountains and Seas, countless possibilities have already unfolded. As the only being in Mountains and Seas who retains memories before and after the drastic changes, I may have unknowingly witnessed many things.'

'This also explains why 'Return to Truth' specifically chose me. Even if Prying Opportunity tried to snatch it, he couldn't move it an inch.'

''Return to Truth' had already seen through endless possibilities long ago. Only I, only me.'

'Can achieve the goal desired by 'Return to Truth' together.'

'It is not solely because I possess infinite True Spirit.'

... Li Fan's thoughts churned, while 'Return to Truth' remained silent as ever.

Ultimately, the entire Mountains and Seas, apart from 'Return to Truth' itself, could only speculate. However, Li Fan believed that the day he discovered the answer was not far off.

Where do I come from? Where do I go? Why do I live? Without resolving these questions, how can one speak of freedom and longevity?

Suppressing his thoughts, Li Fan took his halted steps, re-entering Mountains and Seas.

There was the barrier of Dao Annihilation, but also the interconnected veins of Mountains and Seas. Li Fan walked slowly, his destination not the Other Shore. Instead, he decided to leisurely stroll through Mountains and Seas first. In the past, in order to find the location of the Other Shore, Li Fan had divided his consciousness into countless streams, sailing to various parts of Mountains and Seas in search of possible traces. This targeted search had made him overlook the scenery along the way. Mountains and Seas themselves. In this life, Li Fan temporarily set aside all distracting thoughts and observed the unfolding of everything in Mountains and Seas from a purely observational perspective. At the same time, he mentally chanted, finally selecting the inheritance option he had contemplated for over five hundred years.

'Option three: A summary of the changes in Mountains and Seas from this simulation!' Li Fan stated with certainty.

The flickering characters suddenly stopped. Li Fan's 'Return to Truth' panel seemed to fall into a strange stillness; even the light dimmed. Then, countless points of light floated from the darkness, converging like a sea of stars, composing a long scroll! There were no words, no images. Only constantly flashing starlight! Each beam of light seemed to contain unimaginable, vast information. This was a detailed record of the possibilities observed by 'Return to Truth.' The entire sea of stars, with its countless lights combined, represented the changes in Mountains and Seas! For a transcendent being to read the summary of changes in Mountains and Seas was akin to seeking their own humiliation. Li Fan's form instantly shattered, and his spirit dissolved. But Li Fan showed no panic. Such an anomaly was within his expectations.

'It is precisely by using the changes in Mountains and Seas that I can seize the opportunity for Sainthood in this life!' Without a physical form, only his True Spirit dissipated. In the past, Li Fan would certainly have panicked and hastily activated 'Return to Truth.' But having experienced the descent into the abyss and the encounter with the Shadow of God in the previous life, Li Fan was now remarkably calm.

'Even Saints cannot fully observe the entirety of Mountains and Seas.'

'But I can use my infinite True Spirit...'

'To sculpt Mountains and Seas!' As the thought arose, the infinite True Spirit, against the backdrop of the starlight displayed by 'Return to Truth,' slowly took shape. It formed a 'Map of Mountains and Seas'! Infinite True Spirit, Infinite Mountains and Seas. The Map of Mountains and Seas was also infinite. The infinite True Spirit could bear the infinitude of Mountains and Seas. Though the Map of Mountains and Seas was infinite, it originated from the infinite True Spirit. Therefore, Li Fan could comprehend it all at once.

'Attaining Sainthood, in reality, has another path.' Although he lacked power and only had wisps of consciousness lingering before this map, Li Fan felt an unprecedented sense of strength.

'Without external help, without other methods.'

'Only through myself, becoming one with Mountains and Seas.' Instantly, like the clash of wind and thunder, immense waves of infinite True Spirit surged. From the infinite Map of Mountains and Seas, a figure slowly emerged. It was Li Fan himself! Simultaneously, in the real Mountains and Seas, something seemed to have been sensed. All possibilities trembled in unison! On the Other Shore, in the Grand Palace of Tai Xu. All the Saints cast their gazes upon Li Fan at the same moment. Even the usually stoic Three Saints showed a flicker of surprise in their eyes. Because what they saw was another Mountains and Seas!

'This... did we see incorrectly?'

'Did a new Saint suddenly emerge in Mountains and Seas?'

'And He...'

'Esteemed colleagues, did I perhaps see incorrectly?'

... Li Fan ignored the gazes from all directions and silently contemplated his current state. Having returned to the Saint realm, and far more powerful than the Saints of Xuanpin and Zhou Hui in his previous life. Even 'Return to Truth,' which had always remained silent, transmitted subtle fluctuations, as if in praise, or perhaps with some other special meaning hidden within. Li Fan simply smiled faintly in response, then his expression turned solemn, and he began to expound the Dao! His voice boomed like thunder, echoing throughout the universe. All beings and all possibilities in Mountains and Seas could now hear him.

'The world has the Upper Mountain and the Infinite Sea, sustaining countless beings.'

'Sainthood is to become one with Mountains and Seas.'

'For beings of Mountains and Seas to aspire to Sainthood, one may unify all forms of self, seek the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, or establish a new lineage.'

'Alternatively...'

'Become one with Mountains and Seas.'

... In Li Fan's words, a vast and boundless Map of Mountains and Seas slowly manifested. Initially, the beings did not understand Li Fan's meaning, but upon seeing the Map of Mountains and Seas, they gradually comprehended. Since Sainthood is to become one with Mountains and Seas, then as long as this standard is met, one naturally becomes a Saint! The beings were enlightened, but then became confused again. Was this not simply stating the obvious? If it were that easy to become one with Mountains and Seas, everyone would have become a Saint long ago. It was precisely because it was impossible that they sought other methods. They initially thought this newly emerged Saint of Mountains and Seas had come to expound the Dao, but instead, he was outwardly showing off! At this moment, countless thoughts of this nature arose among the beings. Li Fan ignored them. Indeed, this method of sanctification was unique to him in the entire Mountains and Seas. Otherwise, he would not have shamelessly shared it so openly. First, one needs the 'Summary of Mountains and Seas Changes,' which meticulously records all specific data and information within Mountains and Seas. Then, a target vessel is needed to contain this massive data. Even the Three Saints dared not claim to have fully comprehended the secrets of Mountains and Seas. But 'Return to Truth' could achieve this. And only infinite True Spirit could bear the infinite changes of Mountains and Seas and transform them for one's own use. 'Return to Truth' and infinite True Spirit. Unified within one person, this gave rise to such an incredible method of achieving Sainthood! To become one with Mountains and Seas, body and Mountains and Seas as one!

'Congratulations, Daoist Friend, on attaining the Dao today.' Amidst the beings' thoughts, Li Fan's figure gradually faded. On the Other Shore, the phantom image of Tai Yi actually left the Xuanji Ring to personally congratulate Li Fan. After all, such a heaven-shattering method of attaining the Dao was witnessed for the first time even by the Three Saints. They could not immediately discern how Li Fan had achieved it, so they used congratulating him as an opportunity to probe further. But Li Fan was no longer the same as before. In the past, he could be easily seen through by the Three Saints. Even while wearing the guise of a Saint, he was constantly apprehensive, fearing his thoughts would be exposed. But now... Standing firm like a mountain, unfathomable and mysterious. Tai Yi observed Li Fan, feeling as if he were the embodiment of Mountains and Seas. Boundless and immeasurable, difficult to speculate. He couldn't help but feel even more perplexed. To achieve Sainthood through the Dao of Mountains and Seas, the world should only have Lianshan and Guihai as Saints. Where did this new Saint of Mountains and Seas come from? Tai Yi, who shared the same heart as Lianshan and Guihai, naturally felt the familiar aura of Mountains and Seas emanating from Li Fan. It was undoubtedly genuine! Amidst his shock, he heard Li Fan calmly reply.

'Attaining the Dao is a trivial matter...'

'What is there to celebrate?' Even after living for countless years, very few things could stir Tai Yi's emotions. But upon hearing Li Fan's words, Tai Yi could barely suppress the anger that surged within him.

'Moreover, Mountains and Seas are already in a precarious state. After becoming a Saint, the responsibilities will only increase.'

'True freedom will be further out of reach!' Li Fan sighed lightly. This statement, however, slightly shifted Tai Yi's perception of Li Fan.

'Perhaps you would care to visit the Other Shore?' Tai Yi's phantom image invited. Before he finished speaking, Li Fan looked up towards the Other Shore within Mountains and Seas.

'That would be acceptable.' After a moment of silence, he nodded in agreement. The radiance of the Other Shore illuminated Mountains and Seas. Li Fan, having attained Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, naturally perceived the location of the Other Shore the moment he became a Saint. Tai Yi harbored no suspicion about this. With the strength of two Saints, the boundless Mountains and Seas were like a flat land. They quickly arrived outside the Other Shore, but Li Fan suddenly stopped. He inexplicably smiled at Tai Yi's phantom image.

'Within this ring, there seems to be a unique mystery.' Li Fan spoke meaningfully. Tai Yi's phantom image was about to explain, but was surprised when Li Fan walked directly in, momentarily stunned.

'This individual is indeed quite interesting...' he muttered to himself, following Li Fan in. Within the Xuanji Ring, all the Saints on the Other Shore turned their gazes upon Li Fan. Li Fan, no longer possessing the initial trepidation and fear he felt upon first meeting the Saints, calmly accepted their stares. His form, sculpted from Mountains and Seas, and having achieved Sainthood, was difficult to assess in terms of combat power, but at the very least, none of the Saints present could see through him. Even if the Three Saints themselves were present, it would be the same.

'It is fortunate for us that a new Saint has emerged within Mountains and Seas.' The phantom image of Lianshan was the first to break the silence.

'I have existed for an eternity, yet I never imagined someone could attain the Dao through 'Mountains and Seas.' May I ask how you accomplished this, Daoist Friend? Could you enlighten us?' The phantom image of Guihai, usually taciturn, spoke directly, asking the question.

'It is both difficult and easy. It is merely a matter of the four words, 'Comprehend Mountains and Seas.'' Li Fan did not refuse, stating it simply.

''Comprehend Mountains and Seas?'" The phantom images of all the Saints froze slightly, their expressions varied as they pondered the meaning.

'“Comprehend Mountains and Seas,” well said. With all our efforts, and “Heavenly Creation’s Pillar,” we could only attain either Lianshan or Guihai. Yet, with a few casual words, you have surpassed us. What great power you possess!' Guihai exclaimed loudly, his words carrying a hint of contention. It was not unreasonable for Saint Guihai to have such a peculiar attitude. The Three Saints had existed since the primordial era of Mountains and Seas, for an unimaginably long time, witnessing the birth and destruction of countless beings. They believed they had thoroughly understood the limits of what beings in Mountains and Seas could achieve. Achieving Sainthood from mortality was already difficult. As for Li Fan's method of attaining the Dao... It was simply unheard of, and more importantly, defied common sense. Could there truly be such a monstrous talent in Mountains and Seas? Or perhaps... The Three Saints instinctively began to doubt. As if sensing the doubts in the hearts of the Three Saints, Li Fan calmly and righteously stated, 'It's not a matter of great power. Although I attained Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, I can only grasp the 'form' of Mountains and Seas, not its 'spirit' like the Two Saints Lianshan and Guihai.'

'Lianshan sculpts bones, Guihai cleanses hearts. Standing at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas, there might be potential for further advancement. As for me...' Li Fan sighed regretfully, 'My limit is merely to be as one with Mountains and Seas.' His tone was filled with heartbreak and regret. Li Fan's attainment of Sainthood through Mountains and Seas indeed made it difficult to transcend Mountains and Seas and advance further. But these were obvious words. In the entire Mountains and Seas, aside from the legendary 'God,' who else dared claim to be above Mountains and Seas? To stand at the pinnacle of Mountains and Seas, was he still not satisfied? Within the Xuanji Ring, a peculiar atmosphere began to brew. The intentions of all the Saints towards this newly emerged Saint of Mountains and Seas, who displayed heaven-defying talent and suddenly attained the Dao, were varied. But soon, their attention was completely captivated by the scene Li Fan subsequently presented. It was a scroll depicting an endless Map of Mountains and Seas!

'Everyone, observe. This is the foundation of my Dao!' Li Fan waved his hand gently, unfurling a scroll. Light and shadow flowed incessantly, dreamlike and illusory, appearing both real and false, making it difficult to distinguish. For a time, it even suppressed the Xuanji Ring's white light, making the assembled Saints feel as if they were truly within Mountains and Seas.

'This is...'

'The Mountains and Seas within my eyes!'

'What do you all think?' Li Fan stood with his hands behind his back before the endless Map of Mountains and Seas. His faint words echoed endlessly within the Xuanji Ring. Yet, no one responded. All the Saints' divine senses were already immersed in this endless landscape of light and shadow. Sweeping their divine senses across it, the Saints were horrified to discover that the depicted Map of Mountains and Seas was indistinguishable from the real Mountains and Seas! There might be minor differences, but Mountains and Seas themselves were in constant flux. Regardless of scale or magnitude, Li Fan's Map of Mountains and Seas seemed to be a microcosm of the true Mountains and Seas. Not only the current Mountains and Seas, but all observable Mountains and Seas, from ancient times to the present! Though it was merely a shadow of Mountains and Seas, lacking specific details and divine essence, it was already incredibly miraculous.

'Fellow Daoist, who exactly are you?' The phantom image of Lianshan slowly asked. All the Saints' gazes converged, awaiting Li Fan's answer.

'Me?' Under the collective pressure of the Saints' gazes, Li Fan remained unfazed.

'My name is Li Fan, merely a humble mortal from the Great Xuan Realm.'

'I am even from the same possibility as Fellow Daoist Shou Qiu.'

'As for why I can observe all of Mountains and Seas...'

'It's simply because I can see further than ordinary people.' Li Fan's ambiguous answer did not convince the Saints.

''See further than ordinary people?'" Saint Guihai snorted lightly. Seeing that the Saints did not believe him, Li Fan feigned looking towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas. Although he claimed to be looking, his eyes were tightly closed.

'The Void Realm is vast and can block Saints, but my gaze can occasionally penetrate the Void Realm, allowing me to see more of Mountains and Seas.'

'For instance...' After a brief silence, Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes, a sharp glint within them.

'Ahead in Mountains and Seas, the demise of your three forms!' Extending his finger, he traced a line across the phantom images of Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi.

'The demise of the Three Saints!' Upon hearing Li Fan utter such a world-shattering prophecy, everyone present was stunned. The atmosphere within the Xuanji Ring suddenly dropped to freezing point. Those who were unaware suspected Li Fan had come to deliberately provoke them. The Three Saints of Lianshan, who had been named, were about to say something. But suddenly, their expressions shifted. Following the direction Li Fan had indicated, they all looked towards the same point. Their expressions gradually became extremely grave.

'Fellow Daoist, have you seen how we met our demise?' After a long pause, Lianshan asked. His attitude had subtly changed.

'Void Realm Incarnation.' Li Fan enunciated each word, uttering this sentence.

'So that's how it is.' As if sighing, the phantom image of Lianshan instantly became substantial. He had returned from the depths of the Void Realm. Then came Guihai and Tai Yi. The other Saints also returned one after another. The demise of the Three Saints was a matter of great importance. The operation to reconnect Mountains and Seas in the Void Realm had to be halted. Because no one knew if another Void Realm Incarnation would descend upon the current Mountains and Seas, and kill the Three Saints!

'Could it be that what this Saint of Mountains and Seas said is actually true?' On the Other Shore, the other Saints who had been brought back by the Three Saints looked at Li Fan with surprise in their eyes, tinged with hidden worry. After all, the Three Saints were the strongest among them. If even they could not guarantee their lives...
