'Although we possess the divine ability of 'Boundless Indestructibility,' it is ultimately a last resort. Each time we 'lose' the fortune obtained from reconnecting Mountains and Seas, the potential peak strength we can achieve diminishes slightly. We should not perish unless absolutely necessary.' Tai Yi spoke slowly, setting the tone.

'We are about to perish, yet we have not. Even ants cling to life... We must save ourselves.' Saint Guihai also said gravely.

'But Mountains and Seas have not yet been reconnected. If we forcefully leave now, firstly, we will not gain the merit of reconnecting Mountains and Seas, and our strength will not improve significantly. We might fail to save the situation and lose our own lives. Secondly, traveling to ancient Mountains and Seas is blocked by the Void Realm. Perhaps even the phantom images of the Xuanji Ring cannot remain. If Mountains and Seas lack our presence now...' Lianshan surveyed everyone present and shook his head slightly. Li Fan seemed to understand the thoughts of the Three Saints and smiled.

'It matters not. I have a plan that can resolve your concerns.'

'Oh?' Under the confused gazes of the Three Saints, Li Fan calmly revealed his solution.

'We only need to reconnect Mountains and Seas before the Void Realm Incarnation descends.' Tai Yi frowned slightly.

'Even with your assistance, reconnecting Mountains and Seas is not something one person can achieve alone...' Li Fan waved his hand.

'Allow me to inform you all, the reason my sight can penetrate the Void Realm is thanks to this!' Saying this, as if plucking stars and moon, Li Fan beckoned towards the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas. Like stars descending from the heavens, a vast river formed. Under the public gaze, the endless accumulated True Spirits within the Void Realm were summoned and gathered around Li Fan. The once-hollow Map of Mountains and Seas, which lacked spirit but possessed form, became more vibrant with the appearance of these accumulated True Spirits.

'Hmm?!' The astonishment of all the Saints surpassed that of moments ago.

'Daoist Friend can actually summon and control the accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm?' The voice of Saint Lianshan grew several decibels louder. Not to mention the other Saints within the Xuanji Ring. Their expressions were a mixture of awe and disbelief. After all, a Saint of Mountains and Seas was merely a stronger Saint. To them, it was merely replacing three Saints with four. But Li Fan's ability to summon and utilize accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm was entirely different.

'If it were only this, how could it demonstrate my divine abilities?' Li Fan declared proudly.

'Accumulated True Spirits are inexhaustible. Their usefulness to us is ordinary. Only when they become sustenance for Saints...'

'The more, the better!' Saying this, Li Fan looked towards the real Mountains and Seas. His gaze swept around as if searching for something.

'Could it be...' Seeing Li Fan's actions, the Saints seemed to guess something. But they could not believe it and remained silent, awaiting Li Fan's performance.

'I possess a method to infuse the accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm into Saints, using them to establish Sainthood!' Saying this, Li Fan found Jin Gui. Having existed in the transcendent realm for countless years and being only one step away from achieving Sainthood, he was unable to cross the final threshold of the great chasm. Now, captured by Li Fan, he was initially terrified. However, upon seeing the Saints on the Other Shore present, he immediately paid his respects. Before he could finish his greetings, Li Fan placed a hand on his head.

'Everyone, witness this with peace of mind.' Boundless True Spirits, as if alive, surged into Jin Gui's body under Li Fan's guidance! Under the watchful eyes of the Saints, a stubborn stone gradually transformed into a fine jade! In a short while, the new Saint Jin Gui was born within the Xuanji Ring.

'Thank you, Senior, for this creation!' The newly appointed Saint Jin Gui was overwhelmed with gratitude. The remaining Saints remained speechless for a long time. In such a short period, Li Fan had delivered one shocking revelation after another. Attaining Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, his sight penetrating the Void Realm to reach ancient Mountains and Seas, his ability to summon and utilize accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm. Furthermore, his ability to transform them for his own use and enlighten Saints. All these abilities were concentrated in one individual! Even the Three Saints would need considerable time to accept and process this.

'Delay leads to change. The Three Saints ahead are nearing their end!' Li Fan sighed softly, interrupting the Saints' contemplation. The newly appointed Jin Gui was startled but unsure how to react, remaining silent. The Three Saints had finally made a decision.

'Let us reconnect Mountains and Seas as soon as possible.' This time, after Li Fan achieved Sainthood through Mountains and Seas, his ability to summon and utilize accumulated True Spirits became even more proficient. Even after enlightening Jin Gui, he felt no strain. Just like in the previous life, he found Daode and Bai Xiao separately and enlightened them. With the combined strength of the Saints, Mountains and Seas were quickly reconnected. Amidst roaring sounds, Mountains and Seas naturally began to recover their vitality. All the Saints benefited greatly from this. However, none of their expressions became relaxed. All because of Li Fan's words.

'The demise of the Three Saints lies ahead.' Li Fan looked towards the more ancient segment of Mountains and Seas ahead and spoke softly. Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi sensed for a moment and all nodded slightly.

'The Void Realm Incarnation should have descended. However, our deaths are not imminent. We must plan carefully.' Guihai stated after observing for a long time.

'Although we have gained the fortune of a segment of Mountains and Seas, we do not have a definitive advantage. Of course, if we could gain more assistance...' Tai Yi looked at Li Fan. Li Fan said, 'I still have some capacity left. Those who can be enlightened in this place can all be illuminated by me. With our combined efforts, reconnecting Mountains and Seas would be a trivial matter. But...' Li Fan paused before speaking sternly, 'As Elder Guihai mentioned, the battle with the Void Realm Incarnation is not a matter of days. Six Saints in battle, if without protection, could even affect Mountains and Seas.'

'Furthermore...'

'The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting the Three Saints ahead. If we were to offer our assistance and fail, who knows if the Void Realm would send even stronger Void Realm Incarnations? We may have the strength for one battle, but do we have the strength for a second or third?' Facing Li Fan's questions, all the Saints fell silent. After all, except for the Three Saints, none of them had truly encountered the so-called Void Realm Incarnations.

'Daoist Fan's considerations are indeed thorough. But please rest assured, if the Void Realm Incarnation is defeated swiftly, it will not reappear immediately. At the very least, it will give us some breathing room. And this 'breathing room,' in the timescale of the Void Realm, is an extremely long period from our perspective.' Guihai explained.

'As for affecting Mountains and Seas...' The Three Saints exchanged glances and then looked at Li Fan, saying, 'The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting us. Naturally, we shall deal with it ourselves.'

'And with Daoist Fan presiding over Mountains and Seas, it should remain safe.' The Three Saints' answer was within Li Fan's expectations, but he shook his head slightly.

'I can enlighten Saints, but I cannot protect Mountains and Seas.'

'Firstly, after continuous enlightenments, even Mountains and Seas have become somewhat depleted. Secondly, as you all saw earlier, the Map of Mountains and Seas only possesses the 'form' of Mountains and Seas, not its substance. To withstand the residual waves of battle...'

'I fear my strength is insufficient.' Li Fan said truthfully.

Chapter 1715: Defending the Mound, Turning the Tide

The Tai Yi Saint's method of using the Fate Rope against enemies was not like ordinary ropes that simply bound. Instead, countless finer black threads poured out from it.

Like a pair of invisible, skillful hands rapidly weaving, soon, a 'Shou Qiu' built from hemp ropes appeared in the arena.

The moment the rope puppet was born, it was as if an inexplicable existence locked it and Shou Qiu together through some method.

Facing the sight of another self, Shou Qiu's hair stood on end, instinctively sensing a fatal crisis. And what happened next quickly proved Shou Qiu's premonition.

In the Void Realm, as if a gentle breeze had passed. A thread constituting the rope puppet Shou Qiu suddenly floated out from its body and was instantly swallowed by the surrounding Dao Annihilation. Correspondingly... Shou Qiu truly sensed that a part of himself had been drawn out and dissipated from nothingness!

A turtle shell suppressing from above, an ancestral bone attaching from the brow. Shou Qiu, already in a perilous situation, became even more precarious as his strength instantly declined.

Although his head was still held high, his entire body had been forcefully compressed by a section. Threads of blood seeped out, and the moment they flowed out of his body, they were absorbed by the attached ancestral bone. The process of turning into white bone became more apparent.

Externally, it was as if the entire skeleton was exposed on Shou Qiu's hunched body. Drawing out a thread from a broken rope, hanging by a thread!

The fate rope's extraction continued. Shou Qiu felt more and more clearly that his life force was rapidly draining away.

The Great Dao of Longevity he had comprehended and controlled, under the fatal crisis, unleashed an unprecedented brilliant green light. It maximally repaired Shou Qiu's injuries.

If it were only the pressure from the turtle shell and the ancestral bone, Shou Qiu might have held on for a while longer with the characteristics of the Great Dao of Longevity, but the consumption from the fate rope was a direct extraction of his essence.

As the rope puppet Shou Qiu became increasingly desolate, Shou Qiu's life substance grew thinner and thinner. Even though the power of Longevity continuously replenished his body, it could not stop the reduction of his life's upper limit.

'This fate rope's technique is actually subtly similar to the 'True is False' divine ability!' 'But it does not negate my existence from the Dao of Truth and Falsehood, but rather uses some unknown power to extract my life substance...'

Life was like a candle flame in a fierce wind, about to be extinguished. Shou Qiu's heart was calm, without sadness or joy.

Seizing the last moments of his life, he comprehended the turtle shell, the ancestral bone, and the fate rope, and pondered ways to counter them. He even proactively gave up resisting, using his own faster descent as a price to attempt different coping methods.

'Although the turtle shell is small and thin, it seems to represent the boundless Upper Mountain.' 'The Saints say they are one with Mountains and Seas, but only when Mountains and Seas truly press down upon them can one feel the weight of Mountains and Seas.' 'Even the realm of the Three Saints might not be able to resist it directly.' 'Perhaps I can use my understanding of Mountains and Seas to neutralize some of the pressure, as if I were already in the mountains...'

'The ancestral bone attaches, everything within the body returns to it without resistance, just as all rivers flow east to the sea, as if conforming to heavenly principles. But there are rivers that flow west, forming another ocean! Although you are the ancestor of all beings, I am the Warden of Mountains and Seas!'

Shou Qiu's eyes seemed to burn with fire, as if sensing his thoughts. The flesh and blood flowing towards the ancestral bone within his body also paused, as if caught in a dilemma, unsure what to do.

'As for this fate rope...' 'The method of extracting life substance is truly hard to guard against. The moment the rope puppet is born, all negative effects that happen to it will simultaneously occur to me. This kind of corresponding binding can perhaps only be resolved through the manipulation of truth and falsehood.'

Shou Qiu vaguely found a path to resolution but forcefully suppressed the urge to try. This was different from before; he was already locked onto by the fate puppet, coupled with the parasitic ancestral bone. His internal condition might be perceived by the Void Realm Incarnation. If he were to forcefully use the manipulation of truth and falsehood to resolve it at this moment, the opponent might detect the existence of Return to Truth.

'A dying struggle is meaningless.' 'Forget it.'

On the verge of death, Shou Qiu's heart was completely clear. Because he knew that as long as Li Fan activated Return to Truth again, he would return from nothingness. Without dwelling on the question of whether that 'I' was truly 'me.' The dying Shou Qiu actually felt a sense of melancholy.

It was precisely because he held the idea that he would definitely return that Shou Qiu felt no ordinary emotions in the face of such great horror as life and death. This strangeness made Shou Qiu feel that his lifelong pursuit of 'Longevity' had become worthless.

'If there is no death, what meaning does Longevity have?' 'The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood will exhaust all under heaven!'

...

At this moment, the reinforcement from the Three Saints finally arrived, albeit late. They seemed to be quite wary of using the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope, not as decisive as the Void Realm Incarnations.

Witnessing Shou Qiu about to perish, they finally released the three objects. Silently, they enveloped Shou Qiu.

Compared to what the Void Realm Incarnations released, the Three Saints' objects were... more sinister! The Void Realm Incarnations used pure 'objects.' But what the Three Saints took out now seemed like living beings. Shou Qiu even vaguely felt three different gazes constantly scrutinizing his body. Faint, eerie laughter occasionally echoed in his ears.

A cold, sinister aura infiltrated his body like an unstoppable force, causing Shou Qiu to feel intensely 'uncomfortable.' It was not pain, but instinctive repulsion and avoidance!

Fortunately, the three objects were ultimately controlled by the Three Saints and did not forget their mission. Turtle shell against turtle shell, the continuous phantom of Upper Mountain pressed down, while boundless Upper Mountain resisted. Ancestral bone against ancestral bone, with the infiltration of another force from the ancestor of Mountains and Seas' beings, Shou Qiu's internal flesh and blood loss instantly became disoriented, not knowing where to go. Fate rope against fate rope. In the void, another rope puppet Shou Qiu quietly emerged. The life essence that was invisibly drawn out was slowly replenished by it!

The Three Saints' direct intervention, in an instant, reversed Shou Qiu's precarious situation, pulling him back from the brink of death! The Three Saints and their Void Realm Incarnations were evenly matched, unable to decide a winner!

Shou Qiu, having escaped disaster, had no time to rejoice. Instead, an inexplicable sense of unease arose in his heart. It was not for himself, but for the Three Saints.

'If it was only an even match... How did the Three Saints perish in the previous life's timeline?' 'Could it be...'

Shou Qiu's heart trembled, and just as he was about to speak a warning. But the Void Realm Incarnations seemed to have been waiting for this moment. Just as the Three Saints released the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope to save Shou Qiu, ripples appeared in the Void Realm. Indeed, three more objects descended! Like flying stones from outer space, hurled into the center of the arena.

The countless lines in the battleground of the six Saints were instantly thrown into chaos! The fate rope bound Lianshan; the turtle shell suppressed Guihai; the ancestral bone captured Tai Yi. As if planned, the Void Realm had actually evolved these three objects and imposed them upon the Three Saints!

Witnessing this, Shou Qiu instantly understood. The turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope used by the Void Realm Incarnations were, after all, merely evolutions of the Void Realm's power, not actual existing objects. As long as enough power was invested, it could naturally evolve into a second or third copy. But the Three Saints only possessed the original turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope. At this moment, due to a moment's lapse in judgment used to save Shou Qiu's life, they were now in a perilous situation.

The Three Saints and their Void Realm Incarnations were already evenly matched. Now, the addition of the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope became the final straw that broke the camel's back! The Three Saints wished to recall their treasures to support them, but they were already entangled by their first copies. They had even abandoned their original target, Shou Qiu, and were determined to hold back the opponents, even at the cost of their own forms gradually disintegrating.

Shou Qiu suddenly looked towards the depths of the Void Realm, where it seemed a figure, having made a move, revealed a faint, triumphant smile.

Given Shou Qiu's temperament, he naturally could not stand by and watch the Three Saints perish because of him. Moreover, Li Fan's plan in this life was precisely to save the Three Saints and observe their changes. Instinctively, he wanted to provide aid. But that glance towards the outside of the Void Realm made Shou Qiu hesitate slightly. It was not because he feared death, but rather...

In an instant, after countless deductions, Shou Qiu finally found a suitable method. 'The plan has changed.' 'Daoist Fan, do not reveal yourself. Just observe in secret.' 'If any other anomalies descend from outside the Void Realm...' 'They will only be directed at me.'

After transmitting his message, without waiting for Li Fan's response, Shou Qiu no longer concealed his enlightenment in this life. The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.' Without reservation, he unleashed everything. In just a breath, his body, ravaged by the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope, was fully restored. He took a step, crossing the continuous Void Realm, and arrived in the center where the Three Saints were surrounded.

'The flow of fate, whether true or false, like a dream, like an illusion. To think of it as false, to call it false!' Shou Qiu's voice spread through the Void Realm. Like a gentle breeze passing by. It seemed harmless, but in reality... Turbulent waves were suppressed by a pair of invisible giant hands and forced to calm down. Many of the manifesting figures were drastically reduced. And the three Void Realm Incarnations closest to Shou Qiu had already become transparent! Until the clear breeze passed and they vanished. Only then did the Three Saints' Void Realm Incarnations realize with belated terror.

Chapter 1716: The Behind-the-Scenes Behind the Void Realm Appears

A move that annihilated three Saints, astonishing everyone present!

Although only the Void Realm Incarnations of the Three Saints had disappeared, their strength was undoubtedly on par with their main bodies.

Now that Shou Qiu could instantly kill a Void Realm Incarnation, it meant...

Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi were filled with uncontrollable shock.

Even though they already knew Shou Qiu possessed the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, they never expected that Shou Qiu, affected by the transformation of truth and falsehood, would be so powerful!

In that case, Shou Qiu's actions within the Xuanji Ring for countless years were all an act?

What was his true goal?

Just as the Three Saints were filled with doubts, they suddenly noticed that Shou Qiu's physical form seemed to have become somewhat transparent compared to before.

Although the degree was not very obvious, it did not escape the Three Saints' observation.

"This is..."

"The price of forcefully activating the transformation of truth and falsehood and erasing the Void Realm Incarnations?"

"It seems Shou Qiu's comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood has not yet reached its peak." Thinking this, the Three Saints felt their hearts settle considerably.

But Shou Qiu completely ignored his own condition.

His mind was as clear as a mirror, observing the numerous figures within the surrounding Void Realm.

Wherever he went, he used the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood to forcibly erase the Void Realm Incarnations that had yet to be born or descend.

"What is true, what is false?"

"The existence and non-existence of truth and falsehood are all in a single thought. Indeed, it is profound and beyond the imagination of sentient beings."

As Shou Qiu killed the Void Realm Incarnations that swarmed him as easily as crushing ants, even though he had accomplished all this himself, he felt an overwhelming sense of unreality.

Each activation of "Truth is Falsehood" caused Shou Qiu's comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood to improve slightly.

Amidst countless overlapping shadows, Shou Qiu advanced as he killed, relentlessly progressing.

The Great Dao was like the heavens, but when Shou Qiu effortlessly annihilated all the approaching Void Realm Incarnations, he strangely found that it felt as if he hadn't even moved.

The peak of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood still seemed infinitely far away.

This path of enlightenment truly seemed to have no end.

Shou Qiu let out a wry smile and shook his head slightly, "Indeed. If 'Return to Truth' had taken action, it would not have been so troublesome for me to kill them one by one."

"With a mere thought, Mountains and Seas would be overturned."

Even though the crisis brought by the Void Realm seemed to have been resolved, Shou Qiu did not relax.

In the dead silence of the darkness, a greater storm was brewing.

"In the war of the Void Realm devouring Mountains and Seas, Dao Annihilation can be called a pawn, and the Void Realm Incarnations of the Saints are the capable generals."

"And what will appear next..."

"Can be called a high-ranking general."

Shou Qiu felt something in his heart and focused his attention on a certain area ahead.

The surrounding accumulated Void Realm receded.

As one gained and the other lost, Mountains and Seas were revived and brimmed with vitality.

But whether viewed by Shou Qiu or the Three Saints, the more vitality Mountains and Seas possessed now, the more intense the signs of death became!

All of this originated from the terrifying storm that was about to descend from the Void Realm.

If the previous summoning of the Void Realm Incarnations of the Saints was merely deploying troops, then what was happening now was the true accumulation of power and momentum.

On an almost infinite timescale, the Void Realm, which had been locked in a stalemate with Mountains and Seas, was now concentrating the vast majority of its forces to attack the current segment of Mountains and Seas.

Forming a monstrous tsunami.

Although the waves had not yet arrived, the pressure, as if substantial, had already manifested.

Mountains and Seas were gradually distorting because of it!

It must be known that the prolonged war between Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm was almost evenly matched. The Void Realm held a slight advantage, needing to accumulate over long periods to completely erode Mountains and Seas.

The contraction of the Void Realm's front lines across all temporal nodes now meant that most of its previously accumulated advantage would be lost in an instant.

Mountains and Seas counter-attacked and revived. If the Void Realm wanted to restore its original state, it would have to expend endless time again.

Facing such a heavy price, the Void Realm did so without hesitation.

Shou Qiu seemed to see the determination of the one manipulating the pieces from behind the scenes.

"Such decisiveness is truly admirable."

"Unfortunately, it is destined to be futile."

As the storm approached, Shou Qiu stood like a sword between the Void Realm and this segment of Mountains and Seas, single-handedly shouldering the ever-increasing terrifying pressure from the entire Void Realm.

His figure was like a pond rippling incessantly under a strong wind.

His body became more and more dim and transparent.

Like a dying star, it could be swallowed by darkness at any moment.

But he stood firm, waiting for the arrival of the "high-ranking general."

"With my current physical state, I should be able to hold on for a while longer and explore this opponent's background further."

"The transformation of truth and falsehood is indeed profound. But ordinary beings of Mountains and Seas indeed cannot withstand it."

"Even if one can turn falsehood into truth for all things in a single thought, one's own self will still be affected."

"And during the process of 'Return to Truth' and the reshaping of Mountains and Seas, it is also a process of eliminating oneself through the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. However, unlike our recreation, we still need to maintain our own state and connection with our true selves from the previous life..."

"'Return to Truth' is indeed not something that ordinary people can handle."

Shou Qiu's mind was calmer than ever.

After he could truly unleash some of the power of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, his lingering greed and possessiveness towards 'Return to Truth' completely dissipated.

Others might not understand Shou Qiu's change, but only Li Fan, who was hidden in the shadows, knew everything.

"Shou Qiu Gong's accumulation of billions of years, once he obtained the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood and acted without restraint, caused quite a stir!"

Compared to the current scene, Li Fan deeply felt that what he had done before, even burning mountains and boiling seas, was mere child's play.

"Shou Qiu's words resonate deeply with me."

"Truth and falsehood are esoteric, and there is no need to hide or reveal them. Since 'Return to Truth' is in hand, one should act according to one's heart!"

"In the past, when my strength was weak, being cautious and prioritizing safety was indeed correct."

"But now that I have the capital to contend with the Three Saints, there is no need to be so hesitant."

With the Xuanji Ring's synchronization effect, it was as if he himself had annihilated the Void Realm Incarnations of the Three Saints and suppressed infinite shadowy figures. Li Fan's emotions surged.

It was as if a blocked path had suddenly opened, and his thoughts and ideas were vastly different from before.

As the saying goes, a new situation unfolds.

Of course, despite his excitement, Li Fan did not forget Shou Qiu's instructions and remained hidden in the shadows, not revealing himself.

The pressure from the Void Realm, upon reaching its limit, suddenly lightened.

The accumulated momentum was emptied, replaced by a figure confronting Shou Qiu.

This figure was naturally the manifestation of the Void Realm withdrawing most of its strength, but interestingly, its appearance was exactly that of Shou Qiu.

Having shed the characteristic dim black shadow enveloping the Void Realm Incarnations, Shou Qiu looked at his other self ahead, feeling as if he were looking in a mirror.

It wasn't just similar.

Shou Qiu could also sense that the Void Realm Shou Qiu ahead was actually condensed from data of countless destroyed Shou Qius. In other words, it was a part of himself formed by the collective efforts of countless Void Realm Incarnations.

"Mountains and Seas have countless talented individuals, why should it imitate me?"

Shou Qiu did not believe that the existence behind the Void Realm would act without purpose.

Soon, he understood the reason from the subtle connection that gradually formed between his own body and the Void Realm projection ahead.

"If they succeed in killing me, they can take my place."

"Even if they fail, as long as they can stall me, they can slowly assimilate me through this inexplicable connection."

"This connection originates from my destroyed self in the Dao Annihilation, which cannot be severed. If I didn't have the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood protecting me, and wasn't within the Xuanji Ring, forming a tripartite alliance with Fellow Daoist Fan and Dao De, the speed of assimilation would have been hundreds of times faster."

"The Void Realm's high-ranking general indeed has exceptional methods."

However, this assimilation was merely a minor disturbance stirred up by the high-ranking general before the battle.

When the Void Realm projection Shou Qiu truly made his move, it was a world-shattering storm!

The Dao Annihilation devoured endless Mountains and Seas, reaching the extreme of destruction.

The Void Realm Shou Qiu waved his hand gently, unleashing the ultimate power of the Void Realm.

Countless vortices surged around them, and Shou Qiu felt as if he were trapped in a muddy vortex, almost unable to move.

The power that could swallow Mountains and Seas over an ancient and long period was now concentrated on Shou Qiu alone.

This was the power of encirclement and annihilation across all temporal scales, concentrated in this single instant.

The longer the span of Mountains and Seas' existence, the more the destructive power multiplied.

In the face of this towering wave that could obscure all things, Shou Qiu felt that his past and future were both blocked by wind and frost.

The memories of the past slowly faded, and in the dimness, he could not see the future.

Only the present self remained, struggling to hold on.

Instinctively activating the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood to protect his body, even though many memories had faded, Shou Qiu clearly remembered his mission.

Looking at his other self ahead, Shou Qiu attempted to negate it with a single thought.

But the effect was not as expected.

If the Void Realm Incarnations of the Three Saints he had previously annihilated were merely a thin sheet of paper.

Then the Void Realm Shou Qiu at this moment was formed by the overlap of countless paper figures.

It had gained a corresponding thickness.

Although it could not prevent the annihilation from the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, it could support him for a considerable period!

"It seems my comprehension has not yet reached the essence."

"Otherwise, no matter how thick the accumulation, it could be removed in an instant."

While in a stalemate, Shou Qiu had already thought of a countermeasure.

"This move can cut down the high-ranking general, and perhaps force the mastermind behind the scenes to reveal some of their true face!"

Once the thought arose, Shou Qiu hesitated no longer.

"Fellow Daoist Fan, watch carefully!"

With that said, he abandoned all his defenses and allowed himself to be eroded and assimilated by the Void Realm Shou Qiu. If Shou Qiu truly possessed 'Return to Truth,' he would not have given up so easily.

Alas...

He was merely bait.

"When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth!"

As his body gradually sank into the Void Realm, Shou Qiu sang out loud, resolutely unleashing a "Blade of Truth is Falsehood" upon himself.

Slaying all things is difficult, but slaying oneself is easy!

Having observed Mountains and Seas for countless years, Shou Qiu had long since understood himself, knew himself, and recognized himself.

At this moment, the act of erasing himself was as smooth as a master butcher carving an ox.

With a single slash, Shou Qiu's figure became increasingly transparent.

But it also caused the Shou Qiu projection ahead to dim!

The Void Realm projection was shocked, never expecting that the "Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood" would choose such a mutually destructive method.

But the ripple effect of "Truth is Falsehood" had already spread like a mountain collapse.

The Blade of Truth is Falsehood seemed to ignore space and time, crossing the river of time.

Slaying the current Shou Qiu meant slaying the past Shou Qiu, the future Shou Qiu, and the Shou Qiu devoured by Dao Annihilation.

The countless overlapping data condensed within the Void Realm Shou Qiu, which was meant to deal with Shou Qiu Gong, now became fuel for self-immolation.

"Cleverness backfires!"

Shou Qiu Gong, seizing the advantage, accelerated his integration into the Void Realm while relentlessly slashing himself with the Blade of Truth is Falsehood.

"Since you want to devour me, then I shall fulfill your wish!"

"My life has no shameful past!"

As he was about to perish, Shou Qiu laughed heartily.

The past, the present, and the future would all turn into nothingness.

But Shou Qiu suddenly thought of his name.

Prosperous Virtue.

Shou Qiu of Prosperous Virtue.

...

Shou Qiu's demise was merely the beginning.

Like a chain reaction of fire, like a continuous avalanche.

The Void Realm's accumulated strike, forged over a long period, was rendered null and void.

Instead, it backfired, and the endless transformation of truth and falsehood spread uncontrollably.

Like a beam of sunlight dispelling darkness.

The Void Realm, like pervasive dark clouds, gradually became riddled with holes and disintegrated.

The watching Three Saints finally understood that the Void Realm was not absolute nothingness.

Its existence could still be erased by "Truth and Falsehood."

The fire of truth and falsehood spread and burned. The endless dark clouds covering Mountains and Seas slowly dispersed.

Mountains and Seas revived, and the crisis of merging seemed to have been resolved.

But for some reason, the Three Saints felt an even greater sense of crisis.

As if by telepathy, they simultaneously looked towards a certain spot in the arena.

From Shou Qiu's place of demise, faint black threads, like spider silk, quietly appeared.

In an instant, they wove a net of unfathomable difficulty.

The origin of the threads was unknown, but they were rooted in the void. As they were slowly woven, they actually halted the Void Realm's disintegrating momentum.

It was as if, with these threads, the Void Realm's imminent collapse was being forcefully patched up.

Not only that.

Within the Void Net, a single thread emerged independently.

Originating from Shou Qiu's place of demise.

Heading towards...

The hiding place of a certain person!

The Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood would not easily dissipate like this.

Since Shou Qiu had perished, it meant that the true Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was someone else!

The so-called Shou Qiu was merely a probing chess piece released by him!

Although the Void Realm behind the scenes had suffered a setback.

It quickly realized this.

Seizing the remnants left after Shou Qiu's demise, it attempted to find the person behind it!

Even though the Void Realm had accumulated countless eons, it was not yet defeated.

As long as it could find the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, it would be worthwhile.

The Void Net moved synchronously with the extending thread. Wherever it went, space and time seemed to freeze.

The scale of the net grew larger and larger, and as if sensing the crisis, the reviving Mountains and Seas paused their growth to avoid its edge.

The Three Saints' expressions were grave. While evading, they joined forces to protect themselves.

Initially, the net was only the size of a palm.

But in an instant, it had become a net covering the heavens, encompassing the entire universe!

Chapter 1717: The Truth Really Is

The Void Net instantly enveloped the entire Void Realm battlefield outside Mountains and Seas.

And at its center, the black thread, which had been moving rapidly like a swimming dragon, had also coincidentally completed a circle.

Li Fan...

Was within it!

The moment Shou Qiu Gong perished and the Void Realm mastermind appeared, Li Fan had already silently recited 'Return to Truth' in his heart.

Infinite white mist surged forth, intending to conceal everything.

But this seemed to have accelerated the exposure of Li Fan's hiding place. The Void Net suddenly changed, locking Li Fan within!

Unlike the past when 'Return to Truth' was activated, a completely different scene unfolded.

*Bang!* *Bang!* *Bang!*

As if struck by an invisible heavy hammer, the surrounding white mist was constantly being pounded. Li Fan's vision was filled with continuous tremors.

And the frequency was increasing.

Each strike seemed to correspond precisely to a critical node, causing the process of the white mist devouring everything to be interrupted.

Threads of black lines, like poisonous snakes, wriggled and crawled. Although blocked by the white mist, under the intense pounding, the entire white mist seemed to develop cracks.

This actually gave the Void Realm mastermind an opportunity!

The activation of 'Return to Truth' seemed to be obstructed by the opponent!

Facing such a crisis, Li Fan remained calm despite his shock.

Because of the effect of 'Concentric Unity,' he still seemed to be immersed in Shou Qiu's detached state of mind when he resolutely sacrificed himself to destroy everything.

Fearless of life and death naturally meant fearless of any unexpected events.

Even though this state was rapidly diminishing with Shou Qiu's departure, Li Fan's mind was incredibly clear at this moment.

He had personally witnessed 'Return to Truth' taking action and returning everything to stars with a single thought.

The Void Realm mastermind was clearly not an opponent of the Stars.

Therefore, it was not that the opponent had surpassed the transformation of truth and falsehood of 'Return to Truth.'

"Those rhythmic poundings only interrupted my casting process."

"Although 'Return to Truth' is only a thought away, with the Void Realm mastermind's methods, they could forcefully prolong this brief moment as much as possible."

"As for the countless black threads invading from outside the white mist now..."

In a past life, Yuan Shi Bai Gu had entered the 'Return to Truth' space and accompanied Li Fan in the process of 'Return to Truth.'

What the Void Realm mastermind was doing now was roughly the same.

"The Void Realm mastermind knew they couldn't stop 'Return to Truth,' but they wanted to try and replace me."

"Shou Qiu's enlightenment should be displayed."

"'Return to Truth' is indeed not something ordinary people can wield!"

Li Fan coldly snorted in his heart. He seemed to disregard the thousands of invading black lines as if they were nothing.

Holding his breath and concentrating his mind, he slowly eliminated the disruptive influence from the Void Realm mastermind.

The rhythmic pounding sounds from outside the white mist seemed to diminish significantly.

At the same time, using his hand as a brush, he rapidly wrote in the air.

As his brush strode like a dragon and snake, the traces of his fingertips were exactly the same as the invading black lines.

"When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth!"

With each stroke of Li Fan's brush, one of the Void Realm mastermind's invading methods was forcefully erased by Li Fan!

Under 'Concentric Unity,' Shou Qiu's enlightenment was Li Fan's enlightenment!

Shou Qiu could annihilate the Void Realm Incarnations of countless Saints with a single thought and retreat from the Void Realm's full-power attack.

Li Fan could do the same!

Moreover, compared to Shou Qiu, who would suffer backlash from 'Truth is Falsehood,' Li Fan, who had undergone hundreds of 'Return to Truth' baptisms, could completely ignore the negative effects of 'Truth is Falsehood.'

Initially, Li Fan's writing was somewhat hesitant, as there was still a gap between "comprehension" and "practice."

But with the effects of 'Concentric Unity,' it was as if he had done this all before, and now he was just using a better body. After a brief adaptation, Li Fan's phantom fingers moved rapidly, becoming smoother and smoother.

The myriad black lines created by the Void Realm mastermind were erased one by one by Li Fan.

Even if you have myriad divine abilities, what of it?

Before the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, all are illusions.

The Void Realm mastermind's strength must have been far superior to Li Fan's, but under the 'Truth is Falsehood' divine ability displayed by Li Fan at this moment, they were powerless to use their divine power, despite having immense divine power.

It was resolved with a light flourish.

"This is the authority of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, transcending all."

"Even if residing in the high heavens, one must avoid its edge! Let alone your mere Void Realm!"

After Li Fan erased all the black lines, he suddenly opened his eyes. His spirit was high and his voice boomed like thunder, declaring to the unknown existence outside the white mist.

Unfortunately, he would never hear the Void Realm mastermind's response.

After expelling the influence brought by the Void Realm mastermind, Li Fan's mind returned to normal.

The white mist, which seemed to have been frozen, now surged closer.

This time, there were no more disturbances.

It swallowed all the light, and the familiar darkness returned.

But this time, Li Fan's consciousness did not fall directly into slumber.

Instead, he forced his eyes open, trying to maintain the clarity of his will.

Annihilating the Void Realm Incarnations of myriad Saints and repelling the invading Void Realm enemies.

As all the storms gradually subsided, the surroundings became completely silent.

The entire world seemed to have nothing else but Li Fan.

But Li Fan could faintly glimpse countless rapidly flashing phantom images in the darkness.

These were all the events that Mountains and Seas were supposed to experience.

"At this moment, under the guidance of 'Return to Truth,' I am traversing Mountains and Seas towards its end. Waiting for the appearance of the 'Stars'."

"To put it simply, nothing in Mountains and Seas or the Void Realm is worth 'Return to Truth' taking action. Even the so-called Void Realm mastermind is the same. With my current comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, which can be described as only scratching the surface, I can easily force them back..."

"Only the Stars! Devouring Mountains and Seas and eliminating the Void Realm completely. When the Stars appear, 'Return to Truth' will truly act."

"This is the true indifference to the outcome."

During the traversal, Li Fan could initially maintain a clear consciousness.

But gradually, it was as if he had been working continuously for billions of years without a moment's rest. Waves of fatigue continuously washed over him.

Like a collapsing mountain, Li Fan felt his eyelids growing heavier and heavier, unable to resist this overwhelming drowsiness.

"It's not just an illusion of fatigue. It's..."

"A weariness born from being consumed."

"I... am being consumed?"

In extreme exhaustion, Li Fan finally realized that as he traversed Mountains and Seas, something within his body was also being consumed in parallel.

This made Li Fan unable to focus on the myriad overlapping scenes of Mountains and Seas, but instead concentrated his limited attention on his own body.

The feeling of his body being hollowed out became stronger and stronger.

He even felt as if he were experiencing the illusion of being on the verge of death, and Li Fan gradually felt unprecedented terror.

The transcendent state brought about by Shou Qiu had already receded with the activation of 'Return to Truth.'

At this moment, Li Fan had returned to his original nature.

"'Return to Truth,' what exactly is it?"

"Why is my infinite True Spirit depleting so rapidly?"

"What is being used? Where is it going?"

Fear, confusion, and doubt intermingled, even overshadowing the boundless drowsiness,

causing Li Fan to maintain only a sliver of consciousness, moving only on instinct.

But it was as if he were trapped in a dream, muddled, with only instinctive thoughts flashing.

And no natural thought processes.

After an unknown period, the evolution outside the darkness seemed to stop.

It was as if they had reached the end of Mountains and Seas, and the atmosphere of deathly silence became even more intense.

A ray of starlight seemed to pierce the darkness but was suppressed again.

In this absolute void where a lone star appeared and disappeared, numerous light and shadows rippled again.

Mountains and Seas, and the Void Realm, reappeared!

Li Fan sensed that the consumption within his body had finally stopped, and a string that had been taut in his heart snapped.

Unable to resist the drowsiness any longer, he fell into a deep sleep.

...

Anchor Point Year 1.

When Li Fan regained consciousness, his eyes were initially filled with confusion.

Then, the scenes of Shou Qiu Gong, the Void Realm mastermind, and the subsequent endless extraction of True Spirit...

Scenes surged like a tide.

The feeling of his body being hollowed out remained as if substantial, even after 'Return to Truth.'

This caused Li Fan's pupils to contract sharply.

"'Return to Truth!'"

Li Fan shouted in his heart.

But it was not to activate 'Return to Truth' again.

Instead, he wanted to confront 'Return to Truth' and demand an explanation.

As expected, 'Return to Truth' remained silent.

Li Fan was furious in his heart, but fortunately, after a moment, he calmed down.

"Thinking carefully, countless previous 'Return to Truth' activations were probably no different from this one."

"It's just that I fell into a deep sleep previously, while only this time, I witnessed the entire process of 'Return to Truth' activation with my consciousness completely clear."

"..."

"'Return to Truth' is attached to me and does not leave. It must be for a reason."

"But the reason..."

Li Fan's mouth twitched slightly.

However, having experienced so much, he was no longer a hot-blooded youth acting on impulse.

If 'Return to Truth' was attached to him, and he couldn't get rid of it, then similarly, he couldn't get rid of 'Return to Truth.'

"Moreover, even if I give up and indulge in idleness, 'Return to Truth' will still activate after my death. I would have suffered the torment of being extracted for nothing..."

After careful consideration, Li Fan had to temporarily accept this reality.

His rebellious emotions gradually subsided.

"Fortunately, guided by Shou Qiu, although I maintained a clear consciousness, I only glimpsed the truth of 'Return to Truth's' activation, yet it has caused more doubts..."

"The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood can theoretically create Mountains and Seas. Why extract my infinite True Spirit?"

"To recreate Mountains and Seas?"

"Where did my infinite True Spirit come from?"

Li Fan raised his hand, feeling his mortal body, which had not yet inherited cultivation.

"The feeling of being hollowed out has disappeared."

"I have returned to my normal state."

"Infinite True Spirit, it really seems infinite."

But the feeling of being on the verge of death due to extreme depletion during the activation of 'Return to Truth' was still vivid.

Li Fan's eyelids twitched, and his mind was in turmoil for a long time.

"No wonder you were always so eager to leave. What's the rush?"

In his annoyance, Li Fan directly ignored the character strings of inheritance options flashing before his eyes.

Li Fan walked quickly and arrived at the summit of Jieli Mountain, trying to relieve his inner frustration.

"How laughable that I have been striving for eternal life and freedom all my life."

"'Return to Truth' is both the key to unlocking the path to eternal life and a shackle. Only when I completely cast it aside can I achieve true freedom."

Li Fan suddenly thought of his hundred lifetimes of foundation building.

He suddenly realized how ridiculously wrong he had been.

"My true foundation should not be to forge my Dao foundation by including 'Return to Truth.' Instead, it should be to completely exclude 'Return to Truth' and build my Dao foundation with pure self."

"However, both paths lead to the same result, and both are extremely difficult!"

Li Fan frowned deeply and sat on Jieli Mountain for several years.

He watched the clouds gather and disperse all day long, and finally slowly accepted his current situation.

"Transformation of Truth and Falsehood..."

Li Fan stood up and gently pointed at a blank space on the mountaintop.

A wooden house appeared out of thin air, born from nothingness, both false and real.

Li Fan lightly tapped again, using the divine ability "Truth is Falsehood" to erase it.

He savored the difference between these two actions and revealed a thoughtful expression.

Then, Li Fan on Jieli Mountain repeatedly performed the process of "Falsehood is True, Truth is Falsehood."

Slowly, a realization dawned upon him.

"My level of comprehension of 'Truth is Falsehood, Falsehood is Truth' is not on the same level."

"Especially after experiencing Shou Qiu's annihilation of the Three Saints' Incarnations in the previous life."

"The level of 'Truth is Falsehood' far surpasses that of 'Falsehood is Truth.'"

"If I operate with all my might, I can forcefully erase the effects created by the Void Realm mastermind. But conversely, if I want to generate disasters of that magnitude out of thin air..."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and reached out to the distant sky, making a gentle stroke.

He picked up his brush several times but then put it down gently.

Finally, he let out a sigh and concluded, "I cannot do it."

He then began to ponder again. "Both sides of the same coin, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, unlike the Great Dao of Virtue. Although there may be slight differences in the level of comprehension of 'Dao' and 'Virtue,' they are still within a certain limit. Maintaining corresponding overall perfection."

"But now, the difference in my comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is so huge..."

"It's as if the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is pieced together by two Great Daos."

"'Truth is Falsehood, Falsehood is Truth.' When truth becomes falsehood... falsehood becomes true."

"'Return to Truth.'"

Li Fan seemed to have glimpsed something.

But it was all speculation, with no concrete evidence.

"Perhaps, by going further back in time, and meeting that final Saint again, I might be able to resolve many of these doubts. But..."

"It's meaningless."

"To truly touch the answer and unravel all mysteries, one must stand at the corresponding height."

"God, Stars."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

The desire reignited.

If what had been pushing Li Fan to constantly simulate reincarnations and move forward was the illusory desire for eternal life and freedom, then now it was the instinct to break free from all shackles.

With the experience of the previous life, and after learning the "truth" of 'Return to Truth,' Li Fan's thoughts and actions suddenly changed.

"Even the Void Realm mastermind cannot stop me. Moreover, even if I am no match for them, 'Return to Truth' will act."

"As Shou Qiu said, the esoteric nature of truth and falsehood is never about hiding or revealing. Since 'Return to Truth' is in hand, one must act according to one's heart!"

With this thought, Li Fan no longer hesitated and directly chose to inherit Shou Qiu Gong's memories!

He waved his sleeve, sat down on the ground, and awaited the dramatic changes within the Xuanji Ring on the other shore.

In the Void Realm, Shou Qiu Gong, who was working hard to re-establish Mountains and Seas, showed changes in his expression several times.

Then, the phantom image within the Xuanji Ring quietly left, arriving at the Xuanhuang Realm, the Great Xuan Small World, and Jieli Mountain peak.

"How does it feel to be alive again?" Li Fan asked with a smile.

"Rather... how does it feel to die once?" Shou Qiu pondered for a moment and gave a serious answer.

"...Not bad."

"Well said, Shou Qiu! Shou Qiu is truly open-minded. I am inferior!" Li Fan clapped his hands and praised.

Chapter 1718: Guarding the Mound's Wonderful Aspect Harmonizes

“In my previous life, I entirely relied on Shou Qiu’s assistance to glimpse the true face of the Void Realm’s mastermind. However, I also witnessed the truth of 'Return to Truth.' My heart is truly filled with both joy and sorrow.”

“I don’t fear you laughing at me, Shou Qiu. I spent many years here on Jieli Mountain, yet I still haven’t completely resolved it.” Li Fan sighed as he truthfully recounted his findings after activating 'Return to Truth.'

“Fellow Daoist Fan, you need not be so modest. Possessing the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is a fortune that countless cultivators in Mountains and Seas, and even many Saints, dream of.” Shou Qiu’s phantom image spoke with a solemn expression. After a moment of thought, he continued, “Even if it is as you suspect…”

“'Return to Truth' empowers your infinite True Spirit to continuously reshape Mountains and Seas with the power of truth and falsehood. You also benefit from the convenience of constantly cycling through 'Return to Truth.' In just over a hundred lifetimes, you reached the realm of a Saint of Mountains and Seas. As the saying goes, they are a match made in heaven, inseparable.”

“Fellow Daoist Fan, why don’t you ask yourself, without the help of 'Return to Truth,' how long could you have lived in this Xuanhuang Realm, and to what cultivation realm could you have reached?” Shou Qiu’s phantom image pointed towards the Xuanhuang Realm beyond the hazy clouds atop Jieli Mountain.

Li Fan recalled the various experiences in the Xuanhuang Realm over the years. After a moment of silence, he said helplessly, “I fear I would have struggled to even leave the Great Xuan Small World.”

“Precisely. With 'Return to Truth' in hand, you are already fortunate beyond measure. How could there be no price to pay? If that were the case, wouldn't all the good things in Mountains and Seas be monopolized by you alone?” Shou Qiu chuckled lightly.

“Moreover…”

As if recalling something, Shou Qiu’s smile quickly faded, and he asked, “How do you feel now? Has your infinite True Spirit recovered?”

Li Fan carefully examined himself and nodded slightly, “It should be fine. It’s no different from after every awakening following 'Return to Truth' in the past.”

Shou Qiu couldn’t help but marvel, “Infinite True Spirit, thinking about it now, is truly incredible. Its miraculous fortune is almost on par with 'Return to Truth.' This suggests that the feeling of your body being hollowed out and on the verge of death during your traversals towards the end of Mountains and Seas was likely an illusion caused by the depletion of your True Spirit at an extremely terrifying speed. Once the extraction stops, you naturally recover slowly even without doing anything.”

“Of course, it’s also possible…”

“It was almost entirely depleted. However, after you fell into slumber, you replenished it through some method. Naturally, these two possibilities lead to the same outcome.” Shou Qiu listened to Li Fan’s account and offered another guess.

Li Fan considered it and slowly nodded in agreement.

“Regardless, for now, the workings of 'Return to Truth' haven’t had any major detrimental effects on you. Even the foremost Saints have not yet reached a point where they can participate in the struggle between 'Return to Truth' and the Stars. Fellow Daoist Fan, what you need to focus on now is to improve your own strength as much as possible.” Shou Qiu guided him with earnest advice.

“For this lifetime's inheritance option, it would be best to still choose the ‘Summary of Mountains and Seas Changes.’ It’s truly a waste to use it on inheriting memories. In the previous life, the mastermind behind the Void Realm made a significant impact on Mountains and Seas…”

Li Fan waved his hand, “What’s done is done; it can be observed again. It’s of no consequence. I, however, believe that with your help, Shou Qiu, it is more important. This is also the first time in so many reincarnations that I’ve allowed someone else to inherit…”

Shou Qiu smiled, “What about your aunt? Does she not count?”

Li Fan’s words faltered. He had almost forgotten about that.

However, given his current familiarity with Shou Qiu, he didn’t dwell on it and quickly moved past the topic.

“Shou Qiu, having inherited memories from the previous life, do you feel any changes in yourself?”

“There has indeed been some enhancement. However, the effect is similar to your True Spirit Infusion divine ability. The improvement in aptitude due to increased True Spirit is more significant when the starting point is more ordinary. Once one possesses the potential for Sainthood, even a great increase will not bring about particularly noticeable changes. This is because…”

“The limit of creation in Mountains and Seas lies here.”

“Beings originate from Mountains and Seas, and Saints are on par with Mountains and Seas. Therefore, Saints represent the limit for beings in Mountains and Seas.”

“To go further, to contend with Stars and Gods…”

Shou Qiu looked at Li Fan, “One might need the help of external treasures, or emulate Mountains and Seas swallowing God!”

Li Fan naturally understood what Shou Qiu meant by ‘external treasures’ – it referred to ‘Return to Truth.’ As for emulating Mountains and Seas swallowing God, that was something countless Saints in Mountains and Seas, including the Three Saints, were attempting.

“With the experience from the previous life, the plans for this lifetime can be made more thorough. 'Return to Truth' is truly useful…” Shou Qiu mused as he discussed matters with Li Fan for this lifetime’s endeavors.

“I am essentially your ‘Return to Truth.’ Since you find it useful, let's use it more. As the saying goes, the more the better.”

Having gone through over a hundred reincarnations, Li Fan had always kept the secrets of 'Return to Truth' and his own peculiarities to himself. Now, being able to share everything without reservation brought an unprecedented sense of relief. More importantly, Shou Qiu was trustworthy, and the initiative remained entirely with Li Fan. Whether to inherit or share was entirely Li Fan's decision. If things went wrong, he could choose not to let Shou Qiu inherit in the next lifetime and continue to guard the secrets of 'Return to Truth' alone.

Shou Qiu naturally understood Li Fan's thoughts perfectly. However, he had no objections. Just as he had advised Li Fan, everything in the world comes with a price to pay. Li Fan was fortunate to have the help of 'Return to Truth.' Then, was it not also a fortune for him, Shou Qiu, to be invited into 'Return to Truth'?

“To witness scenery that was previously impossible to see is already a great fortune. There’s no need to be overly demanding. Let’s proceed and observe as we go.”

With this principle in mind, Shou Qiu had no reservations about interacting with Li Fan in this semi-utilitarian, semi-cooperative manner.

“In the previous life, you directly achieved Sainthood using the Shadow of Mountains and Seas, which was too high-profile. You must know that even a single point of True Spirit Infusion was enough to attract the attention of the Three Saints. It would be better to lie low and silently assist the Three Saints in reconnecting Mountains and Seas, moving towards the ancient times.”

“As for the eventual demise of the Three Saints, I suggest observing quietly. Even if the Three Saints disappear for a while, it will not significantly impact their overall strength. Conversely, the weaker you are around the Three Saints, the greater your potential. It might even be possible to change the balance of power within the Xuanji Ring. It’s not impossible.”

“Of course, if you wish to act independently, setting aside the Three Saints, that is also an option. However, my advice is to stay behind the Three Saints upon reaching the initial shores of Mountains and Seas…” Shou Qiu analyzed leisurely, presenting the pros and cons without dictating Li Fan’s choice.

After finishing, Li Fan pondered for a long time before nodding in agreement.

“Shou Qiu’s words are reasonable. It’s better to take shelter under a big tree for shade. Let’s let the Three Saints be our ‘big tree’ for a few more lifetimes!”

“However, that’s for the future. The Void Realm mastermind caused changes in Mountains and Seas, and I must investigate it as soon as possible. I have a vague premonition that it might greatly aid my comprehension of the changes between truth and falsehood, and even the reshaping of Mountains and Seas through 'Return to Truth.'”

Shou Qiu recalled his own experiences from the previous life and nodded thoughtfully, “The battle between the Void Realm and Mountains and Seas is already at the highest level of power clash. It is like a chess game that has been ongoing for countless years.”

“The transformation of truth and falsehood, ‘Remaking Mountains and Seas.’ It could be seen as gathering all scattered chess pieces, both inside and outside the board, back to their original places. By observing the changes on the chessboard, one can glimpse the hand manipulating it from outside…”

“This should be feasible.”

Hearing Shou Qiu’s words, Li Fan’s plan became even more certain. After discussing for a while, they proceeded according to the plan. In this lifetime, having not chosen to inherit cultivation, strictly speaking, Li Fan’s current realm was still that of a mortal. However, with Li Fan’s experience, returning to the Saint realm step by step from a mortal was not a difficult task. To prevent any unexpected accidents, Shou Qiu’s phantom image left behind a trace of power for self-defense before departing. Li Fan no longer relied on the divine shadow of 'God' he had conceived to achieve Sainthood with great fanfare. Instead, he followed the established procedures, cultivating step by step. The path he chose was the Great Dao of 'Cosmic Cycle.' Although he was following the established procedure, given his profound understanding and comprehension of the Great Dao of 'Cosmic Cycle,' as well as his familiarity with the original possibilities, his progress was astonishingly fast. While it took five hundred years in the previous life, this time, he reached Sainthood in just over three hundred years.

This caused a stir throughout Mountains and Seas!

“Reincarnation itself is a great fortune.” In the process of personally re-experiencing it, Li Fan gained new insights into the Great Dao of 'Cosmic Cycle.' Correspondingly, on the 'Great Dao of Return to Truth' panel, the character for ‘Second Cosmic Cycle,’ glowing with seven colors, underwent another change. The radiance gradually faded, as if returning to its unadorned state, revealing its original simple form. On the surface, it appeared no different from the other initial Dao characters. However, as the ‘Lord of ‘Cosmic Cycle,’ Li Fan could clearly sense that the ‘Second Cosmic Cycle’ had now truly been recognized by 'Return to Truth.' Li Fan looked at the other empty positions in the Hall of Great Dao of Return to Truth, a cryptic glint flashing in his eyes. “The Great Dao of Return to Truth might not necessarily be about entering 'Return to Truth,' but rather returning to their original states. The Great Daos of Mountains and Seas all originated from ‘God,’ but after the separation of divine power in Mountains and Seas, they became tainted by the changes in Mountains and Seas. The Daos also changed accordingly. Only by removing the influence of Mountains and Seas can one, to a certain extent, restore their original form and reveal their true appearance.” This realization could only be achieved by Li Fan if he personally walked the path of cultivation again. With Shou Qiu’s influence, by retracing his steps and gaining this enlightenment, Li Fan became even more convinced of the wisdom of bringing Shou Qiu into 'Return to Truth.'

He could share his experiences and insights derived from numerous reincarnations with Shou Qiu, thereby making the plans for this lifetime more comprehensive. Shou Qiu, in turn, could provide guidance based on his vast experience. This was undoubtedly the most prudent course of action. The Saint Emperor Tai Wei’s departure was followed by Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De’s imminent journey into the Void Realm.

On the Other Shore, Shou Qiu offered his parting words, “Looking forward to your good news.” Under the gazes of all the Saints, the three figures successively entered the Void Realm. Initially, they could still sense traces of the three individuals’ auras. But soon, the vast and boundless Void Realm obscured everything. “Let’s hope it is indeed good news.” “This Saint of Mountains and Seas, his thoughts are unfathomable!” “It doesn’t matter. The outcome… should be favorable to us.” In the eyes of Saint Lianshan, countless scenes flashed by in an instant, and he made his judgment. Saint Guihai paused slightly and then nodded in agreement. “Favorable in the moment, but not necessarily for a lifetime. It’s a pity we are trapped and cannot see the full picture,” Saint Tai Yi sighed softly, his gaze deep as he vanished into the depths of the Void Realm.

…

Spanning nearly a hundred thousand years, this journey was extremely long. Even with the Three Saints’ assistance at the beginning, by the time they reached halfway, all their power had been exhausted. Li Fan and Shou Qiu were fine; one was a Saint of Mountains and Seas who wielded the manipulation of truth and falsehood, with unfathomable profundity. The other possessed the Great Dao of Longevity, and simply observing Mountains and Seas was an easy task. But for Dao De, who was merely a newly appointed Saint, and ranked only in the middle among the Saints, he was gradually showing signs of exhaustion.

“Let’s take a break for now.” Resting in the Void Realm was initially a fantasy. However, with Li Fan’s True Spirit Infusion, it became possible. Dao De and Shou Qiu felt the erosion of their existence in the Void Realm gradually being replenished, and even showing signs of improvement. Both lamented, “Daoist Fan’s divine ability is truly incredible! It is indeed the good fortune of Mountains and Seas!”

“Being able to summon and utilize the accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm has immense significance for reconnecting Mountains and Seas,” Shou Qiu said with great excitement, personally feeling the benefits of True Spirit Infusion. And as the two were lamenting, they suddenly discovered that a figure had suddenly descended in the Void Realm. It was Li Fan himself. This phantom image possessed an unfathomable aura. Even in the Void Realm, it attracted the attention of Shou Qiu and Dao De the moment it appeared.

“Daoist Fan… what is this?” Dao De stammered. He could see everything in Mountains and Seas within this blurry and distorted phantom image. Not just the superficial appearances of Mountains and Seas, but even all possible principles within Mountains and Seas! Crucially, Li Fan had never revealed the existence of this phantom image before the Saints in Mountains and Seas.

“This is the Shadow of God.”

“It was obtained by imitating the mystery of the Three Saints' Xuanji Ring.”

“The Mountains and Seas ahead face the Void Realm Incarnations; not a single misstep is allowed.”

“Please, the two of you, join me in the Xuanji!” With that said, a dazzling yet familiar white light erupted from the phantom image. The phantom image vanished, replaced by a white circle extremely similar to the Xuanji Ring on the Other Shore. However, this white circle flickered intermittently, not very stable. In the Void Realm, it seemed on the verge of disappearing at any moment. Li Fan had already taken his seat within it, smiling and waiting for Shou Qiu and Dao De.

“This…” Shou Qiu and Dao De were immediately filled with doubt. It wasn’t that they doubted the authenticity of the Xuanji Ring before them, as they had been seated within it for countless years. The aura was almost identical, and they could clearly distinguish it. It was just that… when did Li Fan become capable of creating the Xuanji Ring like the Three Saints? After all, although the Three Saints had indeed expressed their intention to entrust the secret of the Xuanji Ring to Li Fan in their words, they still needed the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel to forge the Xuanji Ring again. But now, Li Fan had recreated the Xuanji Ring entirely on his own, without relying on the Three Treasures!

“Could it be that in this short time he spent within the Xuanji Ring, he has actually deciphered its mysteries?”

“How is this possible?” The two knew Li Fan could see further, but they couldn’t imagine he could see so far! Li Fan, seeing the subtle changes in Shou Qiu and Dao De’s expressions, chuckled and said, “You two need not hesitate. All your doubts will be resolved once you are seated within the Xuanji. Everything will become clear.”

“Isn’t it said that only those who are the first three to take their seats truly share the same heart and mind?” The Xuanji Ring’s light fluctuated unstably, and Li Fan’s voice sounded like a ghost, “Only those who are the first three to take their seats truly share the same heart and mind.” Shou Qiu and Dao De exchanged glances, and finally, it was Shou Qiu who, undeterred, strode into it.

“I can see that Daoist Fan harbors no ill intentions.”

“This journey is perilous; only by sharing the same heart and mind can we better face the crisis.” Dao De saw this and could only grit his teeth and follow closely behind. With the Three Saints seated, the originally flickering light circle of the Xuanji Ring instantly stabilized. Li Fan’s insights into the Shadow of God truly surfaced like a spring, appearing in their minds. Even for Saints, such insights were an extremely valuable treasure. However, they had no time to pay attention to it now, focusing solely on stabilizing the Xuanji Ring. There were no disturbances. After an unknown period, a new Xuanji Ring, independent of the Three Saints, was born in the Void Realm. And Shou Qiu and Dao De’s expressions changed drastically during this time.

“So that’s how it is! Indeed, Daoist Fan’s gains from this 'Return to Truth' are far beyond my imagination.”

“As expected, only those who wield the manipulation of truth and falsehood can truly comprehend its mighty power. Who would have thought that a mere regression could elevate an ordinary Saint to a level comparable to the Three Saints?” Shou Qiu sighed softly.

“The Three Saints cultivated for countless years to achieve their current divine abilities. Yet, Daoist Fan achieved it in just five hundred cycles… The gap between them is truly astonishing.” Li Fan smiled and replied, “Shou Qiu’s assistance was also indispensable. Otherwise, how could I have understood the Shadow of Mountains and Seas in such a short time?” Compared to Shou Qiu, who had cooperated once before, Dao De seemed somewhat dejected.

“Daoist Fan, you indeed toyed with me several times in the past by relying on the benefits of reincarnation.”

“But my enlightenment of you as a Saint is an undeniable fact,” Li Fan said nonchalantly.

“Alas…” Dao De was rendered speechless. Shou Qiu chuckled and said, “If being toyed with like this could lead to proving the Dao as a Saint, I think countless people in Mountains and Seas would be willing.” Dao De had to admit that Shou Qiu’s words were indeed the truth. All the past events were dismissed with a laugh. Next, it was time for concentricity and trinity!

“So, Daoist Fan’s plan is truly to save the Three Saints?” Shou Qiu asked, surprised upon learning Li Fan’s true intentions. Li Fan nodded slightly, “I have observed the complete ‘Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.’ Although I have grasped the overall changes in Mountains and Seas, there are still many details lacking. Thus, I only have the Shadow of Mountains and Seas, not the Spirit of Mountains and Seas.”

“Therefore, I plan to use the variables of the Three Saints to observe the changes in this segment of Mountains and Seas,” Li Fan pointed ahead and said proudly.

“By gaining one, one can gain all. If we can gain some enlightenment, we can then deduce the entire segment of Mountains and Seas.”

“Moreover…”

“We can hide in the shadows and observe all the methods of the Three Saints. Facing the crisis of life and death, they will surely reveal everything without reservation. Perhaps we can discover their trump cards.”

… Li Fan explained the reasons for his actions. Shou Qiu, after pondering, offered a different opinion.

“Why not try to reverse the situation and eliminate the Three Saints?”

“If we can absorb the Great Daos of Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi into the Hall of Return to Truth, we might be able to settle everything in one go and save a lot of trouble.” Dao De sensed the situation and narrowed his eyes slightly, speaking for Li Fan, “Daoist Fan is afraid.”

“Not only because of the unfathomable divine abilities of the Three Saints, but also because…”

“Tai Yi Saint aside, Lianshan and Guihai, these two are quite hard to fathom.” Li Fan continued slowly, “This is also something I vaguely sensed after observing the ‘Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.’ The so-called Lianshan and Guihai, there are no such Dao paths within Mountains and Seas. The two of them became Saints because of Lianshan and Guihai, rather than proving their Dao through Lianshan and Guihai.”

“Why Lianshan? By what means Guihai?”

“The greatest trump cards of these two, we have never seen clearly.” Shou Qiu nodded in agreement, “Indeed.” Li Fan said, “The Three Saints are from the very beginning of the separation of Mountains and Seas, difficult to fathom by common sense. Perhaps they gained the creation of some primordial ancient artifact, who knows. If we rashly expose 'Return to Truth'…”

“It seems Prying Opportunity's attempt to seize 'Return to Truth,' although unsuccessful, has left you with quite a shadow,” Dao De chuckled. Shou Qiu defended Li Fan, “This is only natural for a person.” After a moment of contemplation, Shou Qiu added, “Steady progress has its merits. For now, our wings are not yet fully grown, and it is indeed not suitable to confront the Three Saints head-on. Especially since you said the Three Saints might have gained the creation of primordial ancient artifacts…”

“I believe it is true!” With their minds aligned, Li Fan quickly reacted, “Shou Qiu’s suspicion stems from the Shadow of God?” Shou Qiu nodded, “In my previous life, when I saw the Shadow of God, I merely thought the Three Saints had reached the pinnacle of their cultivation and could actually glimpse the existence of ‘God.’ However, after reading the ‘Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes’ through 'Return to Truth,' I have a new idea.”

“With the power of 'Return to Truth,' I finally obtained this scroll that only recorded the shadow, not the spirit of God. How did the Three Saints obtain the spirit of Mountains and Seas? Was it truly just through their peerless talent?” Upon hearing this, Li Fan and Dao De both fell silent.

“There are countless beings in the world, and some may indeed be extraordinary, but there is always a limit. And some things clearly transcend this limit. The Three Saints, from nothingness to creation, are indeed divinely talented. But I believe…”

“Beings of Mountains and Seas, after all, are born from Mountains and Seas. To see the true God, one can only rely on external means.” Shou Qiu gazed at the Shadow of God floating above Li Fan’s head, feeling inspired and sighing. Li Fan could faintly empathize with Shou Qiu’s thoughts. Although Shou Qiu often modestly claimed his cultivation was mediocre, he had, after all, cultivated from being a mere Warden of the Sea to a Saint. He definitely possessed his own pride. But all of this was instantly smoothed away upon truly witnessing the power of 'Return to Truth.' Talent and effort were all irrelevant before 'Return to Truth.' Even after cultivating diligently for billions of years, the scenery that was still hard to glimpse was now clearly visible under the guidance of 'Return to Truth.'

“This is not a matter of talent, but a limitation of our origin.”

“The creations of Mountains and Seas are destined to be confined within these Mountains and Seas. To aspire to see the True God, one must rely on external objects.” Shou Qiu said slowly, “Daoist Fan, since you started as a mortal and had the treasure of 'Return to Truth' by your side, perhaps you don’t empathize deeply with this. Dao De should have a more profound experience.” After a long period of silence, Li Fan finally agreed with Shou Qiu’s conjecture. His estimation of the Three Saints’ strength, unknowingly, rose another level.

“Taking advantage of this opportune moment, perhaps we can use the Void Realm Incarnations to thoroughly investigate the secrets of the Three Saints.” After resting, the three set off again towards their destination. However, this time, Li Fan and Dao De would provide protection, while Shou Qiu immersed himself in seclusion. Li Fan, having obtained the ‘Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes,’ could comprehend the Shadow of God. Shou Qiu, naturally, also gained something. Moreover, over the years, he had personally witnessed the changes in Mountains and Seas. The detailed entries in the manual were as if everything he had experienced. Everything was vivid. As if going through another cycle of Mountains and Seas' changes, Shou Qiu’s aura became increasingly ethereal.

“In the previous life, after comprehending the manipulation of truth and falsehood, Shou Qiu could instantly kill four Saints.”

“In this life, after obtaining the ‘Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes’ through 'Return to Truth,' who knows how much stronger he has become.” Li Fan looked at the meditating Shou Qiu, as if he had gained a sense of confidence out of thin air. Even if the six Saints were in a fierce battle ahead, there was no longer any need to be so timid.

Chapter 1719: Situations Change With Worldly Affairs

Li Fan's words left everyone speechless. Influenced by the 'Concentric Unity' of the Xuanji Ring, the Saints themselves were reluctant to see the three Saints of the Mountains and Seas perish in front of them. However, the Three Saints' strength was extraordinary, far surpassing that of others. Even if they were willing to aid, they feared they would be powerless.

Shou Qiu Gong, at this moment, also revealed a look of worry and said, "If the Three Saints perish, the Mountains and Seas will be without leaders. I fear we won't be able to withstand the catastrophe of Dao Annihilation. If two more segments of Mountains and Seas are lost to Dao Annihilation..."

"May I ask the Three Saints, how long do the preceding Void Realms span?"

Saint Gui Hai replied in a deep voice, "The preceding Void Realms have already spanned nearly a hundred thousand years. If the Mountains and Seas are destroyed again, our grand plan to reconnect them will fail."

The inevitable outcome was laid bare before all the Saints. No matter how slim the hope, they had to fight.

"Although we may perish, we must not act rashly. First, let us successfully reconnect the hundred thousand years of Void Realms, and simultaneously carry out the rescue.
