As long as we can hold on until we reconnect the Mountains and Seas, we will gain a segment of creation's assistance, and perhaps we can directly resolve the crisis."

"Therefore, we don't necessarily have to win. We merely need to help us stall the battle."

Li Fan's arrival at a different point in time, and the resulting situation, led the Three Saints to make different resolutions. But in unison, they turned their gaze to Li Fan. After a moment of contemplation, they did not ask Li Fan forward.

"True Spirit Infusion is extraordinary. As long as Daoist Fan is here, the reconnection of Mountains and Seas can be achieved one day sooner. If we were to drag you down and cause you to perish, then we would regret it immensely," Saint Tai Yi said, shaking his head.

Li Fan smiled, but still voluntarily offered, "The Three Saints' concerns are not unreasonable. My True Spirit Infusion and assistance in reconnecting Mountains and Seas are merely a part of it. Who says only my true body can accomplish this?"

Saying this, Li Fan took a deep breath and reached out towards the Void Realm outside the Mountains and Seas. It was as if a vast tide was being stirred by him, threatening to engulf the Mountains and Seas. Even the Other Shore felt its power, trembling slightly. It seemed to be incredibly strenuous, as Li Fan's brow furrowed and his expression became solemn. The Three Saints followed the direction of Li Fan's gesture, their eyes revealing surprise.

"Could it be..."

Only then did all the Saints realize that Li Fan was extracting True Spirits from the Void Realm. But with such a grand display, how many True Spirits was he drawing? Soon, they would know the answer. Even with the collective knowledge of all the Saints, they could not help but be dumbfounded.

"Shou Qiu Gong, lend me a hand!"

As if reaching his limit, Li Fan suddenly gritted his teeth and shouted. Shou Qiu Gong responded, supporting him with the infinite life force of the Great Dao of Longevity. Infused with vitality, Li Fan's drawing power seemed to multiply infinitely. Finally, he drew the accumulated True Spirits from the Void Realm and brought them to the Mountains and Seas. At this moment, because of this boundless, immeasurable accumulated True Spirit, the current Mountains and Seas trembled. The continuous Mountains and Seas seemed to reveal layers of overlapping shadows, giving the illusion that another set of Mountains and Seas appeared above the existing ones. All this was because Li Fan had forcibly summoned the accumulated True Spirits from the Void Realm, which could almost reshape a segment of Mountains and Seas anew! Although True Spirits were formless and intangible, such a massive accumulation would inevitably have impacted the Mountains and Seas. However, all the Saints observed that all the extracted True Spirits were skillfully confined by Li Fan within a circle. It seemed like a simple circle, but it contained infinite cycles, ingeniously resolving the impact of the accumulated True Spirits. The weight of a circle was immeasurable, as if supporting the Mountains and Seas. Yet, Li Fan handled it with ease, as if it weighed nothing.

"The Dao of Universe Cycle, reaching the pinnacle!" "Coupled with the divine ability of True Spirit Infusion... Below the Three Saints, he is perhaps the strongest." Amidst the Saints' exclamations, they also vaguely glimpsed Li Fan's true strength. "Fortunately, I have not disgraced my mission." Having successfully gathered the Ring of True Spirits within the Other Shore, Li Fan let out a long sigh and cupped his hands in salutation. He paused slightly before pointing to the peculiar circle and saying, "The True Spirits accumulated in this ring are absolutely sufficient to meet the needs of all the Saints in reconnecting the Mountains and Seas. At the same time, I will leave behind a phantom image to cooperate." "Furthermore, if the situation becomes truly dire, this Ring of True Spirits can be forcibly broken. With the dispersion of immeasurable accumulated True Spirits, we can temporarily resist the impact of Dao Annihilation and gain a brief respite." Li Fan slowly explained the marvelous aspects of this ring to everyone. Saint Tai Yi nodded slightly, "What Daoist Fan says is true. We truly did not expect that a Saint who had just attained the Dao would possess such power. To support the Mountains and Seas with such ease..." Li Fan laughed and said, "Everyone sees this Ring of True Spirits as having the weight of Mountains and Seas, but in my eyes, it is merely an extension of my arms. It is just slightly heavier." "Even so, without Shou Qiu Gong's assistance, I would have almost failed. It was truly a bit embarrassing." He attributed all his accomplishments to that peculiar ability to manipulate True Spirits. And Li Fan had previously stated that this ability seemed related to the transcendent Immortal Realm that had vanished. The current Mountains and Seas could not be investigated. Even the Three Saints found it difficult to discern the truth of Li Fan's words. Moreover, now was not the time to delve into such matters. Since the crucial logistical problem had been resolved, the next step was to formally discuss the aid plan. The principle remained the same. Reconnecting the Mountains and Seas required the Three Saints to bear the brunt. Their true bodies naturally could not leave. And without the merit of reconnecting the Mountains and Seas, even if they went, it would not have a significant effect of increasing their strength. But if the Three Saints could receive Li Fan's support, perhaps the outcome of their demise could be altered. The miraculous effects of True Spirit Infusion had already been witnessed by all the Saints collectively. "I need Shou Qiu Gong and Dao De to accompany me, and also..." Like in the previous life, Li Fan selected his companions. "I request that the Three Saints kindly disclose all their divine abilities. Only then can I be prepared." Li Fan's gaze was fervent, and his expression was calm as he stared at the Three Saints. In the Xuanji Ring, there was a moment of silence. Although they were united in heart and mind, in reality, the Three Saints knew the others, but the others could not truly know the Three Saints. Li Fan, under the guise of supporting the rescue, wished to seek the foundation of the Three Saints. This was justifiable from both reason and emotion. The Three Saints did not remain silent for too long. "It is as it should be." "Listen carefully." What followed was not solely transmitted to Li Fan, Shou Qiu Gong, and Dao De, but was openly declared within the Xuanji Ring. "Apart from our respective Dao of Proof divine abilities such as Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi, we also possess some magical treasures." "The Lianshan Staff, Guihai Shovel, and All Beings Cudgel, you may have seen them before." "However, besides these, there are three innate malevolent items that have never been revealed to others." "We only use them to fight enemies when our lives are in danger, rather than in ordinary times." As these words were spoken, they immediately attracted the attention of all the Saints. "Innate malevolent items? What are these?" "I have heard of the creation of the Primordial Beginning. These innate malevolent items are unheard of." Saint Tai Yi provided the answer for everyone. "Mountains and Seas are divided into spirits. Although God perished, at the moment of his passing, immeasurable malevolent energy scattered. Mountains and Seas evolved, and some of them were contaminated, thus becoming innate malevolent items." "Originating from God, yet contaminated by some of God's divine abilities. They are not within the scope of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, and are exceedingly mysterious." Saying this, Saint Tai Yi took out an object. It was the 'Fate Rope' that Li Fan had seen in his previous life! "It looks like ordinary hemp rope," Bai Xiao muttered softly. Saint Tai Yi chuckled lightly and tossed the hemp rope towards Bai Xiao. Countless fine threads, like dancing dragons, instantly wove a straw puppet in front of Bai Xiao. It was in the likeness of Bai Xiao. The moment the rope puppet was born, it was as if an inexplicable existence had locked onto it and the true Shou Qiu through some method. Facing the sight of another self, Shou Qiu Gong's hair stood on end, instinctively sensing a fatal crisis. And what happened next quickly proved Shou Qiu Gong's premonition. As if a gentle breeze had passed in the Void Realm, a thread constituting the rope puppet Shou Qiu Gong suddenly floated out from its body and was instantly swallowed by the surrounding Dao Annihilation. Correspondingly... Shou Qiu Gong truly sensed that a part of himself had been drawn out and dissipated from nothingness! A turtle shell suppressed from above, an ancestral bone attached from the brow. Shou Qiu Gong, already in a perilous situation, became even more precarious as his strength instantly declined. Although his head was still held high, his entire body had been forcefully compressed by a section. Threads of blood seeped out, and the moment they flowed out of his body, they were absorbed by the attached ancestral bone. The process of turning into white bone became more apparent. Externally, it was as if the entire skeleton was exposed on Shou Qiu Gong's hunched body. Drawing out a thread from a broken rope, hanging by a thread! The fate rope's extraction continued. Shou Qiu Gong felt more and more clearly that his life force was rapidly draining away. The Great Dao of Longevity he had comprehended and controlled, under the fatal crisis, unleashed an unprecedented brilliant green light. It maximally repaired Shou Qiu Gong's injuries. If it were only the pressure from the turtle shell and the ancestral bone, Shou Qiu Gong might have held on for a while longer with the characteristics of the Great Dao of Longevity, but the consumption from the fate rope was a direct extraction of his essence. As the rope puppet Shou Qiu Gong became increasingly desolate, Shou Qiu Gong's life substance grew thinner and thinner. Even though the power of Longevity continuously replenished his body, it could not stop the reduction of his life's upper limit. "This fate rope's technique is actually subtly similar to the 'Truth is Falsehood' divine ability!" "But it does not negate my existence from the Dao of Truth and Falsehood, but rather uses some unknown power to extract my life substance..." Life was like a candle flame in a fierce wind, about to be extinguished. Shou Qiu Gong's heart was calm, without sadness or joy. Seizing the last moments of his life, he comprehended the turtle shell, the ancestral bone, and the fate rope, and pondered ways to counter them. He even proactively gave up resisting, using his own faster descent as a price to attempt different coping methods. "Although the turtle shell is small and thin, it seems to represent the boundless Upper Mountain." "The Saints say they are one with Mountains and Seas, but only when Mountains and Seas truly press down upon them can one feel the weight of Mountains and Seas." "Even the realm of the Three Saints might not be able to resist it directly." "Perhaps I can use my understanding of Mountains and Seas to neutralize some of the pressure, as if I were already in the mountains..." "The ancestral bone attaches, everything within the body returns to it without resistance, just as all rivers flow east to the sea, as if conforming to heavenly principles. But there are rivers that flow west, forming another ocean! Although you are the ancestor of all beings, I am the Warden of Mountains and Seas!" Shou Qiu Gong's eyes seemed to burn with fire, as if sensing his thoughts. The flesh and blood flowing towards the ancestral bone within his body also paused, as if caught in a dilemma, unsure what to do. "As for this fate rope..." "The method of extracting life substance is truly hard to guard against. The moment the rope puppet is born, all negative effects that happen to it will simultaneously occur to me. This kind of corresponding binding can perhaps only be resolved through the manipulation of truth and falsehood." Shou Qiu Gong vaguely found a path to resolution but forcefully suppressed the urge to try. This was different from before; he was already locked onto by the fate puppet, coupled with the parasitic ancestral bone. His internal condition might be perceived by the Void Realm Incarnation. If he were to forcefully use the manipulation of truth and falsehood to resolve it at this moment, the opponent might detect the existence of Return to Truth. "A dying struggle is meaningless." "Forget it." On the verge of death, Shou Qiu Gong's heart was completely clear. Because he knew that as long as Li Fan activated Return to Truth again, he would return from nothingness. Without dwelling on the question of whether that 'I' was truly 'me.' The dying Shou Qiu Gong actually felt a sense of melancholy. It was precisely because he held the idea that he would definitely return that Shou Qiu Gong felt no ordinary emotions in the face of such great horror as life and death. This strangeness made Shou Qiu Gong feel that his lifelong pursuit of 'Longevity' had become worthless. "If there is no death, what meaning does Longevity have?" "The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood will exhaust all under heaven!" ... At this moment, the reinforcement from the Three Saints finally arrived, albeit late. They seemed to be quite wary of using the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope, not as decisive as the Void Realm Incarnations. Witnessing Shou Qiu Gong about to perish, they finally released the three objects. Silently, they enveloped Shou Qiu Gong. Compared to what the Void Realm Incarnations released, the Three Saints' objects were... more sinister! The Void Realm Incarnations used pure 'objects.' But what the Three Saints took out now seemed like living beings. Shou Qiu Gong even vaguely felt three different gazes constantly scrutinizing his body. Faint, eerie laughter occasionally echoed in his ears. A cold, sinister aura infiltrated his body like an unstoppable force, causing Shou Qiu Gong to feel intensely 'uncomfortable.' It was not pain, but instinctive repulsion and avoidance! Fortunately, the three objects were ultimately controlled by the Three Saints and did not forget their mission. Turtle shell against turtle shell, the continuous phantom of Upper Mountain pressed down, while boundless Upper Mountain resisted. Ancestral bone against ancestral bone, with the infiltration of another force from the ancestor of Mountains and Seas' beings, Shou Qiu Gong's internal flesh and blood loss instantly became disoriented, not knowing where to go. Fate rope against fate rope. In the void, another rope puppet Shou Qiu Gong quietly emerged. The life essence that was invisibly drawn out was slowly replenished by it! The Three Saints' direct intervention, in an instant, reversed Shou Qiu Gong's precarious situation, pulling him back from the brink of death! The Three Saints and their Void Realm Incarnations were evenly matched, unable to decide a winner! Shou Qiu Gong, having escaped disaster, had no time to rejoice. Instead, an inexplicable sense of unease arose in his heart. It was not for himself, but for the Three Saints. "If it was only an even match... How did the Three Saints perish in the previous life's timeline?" "Could it be..." Shou Qiu Gong's heart trembled, and just as he was about to speak a warning. But the Void Realm Incarnations seemed to have been waiting for this moment. Just as the Three Saints released the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope to save Shou Qiu Gong, ripples appeared in the Void Realm. Indeed, three more objects descended! Like flying stones from outer space, hurled into the center of the arena. The countless lines in the battleground of the six Saints were instantly thrown into chaos! The fate rope bound Lianshan; the turtle shell suppressed Guihai; the ancestral bone captured Tai Yi. As if planned, the Void Realm had actually evolved these three objects and imposed them upon the Three Saints! Witnessing this, Shou Qiu Gong instantly understood. The turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope used by the Void Realm Incarnations were, after all, merely evolutions of the Void Realm's power, not actual existing objects. As long as enough power was invested, it could naturally evolve into a second or third copy. But the Three Saints only possessed the original turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope. At this moment, due to a moment's lapse in judgment used to save Shou Qiu Gong's life, they were now in a perilous situation. The Three Saints and their Void Realm Incarnations were already evenly matched. Now, the addition of the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope became the final straw that broke the camel's back! The Three Saints wished to recall their treasures to support them, but they were already entangled by their first copies. They had even abandoned their original target, Shou Qiu Gong, and were determined to hold back the opponents, even at the cost of their own forms gradually disintegrating. Shou Qiu Gong suddenly looked towards the depths of the Void Realm, where it seemed a figure, having made a move, revealed a faint, triumphant smile. Given Shou Qiu Gong's temperament, he naturally could not stand by and watch the Three Saints perish because of him. Moreover, Li Fan's plan in this life was precisely to save the Three Saints and observe their changes. Instinctively, he wanted to provide aid. But that glance towards the outside of the Void Realm made Shou Qiu Gong hesitate slightly. It was not because he feared death, but rather... In an instant, after countless deductions, Shou Qiu Gong finally found a suitable method. "The plan has changed." "Daoist Fan, do not reveal yourself. Just observe in secret." "If any other anomalies descend from outside the Void Realm..." "They will only be directed at me." After transmitting his message, without waiting for Li Fan's response, Shou Qiu Gong no longer concealed his enlightenment in this life. The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.' Without reservation, he unleashed everything. In just a breath, his body, ravaged by the turtle shell, ancestral bone, and fate rope, was fully restored. He took a step, crossing the continuous Void Realm, and arrived in the center where the Three Saints were surrounded. "The flow of fate, whether true or false, like a dream, like an illusion. To think of it as false, to call it false!" Shou Qiu Gong's voice spread through the Void Realm. Like a gentle breeze passing by. It seemed harmless, but in reality... Turbulent waves were suppressed by a pair of invisible giant hands and forced to calm down. Many of the manifesting figures were drastically reduced. And the three Void Realm Incarnations closest to Shou Qiu Gong had already become transparent! Until the clear breeze passed and they vanished. Only then did the Three Saints' Void Realm Incarnations realize with belated terror.

Chapter 1720: Inheriting the Divine Power of the Three Sages

"Daoist Fan's sermon on Mountains and Seas upon achieving Sainthood caused quite a stir in the Saint Dynasty, requiring considerable effort to quell it." Before Saint Tai Wei departed, he suddenly uttered this.

Li Fan instantly understood the reason behind this.

The subjects of the Saint Dynasty lived forever under the protection of Saint Tai Wei, without disasters or misfortunes. Although it could be called happiness, they were completely unaware of anything outside the Saint Dynasty.

Beings like True Immortals, Nameless Ones, Transcended Ones, and even Mountains and Seas, were all unheard of to the subjects of the Saint Dynasty.

Li Fan's attainment of the Dao in one fell swoop revealed the secrets of the Saints of Mountains and Seas.

This led countless subjects of the Saint Dynasty to glimpse a world they should not have seen.

They learned that the Saint Emperor was not the greatest existence in all of Mountains and Seas, and that they too could become as strong as the Saint Emperor.

Even surpass him!

The hearts of the people were stirred, and the stability of the peaceful Saint Dynasty was disrupted.

Although it was decisively suppressed by the Saint Emperor Tai Wei, it still caused considerable loss. It wasn't a fatal blow, but it was a severe injury.

This had never happened in the history of the Saint Dynasty, which was why Saint Tai Wei made such a remark.

"What is bound to come, will eventually come. I merely brought it forward. Perhaps it is even more beneficial for you," Li Fan said meaningfully.

With his hand, he beckoned towards the Void Realm, drawing a mass of accumulated True Spirit and infusing it into a Saintly Fortune Elixir in his hand.

"This elixir is compensation and can make up for Daoist's loss. Also, if there truly are individuals among the countless subjects of the Saint Dynasty who are exceptionally talented, what harm is there in opening a path for them?"

Saint Tai Wei knew that Li Fan's sight could penetrate the Void Realm's obstruction, thus being far-sighted.

"Does he perhaps see something in the future?"

"For instance, my demise?"

Li Fan's attitude made Saint Tai Wei secretly ponder, as he took the Saintly Fortune Elixir infused with True Spirit and pondered Li Fan's words.

"Perhaps Daoist Fan is right. If there truly are those with the potential to become Saints, what harm is there in letting them prove their Dao? Emerging from the Saint Dynasty, they would naturally be our allies in the future. Perhaps they could even assist me in refining Saintly Fortune Elixirs, so I wouldn't have to work so hard in the future..."

Saint Tai Wei's heart stirred, and his beliefs were unknowingly rewritten.

The Saint Emperor took his leave and departed.

Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De were also about to set off for the Void Realm ahead.

"Looking forward to your good news."

Under the gaze of all the Saints, the three figures successively entered the Void Realm.

Initially, they could still sense some traces of the three individuals' auras. But soon, the vast and boundless Void Realm obscured everything.

"Hope it is indeed good news."

"This Saint of Mountains and Seas, his thoughts are unfathomable!"

"No matter. The outcome... should be favorable to us."

In the eyes of Saint Lianshan, countless scenes flashed by in an instant, and he made his judgment.

Saint Guihai paused slightly and then nodded in agreement.

"Favorable in the moment, but not necessarily for a lifetime. It's a pity we are trapped and cannot see the full picture," Saint Tai Yi sighed softly, his gaze deep as he vanished into the depths of the Void Realm.

...

Spanning nearly a hundred thousand years, this journey was extremely long.

Even with the Three Saints' assistance at the beginning, by the time they reached halfway, all their power had been exhausted.

Li Fan and Shou Qiu were fine; one was a Saint of Mountains and Seas who wielded the manipulation of truth and falsehood, with unfathomable profundity. The other possessed the Great Dao of Longevity, and simply observing Mountains and Seas was an easy task.

But for Dao De, who was merely a newly appointed Saint, and ranked only in the middle among the Saints, he was gradually showing signs of exhaustion.

"Let's take a break for now."

Resting in the Void Realm was initially a fantasy. However, with Li Fan's True Spirit Infusion, it became possible.

Dao De and Shou Qiu felt the erosion of their existence in the Void Realm gradually being replenished, and even showing signs of improvement. Both lamented, "Daoist Fan's divine ability is truly incredible! It is indeed the good fortune of Mountains and Seas!"

"Being able to summon and utilize the accumulated True Spirits of the Void Realm has immense significance for reconnecting Mountains and Seas," Shou Qiu said with great excitement, personally feeling the benefits of True Spirit Infusion.

And as the two were lamenting, they suddenly discovered that a figure had suddenly descended in the Void Realm.

It was Li Fan himself.

This phantom image possessed an unfathomable aura. Even in the Void Realm, it attracted the attention of Shou Qiu and Dao De the moment it appeared.

"Daoist Fan... what is this?" Dao De stammered.

He could see everything in Mountains and Seas within this blurry and distorted phantom image.

Not just the superficial appearances of Mountains and Seas, but even all possible principles within Mountains and Seas!

Crucially, Li Fan had never revealed the existence of this phantom image before the Saints in Mountains and Seas.

"This is the Shadow of God."

"It was obtained by imitating the mystery of the Three Saints' Xuanji Ring."

"The Mountains and Seas ahead face the Void Realm Incarnations; not a single misstep is allowed."

"Please, the two of you, join me in the Xuanji!"

With that said, a dazzling yet familiar white light erupted from the phantom image.

The phantom image vanished, replaced by a white circle extremely similar to the Xuanji Ring on the Other Shore.

However, this white circle flickered intermittently, not very stable. In the Void Realm, it seemed on the verge of disappearing at any moment.

Li Fan had already taken his seat within it, smiling and waiting for Shou Qiu and Dao De.

"This..."

Shou Qiu and Dao De were immediately filled with doubt.

It wasn't that they doubted the authenticity of the Xuanji Ring before them, as they had been seated within it for countless years. The aura was almost identical, and they could clearly distinguish it.

It was just that... when did Li Fan become capable of creating the Xuanji Ring like the Three Saints?

After all, although the Three Saints had indeed expressed their intention to entrust the secret of the Xuanji Ring to Li Fan in their words, they still needed the Lianshan Staff, the Guihai Shovel, and the All Beings Cudgel to forge the Xuanji Ring again.

But now, Li Fan had recreated the Xuanji Ring entirely on his own, without relying on the Three Treasures!

"Could it be that in this short time he spent within the Xuanji Ring, he has actually deciphered its mysteries?"

"How is this possible?"

The two knew Li Fan could see further, but they couldn't imagine he could see so far!

Li Fan, seeing the subtle changes in Shou Qiu and Dao De's expressions, chuckled and said, "You two need not hesitate. All your doubts will be resolved once you are seated within the Xuanji. Everything will become clear."

"Isn't it said that only those who are the first three to take their seats truly share the same heart and mind?"

The Xuanji Ring's light fluctuated unstably, and Li Fan's voice sounded like a ghost, "Only those who are the first three to take their seats truly share the same heart and mind."

Shou Qiu and Dao De exchanged glances, and finally, it was Shou Qiu who, undeterred, strode into it.

"I can see that Daoist Fan harbors no ill intentions."

"This journey is perilous; only by sharing the same heart and mind can we better face the crisis."

Dao De saw this and could only grit his teeth and follow closely behind.

With the Three Saints seated, the originally flickering light circle of the Xuanji Ring instantly stabilized.

Li Fan's insights into the Shadow of God truly surfaced like a spring, appearing in their minds.

Even for Saints, such insights were an extremely valuable treasure.

However, they had no time to pay attention to it now, focusing solely on stabilizing the Xuanji Ring.

There were no disturbances.

After an unknown period, a new Xuanji Ring, independent of the Three Saints, was born in the Void Realm.

And Shou Qiu and Dao De's expressions changed drastically during this time.

"So that's how it is! Indeed, Daoist Fan's gains from this 'Return to Truth' are far beyond my imagination."

"As expected, only those who wield the manipulation of truth and falsehood can truly comprehend its mighty power. Who would have thought that a mere regression could elevate an ordinary Saint to a level comparable to the Three Saints?" Shou Qiu sighed softly.

"The Three Saints cultivated for countless years to achieve their current divine abilities. Yet, Daoist Fan achieved it in just five hundred cycles... The gap between them is truly astonishing."

Li Fan smiled and replied, "Shou Qiu's assistance was also indispensable. Otherwise, how could I have understood the Shadow of Mountains and Seas in such a short time?"

Compared to Shou Qiu, who had cooperated once before, Dao De seemed somewhat dejected.

"Daoist Fan, you indeed toyed with me several times in the past by relying on the benefits of reincarnation."

"But my enlightenment of you as a Saint is an undeniable fact," Li Fan said nonchalantly.

"Alas..." Dao De was rendered speechless.

Shou Qiu chuckled and said, "If being toyed with like this could lead to proving the Dao as a Saint, I think countless people in Mountains and Seas would be willing."

Dao De had to admit that Shou Qiu's words were indeed the truth.

All the past events were dismissed with a laugh.

Next, it was time for concentricity and trinity!

"So, Daoist Fan's plan is truly to save the Three Saints?" Shou Qiu asked, surprised upon learning Li Fan's true intentions.

Li Fan nodded slightly, "I have observed the complete 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.' Although I have grasped the overall changes in Mountains and Seas, there are still many details lacking. Thus, I only have the Shadow of Mountains and Seas, not the Spirit of Mountains and Seas."

"Therefore, I plan to use the variables of the Three Saints to observe the changes in this segment of Mountains and Seas." Li Fan pointed ahead and said proudly.

"By gaining one, one can gain all. If we can gain some enlightenment, we can then deduce the entire segment of Mountains and Seas."

"Moreover..."

"We can hide in the shadows and observe all the methods of the Three Saints. Facing the crisis of life and death, they will surely reveal everything without reservation. Perhaps we can discover their trump cards."

...

Li Fan explained the reasons for his actions.

Shou Qiu, after pondering, offered a different opinion.

"Why not try to reverse the situation and eliminate the Three Saints?"

"If we can absorb the Great Daos of Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi into the Hall of Return to Truth, we might be able to settle everything in one go and save a lot of trouble."

Dao De sensed the situation and narrowed his eyes slightly, speaking for Li Fan, "Daoist Fan is afraid."

"Not only because of the unfathomable divine abilities of the Three Saints, but also because..."

"Tai Yi Saint aside, Lianshan and Guihai, these two are quite hard to fathom."

Li Fan continued slowly, "This is also something I vaguely sensed after observing the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes.' The so-called Lianshan and Guihai, there are no such Dao paths within Mountains and Seas. The two of them became Saints because of Lianshan and Guihai, rather than proving their Dao through Lianshan and Guihai."

"Why Lianshan? By what means Guihai?"

"The greatest trump cards of these two, we have never seen clearly."

Shou Qiu nodded in agreement, "Indeed."

Li Fan said, "The Three Saints are from the very beginning of the separation of Mountains and Seas, difficult to fathom by common sense. Perhaps they gained the creation of some primordial ancient artifact, who knows. If we rashly expose Return to Truth..."

"It seems Prying Opportunity's attempt to seize Return to Truth, although unsuccessful, has left you with quite a shadow," Dao De chuckled.

Shou Qiu defended Li Fan, "This is only natural for a person."

After a moment of contemplation, Shou Qiu added, "Steady progress has its merits. For now, our wings are not yet fully grown, and it is indeed not suitable to confront the Three Saints head-on. Especially since you said the Three Saints might have gained the creation of primordial ancient artifacts..."

"I believe it is true!"

With their minds aligned, Li Fan quickly reacted, "Shou Qiu's suspicion stems from the Shadow of God?"

Shou Qiu nodded, "In my previous life, when I saw the Shadow of God, I merely thought the Three Saints had reached the pinnacle of their cultivation and could actually glimpse the existence of 'God.' However, after reading the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes' through Return to Truth, I have a new idea."

"With the power of Return to Truth, I finally obtained this scroll that only recorded the shadow, not the spirit of God. How did the Three Saints obtain the spirit of Mountains and Seas? Was it truly just through their peerless talent?"

Upon hearing this, Li Fan and Dao De both fell silent.

"There are countless beings in the world, and some may indeed be extraordinary, but there is always a limit. And some things clearly transcend this limit. The Three Saints, from nothingness to creation, are indeed divinely talented. But I believe..."

"Beings of Mountains and Seas, after all, are born from Mountains and Seas. To see the True God, one can only rely on external means."

Shou Qiu gazed at the Shadow of God floating above Li Fan's head, feeling inspired and sighing.

Li Fan could faintly empathize with Shou Qiu's thoughts.

Although Shou Qiu often modestly claimed his cultivation was mediocre, he had, after all, cultivated from being a mere Warden of the Sea to a Saint. He definitely possessed his own pride.

But all of this was instantly smoothed away upon truly witnessing the power of Return to Truth.

Talent and effort were all irrelevant before Return to Truth.

Even after cultivating diligently for billions of years, the scenery that was still hard to glimpse was now clearly visible under the guidance of Return to Truth.

"This is not a matter of talent, but a limitation of our origin."

"The creations of Mountains and Seas are destined to be confined within these Mountains and Seas. To aspire to see the True God, one must rely on external objects."

Shou Qiu said slowly, "Daoist Fan, since you started as a mortal and had the treasure of Return to Truth by your side, perhaps you don't empathize deeply with this. Dao De should have a more profound experience."

After a long period of silence, Li Fan finally agreed with Shou Qiu's conjecture.

His estimation of the Three Saints' strength, unknowingly, rose another level.

"Taking advantage of this opportune moment, perhaps we can use the Void Realm Incarnations to thoroughly investigate the secrets of the Three Saints."

After resting, the three set off again towards their destination.

However, this time, Li Fan and Dao De would provide protection, while Shou Qiu immersed himself in seclusion.

Li Fan, having obtained the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes,' could comprehend the Shadow of God.

Shou Qiu, naturally, also gained something.

Moreover, over the years, he had personally witnessed the changes in Mountains and Seas.

The detailed entries in the manual were as if everything he had experienced.

Everything was vivid.

As if going through another cycle of Mountains and Seas' changes, Shou Qiu's aura became increasingly ethereal.

"In the previous life, after comprehending the manipulation of truth and falsehood, Shou Qiu could instantly kill four Saints."

"In this life, after obtaining the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes' through Return to Truth, who knows how much stronger he has become." Li Fan looked at the meditating Shou Qiu, as if he had gained a sense of confidence out of thin air.

Even if the six Saints were in a fierce battle ahead, there was no longer any need to be so timid.

Chapter 1721: Observing the Saints and Understanding the Law

In the Mountains and Seas ahead, the six Saints' fierce battle seemed to have just begun.

Ripples emanated from the Void Realm, but the Three Saints' true forms had not yet shown signs of defeat. Thus, the Mountains and Seas were still unharmed, and the Saints within the Xuanji Ring remained seated.

However, Shou Qiu, having traversed the void and merged with his temporal self,

his expression shifted several times before he abruptly rose.

Under the watchful eyes of all, he moved towards the scene of the six Saints' battle.

The other Saints were surprised and hesitant, but no one chose to follow.

"We should still abide by the Three Saints' words and quietly observe the changes."

"Indeed. The Three Saints haven't specified the dangers within the Void Realm. But since it's a trouble even they find difficult, we certainly aren't qualified to intervene. Going there would not only be unhelpful but would also become a burden."

"The Three Saints said to wait patiently, and perhaps a variable would arise. But from where exactly would that variable come?"

"Shou Qiu has always been steady; why this sudden change in his behavior?"

Prying Opportunity, Oracle Prediction, and others' thoughts churned, but they couldn't fathom a reason.

Meanwhile, Shou Qiu and Dao De, having completed their self-merging, had quietly arrived at the scene of the six Saints' battle in the Void Realm with Li Fan.

With the experience of the previous life, this time they concealed themselves even more patiently.

They merely hid in the shadows, observing every change in the battlefield.

Even as the Three Saints' true forms gradually fell into peril, they did not reveal themselves easily.

It was not until the Void Realm Incarnations, determined to achieve complete victory, first unleashed the Innate Malevolent Artifacts.

The Fate Rope bound Lianshan, the Turtle Shell suppressed Guihai, and the Ancestral Bone captured Tai Yi!

The Three Saints initially refused to deploy their own Innate Malevolent Artifacts against their foes, seemingly still wary of something deep within their hearts.

It was only when they could no longer sustain themselves that they were finally forced to use them.

The Innate Malevolent Artifacts countered each other, instantly averting the crisis.

The situation once again fell into a stalemate.

Li Fan and his two companions observed every subtle change.

"Shou Qiu, do you know what the Three Saints are so wary of?"

Dao De and Shou Qiu also sensed the Three Saints' hesitation.

"Even if they die, it's merely a disappearance from one timeline. On the overall level of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints still exist. Furthermore, the Three Saints possess the Divine Ability of 'Boundless Indestructibility,' so the losses incurred by their demise might be even less than we imagine. Compared to being killed by the Void Realm Incarnations, the Three Saints are more concerned about Mountains and Seas being completely severed."

"From the Three Saints' current actions, it seems the Innate Malevolent Artifacts, though suppressed and subdued by them, still pose a threat of backlash. And once they back-lash..."

"I'm afraid the impact would not be limited to just the Three Saints in a specific timeline," Shou Qiu slowly stated after observing for a while, his gaze profound.

Dao De also appeared thoughtful: "Dao Annihilation divides Mountains and Seas into countless segments, each severed and unable to connect. However, the Innate Malevolent Artifacts, after all, originated from the fallen True God, and perhaps can penetrate the Void Realm's obstruction. There might still be subtle connections between them."

"If an Innate Malevolent Artifact could successfully backlash the Three Saints within one segment of Mountains and Seas, it could then seize the opportunity to expand its influence throughout the entire Mountains and Seas, thereby escaping its fate of being suppressed."

"Thus, it seems the Three Saints' subduing of the Innate Malevolent Artifacts was not as easy as they claimed. The fraction of their divine will that each of them sent out and imposed upon us..."

Recalling the unprecedented caution the Three Saints displayed when sending out their divine fractions, Li Fan nodded slightly.

The battle continued in the Void Realm.

The Void Realm Incarnations, relying on the seemingly inexhaustible power support of the Void Realm, acted recklessly and without regard for consumption.

Though the Three Saints were at a disadvantage, their foundation was deep.

They were in danger but not yet vanquished.

Li Fan and his two companions, however, knew the inevitable demise of the Three Saints and never revealed themselves.

They patiently waited, comprehending the six Saints' battle.

All three possessed top-tier comprehension in Mountains and Seas. Their life experiences and chosen paths differed,

resulting in varied angles of comprehension. Under the blessing of shared understanding, their insights intertwined and became fully integrated.

Their progress was more than a thousand miles a day.

Their efficiency was almost on par with Li Fan's direct Dao comprehension within the Hall of Return to Truth.

As the saying goes, 'know thyself and thy enemy.' Although he wielded the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, Li Fan did not believe that comprehending the Three Saints' Dao was useless.

"The civilizations of Mountains and Seas, the beings of Mountains and Seas, the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas."

"We see the Three Saints, almost as if we see Mountains and Seas themselves."

His internal insights, combined with the 'Mountains and Seas Changes Manual' obtained from Return to Truth, gradually made the formerly hollow data projections become robust.

Li Fan had a premonition that if he were to achieve Sainthood of Mountains and Seas again in the next life, his might would surpass that of the past.

The three ravenously absorbed nourishment from the six Saints' fierce battle.

And the final act of this battle finally unfolded silently.

Around the Three Saints, the countless delicate threads representing Mountains and Seas, as if ravaged by wind and frost, had become rusty and brittle. Their movements became slower and slower, and a sense of deathly stillness slowly ascended.

Sensing the imminent demise of the Three Saints, dark undercurrents stirred within the Void Realm.

The Void Realm specters, with fierce expressions, manifested new Innate Malevolent Artifacts from the Void Realm.

And descended upon the true bodies!

"Move!"

Before Shou Qiu's words had even faded, he stepped forward, instantly appearing in the arena.

Wielding the divinity of Guihai, he moved to resolve Tai Yi's crisis.

Just as the second Ancestral Bone was about to adhere to Tai Yi's body, Shou Qiu gently blocked it.

Li Fan and Dao De also acted simultaneously.

Dao De, carrying the divinity of Tai Yi, helped Lianshan resist the encroachment of the Fate Rope.

Li Fan, embodying the divinity of Lianshan, aided Guihai in escaping the fate of being suppressed by the Turtle Shell.

The Three Saints, who were on the verge of demise, finally showed a trace of bewilderment on their usually calm faces as they beheld the suddenly appearing Li Fan and his two companions.

But soon, sensing the wisp of their own divine thought carried by the newcomers, they instantly understood.

"Restrain them with spirit, descend upon them with thought."

The Three Saints' telepathic message spoke of the same key to subduing the Innate Malevolent Artifacts.

Although they were fighting separately, under the influence of their shared understanding, the three were like one, simultaneously witnessing the onslaught of the Innate Malevolent Artifacts.

Heaven and earth roared, and in the first evolution after the division of the Mountains and Seas' divine power, relics were born.

These were both the essence of Mountains and Seas itself and represented all things discarded by the new Mountains and Seas,

the old past. Their power was immeasurable, and they were imbued with the boundless resentment of Mountains and Seas.

"Why were we abandoned? Why were we changed?"

"Abandoned means useless, change means death!"

"Die, die, die, die, die, die!"

From a tiny turtle shell, malevolent energy soared to the heavens, carrying the immense weight of Mountains and Seas, and smashed down fiercely on Li Fan's head.

"You gave birth to me, nourished me, why kill me?"

"If I am unforgivable, then what are you?"

"Come with me to the end!"

It was as if flesh and blood grew from the Ancestral Bone, and a figure long dead seemed to come alive at that instant, staring at Shou Qiu with venomous resentment.

"Born to a fixed fate, why live?"

"If one's life is destined to end, what is the meaning of all the toil?"

"It is naught but an empty dream!"

Amidst the weaving of the Fate Rope, Dao De vaguely saw another version of himself.

...

"Restrain them with spirit, descend upon them with thought."

The Three Saints' reminder echoed in their minds once more.

At the same time, the Three Saints' divine projections emerged, floating out.

As if to demonstrate, they met the Innate Malevolent Artifacts head-on.

"The old die, the weak die, those who deserve to die, die!" Facing the Turtle Shell descending with boundless resentment, the Spirit of Lianshan replied coldly.

With a gentle raise of his hand, he pointed, instantly halting the Turtle Shell's momentum.

Chapter 1722: The Void Realm Raises Troops Again

The one residing in Li Fan's body was merely a wisp of divine thought split off by Lianshan. Naturally, it couldn't directly resolve the turtle shell's oppressive power.

The reason it appeared to "halt" was because this divine thought almost completely restrained the turtle shell's malevolent aura.

This caused its surging descent to suddenly stagnate.

Due to the vast disparity in power between the two sides, a single wisp of Lianshan's divine thought was destined not to last long.

However, Li Fan quickly took over.

Embodying the spirit of Lianshan, it was as if he were there himself.

Li Fan deeply agreed: "Well said, what deserves to die, indeed must die. Gone are the old things; no matter how unwilling the heart, it is useless. Just honestly accept your fate!"

In an instant, Li Fan's figure seemed to merge with the spirit of Lianshan, and his boundless will collided with the remnant of Mountains and Seas!

In a trance, amidst the myriad patterns on the turtle shell before him, Li Fan seemed to glimpse the Mountains and Seas of the past.

It was vastly different from the current appearance of Mountains and Seas.

Nor was it the Primordial Immortal Realm of the so-called nascent Mountains and Seas.

It was an even more ancient past.

The Mountains and Seas at the time of the Divine Split!

As one of the beings evolved from Mountains and Seas, it was hard for those dwelling within to imagine what Mountains and Seas looked like without the power of the Divine. But now, Li Fan could glimpse a part of it.

It lacked the quality of "infinity."

The mountains ascended to their utmost, yet eventually reached their peak, after which came decline from their zenith.

The sea appeared boundless, yet inevitably suffered the calamity of drying up.

The drying of seas and crumbling of rocks was the inevitable tribulation of Mountains and Seas.

Even though the life forms of Mountains and Seas had become unimaginably powerful, they still could not escape this limitation.

Thus, Mountains and Seas desired to swallow the Divine!

As for how the "Divine," the source of all things and the origin of existence, had fallen, there was naturally no record of it in the turtle shell.

Only the Mountains and Seas after the Divine Split utterly abandoned their past selves without hesitation.

"Having gained divine power, the crude past is naturally discarded like old shoes."

"Yet it still dreams of a comeback."

"Truly asking for trouble!"

With such thoughts, as if rooted to the ground, Li Fan remained unmoved, despite the turtle shell carrying monstrous malevolence.

Of course, this was only a feeling on the spiritual level. The actual pressure from the Mountains and Seas remnant was still very real.

However, Li Fan had his own way of resolving it.

Suddenly, circles of faint lines of light appeared around Li Fan's body.

This was not the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, but a clever resolution directly using the cyclical power of the Cosmic Cycle.

The weight that the beings of Mountains and Seas could hardly bear, what if it were distributed among the countless beings in endless cycles?

The beings would only feel a slight burden, nothing more.

Initially, the cyclical threads bent slightly under the sudden immense force. But as the cycle infinitely expanded, it bore all the pressure brought by the Mountains and Seas remnant.

The divine could not harm Li Fan, nor could raw force.

The attack from the Void Realm's turtle shell was thus destined to be useless.

Seemingly effortless, Li Fan had actually pushed his understanding of the Cosmic Cycle to its limit. This was also under the guidance of Lianshan's spirit, allowing his mind to successfully ignore the influence of the innate malevolence.

Otherwise, without using the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, given Li Fan's current strength, he might not have been able to fully withstand a strike from the turtle shell.

It could be said that innate malevolence, even when simulated by the Void Realm, was indeed extremely formidable.

Since he was unharmed, Li Fan was able to divert his attention to the battle conditions of Shou Qiu and Dao De.

Shou Qiu's performance was undoubtedly much better than Li Fan's.

"Since I can give you life, I can also take it."

Facing the ancestral bone, which was filled with monstrous malevolence and resentment, Shou Qiu merely uttered these faint words and easily fended off its erosion. No matter how frantically the ancestral bone tried to take root and penetrate, Shou Qiu stood firm like a majestic mountain.

The only one facing a slight risk among the three was Dao De.

"If one's fate is already decided, what is the point of all the struggle?"

If it were just Dao De himself, facing the Soul Binding Rope's direct questioning of his very soul, he would undoubtedly fall into wavering and turmoil.

But since Dao De was already within the Mysterious Ring, things were naturally different.

Even without the guidance of the Tai Yi incarnation, Dao De's divine perception would not be significantly affected.

After all, Li Fan had said that after this life, a share of inherited memories would surely be his.

To be able to truly experience and benefit from the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. How many people in all of Mountains and Seas could say the same?

What great fortune!

Even if he were to die at this moment, he would have no regrets.

Dao De's disadvantage was that his strength was, after all, a bit weaker.

Li Fan's sudden enlightenment of him in this life lacked the long accumulation and gradual blossoming that Shou Qiu possessed.

Relying on his perfected Virtue, he could continuously resolve the influence of the Soul Binding Rope.

But it was not as effortless as Li Fan and Shou Qiu.

He was constantly on the brink of life and death.

Fortunately, with Li Fan occasionally providing True Spirit nourishment, he could withstand the consumption.

The three Saints of Truth and Falsehood continued their fierce struggle.

The Void Realm's subsequent innate malevolence was nullified by the sudden appearance of Li Fan and his two companions.

The battlefield once again fell into a stalemate.

The Void Realm's mastermind's reaction was not as intense as in the previous life when it encountered the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood.

Instead, it fell into an eerie silence.

It seemed to be contemplating whether it was worth it to deploy more forces here.

After all, the Void Realm was fighting against Mountains and Seas across the entire timeline. If it deployed more here, it would inevitably have to curtail some of its Dao Annihilation erosion efforts at other temporal nodes.

This loss on one side meant a gain on the other, sparking a chain reaction. Every move by the Void Realm's mastermind was extremely cautious.

It didn't deliberate for too long.

After a brief silence in the Void Realm, rolling waves suddenly surged.

"Be careful!"

As if having glimpsed a clue, even the three original Saints couldn't help but send telepathic warnings.

Li Fan looked towards the turbulent part of the Void Realm and saw over a dozen anomalies approaching.

His expression couldn't help but change slightly: "The Void Realm's mastermind has a grand scheme and decisive planning."

"Even if we haven't revealed the true traces of the Great Dao, which it must obtain, it is willing to deploy four times the power again!"

With only three innate malevolent artifacts, everyone was already barely coping.

With twelve more innate malevolent artifacts approaching, under normal circumstances, it would be impossible to resist.

"Should we...?" Dao De's heart stirred, and he asked.

Shou Qiu's expression was grave as he looked at Li Fan.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then grit his teeth and said, "No. If we use the transformation of truth and falsehood, the outcome will inevitably be the same as in the previous life. What is the meaning of our current attempt then?"

"We'll resist it head-on! Let's test our limits!"

"Rest assured, even if we perish, we'll just start over! In the past, I cultivated a hundred lifetimes, turning the impossible into possible."

"What we face today..."

"Is no harder than before!"

Li Fan's thoughts deeply influenced Shou Qiu and Dao De.

Shou Qiu's solemn face instantly relaxed.

With a slight smile, he faced the surging twelve innate malevolent artifacts, returning to his usual detached demeanor.

Dao De also let out a cold snort, adjusting himself to his peak state.

"If we're not afraid of death, why fear these innate malevolent artifacts?"

"They are nothing but pawns."

Chapter 1723: Resolving the Danger

The multiple instances of Innate Malevolence, in addition to bringing more powerful spiritual erosion, also presented an overwhelming, tangible pressure that rapidly escalated.

Each piece of Innate Malevolence, under a sneak attack, was capable of inflicting fatal damage upon the Three Saints.

Now, with fifteen such objects attacking simultaneously, although not comparable to the thousands of Saint phantoms in the previous life, the combined might instantly put Li Fan and his two companions' defenses in dire straits.

The Turtle Shell, Ancestral Bone, and Fate Rope—each additional one doubled the pressure.

That they did not collapse instantly already spoke volumes of their profound foundations.

Facing such a desperate situation, they harbored no thoughts of surrender.

Instead, they strained their minds, seeking a glimmer of survival amidst the impossible.

"One heart, one mind, a trinity."

Li Fan and his two companions were slowly compressed into a single point by the onslaught of the fifteen Innate Malevolence, forming a defensive triangle, their backs to each other.

One's vision became the eyes of all three. What one saw, all three observed.

One's heart, the will of all three.

The influence from different Innate Malevolence simultaneously assailed them.

However, Li Fan, at this moment, fully possessed his own creative power, combined with Shou Qiu's foresight and open-mindedness, as well as Dao De's completeness.

The boundless malevolence, like tumultuous waves, crashed upon them.

Yet, he skillfully defused it one by one, leveraging the shared will of the three.

Shou Qiu and Dao De experienced the same.

The Innate Malevolence gained a fivefold amplification, but Li Fan's defense also instantly tripled.

And as the external pressure continuously mounted, Li Fan also felt the "one heart, one mind" growing more harmonious and seamless.

He could, with the Cosmic Cycle Great Dao, weave endless reincarnations. He could also grasp Longevity, observing mountains from the sea. And he could be complete in virtue, with an inexhaustible source.

Not only did the three share "one heart, one mind" subjectively, but even the Great Daos they controlled began to acknowledge each other.

Li Fan instantly had an epiphany. In a lull between the onslaughts of the Innate Malevolence, he drew a massive amount of accumulated True Spirit from the Void Realm.

"Behold, Shou Qiu of Fan!"

His expression solemn, he pointed outside his body.

True Spirit surged, a radiant flow of light. A phantom figure slowly walked forth from it.

Its divine aura and demeanor bore a striking resemblance to Shou Qiu. Yet, its appearance was eighty percent similar to Li Fan.

It could be called Li Fan, the Shou Qiu version.

This was Li Fan, using his mastery of the Longevity Great Dao and mobilizing infinite True Spirit, to achieve Sainthood once more in an instant!

Under normal circumstances, there would never be two Saints with the same Dao path in Mountains and Seas.

But under the profound effect of "one heart, one mind," the inexplicable influence of the Return to Truth inheritance, and the immense pressure from external forces,

even the Mountains and Seas Great Dao gradually regarded Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De as one entity.

Since they were one, there was no longer any conflict to speak of.

As soon as the Shou Qiu Incarnation of Fan appeared, it joined the trio's defense.

Still one heart and one mind, without any gaps.

Its form was majestic like mountains and seas, shielding them from the external winds and rains.

"Behold, Dao De of Fan!"

Li Fan wasted no time, continuing to create his Dao De doppelganger.

Amidst the circulating two energies, the Dao De of Li Fan strode forth.

His face bore a half-smile, half-frown, both righteous and wicked.

Around his body, black and white swirled, sharing the burden of the storms endured by the group.

It wasn't just Li Fan.

At the same instant, Shou Qiu and Dao De also each manifested two doppelgangers.

Corresponding to the other two.

In a moment, six top-tier Saints were added as reinforcements.

The pressure they faced instantly lightened.

With the three main bodies at the core, the six doppelgangers enveloped them.

Wherever the defense was weakest, their combined strength converged instantly.

Where their thoughts reached, their power followed.

The result was as if Li Fan and his two companions could simultaneously wield nine times their power.

And the defensive line they formed still operated freely, without any awkwardness or flaws.

On the other hand, the Void Realm's offensive, though seemingly vast and terrifying, consisting of fifteen Innate Malevolence,

was actually fragmented, each fighting for itself, and merely fivefold duplicates.

Once they had adapted to the attack of one, the threat from the other four duplicates seemed to become less lethal.

Li Fan and his two companions, along with the six doppelgangers, began to cooperate even more seamlessly.

They could even contemplate the Dao and gain insights while simultaneously deflecting the Innate Malevolence's attacks.

"In fact, if truly pushed to the brink, and without resorting to the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, we still have one last desperate measure."

"Just as Dao De did before achieving Sainthood, we could perform the act of splitting the Dao!"

"Each body could do so. This would instantly double our combat power!"

"However, it is easy to split but not so easy to achieve completeness again. The consequence is likely for us to fall from the Saint realm, or even have our 'one heart, one mind' shatter, leading to internal strife," Li Fan's mind churned, rapidly calculating.

Dao De agreed wholeheartedly: "But with Return to Truth, there's no need to consider so much. Let's overcome this calamity first, and observe the changes in Mountains and Seas!"

Shou Qiu gazed into the depths of the Void Realm, deep in thought: "The withdrawal of twelve Innate Malevolence has had no small impact on the Mountains and Seas battlefield. I have a premonition that the summary of Mountains and Seas changes after this Return to Truth might bring a pleasant surprise."

...

Every insight gained by the trio in battle was shared and circulated telepathically.

Compared to the Innate Malevolence, which was destined to remain unchanged from the moment it manifested in this world, Li Fan and his companions grew demonstrably stronger with each passing moment.

And their rate of improvement was astonishingly fast.

The outcome of this battle was already decided at this moment.

Provided that the mastermind behind the Void Realm did not introduce further variables.

Of course, even with "one heart, one mind," the power of the trio had a limit.

Even with Li Fan's envisioned Dao De split, they would at most add eighteen Mountains and Seas Saints.

If the Void Realm mastermind, like in the previous life, without regard for cost, summoned thousands of Saint phantoms from other temporal nodes, then Li Fan and his companions' defense would be instantly shattered.

But in this life, Li Fan and his companions had not displayed any signs related to the transformation of truth and falsehood.

In the eyes of the Void Realm mastermind, they were merely Saints who were a bit stronger and had more novel methods.

As a rational commander, it would never make such a foolish move.

Thus, after a final assessment of the current situation, it decisively chose to withdraw its forces.

Faster than they came, the Innate Malevolence and the Three Saints' Void Realm Incarnations instantly vanished without a trace.

However, a temporary retreat did not mean the Void Realm had given up its claim on the current Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan keenly noticed that as the Three Saints' Void Realm Incarnations departed, the obstructing Dao Annihilation ahead became even more profound.

Although it could not harm forces at the level of the Three Saints, it was an increasingly destructive blow to ordinary Saints and Mountains and Seas.

Since it couldn't be taken down for now, the plan was to tie it up.

Once its forces at other temporal nodes were dealt with, it would then deploy a large army and crush them with absolute strength.

On some level, the Void Realm mastermind's choice was not necessarily wrong.

It was only a pity that when the lone star appeared, even the entire Void Realm was swallowed, and then reset with the activation of Return to Truth.

Thus, it was unaware that it had relinquished the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood!

Without external threats, the atmosphere in the arena did not lighten.

The Three Saints and Li Fan's trio exchanged glances, each with their own thoughts.

There was no need for Li Fan and his companions to explain their origins.

After resolving the crisis of the Three Saints' demise, the Three Saints' divine senses they held automatically departed their bodies.

Returning to the main bodies of the Three Saints.

Thus, the Three Saints learned all the causes and consequences.

Yet, even now, they found it somewhat inconceivable that Li Fan and his two companions had successfully repelled the onslaught of fifteen times the Innate Malevolence.

"Three fellow Daoists, what great divine abilities!" Saint Gui Hai's gaze swept over them, praising.

"It was merely luck. After a prolonged battle, we were already at the end of our reserves. Had the Void Realm not timely retreated, we would have almost perished on the spot!" Li Fan said without batting an eyelid.

Shou Qiu also smiled: "We also have to thank the Three Saints for the gift of 'one heart, one mind.' Otherwise, we would never have been able to resist."

Dao De also nodded in agreement: "Had it not been for this 'one heart, one mind,' we wouldn't have known how compatible we truly are."

They knew their own strength.

As the creators of the Xuanji Ring, the Three Saints naturally understood that "one heart, one mind" could indeed multiply combat power. However, it was difficult to achieve the tenfold increase that Li Fan and his companions had displayed.

However, from their performance in the previous battle, the combat power of Li Fan's trio was already not inferior to theirs.

So it was not appropriate to press the matter.

"The Void Realm's turbulence has not yet subsided. For now, let us first reconnect Mountains and Seas."

The six exchanged glances, signifying a temporary consensus.

They turned back to face the two segments of Mountains and Seas separated by the Void Realm.

No longer the same as before.

With the Three Saints present in both segments of Mountains and Seas, and Li Fan's support,

even a hundred thousand years swallowed by Dao Annihilation could be easily restored.

Under the concerted efforts of all Saints, tendrils of Mountains and Seas returned to the Void Realm.

First, a ray of light pierced the darkness.

Then, myriad lights shone forth, illuminating everything.

Mountains and Seas revived.

At the moment of reconnection, all the Saints seated on the Other Shore experienced a surge of vitality.

Clearly, they had received immense benefits.

After all, they had gained an additional hundred thousand years of accumulation, coupled with the merit of reconnecting Mountains and Seas.

Their strength, if not doubled, had certainly advanced significantly.

Perhaps the only exception was Li Fan.

This segment of Mountains and Seas did not contain his existence, so there was no corresponding merging.

However, the commotion emanating from him was in no way inferior to the others.

Besides the disguise created by his surging accumulated True Spirit, there was also the feedback from Shou Qiu and Dao De's gains.

Now, although still seated within the Xuanji Ring, directly facing the Three Saints,

Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De had become a unified entity.

They could subtly contend with the Three Saints, and their actions no longer needed to be as timid as before.

However, it seemed that the greatest beneficiaries of this reconnection were the Three Saints, Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi.

Originally, Li Fan had full confidence when facing them.

But with another reconnection of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints once again became unfathomable.

"After all, they are ancient beings who have existed since the beginning of Mountains and Seas' evolution."

"Shou Qiu's foundation is already unimaginable, let alone the Three Saints?"

"The sum total of Mountains and Seas' civilizations, beings, and Great Daos will certainly grow stronger with the reconnection of Mountains and Seas."

"Or rather, they would recover their original strength."

Li Fan had long anticipated this.

Even so, Li Fan believed that the Three Saints would not be able to distinguish between his trio and Shou Qiu and Dao De in the short term.

With the shared goal of saving Mountains and Seas, the balance would not be easily broken.

"The reconnection of Mountains and Seas has successfully restored a hundred thousand years of time. This is truly a great fortune!"

"However, although the reconnection was successful, why do I always feel that this newly born Mountains and Seas... is a bit strange?" Bai Xiao suddenly asked, looking at the newly born hundred thousand year Mountains and Seas.

Saint Lianshan spoke: "It is not your illusion. Mountains and Seas have, after all, been separated by the Void Realm for too long. Although they can be recreated from nothingness with past脈絡 as a guide, there will inevitably be some differences between the current Mountains and Seas and the former Mountains and Seas."

"Some possibilities might no longer exist. Others might become completely unrecognizable."

"Correspondingly, the entire downstream Mountains and Seas will be slightly affected."

"However, this is beneficial, not detrimental, to the overall trend of Mountains and Seas."

Shou Qiu suddenly spoke to Li Fan in his mind: "The trace of Heavenly Net Emperor's existence has vanished."

Li Fan was astonished and looked towards the original possibilities within Mountains and Seas.

In the Primordial Immortal Realm, it should have been Heavenly Net Immortal Emperor in charge.

The newly born Mountains and Seas should have followed past inertia, recreating all past events.

But for some unknown reason, in the newly born original possibilities, the Heavenly Net Emperor was absent.

Instead, another Immortal Emperor named [Ling Xi] was in his place.

The waters of the upstream had audaciously changed course.

Causing the original possibilities to subtly shift.

Li Fan clearly saw that it was as if a blade had sliced through it, giving rise to two distinctly different possibilities.

The one that was flourishing was naturally the continuation of the newly emerged original possibility, having inherited [Ling Xi] Immortal Emperor.

While the original one Li Fan was familiar with...

Had truly become a rootless source, a water without origin. Without the infusion of power from the upstream of Mountains and Seas, it was destined to gradually wither away.

"What is the meaning of this?" Li Fan furrowed his brow slightly.

He naturally wasn't worried about his trio, who originated from the Primordial, being affected by these anomalies.

Transcendent beings were already free from the constraints of their originating possibilities, let alone those of their current strength.

"Mountains and Seas revived, but Heavenly Net is not among them."

"Could it be..."

Shou Qiu was momentarily unsure.

"What the Three Saints said earlier, that they haven't seen Heavenly Net Immortal Emperor transcend the entire Immortal Realm, might not be entirely true."

"We still need to uncover the truth for ourselves." Dao De secretly muttered.

"In the revived Mountains and Seas, there are no traces of Heavenly Net. What truly happened back then might be lost to time. We can only infer it by finding the so-called 'opportunity' that Heavenly Net Immortal Emperor once found in the lower realm from even more ancient times in Mountains and Seas." Shou Qiu's gaze turned towards the Mountains and Seas ahead.

"If my estimation is correct, it should be within the Mountains and Seas ahead."

Li Fan, hearing this, felt somewhat disoriented: "I always thought the matter of Heavenly Net Emperor was in the distant past. Yet, we have only taken two or three steps within Mountains and Seas. In the grand scheme of Mountains and Seas, it's merely an insignificant period of time."

Dao De also seemed lost in thought: "The anomaly of Heavenly Net only occurred at the end of his reign. It's likely that he changed after finding the so-called 'creation.' Indeed, we can glimpse its secret."

"However..."

"If it truly was a significant opportunity to transcend Mountains and Seas, it might be lost forever." Dao De suddenly said.

Chapter 1724: The Hidden Veins of Mountains and Seas

Li Fan nodded slightly at Shou Qiu. Even Saints who had experienced the rebirth of Mountains and Seas would not know about such profound future prospects, let alone the great opportunities that might allow the entire Immortal Realm to transcend.

"Such secrets, yet to be known. Truly a great regret," Dao De sighed.

"In Mountains and Seas, there are infinite matters. Even the Three Saints, who in a sense represent Mountains and Seas themselves, cannot know everything. We, with the transformation of truth and falsehood upon us, have already received immense fortune," Shou Qiu smiled, not bothering himself with it.

Li Fan, however, suddenly uttered something astonishing: "I have an idea. As recorded in 'Return to Truth,' the Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes might contain clues related to the True Emperor."

"It may not directly record that unknown creation opportunity, but by comparing the changes in Mountains and Seas before and after the vanishing of the Primordial Immortal Realm, we might glean something."

"I already possess the Outline of Changes for the later period. I only need to derive an Outline for the period before the Primordial Immortal Realm's disappearance. By comparing the two, we might be able to discern something."

The three shared a unified heart and mind, so they naturally knew how detailed the Outline obtained by 'Return to Truth' was. Li Fan could even use it as a template to achieve Sainthood in Mountains and Seas.

"Since 'Return to Truth' can reshape Mountains and Seas time and again, all changes within Mountains and Seas naturally escape its notice," Shou Qiu pondered for a moment and then nodded in agreement.

"If that's the case, it's simple. We merely need to reconnect again, pushing the time node back before the True Emperor's disappearance, and then use 'Return to Truth.' This way, we can both observe the impact of the Three Saints' demise on the changes in Mountains and Seas and investigate the True Emperor's secrets."

The three communicated silently.

Within the Xuanji Ring, the Saints were already discussing the next event of reconnecting Mountains and Seas. Until the threat of Mountains and Seas being annihilated was completely resolved, the Saints had no concept of rest. Fortunately, with their repeated victories, and even cooperating to escape mortal danger from Void Realm Incarnations, the morale among the Saints was high.

"The Void Realm ahead spans only thirty thousand years of time. Compared to our hundred thousand years of reconnection, it is but a trifle. However..."

"It is not something that can be easily overcome." Saint Lianshan's words immediately silenced the excited emotions stirring in the hearts of the Saints.

"Do you all know why the Void Realm manifested our incarnations to attack us in the Void Realm?"

Facing Saint Lianshan's question, all the Saints seemed to have thought of something simultaneously, their expressions subtly shifting.

"Before this reconnection of Mountains and Seas, we, who were ambushed, were not particularly special. In terms of strength, we were no stronger than beings existing at other points in time; nor did we do anything to specifically draw the attention of the Void Realm..."

"We were merely obstructed by the Void Realm on our way to the Mountains and Seas ahead."

Through these two tentative encounters with the mastermind behind the Void Realm, Li Fan had gained some understanding of its operating methods. It was an extremely calm and rational decision-maker, doing nothing without purpose. Yet, at crucial moments, it would spare no expense, gambling everything in a desperate struggle. Hearing the Three Saints speak now, Li Fan immediately understood.

The struggle between Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm was a vast battlefield. If it were an insignificant corner, the mastermind behind the Void Realm would not have diverted power without reason to intercept the Three Saints.

"That is to say..."

"The Mountains and Seas ahead are like a strategic mountain pass, a military stronghold, a crucial point that must be fought for. To prevent any possible unexpected situations, they dispatched forces to eliminate them before the Three Saints could make contact."

Li Fan and the other two exchanged glances. Shou Qiu directly asked, "May I dare to ask Saint Lianshan, what special significance do the Mountains and Seas ahead hold?"

Saint Lianshan pondered for a moment, then did not answer directly but began to explain to everyone. "Mountains and Seas are a continuous existence along the entire timeline, from antiquity to the present, and into the future. Within Mountains and Seas themselves, infinite possibilities are derived. Mountains and Seas themselves are also in constant flux."

"But the overall trend of Mountains and Seas remains unchanged. After the division of spirit in Mountains and Seas, they were interconnected, inseparable. Then, they ultimately moved towards the end of time, ushering in their final doom. This is the destiny of Mountains and Seas."

"The actions of the beings of Mountains and Seas, even ourselves as Saints, might influence numerous possibilities within Mountains and Seas. However..."

"It is difficult to affect the overall trend of Mountains and Seas!" Saint Lianshan waved his hand gently, and an image of the continuous Mountains and Seas appeared before everyone. Compared to the Mountains and Seas that the current Saints saw, the scene before them was more complete. From the inaccessible beginning of Mountains and Seas to the dark and traceless end, the continuity and length of Mountains and Seas were manifested in this manner.

"It seems that after three reconnecting events, the strength of the Three Saints has indeed greatly improved."

"Saint Lianshan's casual gesture already embodies a modicum of the essence of the 'Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes.'" Li Fan observed the scene before him, inwardly astonished. He could see the complete picture of Mountains and Seas because 'Return to Truth' bestowed upon him the Outline. But the Three Saints had gained it through their own comprehension.

Ignoring the inner thoughts of the Saints in the arena, Saint Lianshan continued his discourse. "The flow of Mountains and Seas remains unchanged in form. Even if cut apart piece by piece by the Void Realm, it still maintains its overall posture."

"Even with the immense power of the Void Realm, it is still so. What about us?"

"Mountains and Seas are difficult to change, precisely because of this." Saint Lianshan paused here. Then, he suddenly shifted his tone. "Although difficult to change, it is not impossible. We often say that certain matters in Mountains and Seas are irrelevant to the final outcome and need not be concerned about. This is not because we are careless, but because even if they exert their maximum influence, they cannot shake the overall trend of Mountains and Seas. Truly, they are 'irrelevant to the final outcome.'"

"Even if an entire segment of Mountains and Seas is annihilated, as long as the overall veins of Mountains and Seas remain, there is a possibility of rebirth."

"However, there are existences that can truly alter the form of Mountains and Seas. Throughout the long lifespan of Mountains and Seas, there have only been a few such critical junctures."

"We are currently facing one of them." Saint Lianshan's words caused all the Saints in the Xuanji Ring to become solemn. Shou Qiu recalled his past observations but did not notice anything peculiar. The other Saints in the Xuanji Ring were similarly bewildered. Lianshan seemed to perceive the inner thoughts of the Saints. "Beings possess the instinct to conceal themselves, and Mountains and Seas are no different. These few critical junctures are like the vital points of a person. Mountains and Seas will naturally conceal them."

"Even ordinary Saints, if placed within them, would find it difficult to perceive."

"Only those who can survey the entirety of Mountains and Seas, observing from a global perspective, can vaguely discern its veins. Matters concerning the lifeblood of Mountains and Seas should not be easily revealed. However, given that Mountains and Seas have already fallen into peril, this situation is now inconsequential." Saying this, Saint Lianshan made a gesture, and Saint Guihai instantly magnified a segment of the panoramic view of Mountains and Seas for all the Saints.

"As the saying goes, 'traces of snakes and ants, a thousand miles hidden.' The affairs and people who seem insignificant might have unimaginable impacts on the overall trend of Mountains and Seas. Initially unnoticeable, they may erupt after a long time." The image continued to enlarge, focusing on a specific possibility, a particular cultivator. This cultivator had already reached the realm of Transcension. He could leap out of his own possibility at any moment, yet for some unknown reason, he repeatedly looked up at the sky, sighed, and ultimately gave up. He did not truly transcend and leave.
