The realm of Transcension was insignificant in the eyes of the Saints. Seeing this scene, they all felt somewhat perplexed.

Li Fan, however, felt a stir in his heart. "Shou Qiu, do you find this cultivator somewhat familiar?" "Although there are only a few similarities, it should be confirmed that he is related to that person."

"The final Saint of Mountains and Seas, Qiu Xin Hui?" Dao De also discerned some clues. The Three Saints did not continue to play coy. "This cultivator is named Qiu Tian Hui. He lingered at the threshold of Transcension, not due to insufficient talent, but because..."

"Let us listen to his inner thoughts." Saint Tai Yi flicked his finger, and as a speck of light shot into the image of Mountains and Seas, merging with Qiu Tian Hui's figure. His inner thoughts then echoed in the Xuanji Ring, reaching the ears of all the Saints. "Troublesome, annoying." "To leap beyond possibility, yet still be trapped and separated within Mountains and Seas. What kind of transcendence is this?" "This step, it would have been better not to take!" "I wonder, is there a more perfect method in the world?" ... Qiu Tian Hui's inner thoughts resounded, and all the Saints raised their eyebrows, finding it somewhat unbelievable. "Before even taking the step of Transcension, he could see the truth of Mountains and Seas? From within a well, yet observe the entire heavens?" "When I transcended, I was far from this troubled. Is Truth truly Falsehood?" The Saints were shaken, and the scene of Qiu Tian Hui continued to unfold. He pondered for several years, finding no solution. So, he left his homeland and wandered in various places. Of course, he did not leave that possibility, merely changing star systems. Time flowed, and countless years passed. Qiu Tian Hui remained unkempt, appearing increasingly疯疯癫癫. This day, he suddenly sensed something, and his expression of absentmindedness instantly returned to normal. He flashed to the side of an ordinary small pond. "This place... seems somewhat strange?" All the Saints in the Xuanji Ring, some had already recognized the origin of the pond. "The Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground?" Qiu Tian Hui's initial expression was extremely solemn, but then he rejoiced, clapping his hands and exclaiming, "The path to escape lies within this!" Saying this, he leaped down and plunged into the pond water. Li Fan knew the profound mystery of the so-called Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground, also known as the Fishing Pond. Only the true angler could see the myriad mysteries within the Fishing Pond. Only by truly engaging in fishing could one hook various treasures from the Fishing Pond. And what Qiu Tian Hui did next greatly exceeded Li Fan's expectations. He did not hold a fishing rod, but used himself as bait. He lured the Mountains and Seas Angler from the other side of the Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground! "Could it be that he intends to escape Mountains and Seas with the help of the Mountains and Seas Angler?" "It's merely moving from one cage to another, perhaps even falling into the Angler's net, losing control of himself, and meeting a more tragic end." "With his perception and wisdom, he should not take such an unwise action." While the Saints were still discussing, Qiu Xin Hui had already been pulled away by the Mountains and Seas Angler in an instant. There was nothing unexpected about it. The Mountains and Seas Angler was also a Saint-level existence in Mountains and Seas. The gap between him and a cultivator who had not yet transcended was immeasurable. Qiu Tian Hui had no room to resist, which was normal. If he could contend with the Sea Angler... then he would absolutely possess a great fortune like Li Fan, who had 'Return to Truth.' Unfortunately, he did not. The Xuanji Ring fell into silence, and all the Saints looked to the Three Saints for an answer. Saint Lianshan merely signaled gently, and the Saints continued to watch. As expected, after Qiu Tian Hui disappeared and the Fishing Pond fell silent for a period, changes occurred again. The pond water churned, intensifying. It was as if something was about to emerge from the pond. After a moment, with a bang, the entire Fishing Pond exploded. This Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground vanished from this possibility, and a figure, having departed, reappeared in this place. It was Qiu Tian Hui himself! Although he seemed to have only left for a short time, Qiu Tian Hui's clothing, appearance, and even his spiritual state were vastly different from before. He bowed respectfully towards the original location of the Fishing Pond. Qiu Tian Hui looked up at the sky again, his previous confusion completely gone. "Just as I suspected before, although Mountains and Seas are separated by Dao Annihilation, as long as Mountains and Seas themselves still exist, it means that the disconnected segments of Mountains and Seas are faintly connected by veins. Ordinary means cannot perceive them. Only through various special methods can one follow these veins." "The Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground is one such method. However, it is already occupied by Senior Angler; it can no longer accommodate others. I can only find another way..." Qiu Tian Hui waved his hand, restoring the damage caused by the annihilation of the Fishing Pond to its original state, and then turned to return home. Indeed, Qiu Tian Hui had a Taoist companion. They had grown up together, supporting each other on their cultivation journey, and had reached this point together. Qiu Tian Hui's cultivation had reached the pinnacle of possibility, and his companion was only slightly inferior, having long ago attained the realm of the Nameless True Immortal. She was only half a step away from Transcension. Her name was Shao Zi Dai. Her path was one of love! Qiu Tian Hui had disappeared for several years, his whereabouts unknown, his life or death uncertain. However, Shao Zi Dai had never worried that he would leave her someday. She firmly believed that no matter what happened, Qiu Tian Hui would eventually return. At this moment, Qiu Tian Hui reappeared, their eyes met, and a thousand unspoken words were conveyed in a gentle embrace. This was followed by a passionate spiritual and physical union. Qiu Tian Hui's experiences were all known to Shao Zi Dai during this cultivation. "In that case, Senior Angler is truly a pure angler. Only interested in the act of fishing itself, not the prey. It's quite fortunate that you could escape..." Shao Zi Dai murmured with a light laugh, nestled in Qiu Tian Hui's embrace. Qiu Tian Hui said with some self-satisfaction, "Where is it mere luck? The moment I saw that Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground, I discerned the true nature of the Angler on the other side. That's why I dared to use myself as bait and venture into the unknown." "Then has Husband thought of a complete plan?" Shao Zi Dai did not refute but asked again. Qiu Tian Hui's expression suddenly turned solemn. "I already have a vague idea. That is..." "Mountains and Seas Together!" "Mountains and Seas Together? What does these four words mean?" Not only Shao Zi Dai, but all the Saints in the Xuanji Ring could not help but lend their ears. "The veins of Mountains and Seas run through antiquity and into the distant, unknowable future." "For us to transcend, to take this step, we should not cross into the interior of Mountains and Seas. Instead, we should walk along the direction of Mountains and Seas' life," Qiu Tian Hui said, his eyes bright, pointing upwards.

Chapter 1725: Giving Birth to a Saint Alive

Qiu Tianhui’s gesture, perhaps by mere coincidence, happened to be directed towards the Saints observing from outside the projected image.

The Saints remained impassive, listening as Qiu Tianhui continued.

“Mountains and Seas have existed continuously since antiquity, like a rushing river. To be immersed within it, it is naturally difficult to alter its form; one can only follow the flow.”

“Ordinary methods of transcendence involve leaping out and standing above the river. If one is sufficiently strong and positioned high enough, one can then survey the entire panorama of Mountains and Seas!”

“However, situated in the later stages of Mountains and Seas’ life cycle, many opportunities have been depleted, and hidden powerful beings lie in wait. Even those of extraordinary talent would find it difficult to change this situation.”

Shao Zidai cast her gaze beyond the heavens, as if perceiving the true state of Mountains and Seas, and nodded slightly in agreement. “Then, what is the method of transcendence your husband speaks of?”

“To align with the form of Mountains and Seas, and harmonize with its intent. Continuing like the ever-present, spontaneously regenerating. Then one’s fate will be intertwined with Mountains and Seas, and one’s spirit will coexist with Mountains and Seas,” Qiu Tianhui’s answer was exceedingly esoteric.

Yet, Shao Zidai seemed to be in perfect sync with his thoughts. As her eyes shifted, she understood his intention.

With a gentle wave of her hand, a phantom image of a rushing river appeared before them.

The image focused on the underwater, where a nascent undercurrent grew vigorously. Following the direction of the river’s flow, it strived to extend and perpetuate itself.

“My husband’s meaning is to be like this undercurrent, utilizing the continuous momentum of Mountains and Seas to bolster our lifespans.”

Qiu Tianhui smiled slightly. “You understand me best, Zidai!”

His expression was filled with pride. “The lifespans of beings within Mountains and Seas are finite. Even so-called transcendent experts cannot escape the tribulation of decay. Yet, this method borrows the grand momentum of Mountains and Seas to extend one’s own lifespan. For as long as Mountains and Seas endure, one’s life will continue indefinitely, free from the anxieties of ordinary lifespans!”

“And as one’s own life extends, one occupies more of Mountains and Seas. Until…”

Qiu Tianhui pointed at the vision Shao Zidai had conjured. Originally, the undercurrent was only as thick as a thumb.

But as it continually surged forward, gathering more and more surrounding vapor, its form gradually thickened.

By the end of the river, it had actually come to occupy half of the underwater territory.

It was almost on par with the entirety of Mountains and Seas!

“This is what is meant by ‘Mountains and Seas Together’!”

Shao Zidai gazed at the scene her husband had conjured for her, captivated and lost in thought.

“It sounds plausible, but is it truly feasible?” After a long silence, she still harbored some doubts.

“I’ve heard that Mountains and Seas are separated by Dao Annihilation. Are we not like fish trapped in a pond? How can we achieve continuous existence like Mountains and Seas themselves?”

“Ordinary methods of transcendence are fraught with immense difficulty. Let alone this unconventional method of transcendence. It is akin to stealing the divine essence of Mountains and Seas and altering its very form. Without great fortune, great perseverance, and great destiny, it cannot be accomplished.”

“Given our origins as beings of Mountains and Seas, attempting such a rebellious act is like throwing an egg against a rock. However…”

“My dear, do not forget that Mountains and Seas are not eternally prosperous.Judging from the current scene of Dao Annihilation raging, it seems Mountains and Seas are gradually losing the battle. Mountains and Seas are in decline and are struggling to manage themselves. This presents us with an opportunity!”

Shao Zidai vaguely understood Qiu Tianhui’s intention.

But then she frowned slightly. “Together with Mountains and Seas. Yet Mountains and Seas are ultimately in decline. This method…”

Qiu Tianhui chuckled. “Where in the world is there a perfect method? My dear, you should not be too greedy. Given our origins, if we are fortunate enough to cultivate to a level of parity with Mountains and Seas, that would already be more than enough. Furthermore…”

“Let’s take it one step at a time. Once we reach that level, perhaps new methods will emerge. A living being will not be suffocated to death.”

Shao Zidai also laughed, no longer dwelling on the issue.

The two then spent several hundred years intimately discussing this so-called “Mountains and Seas Together” method, never leaving their cave dwelling.

Then, the scene abruptly cut off.

Within the Xuanji Ring, all the Saints looked at the Three Saints in bewilderment.

They did not understand the meaning.

“This method of ‘Mountains and Seas Together,’ while sounding plausible, requires immense effort to truly succeed… Even with our talents, it seems difficult,” Prying Opportunity frowned deeply, shaking his head after careful consideration. “But since the Three Saints said it is a crucial node of the Mountains and Seas’ veins… could it be that he actually succeeded?” Bai Xiao was somewhat incredulous.

“But if he really succeeded, why have we never seen these two individuals in the subsequent Mountains and Seas?” Judgment asked again, scanning the current Mountains and Seas outside the Xuanji Ring.

Indeed, Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai were nowhere to be found among them.

“Are they truly absent?”

“Although Qiu Tianhui is not present, there is Li Tianhui and Zhang Tianhui. Although Shao Zidai is not present, there is Xia Zidai and Bai Zidai.”

As Saint Lianshan spoke, numerous light spots appeared scattered throughout the Mountains and Seas.

Following their gaze, they saw beings across different possibilities within Mountains and Seas.

Their origins, circumstances, realms, and strengths were all different.

If Saint Lianshan had not collectively marked them, even with the combined eyesight of the Saints present, it would have been difficult to discern their commonalities.

“Could it be that these individuals are incarnations of Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai? Impossible!” The Saints, confident in their own perception, observed carefully for another moment and then unanimously shook their heads in disbelief.

At this moment, Shou Qiu spoke, “They are not Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai themselves, but their descendants. Indeed, a remarkable technique!”

“Descendants?” The Saints were stunned and looked again.

However, they became even more confused.

“Shou Qiu Gong, what do you mean by that? If there is a blood relationship between them, we would not be unable to distinguish it.”

Shou Qiu Gong said, “Of course, I am not referring to ordinary blood descendants. Rather…”

“If Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai did not exist, these beings would not have appeared in Mountains and Seas. By borrowing the power of Mountains and Seas, they gave birth to these beings. This can also be called their parents.”

“Precisely so.” Saint Guihai spoke up in agreement at this moment, providing the answer.

“Giving birth to beings by borrowing the power of Mountains and Seas?” The Saints savored these words and slowly began to understand what Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai had been doing in their cave dwelling for hundreds of years.

They were not indulging in physical pleasure but were truly cultivating and comprehending the Dao!

“The evolution of beings in Mountains and Seas is one of the fundamental Daos of Mountains and Seas itself. How could Qiu Tianhui and his wife meddle in it?” The Saints were all somewhat shocked, looking towards Saint Guihai.

Saint Guihai’s expression was impassive. “It is not exactly meddling. Just as Qiu Tianhui said before, they are merely borrowing the momentum of Mountains and Seas. As long as Mountains and Seas exist for a day, they will continue to evolve beings. This is one of the hidden important veins of Mountains and Seas.”

“This couple is indeed exceptionally talented, to have actually glimpsed its mystery and intertwined their power within it.”

Saint Lianshan pointed to various spots on the panoramic view of Mountains and Seas again. Countless light spots, like stars, lit up simultaneously. They were dense and covered the entire Mountains and Seas! From the Mountains and Seas where Qiu Tianhui originated, all the way to the end of time. Although Mountains and Seas were gradually declining, the starlight never ceased!

“As expected!”

Li Fan squinted his eyes and looked at the end of Mountains and Seas, recalling Qiu Xinhui, the last Saint of Mountains and Seas.

“At the end of time, the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas had withered to such an extent, yet such an astonishing figure as the Last Saint, Qiu Xinhui, was born, as if he alone occupied most of the spiritual energy at the end of Mountains and Seas. Yet, his origin was ordinary, with no family heritage. If Qiu Tianhui’s ‘Mountains and Seas Together’ method is the crystallization condensed from the end of Mountains and Seas after a lifetime, then it makes sense.”

Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De shared the same heart and mind. As their thoughts turned rapidly, Li Fan’s idea was met with agreement from the other two.

“This method of Qiu Tianhui’s, borrowing the momentum of Mountains and Seas to strengthen oneself. The weaker Mountains and Seas become, the stronger he becomes. Until the end of time, when Mountains and Seas are at their weakest, his power can be maximized. The Last Saint, Qiu Xinhui, truly fulfilled what Qiu Tianhui demonstrated countless years ago, acting as an equal counterweight to Mountains and Seas itself. He could even do things that Mountains and Seas could not, single-handedly changing the tide and saving Mountains and Seas from Dao Annihilation.” Shou Qiu commented.

“However, Qiu Tianhui and Qiu Xinhui do not seem to be the same person. This so-called method of transcendence…”

“It’s truly hard to say,” Dao De mused.

Meanwhile, in the Xuanji Ring, Saint Lianshan spoke again. “Qiu Tianhui and his wife, although they hid in the forefront Mountains and Seas, have directly influenced the crucial vein of the evolution of beings in Mountains and Seas, connecting them across millennia.”

“Mountains and Seas are constantly changing. The evolution and birth of beings are also ceaseless. Billions of beings, compared to Mountains and Seas, are merely ants. But after all, they are born from Mountains and Seas and grow within Mountains and Seas. If such a large number of beings were to instantly disappear on the scale of Mountains and Seas…”

“It would be enough to cause severe damage to Mountains and Seas. More importantly…”

Saint Lianshan’s expression became solemn. “We still do not know how Qiu Tianhui and his wife intervened in the vein of the evolution of beings in Mountains and Seas. If this method is controlled by the Void Realm…”

“Then the Void Realm could, just like Qiu Tianhui, instantly deploy countless clones of Dao Annihilation throughout the interior of Mountains and Seas. The defenses of Mountains and Seas would likely be riddled with holes in an instant.”

“This is also why the Mountains and Seas ahead are such an important node.”

After the explanation from the Three Saints, everyone finally understood.

“May I ask Saint Lianshan, what is the actual strength of this Qiu Tianhui? Logically speaking, being able to interfere with the Great Dao of Beings in Mountains and Seas would at least require Saint cultivation. Yet, his method of transcendence seems unable to feed back to himself…” Prying Opportunity said uncertainly.

It was Saint Guihai who answered.

Guihai pointed to the myriad beings like stars in the panoramic view of Mountains and Seas. “These beings were born because of them, and they are the crystallization of this couple’s Dao. The more beings there are, the stronger their power naturally becomes. They do not need the so-called ordinary methods of feedback, because they are borrowing the momentum of Mountains and Seas, so each birth of a being represents an improvement in their cultivation.”

“Therefore, in the previous scene, we only observed so much. At a certain moment, they suddenly disappeared from our sight, which means that through continuous accumulation, they are no longer inferior to us.”

The Saints were instantly silenced upon hearing this.

With their knowledge and experience, they found it truly difficult to imagine that there was such an unconventional cultivation method in Mountains and Seas.

Directly leaping from the realm of Nameless True Immortal to a Saint of Mountains and Seas. And not just any Saint, but a top-tier one.

“What a grand method of borrowing the momentum of Mountains and Seas. I see that Mountains and Seas are declining day by day, and I suppose these two are partly responsible,” Saint Xuanpin snorted coldly, filled with indignation.

Saint Tai Yi smiled. “The demise of Mountains and Seas began with the story of devouring the Gods in the past. Due to the act of splitting their spirits back then, Dao Annihilation emerged. The merging, combining, and eventual dissolution of Mountains and Seas is their destined fate. It has nothing to do with Qiu Tianhui and his wife.”

“Even without Qiu Tianhui, the fate of Mountains and Seas at the end of time would not have been much better.”

“Strictly speaking, this couple, with mortal bodies, differentiated, stole, and occupied parts of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas. As their Dao was achieved, they can be considered a part of Mountains and Seas.”

Xuanpin’s indignant expression instantly vanished. Tai Yi’s words had already made it very clear. In a sense, Qiu Tianhui and his wife were of the same nature as Lianshan, Guihai, and Tai Yi. It was just that one was a manifestation of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, while the other had stolen and seized partial control of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas through beings.

“Since they are a part of Mountains and Seas, they should be able to jointly resist the Void Realm.”

“However, the reality is not so.”

“Do you all remember Qiu Tianhui’s words earlier, ‘take it one step at a time’?”

“I don’t know what he saw, but facing the conflict between Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm, he directly chose to hide.” Saint Lianshan said with a smile.

“We can only be sure that the couple is still in the Mountains and Seas ahead. But we don’t know where they are hiding.”

Upon hearing this, the Saints couldn’t help but frown. With strength comparable to the Three Saints, if they truly intended to hide, it would indeed be difficult to find them.

“Could it be that even if Mountains and Seas fall, they can still hide indefinitely?” Li Fan suddenly blurted out.

“Daoist Universe Cycle, don’t speak in anger. Although they are difficult to find, there are still traces to follow. If Mountains and Seas were truly swallowed by Dao Annihilation, the Void Realm would definitely dispatch forces from various timelines to seize the secrets of Mountains and Seas’ beings. The situation would become even more difficult to handle,” Bai Xiao said with a bitter smile.

The Saints pondered amongst themselves, and finally, their gazes converged back on the Three Saints.

“What is the plan now?”

“Not long ago, the Void Realm attempted to kill us and failed. However, their containment force on the Mountains and Seas ahead has not diminished but increased. Although we have the boost of True Spirit Infusion, reconnecting Mountains and Seas will not be as easy as before.”

“In addition to Dao Annihilation’s invasion, any Void Realm Incarnations could launch surprise attacks.”

Upon hearing this, all the Saints present, except for Li Fan and his companions, changed their expressions slightly.

Saint Lianshan continued, “Forcibly reconnecting Mountains and Seas might provoke extreme reactions from the Void Realm. We need to proceed slowly.”

“On one hand, we need to ensure the safety of the Mountains and Seas ahead.”

“On the other hand…”

“We need to find Qiu Tianhui and his wife.”

“They are the biggest variables in this battle. If they are not under control…”

Saint Lianshan’s voice became a little deeper.

“Although they are hiding, they have never stopped borrowing the momentum of beings. We can start from here to track their whereabouts,” Saint Guihai added.

“Ordinary methods cannot trace the beings of Mountains and Seas. Only by constantly reincarnating within Mountains and Seas. If we happen to encounter Qiu Tianhui and his wife during the ‘birth of beings’…”

“There will be a connection. We can then trace their whereabouts backwards.”

The Three Saints exchanged glances and then looked at Li Fan, saying, “The Void Realm Incarnation is specifically targeting us. Naturally, we shall deal with it ourselves.”

“And with Daoist Fan presiding over Mountains and Seas, it should remain safe.” The Three Saints’ answer was within Li Fan’s expectations, but he shook his head slightly.

“I can enlighten Saints, but I cannot protect Mountains and Seas.”

“Firstly, after continuous enlightenments, even Mountains and Seas have become somewhat depleted. Secondly, as you all saw earlier, the Map of Mountains and Seas only possesses the ‘form’ of Mountains and Seas, not its substance. To withstand the residual waves of battle…”

“I fear my strength is insufficient.” Li Fan said truthfully.

Chapter 1726: The End Reaches the Beginning

"A move that annihilated three Saints, astonishing everyone present!"

The Three Saints were filled with uncontrollable shock. Even though they knew Shou Qiu possessed the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, they had never expected his transformation to be so powerful!

As Shou Qiu erased the Void Realm Incarnations in the surrounding void, the Three Saints noticed his physical form becoming transparent. They deduced it was the price of forcefully activating his Great Dao. However, Shou Qiu's comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood had not yet reached its peak.

Shou Qiu continued to dominate the battlefield, erasing Void Realm Incarnations with ease. He mused that with "Return to Truth," this process would have been much simpler. He felt a greater storm brewing from the Void Realm. He recognized Dao Annihilation as pawns and Void Realm Incarnations as generals, but the next arrivals would be high-ranking generals.

The Void Realm was concentrating its forces to attack this segment of Mountains and Seas, forming a monstrous, pressure-filled tsunami. Shou Qiu stood firm, shouldering the terrifying pressure, his body becoming increasingly dim and transparent. He reflected on the profoundness of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood and the self-destructive price of its use. Li Fan, hidden in the shadows, felt Shou Qiu's words resonate deeply and resolved to act according to his heart now that he had the strength to contend with the Three Saints.

The pressure from the Void Realm suddenly lightened, replaced by a figure confronting Shou Qiu—an exact manifestation of Shou Qiu himself, condensed from the data of countless destroyed Shou Qius. Shou Qiu realized this opponent was a part of himself, formed by the collective efforts of countless Void Realm Incarnations, designed to stall or assimilate him.

The Void Realm Shou Qiu attacked with world-shattering power, trapping Shou Qiu in a vortex of destruction. Shou Qiu activated the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood to protect himself, but his attempt to negate the Void Realm Shou Qiu was less effective, as this opponent had gained thickness from the accumulation of countless paper figures. Shou Qiu devised a countermeasure: a mutually destructive move to cut down the high-ranking general and perhaps force the mastermind to reveal themselves.

He abandoned his defenses, allowing himself to be assimilated while unleashing a "Blade of Truth is Falsehood" upon himself. This self-slaughter, smoother than carving an ox, caused Shou Qiu's projection to dim. The Void Realm Shou Qiu was shocked, but the ripple effect of "Truth is Falsehood" traversed time, slaying the past, present, and future Shou Qius, fueling the Void Realm Shou Qiu's self-immolation. Shou Qiu laughed heartily as he perished, turning everything into nothingness.

Shou Qiu's demise was a chain reaction, nullifying the Void Realm's strike and causing the transformation of truth and falsehood to spread uncontrollably, disintegrating the Void Realm. The Three Saints realized the Void Realm could be erased by "Truth and Falsehood." However, they felt a greater sense of crisis as faint black threads, like spider silk, wove a net, halting the Void Realm's disintegration and patching it up. A single thread emerged, originating from Shou Qiu's demise and heading towards Li Fan's hiding place. The Void Realm, realizing Shou Qiu was merely a probing piece, was attempting to find the true Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood.

Chapter 1727: The Invisible Net Descends from the Sky

The Void Net enveloped the battlefield. Li Fan, who had silently recited 'Return to Truth' upon Shou Qiu's demise, found his hiding place locked by the Void Net. The rhythmic poundings of an invisible hammer interrupted his casting process, causing cracks in the white mist of 'Return to Truth.' The Void Realm mastermind had found an opportunity.

Li Fan remained calm, drawing upon Shou Qiu's detached state of mind. He understood that the rhythmic poundings only interrupted his casting and that the Void Realm mastermind couldn't stop 'Return to Truth' but could prolong the brief moment. He recognized the black threads invading were akin to Yuan Shi Bai Gu's methods in a past life. The Void Realm mastermind knew they couldn't stop 'Return to Truth' but wanted to replace Li Fan.

Li Fan coldly snorted and began to eliminate the disruptive influence. He used his fingertips like a brush, writing in the air with strokes mirroring the invading black lines. "When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth!" Each stroke erased a method of the Void Realm mastermind. Under 'Concentric Unity,' Shou Qiu's enlightenment became Li Fan's enlightenment. He could now do as Shou Qiu did, annihilating Saints' incarnations and repelling Void Realm attacks. Unlike Shou Qiu, Li Fan, having undergone hundreds of 'Return to Truth' baptisms, ignored the negative effects of 'Truth is Falsehood.'

His writing became smoother, erasing all black lines. He declared the authority of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, transcending all. The white mist then swallowed all light, and darkness returned. Li Fan, however, forced his eyes open, traversing towards the end of Mountains and Seas, waiting for the appearance of the 'Stars.' He realized only the Stars were worth 'Return to Truth's' action.

Fatigue washed over him, a weariness born from being consumed. Li Fan realized he was being consumed, his True Spirit depleting, experiencing a feeling of death. The transcendent state brought by Shou Qiu had receded. Fear, confusion, and doubt overshadowed his drowsiness, maintaining only a sliver of consciousness.

After an unknown period, the consumption stopped. He sensed the end of Mountains and Seas, a ray of starlight piercing the darkness. Mountains and Seas, and the Void Realm, reappeared. Li Fan fell into a deep sleep.

Anchor Point Year 1. Li Fan, upon regaining consciousness, was initially confused but then recalled Shou Qiu's sacrifice, the Void Realm mastermind, and the True Spirit extraction. The hollow feeling remained. He called out to 'Return to Truth,' demanding an explanation. He realized previous activations were similar, but this time he witnessed the entire process. He pondered why 'Return to Truth' was attached to him, its purpose unknown.

He accepted this reality, realizing 'Return to Truth' would activate even after his death. He had glimpsed the truth of its activation, but it brought more doubts. Why extract his True Spirit to recreate Mountains and Seas? Where did his infinite True Spirit come from? The hollow feeling had disappeared, but the near-death experience was vivid. He realized his foundation should be built excluding 'Return to Truth,' not including it.

He sat on Jieli Mountain for years, accepting his situation. He practiced "Truth is Falsehood, Falsehood is Truth," realizing his comprehension of 'Truth is Falsehood' far surpassed 'Falsehood is Truth.' He could erase Void Realm's effects but not generate disasters out of thin air. He concluded the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was pieced together by two Daos: 'Truth is Falsehood, Falsehood is Truth' and 'Return to Truth.' He felt he needed to reach a higher state, like God or the Stars, to unravel mysteries. The desire to break free from all shackles reignited. He decided to inherit Shou Qiu Gong's memories and await changes within the Xuanji Ring.

Chapter 1728: Great Micro Holy Emperor's Transformation

Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De entered the Void Realm. The Three Saints and other Saints observed, discussing the variable Shou Qiu might bring. Shou Qiu, having merged with his other self, headed towards the battle. Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De hid in the shadows, observing the six-Saint battle.

When the Void Realm Incarnations unleashed their primordial malevolence—the Fate Rope binding Lianshan, the Turtle Shell suppressing Guihai, and the Ancestral Bone capturing Tai Yi—the Three Saints were forced to unleash their own. A stalemate ensued.

Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De, witnessing the Three Saints' hesitation, realized they feared severing connections within Mountains and Seas, not death itself. Shou Qiu speculated that their primordial malevolence, originating from a fallen True God, might pierce the Void Realm's obstruction and expand to the entire Mountains and Seas.

The Void Realm Incarnations, with near-limitless power, attacked recklessly. The Three Saints, though disadvantaged, held their ground. Li Fan and his companions, knowing the Three Saints' fated demise, patiently observed, gaining insights into the Daos of Mountains and Seas. Li Fan felt his next life as a Saint of Mountains and Seas would be even more powerful.

As the battle culminated, the Three Saints' 'Lines of Mountains and Seas' began to erode. New primordial malevolence from the Void Realm descended upon their main bodies. Shou Qiu, with Guihai's divine essence, moved to rescue Tai Yi. Li Fan, embodying Lianshan's divine essence, aided Guihai, while Dao De, with Tai Yi's divine essence, helped Lianshan.

The Three Saints, sensing their own spiritual senses on Li Fan and his companions, understood their method: "Using divine essence to restrain, using spiritual sense to subdue." The primordial malevolence, embodying the resentment of discarded remnants of Mountains and Seas, attacked fiercely. Li Fan described the situation as "mountains collapsing and seas boiling," a world-ending catastrophe. He used the Universe Cycle Great Dao to resolve the pressure, pushing his comprehension to its limit.

Shou Qiu easily blocked the Ancestral Bone, while Dao De, though weaker, continuously dissolved the Fate Rope's influence with Li Fan's True Spirit replenishment. The Void Realm mastermind, seeing the primordial malevolence neutralized, fell into contemplation. After a moment, twelve more instances of primordial malevolence attacked. Li Fan, realizing using the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood would lead to the same outcome as before, decided to resist head-on. He declared they would test their limits, drawing inspiration from his hundred lifetimes of foundation building. Shou Qiu and Dao De agreed, their confidence bolstered. The Void Realm mastermind, seeing Li Fan and his companions' strength and their concealed use of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, decided to withdraw its forces, deeming it not worth the cost.

Chapter 1729: The Mountains and Seas Are Extreme and Devour

The Void Realm's forces withdrew, but the Dao Annihilation barrier ahead intensified. Li Fan sensed the Void Realm's plan to delay until other temporal nodes were resolved. He reflected on the irony of the Void Realm abandoning the very place where the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood resided.

The Three Saints, their imminent doom averted, acknowledged Li Fan's group's strength. Li Fan, downplaying his own abilities, credited the 'shared heart and mind' with Shou Qiu and Dao De. The Three Saints, impressed by their amplified combat power, decided to proceed with reconnecting Mountains and Seas.

With Li Fan's support in True Spirit Infusion and the combined efforts of six Saints, the hundred thousand years of separated Mountains and Seas were reconnected. All Saints benefited, their strength significantly increasing. Li Fan, however, noticed a change: the True Emperor's existence had vanished from the newly formed Mountains and Seas, replaced by an Immortal Emperor named [Lingxi]. This divergence into two possibilities worried Li Fan and Shou Qiu. They speculated that the True Emperor's fate at the end of his reign, possibly linked to an opportunity for transcendence, might hold the key. Shou Qiu suggested that the "Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes," combined with the 'Return to Truth,' might offer clues.
